 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
 devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet
 oṃ namo bhagavate tasmai vyāsāyāmitatejase
 yasya prasādād vakṣyāmi nārāyaṇakathāṃ śubhām                 
 tato 'jñānatamondhasya kāvasthā jagato bhavet
 janamejaya uvāca
 mayasya tu kathāṃ divyāṃ śrotum icchāmi sattama
 sabhāṃ caiva kṛtāṃ tena dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
 janamejaya uvāca
 rakṣitaḥ pāṇḍavā   mayo nāma mahāsuraḥ
 kṛṣṇāc ca pāvakāc caiva pārthenāmitatejasā
 sa cakāra yad ūrdhvaṃ vai karma pratyayakārakam
 tad brūhi bhagavan sarvaṃ prāṇadāya kirīṭine
 janamejayaḥ
 arjuno jayatāṃ śreṣṭho mokṣayitvā mayaṃ tadā
 kiṃ cakāra mahātejās tan me brūhi dvijottama
 śṛṇu rājann avahitaś caritaṃ pūrvakasya te
 mokṣayitvā mayaṃ tatra pārthaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
 gāṇḍīvaṃ kārmukaśreṣṭhaṃ tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau
 divyāny astrāṇi rājendra durlabhāni nṛpair bhuvi
 rathadhvajaṃ patākāś ca śvetāśvaiḥ saha vīryavān
 etāni pāvakāt prāpya mudā paramayā yutaḥ
 tasthau pārtho mahāvīryas tadā saha mayena saḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato 'bravīn mayaḥ pārthaṃ vāsudevasya saṃnidhau
b pāṇḍavena paritrātas tatkṛtaṃ pratyanusmaran
c prāñjaliḥ ślakṣṇayā vācā pūjayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
a asmāc ca kṛṣṇāt saṃkruddhāt pāvakāc ca didhakṣataḥ
c tvayā trāto 'smi kaunteya brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
d ahaṃ hi viśvakarmā vai asurāṇāṃ paraṃtapa
d tasmāt te vismayaṃ kiṃ cit kuryām anyaiḥ suduṣkaram
d evam ukto mahāvīryaḥ pārtho māyāvidaṃ mayam
d dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ kaunteyaḥ prahasan vākyam abravīt
 arjuna uvāca
a kṛtam eva tvayā sarvaṃ svasti gaccha mahāsura
c prītimān bhava me nityaṃ prītimanto vayaṃ ca te
d prāptopakārād arthaṃ hi nāharāmīti me vratam
 maya uvāca
a yuktam etat tvayi vibho yathāttha puruṣarṣabha
c prītipūrvam ahaṃ kiṃ cit kartum icchāmi bhārata
a ahaṃ hi viśvakarmā vai dānavānāṃ mahākaviḥ
c so 'haṃ vai tvatkṛte kiṃ cit kartum icchāmi pāṇḍava
d dānavānāṃ purā pārtha prāsādā hi mayā kṛtāḥ
d ramyāṇi sukhadarśāni bhogāḍhyāni sahasraśaḥ
d udyānāni ca ramyāṇi sarāṃsi vividhāni ca
d vicitrāṇi ca śastrāṇi rathāḥ kāmagamās tathā
d nagarāṇi viśālāni sāṭṭaprākāratoraṇaiḥ
d vāhanāni ca mukhyāni vicitrāṇi sahasraśaḥ
d bilāni ramaṇīyāni sukhayuktāni vai bhṛśam
d ete kṛtā mayā sarve tasmād icchāmi phalguna
 arjuna uvāca
a prāṇakṛcchrād vimuktaṃ tvam ātmānaṃ manyase mayā
c evaṃ gate na śakṣyāmi kiṃ cit kārayituṃ tvayā
a na cāpi tava saṃkalpaṃ mogham icchāmi dānava
c kṛṣṇasya kriyatāṃ kiṃ cit tathā pratikṛtaṃ mayi
d mayaḥ
d vāsudeva mayā kartuṃ kim icchasi śubhānana
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a codito vāsudevas tu mayena bharatarṣabha
c muhūrtam iva saṃdadhyau kim ayaṃ codyatām iti
d naipuṇaṃ divi śilpasya saṃcintya mayam abravīt
d tato vicintya manasā lokanāthaḥ prajāpatiḥ
a codayām āsa taṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sabhā vai kriyatām iti
b yadi tvaṃ kartukāmo 'si priyaṃ śilpavatāṃ vara
c dharmarājasya daiteya yādṛśīm iha manyase
d anavāpyāṃ manuṣyeṇa tādṛśīṃ kuru vai sabhām
d asurān mānuṣān devān gandharvān rākṣasān api
a yāṃ kṛtāṃ nānukuryus te mānavāḥ prekṣya vismitāḥ
c manuṣyaloke kṛtsne 'smiṃs tādṛśīṃ kuru vai sabhām
a yatra divyān abhiprāyān paśyema vihitāṃs tvayā
c āsurān mānuṣāṃś caiva tāṃ sabhāṃ kuru vai maya
a pratigṛhya tu tad vākyaṃ saṃprahṛṣṭo mayas tadā
c vimānapratimāṃ cakre pāṇḍavasya sabhāṃ mudā
a tataḥ kṛṣṇaś ca pārthaś ca dharmarāje yudhiṣṭhire
c sarvam etad yathāvedya darśayām āsatur mayam
a tasmai yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pūjāṃ yathārham akarot tadā
b āsanaṃ kalpayām āsa pūjayām āsa ca prabhuḥ
c sa tu tāṃ pratijagrāha mayaḥ satkṛtya satkṛtaḥ
a sa pūrvadevacaritaṃ tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
b saṃprahṛṣṭo mayo rājan pāṇḍavasya ca tattvataḥ
c kathayām āsa daiteyaḥ pāṇḍuputreṣu bhārata
a sa kālaṃ kaṃ cid āśvasya viśvakarmā pracintya ca
c sabhāṃ pracakrame kartuṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
a abhiprāyeṇa pārthānāṃ kṛṣṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
c puṇye 'hani mahātejāḥ kṛtakautukamaṅgalaḥ
a tarpayitvā dvijaśreṣṭhān pāyasena sahasraśaḥ
c dhanaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dattvā tebhya eva ca vīryavān
d iti sarvavidhiṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam avartata
a sarvartuguṇasaṃpannāṃ divyarūpāṃ manoramām
b janaughasya rathaughasya yānayugyasya caiva hi
c daśakiṣkusahasrāṃ tāṃ māpayām āsa sarvataḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a uṣitvā khāṇḍavaprasthe sukhavāsaṃ janārdanaḥ
c pārthaiḥ prītisamāyuktaiḥ pūjanārho 'bhipūjitaḥ
a gamanāya matiṃ cakre pitur darśanalālasaḥ
c dharmarājam athāmantrya pṛthāṃ ca pṛthulocanaḥ
a vavande caraṇau mūrdhnā jagadvandyaḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ
c sa tayā mūrdhny upāghrātaḥ pariṣvaktaś ca keśavaḥ
a dadarśānantaraṃ kṛṣṇo bhaginīṃ svāṃ mahāyaśāḥ
c tām upetya hṛṣīkeśaḥ prītyā bāṣpasamanvitaḥ
a arthyaṃ tathyaṃ hitaṃ vākyaṃ laghu yuktam anuttamam
c uvāca bhagavān bhadrāṃ subhadrāṃ bhadrabhāṣiṇīm
a tayā svajanagāmīni śrāvito vacanāni saḥ
c saṃpūjitaś cāpy asakṛc chirasā cābhivāditaḥ
a tām anujñāpya vārṣṇeyaḥ pratinandya ca bhāminīm
c dadarśānantaraṃ kṛṣṇāṃ dhaumyaṃ cāpi janārdanaḥ
a vavande ca yathānyāyaṃ dhaumyaṃ puruṣasattamaḥ
c draupadīṃ sāntvayitvā ca āmantrya ca janārdanaḥ
a bhrātṝn abhyagamad dhīmān pārthena sahito balī
c bhrātṛbhiḥ pañcabhiḥ kṛṣṇo vṛtaḥ śakra ivāmaraiḥ
d yātrākālasya yogyāni karmāṇi garuḍadhvajaḥ
d kartukāmaḥ śucir bhūtvā snātavān samalaṃkṛtaḥ
d āmantrya ca pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pratasthe tasthuṣāṃ varaḥ
d āmantrya ca pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ dhaumyaṃ ca puruṣottamaḥ
a arcayām āsa devāṃś ca dvijāṃś ca yadupuṃgavaḥ
c mālyajapyanamaskārair gandhair uccāvacair api
e sa kṛtvā sarvakāryāṇi pratasthe tasthuṣāṃ varaḥ
f upetya sa yaduśreṣṭho bāhyakakṣāṃ vinirgataḥ
a svasti vācyārhato viprān dadhipātraphalākṣataiḥ
c vasu pradāya ca tataḥ pradakṣiṇam avartata
d tatas tu kṛtamāṅgalyo brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ
a kāñcanaṃ ratham āsthāya tārkṣyaketanam āśugam
c gadācakrāsiśārṅgādyair āyudhaiś ca samanvitam
a tithāv atha ca nakṣatre muhūrte ca guṇānvite
c prayayau puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ sainyasugrīvavāhanaḥ
a anvāruroha cāpy enaṃ premṇā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c apāsya cāsya yantāraṃ dārukaṃ yantṛsattamam
e abhīṣūn saṃprajagrāha svayaṃ kurupatis tadā
a upāruhyārjunaś cāpi cāmaravyajanaṃ sitam
c rukmadaṇḍaṃ bṛhan mūrdhni dudhāvābhipradakṣiṇam
a tathaiva bhīmaseno 'pi yamābhyāṃ sahito vaśī
a   ratham āruhya vīryavān
a chatraṃ śataśalākaṃ ca divyamālyopaśobhitam
a vaiḍūryamaṇidaṇḍaṃ ca cāmīkaravibhūṣitam
a dadhāra tarasā bhīmaś chatraṃ tac chārṅgadhanvane
a upāruhya rathaṃ śīghraṃ cāmaravyajane site
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhūyamānau janārdanam
a bhīmasenārjunau cāpi
c pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayau kṛṣṇam ṛtvik paurajanair vṛtaḥ
a sa tathā bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ keśavaḥ paravīrahā
c anugamyamānaḥ śuśubhe śiṣyair iva guruḥ priyaiḥ
d abhimanyuṃ ca saubhadraṃ vṛddhaiḥ parivṛtas tadā
d ratham āropya niryāto dhaumyo brāhmaṇapuṃgavaḥ
d indraprastham atikramya krośamātraṃ mahādyutiḥ
a pārtham āmantrya govindaḥ pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ pūjayitvā bhīmasenaṃ yamau tathā
a pariṣvakto bhṛśaṃ tābhyāṃ yamābhyām abhivāditaḥ
c tatas taiḥ saṃvidaṃ kṛtvā yathāvan madhusūdanaḥ
d yojanārdham atho gatvā kṛṣṇaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samāmantrya nivartasveti bhārata
d tato 'bhivādya govindaḥ pādau jagrāha dharmavit
d utthāpya dharmarājas tu mūrdhny upāghrāya keśavam
d pāṇḍavo yādavaśreṣṭhaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam
d gamyatām ity anujñāpya dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a nivartayitvā ca tadā pāṇḍavān sapadānugān
c svāṃ purīṃ prayayau kṛṣṇaḥ puraṃdara ivāparaḥ
a locanair anujagmus te tam ā dṛṣṭipathāt tadā
b pāṇḍavā yādavaśreṣṭhaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam
c manobhir anujagmus te kṛṣṇaṃ prītisamanvayāt
a atṛptamanasām eva teṣāṃ keśavadarśane
c kṣipram antardadhe śauriś cakṣuṣāṃ priyadarśanaḥ
a akāmā iva pārthās te govindagatamānasāḥ
c nivṛtyopayayuḥ sarve svapuraṃ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
e syandanenātha kṛṣṇo 'pi samaye dvārakām agāt
f sātvatena ca vīreṇa pṛṣṭhato yāyinā tadā
f dārukeṇa ca sūtena sahito devakīsutaḥ
f vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
f sa gato dvārakāṃ viṣṇur garutmān iva vegavān
f nivṛtya dharmarājas tu saha bhrātṛbhir acyutaḥ
f suhṛtparivṛto rājā praviveśa purottamam
f visṛjya suhṛdaḥ sarvān bhrātṝn putrāṃś ca dharmarāṭ
f mumoda puruṣavyāghro draupadyā sahito nṛpa
f keśavo 'pi mudā yuktaḥ praviveśa purottamam
f pūjyamāno yaduśreṣṭhair ugrasenamukhais tathā
f āhukaṃ pitaraṃ vṛddhaṃ mātaraṃ ca yaśasvinīm
f abhivādya balaṃ caiva sthitaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
f pradyumnasāmbaniśaṭhāṃś cārudeṣṇaṃ gadaṃ tathā
f aniruddhaṃ ca bhānuṃ ca pariṣvajya janārdanaḥ
f sa vṛddhair abhyanujñāto rukmiṇyā bhavanaṃ yayau
f mayo 'pi sa mahābhāgaḥ sarvaratnavibhūṣitām
f vidhivat kalpayām āsa sabhāṃ dharmasutāya vai
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a athābravīn mayaḥ pārtham arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varam
c āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi kṣipram eṣyāmi cāpy aham
a uttareṇa tu kailāsaṃ mainākaṃ parvataṃ prati
c yakṣyamāṇeṣu sarveṣu dānaveṣu tadā mayā
e kṛtaṃ maṇimayaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ ramyaṃ bindusaraḥ prati
a sabhāyāṃ satyasaṃdhasya yad āsīd vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ
c āgamiṣyāmi tad gṛhya yadi tiṣṭhati bhārata
d viśrutāṃ triṣu lokeṣu pārtha divyāṃ sabhāṃ tava
d prāṇināṃ vismayakarīṃ tava prītivivardhinīm
d pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kariṣyāmi dhanaṃjaya
a tataḥ sabhāṃ kariṣyāmi pāṇḍavāya yaśasvine
c manaḥprahlādinīṃ citrāṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitām
a asti bindusarasy eva gadā śreṣṭhā kurūdvaha
c nihitā yauvanāśvena rājñā hatvā raṇe ripūn
e suvarṇabindubhiś citrā gurvī bhārasahā dṛḍhā
f svarṇabhārasahasreṇa nirmitā śatrughātinī
a sā vai śatasahasrasya saṃmitā sarvaghātinī
c anurūpā ca bhīmasya gāṇḍīvaṃ bhavato yathā
a vāruṇaś ca mahāśaṅkho devadattaḥ sughoṣavān
c sarvam etat pradāsyāmi bhavate nātra saṃśayaḥ
e ity uktvā so 'suraḥ pārthaṃ prāgudīcīm agād diśam
a uttareṇa tu kailāsaṃ mainākaṃ parvataṃ prati
c hiraṇyaśṛṅgo bhagavān mahāmaṇimayo giriḥ
a ramyaṃ bindusaro nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathīṃ gaṅgām uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ
a yatreṣṭvā sarvabhūtānām īśvareṇa mahātmanā
c āhṛtāḥ kratavo mukhyāḥ śataṃ bharatasattama
a yatra yūpā maṇimayāś cityāś cāpi hiraṇmayāḥ
c śobhārthaṃ vihitās tatra na tu dṛṣṭāntataḥ kṛtāḥ
a yatreṣṭvā sa gataḥ siddhiṃ sahasrākṣaḥ śacīpatiḥ
c yatra bhūtapatiḥ sṛṣṭvā sarvalokān sanātanaḥ
e upāsyate tigmatejā vṛto bhūtaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
f yatreṣṭaṃ munibhiḥ sarvair nāradādyair mumukṣubhiḥ
a naranārāyaṇau brahmā yamaḥ sthāṇuś ca pañcamaḥ
c upāsate yatra satraṃ sahasrayugaparyaye
a yatreṣṭaṃ vāsudevena satrair varṣasahasrakaiḥ
c śraddadhānena satataṃ śiṣṭasaṃpratipattaye
a suvarṇamālino yūpāś cityāś cāpy atibhāsvarāḥ
c dadau yatra sahasrāṇi prayutāni ca keśavaḥ
a tatra gatvā sa jagrāha gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca bhārata
b tasmād girer upādāya śilāḥ surucirāḥ śubhāḥ
c sphāṭikaṃ ca sabhādravyaṃ yad āsīd vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ
e kiṃkaraiḥ saha rakṣobhir agṛhṇāt sarvam eva tat
f tad agṛhṇān mayas tatra gatvā sarvaṃ mahāsuraḥ
a tad āhṛtya tu tāṃ cakre so 'suro 'pratimāṃ sabhām
c viśrutāṃ triṣu lokeṣu divyāṃ maṇimayīṃ śubhām
a gadāṃ ca bhīmasenāya pravarāṃ pradadau tadā
c devadattaṃ ca pārthāya dadau śaṅkham anuttamam
d yasya śaṅkhasya nādena bhūtāni pracakampire
a sabhā tu sā mahārāja śātakumbhamayadrumā
c daśa kiṣkusahasrāṇi samantād āyatābhavat
a yathā vahner yathārkasya somasya ca yathaiva sā
c bhrājamānā tathā divyā babhāra paramaṃ vapuḥ
a pratighnatīva prabhayā prabhām arkasya bhāsvarām
c prababhau jvalamāneva divyā divyena varcasā
a nagameghapratīkāśā divam āvṛtya viṣṭhitā
c āyatā vipulā ślakṣṇā vipāpmā vigataklamā
a uttamadravyasaṃpannā maṇiprākāramālinī
c bahuratnā bahudhanā sukṛtā viśvakarmaṇā
a na dāśārhī sudharmā vā brahmaṇo vāpi tādṛśī
c āsīd rūpeṇa saṃpannā yāṃ cakre 'pratimāṃ mayaḥ
c   śaṃbhor vātha mahātmanaḥ
c atīva rūpasaṃpannāṃ
a tāṃ sma tatra mayenoktā rakṣanti ca vahanti ca
c sabhām aṣṭau sahasrāṇi kiṃkarā nāma rākṣasāḥ
a antarikṣacarā ghorā mahākāyā mahābalāḥ
c raktākṣāḥ piṅgalākṣāś ca śuktikarṇāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ nalinīṃ cakārāpratimāṃ mayaḥ
c vaiḍūryapatravitatāṃ maṇinālamayāmbujām
a padmasaugandhikavatīṃ nānādvijagaṇāyutām
c puṣpitaiḥ paṅkajaiś citrāṃ kūrmamatsyaiś ca śobhitām
a sūpatīrthām akaluṣāṃ sarvartusalilāṃ śubhām
c mārutenaiva coddhūtair muktābindubhir ācitām
d mahāmaṇiśilāpaṭṭabaddhaparyantavedikām
a maṇiratnacitāṃ tāṃ tu ke cid abhyetya pārthivāḥ
c dṛṣṭvāpi nābhyajānanta te 'jñānāt prapatanty uta
a tāṃ sabhām abhito nityaṃ puṣpavanto mahādrumāḥ
c āsan nānāvidhā nīlāḥ śītacchāyā manoramāḥ
a kānanāni sugandhīni puṣkariṇyaś ca sarvaśaḥ
c haṃsakāraṇḍavayutāś cakravākopaśobhitāḥ
a jalajānāṃ ca mālyānāṃ sthalajānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c māruto gandham ādāya pāṇḍavān sma niṣevate
d aṣṭau tāni sahasrāṇi kiṃkarā nāma rākṣasāḥ
d ayasmayapraharaṇāḥ śūlamudgarapāṇayaḥ
d upagūḍhāḥ pranṛtyanti ramayanti sma pāṇḍavān
d prākāreṇa parikṣiptāṃ ratnajālavibhūṣitām
a īdṛśīṃ tāṃ sabhāṃ kṛtvā māsaiḥ paricaturdaśaiḥ
c niṣṭhitāṃ dharmarājāya mayo rājñe nyavedayat
 tāṃ tu kṛtvā sabhāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ mayaś cārjunam abravīt
 bhūtānāṃ ca mahāvīryo dhvajāgre kiṃkaro gaṇaḥ
 tava viṣphāraghoṣeṇa meghavan ninadiṣyati
 ayaṃ hi sūryasaṃkāśo jvalanasya rathottamaḥ
 ime ca divijāḥ śvetā vīryavanto hayottamāḥ
 māyāmayaḥ kṛto hy eṣa dhvajo vānaralakṣaṇaḥ
 asajyamāno vṛkṣeṣu dhūmaketur ivocchritaḥ
 bahuvarṇaṃ hi lakṣyeta dhvajaṃ vānaralakṣaṇam
 dhvajotkaṭaṃ hy anavamaṃ yuddhe drakṣyasi viṣṭhitam
 ity uktvāliṅgya bībhatsuṃ visṛṣṭaḥ prayayau mayaḥ
 eṣā sabhā savyasācin dhvajo 'gryas te bhaviṣyati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ praveśanaṃ cakre tasyāṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c ayutaṃ bhojayām āsa brāhmaṇānāṃ narādhipaḥ
a ghṛtapāyasena madhunā bhakṣyair mūlaphalais tathā
c ahataiś caiva vāsobhir mālyair uccāvacair api
a dadau tebhyaḥ sahasrāṇi gavāṃ pratyekaśaḥ prabhuḥ
c puṇyāhaghoṣas tatrāsīd divaspṛg iva bhārata
a vāditrair vividhair gītair gandhair uccāvacair api
b bhakṣyair mūlaiḥ phalaiś caiva māṃsair vārāhahāriṇaiḥ
b kṛsareṇātha jīvantyā haviṣyeṇa ca sarvaśaḥ
b māṃsaprakārair vividhaiḥ khādyaiś cāpi tathā nṛpa
b coṣyaiś ca vividhai rājan peyaiś ca bahuvistaraiḥ
c pūjayitvā kuruśreṣṭho daivatāni niveśya ca
d tarpayām āsa viprendrān nānādigbhyaḥ samāgatān
a tatra mallā naṭā jhallāḥ sūtā vaitālikās tathā
c upatasthur mahātmānaṃ saptarātraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a tathā sa kṛtvā pūjāṃ tāṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pāṇḍavaḥ
c tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ ramyāyāṃ reme śakro yathā divi
a sabhāyām ṛṣayas tasyāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha āsate
c āsāṃ cakrur narendrāś ca nānādeśasamāgatāḥ
a asito devalaḥ satyaḥ sarpamālī mahāśirāḥ
c arvāvasuḥ sumitraś ca maitreyaḥ śunako baliḥ
d ātreyaḥ kaṇvajaṭharau maudgalyo hastikāśyapau
a bako dālbhyaḥ sthūlaśirāḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ śukaḥ
c sumantur jaiminiḥ pailo vyāsaśiṣyās tathā vayam
a tittirir yājñavalkyaś ca sasuto lomaharṣaṇaḥ
b satyāṣāḍhaś ca durvāsā bhāradvājas tathaiva ca
b śunaḥśepho vasiṣṭhaś ca kaṇḍur uddālakas tathā
b śvetaketuḥ sahaś caiva kapardī cāśvalāyanaḥ
b bodhāyano bharadvāja āpastambas tathaiva ca
c apsuhomyaś ca dhaumyaś ca āṇīmāṇḍavyakauśikau
a dāmoṣṇīṣas traivaṇiś ca parṇādo ghaṭajānukaḥ
c mauñjāyano vāyubhakṣaḥ pārāśaryaś ca sārikau
a balavākaḥ śinīvākaḥ sutyapālaḥ kṛtaśramaḥ
c jātūkarṇaḥ śikhāvāṃś ca subalaḥ pārijātakaḥ
a parvataś ca mahābhāgo mārkaṇḍeyas tathā muniḥ
c pavitrapāṇiḥ sāvarṇir bhālukir gālavas tathā
a jaṅghābandhuś ca raibhyaś ca kopavegaśravā bhṛguḥ
c haribabhruś ca kauṇḍinyo babhrumālī sanātanaḥ
a kakṣīvān auśijaś caiva nāciketo 'tha gautamaḥ
c paiṅgo varāhaḥ śunakaḥ śāṇḍilyaś ca mahātapāḥ
e karkaro veṇujaṅghaś ca kalāpaḥ kaṭha eva ca
f śārṅgaras tailakupyaś ca parṇavalkas tathaiva ca
a munayo dharmasahitā dhṛtātmāno jitendriyāḥ
c ete cānye ca bahavo vedavedāṅgapāragāḥ
a upāsate mahātmānaṃ sabhāyām ṛṣisattamāḥ
c kathayantaḥ kathāḥ puṇyā dharmajñāḥ śucayo 'malāḥ
a tathaiva kṣatriyaśreṣṭhā dharmarājam upāsate
c śrīmān mahātmā dharmātmā muñjaketur vivardhanaḥ
a saṃgrāmajid durmukhaś ca ugrasenaś ca vīryavān
c kakṣasenaḥ kṣitipatiḥ kṣemakaś cāparājitaḥ
e kāmbojarājaḥ kamalaḥ kampanaś ca mahābalaḥ
a satataṃ kampayām āsa yavanān eka eva yaḥ
b balapauruṣasaṃpannān kṛtāstrān amitaujasaḥ
c yathāsurān kālakeyān devo vajradharas tathā
a jaṭāsuro madrakāntaś ca rājā
kuntiḥ kuṇindaś ca kirātarājaḥ
c tathāṅgavaṅgau saha puṇḍrakeṇa
pāṇḍyoḍrarājau saha cāndhrakeṇa
d jaṭāsuro madrakaś ca rājā kuntiḥ pulindakaḥ
d kirātarājaś ca tathā vaṅgeśaḥ sahapuṇḍrakaḥ
d pāṇḍyaś ca rājā sumahān andhrakeṇa mahātmanā
d aṅgo vaṅgaḥ sumitraś ca śaibyaś cāmitrakarśanaḥ
a kirātarājaḥ sumanā yavanādhipatis tathā
b pāñcālaś ca virāṭaś ca drumaśalyaḥ pṛthuśravāḥ
c cāṇūro devarātaś ca bhojo bhīmarathaś ca yaḥ
a śrutāyudhaś ca kāliṅgo jayatsenaś ca māgadhaḥ
c suśarmā cekitānaś ca suratho 'mitrakarṣaṇaḥ
a ketumān vasudānaś ca vaideho 'tha kṛtakṣaṇaḥ
c sudharmā cāniruddhaś ca śrutāyuś ca mahābalaḥ
a anūparājo durdharṣaḥ kṣemajic ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
c śiśupālaḥ sahasutaḥ karūṣādhipatis tathā
d pāntyāndhrarājau sahitādaṃ   na mahātmanām
a vṛṣṇīnāṃ caiva durdharṣāḥ kumārā devarūpiṇaḥ
c āhuko vipṛthuś caiva gadaḥ sāraṇa eva ca
a akrūraḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātyakiś ca śineḥ sutaḥ
c bhīṣmako 'thāhṛtiś caiva dyumatsenaś ca vīryavān
e kekayāś ca maheṣvāsā yajñasenaś ca saumakiḥ
f ketumān vasumāṃś caiva kṛtāstraś ca mahābalaḥ
f ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kṣatriyā mukhyasaṃmatāḥ
f upāsate sabhāyāṃ sma kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a arjunaṃ cāpi saṃśritya rājaputrā mahābalāḥ
c aśikṣanta dhanurvedaṃ rauravājinavāsasaḥ
a tatraiva śikṣitā rājan kumārā vṛṣṇinandanāḥ
c raukmiṇeyaś ca sāmbaś ca yuyudhānaś ca sātyakiḥ
d sudharmā cāniruddhaś ca śaibyaś ca narapuṃgavaḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavo rājānaḥ pṛthivīpate
b dhanaṃjayam upātiṣṭhan dhanurvedacikīrṣavaḥ
c dhanaṃjayasakhā cātra nityam āste sma tumburuḥ
d upāsate mahātmānam āsīnaṃ saptaviṃśatiḥ
a citrasenaḥ sahāmātyo gandharvāpsarasas tathā
b tasyāṃ sabhāyām āste sma bahubhiḥ parivāritaḥ
c gītavāditrakuśalāḥ śamyātālaviśāradāḥ
a pramāṇe 'tha layasthāne kiṃnarāḥ kṛtaniśramāḥ
c saṃcoditās tumburuṇā gandharvāḥ sahitā jaguḥ
a gāyanti divyatānais te yathānyāyaṃ manasvinaḥ
b devatāṃś ca munīṃś caiva pārthivāṃś caiva toṣayan
b śamyātāleṣu kuśalāḥ kuśalā gītavādane
c pāṇḍuputrān ṛṣīṃś caiva ramayanta upāsate
d hāhāhūhūḥ parvataś ca nāradaś ca pṛthuśravāḥ
d gāyanti ca pranṛtyanti urvaśyādyapsarogaṇaiḥ
a tasyāṃ sabhāyām āsīnāḥ suvratāḥ satyasaṃgarāḥ
c divīva devā brahmāṇaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram upāsate
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā tatropaviṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
c mahatsu copaviṣṭeṣu gandharveṣu ca bhārata
d vedopaniṣadāṃ vettā ṛṣiḥ suragaṇārcitaḥ
d itihāsapurāṇajñaḥ purākalpaviśeṣavit
d nyāyavid dharmatattvajñaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavid anuttamaḥ
d aikyasaṃyoganānātvasamavāyaviśāradaḥ
d vaktā pragalbho medhāvī smṛtimān nayavit kaviḥ
d parāparavibhāgajñaḥ pramāṇakṛtaniścayaḥ
d pañcāvayavayuktasya vākyasya guṇadoṣavit
d uttarottaravaktā ca vadato 'pi bṛhaspateḥ
d dharmakāmārthamokṣeṣu yathāvat kṛtaniścayaḥ
d tathā bhuvanakośasya sarvasyāsya mahāmatiḥ
d pratyakṣadarśī lokasya tiryag ūrdhvam adhas tathā
d sāṃkhyayogavibhāgajño nirvivitsuḥ surāsurān
d saṃdhivigrahatattvajñas tv anumānavibhāgavit
d ṣāḍguṇyavidhiyuktaś ca sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
d yuddhagāndharvasevī ca sarvatrāpratighas tathā
d etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhir yukto guṇagaṇair muniḥ
a lokān anucaran sarvān āgamat tāṃ sabhām ṛṣiḥ
c nāradaḥ sumahātejā ṛṣibhiḥ sahitas tadā
a pārijātena rājendra raivatena ca dhīmatā
c sumukhena ca saumyena devarṣir amitadyutiḥ
e sabhāsthān pāṇḍavān draṣṭuṃ prīyamāṇo manojavaḥ
f jayāśīrbhiḥ stutaṃ vipro dharmarājānam ārcayat
a tam āgatam ṛṣiṃ dṛṣṭvā nāradaṃ sarvadharmavit
c sahasā pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaḥ pratyutthāyānujaiḥ saha
e abhyavādayata prītyā vinayāvanatas tadā
a tadarham āsanaṃ tasmai saṃpradāya yathāvidhi
b gāṃ caiva madhuparkaṃ ca saṃpradāyārdhyam eva ca
c arcayām āsa ratnaiś ca sarvakāmaiś ca dharmavit
d tutoṣa ca yathāvac ca pūjāṃ prāpya yudhiṣṭhirāt
a so 'rcitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sarvair maharṣir vedapāragaḥ
c dharmakāmārthasaṃyuktaṃ papracchedaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
 nārada uvāca
a kaccid arthāś ca kalpante dharme ca ramate manaḥ
c sukhāni cānubhūyante manaś ca na vihanyate
a kaccid ācaritāṃ pūrvair naradeva pitāmahaiḥ
c vartase vṛttim akṣīṇāṃ dharmārthasahitāṃ nṛṣu
a kaccid arthena vā dharmaṃ dharmeṇārtham athāpi vā
c ubhau vā prītisāreṇa na kāmena prabādhase
a kaccid arthaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca jayatāṃ vara
c vibhajya kāle kālajña sadā varada sevase
a kaccid rājaguṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saptopāyāṃs tathānagha
c balābalaṃ tathā samyak caturdaśa parīkṣase
a kaccid ātmānam anvīkṣya parāṃś ca jayatāṃ vara
c tathā saṃdhāya karmāṇi aṣṭau bhārata sevase
a kaccit prakṛtayaḥ ṣaṭ te na luptā bharatarṣabha
c āḍhyās tathāvyasaninaḥ svanuraktāś ca sarvaśaḥ
a kaccin na tarkair dūtair vā ye cāpy apariśaṅkitāḥ
c tvatto vā tava vāmātyair bhidyate jātu mantritam
d mitrodāsīnaśatrūṇāṃ kaccid vetsi cikīrṣitam
a kaccit saṃdhiṃ yathākālaṃ vigrahaṃ copasevase
c kaccid vṛttim udāsīne madhyame cānuvartase
a kaccid ātmasamā buddhyā śucayo jīvitakṣamāḥ
c kulīnāś cānuraktāś ca kṛtās te vīra mantriṇaḥ
a vijayo mantramūlo hi rājñāṃ bhavati bhārata
c susaṃvṛto mantradhanair amātyaiḥ śāstrakovidaiḥ
d rāṣṭraṃ surakṣitaṃ tāta śatrubhir na vilupyate
a kaccin nidrāvaśaṃ naiṣi kaccit kāle vibudhyase
c kaccic cāpararātreṣu cintayasy artham arthavit
a kaccin mantrayase naikaḥ kaccin na bahubhiḥ saha
c kaccit te mantrito mantro na rāṣṭram anudhāvati
a kaccid arthān viniścitya laghumūlān mahodayān
c kṣipram ārabhase kartuṃ na vighnayasi tādṛśān
a kaccin na sarve karmāntāḥ parokṣās te viśaṅkitāḥ
b parokṣā vā mahārāja madhyaṃ hy atra praśasyate
b āptair alubdhaiḥ kramikais te ca kaccid anuṣṭhitāḥ
c sarve vā punar utsṛṣṭāḥ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ hy atra kāraṇam
a kaccid rājan kṛtāny eva kṛtaprāyāṇi vā punaḥ
c vidus te vīra karmāṇi nānavāptāni kāni cit
a kaccit kāraṇikāḥ sarve sarvaśāstreṣu kovidāḥ
c kārayanti kumārāṃś ca yodhamukhyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
a kaccit sahasrair mūrkhāṇām ekaṃ krīṇāsi paṇḍitam
c paṇḍito hy arthakṛcchreṣu kuryān niḥśreyasaṃ param
a kaccid durgāṇi sarvāṇi dhanadhānyāyudhodakaiḥ
c yantraiś ca paripūrṇāni tathā śilpidhanurdharaiḥ
a eko 'py amātyo medhāvī śūro dānto vicakṣaṇaḥ
c rājānaṃ rājaputraṃ vā prāpayen mahatīṃ śriyam
a kaccid aṣṭādaśānyeṣu svapakṣe daśa pañca ca
c tribhis tribhir avijñātair vetsi tīrthāni cārakaiḥ
a kaccid dviṣām aviditaḥ pratiyattaś ca sarvadā
c nityayukto ripūn sarvān vīkṣase ripusūdana
a kaccid vinayasaṃpannaḥ kulaputro bahuśrutaḥ
c anasūyur anupraṣṭā satkṛtas te purohitaḥ
a kaccid agniṣu te yukto vidhijño matimān ṛjuḥ
c hutaṃ ca hoṣyamāṇaṃ ca kāle vedayate sadā
a kaccid aṅgeṣu niṣṇāto jyotiṣāṃ pratipādakaḥ
c utpāteṣu ca sarveṣu daivajñaḥ kuśalas tava
a kaccin mukhyā mahatsv eva madhyameṣu ca madhyamāḥ
c jaghanyāś ca jaghanyeṣu bhṛtyāḥ karmasu yojitāḥ
a amātyān upadhātītān pitṛpaitāmahāñ śucīn
c śreṣṭhāñ śreṣṭheṣu kaccit tvaṃ niyojayasi karmasu
a kaccin nogreṇa daṇḍena bhṛśam udvejitaprajāḥ
c rāṣṭraṃ tavānuśāsanti mantriṇo bharatarṣabha
a kaccit tvāṃ nāvajānanti yājakāḥ patitaṃ yathā
c ugrapratigrahītāraṃ kāmayānam iva striyaḥ
d kaccin na vidyate rāṣṭre tava kīrtivināśakāḥ
a kaccid dhṛṣṭaś ca śūraś ca matimān dhṛtimāñ śuciḥ
c kulīnaś cānuraktaś ca dakṣaḥ senāpatis tava
a kaccid balasya te mukhyāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
c dṛṣṭāpadānā vikrāntās tvayā satkṛtya mānitāḥ
a kaccid balasya bhaktaṃ ca vetanaṃ ca yathocitam
c saṃprāptakālaṃ dātavyaṃ dadāsi na vikarṣasi
a kālātikramaṇād dhy ete bhaktavetanayor bhṛtāḥ
c bhartuḥ kupyanti daurgatyāt so 'narthaḥ sumahān smṛtaḥ
d kaccit sarve mahīpālās tvadājñā mūrdhni dhāritāḥ
d kaccit suhṛhayāḥ sarve hy arcayanti bhavatkṛte
d kaccid antapurā devā kāle saṃsevitās tvayā
d kaccid rājapurandhrībhiḥ prasūyante kulocitāḥ
d kumārā dhārmikāḥ śūrā rājadharmaviśāradāḥ
d kaccit teṣāṃ ca putrāṇāṃ vivāhaḥ kriyate tvayā
d saṃtānārthaṃ tu vaṃśasya doṣaṃ tasya mahīyasaḥ
d kaccid āśvāsirājaṃs tvayā śaraṇam āgatān
d devādīn bhayasaṃtrastān akārpaṇyadhiyā bhṛśam
a kaccit sarve 'nuraktās tvāṃ kulaputrāḥ pradhānataḥ
c kaccit prāṇāṃs tavārtheṣu saṃtyajanti sadā yudhi
a kaccin naiko bahūn arthān sarvaśaḥ sāṃparāyikān
c anuśāssi yathākāmaṃ kāmātmā śāsanātigaḥ
a kaccit puruṣakāreṇa puruṣaḥ karma śobhayan
c labhate mānam adhikaṃ bhūyo vā bhaktavetanam
a kaccid vidyāvinītāṃś ca narāñ jñānaviśāradān
c yathārhaṃ guṇataś caiva dānenābhyavapadyase
a kaccid dārān manuṣyāṇāṃ tavārthe mṛtyum eyuṣām
c vyasanaṃ cābhyupetānāṃ bibharṣi bharatarṣabha
a kaccid bhayād upanataṃ klībaṃ vā ripum āgatam
c yuddhe vā vijitaṃ pārtha putravat parirakṣasi
a kaccit tvam eva sarvasyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ pṛthivīpate
c samaś ca nābhiśaṅkyaś ca yathā mātā yathā pitā
a kaccid vyasaninaṃ śatruṃ niśamya bharatarṣabha
c abhiyāsi javenaiva samīkṣya trividhaṃ balam
d yātrām ārabhase diṣṭyā prāptakālam ariṃdama
a pārṣṇimūlaṃ ca vijñāya vyavasāyaṃ parājayam
c balasya ca mahārāja dattvā vetanam agrataḥ
a kaccic ca balamukhyebhyaḥ pararāṣṭre paraṃtapa
c upacchannāni ratnāni prayacchasi yathārhataḥ
a kaccid ātmānam evāgre vijitya vijitendriyaḥ
c parāñ jigīṣase pārtha pramattān ajitendriyān
a kaccit te yāsyataḥ śatrūn pūrvaṃ yānti svanuṣṭhitāḥ
c sāma dānaṃ ca bhedaś ca daṇḍaś ca vidhivad guṇāḥ
a kaccin mūlaṃ dṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā yātrāṃ yāsi viśāṃ pate
c tāṃś ca vikramase jetuṃ jitvā ca parirakṣasi
a kaccid aṣṭāṅgasaṃyuktā caturvidhabalā camūḥ
c balamukhyaiḥ sunītā te dviṣatāṃ pratibādhanī
a kaccil lavaṃ ca muṣṭiṃ ca pararāṣṭre paraṃtapa
c avihāya mahārāja vihaṃsi samare ripūn
a kaccit svapararāṣṭreṣu bahavo 'dhikṛtās tava
c arthān samanutiṣṭhanti rakṣanti ca parasparam
a kaccid abhyavahāryāṇi gātrasaṃsparśakāni ca
c ghreyāṇi ca mahārāja rakṣanty anumatās tava
a kaccit kośaṃ ca koṣṭhaṃ ca vāhanaṃ dvāram āyudham
c āyaś ca kṛtakalyāṇais tava bhaktair anuṣṭhitaḥ
a kaccid ābhyantarebhyaś ca bāhyebhyaś ca viśāṃ pate
c rakṣasy ātmānam evāgre tāṃś ca svebhyo mithaś ca tān
a kaccin na pāne dyūte vā krīḍāsu pramadāsu ca
c pratijānanti pūrvāhṇe vyayaṃ vyasanajaṃ tava
a kaccid āyasya cārdhena caturbhāgena vā punaḥ
c pādabhāgais tribhir vāpi vyayaḥ saṃśodhyate tava
a kaccij jñātīn gurūn vṛddhān vaṇijaḥ śilpinaḥ śritān
c abhīkṣṇam anugṛhṇāsi dhanadhānyena durgatān
a kaccid āyavyaye yuktāḥ sarve gaṇakalekhakāḥ
c anutiṣṭhanti pūrvāhṇe nityam āyavyayaṃ tava
a kaccid artheṣu saṃprauḍhān hitakāmān anupriyān
c nāpakarṣasi karmabhyaḥ pūrvam aprāpya kilbiṣam
a kaccid viditvā puruṣān uttamādhamamadhyamān
c tvaṃ karmasv anurūpeṣu niyojayasi bhārata
a kaccin na lubdhāś caurā vā vairiṇo vā viśāṃ pate
c aprāptavyavahārā vā tava karmasv anuṣṭhitāḥ
a kaccin na lubdhaiś caurair vā kumāraiḥ strībalena vā
c tvayā vā pīḍyate rāṣṭraṃ kaccit puṣṭāḥ kṛṣīvalāḥ
a kaccid rāṣṭre taḍāgāni pūrṇāni ca mahānti ca
c bhāgaśo viniviṣṭāni na kṛṣir devamātṛkā
a kaccid bījaṃ ca bhaktaṃ ca karṣakāyāvasīdate
c pratikaṃ ca śataṃ vṛddhyā dadāsy ṛṇam anugraham
d kacit te dayitāḥ sarve kṛṣigorakṣajīvinaḥ
a kaccit svanuṣṭhitā tāta vārttā te sādhubhir janaiḥ
c vārttāyāṃ saṃśritas tāta loko 'yaṃ sukham edhate
a kaccic chucikṛtaḥ prājñāḥ pañca pañca svanuṣṭhitāḥ
c kṣemaṃ kurvanti saṃhatya rājañ janapade tava
a kaccin nagaraguptyarthaṃ grāmā nagaravat kṛtāḥ
c grāmavac ca kṛtā rakṣā te ca sarve tadarpaṇāḥ
a kaccid balenānugatāḥ samāni viṣamāṇi ca
c purāṇacaurāḥ sādhyakṣāś caranti viṣaye tava
a kaccit striyaḥ sāntvayasi kaccit tāś ca surakṣitāḥ
c kaccin na śraddadhāsy āsāṃ kaccid guhyaṃ na bhāṣase
a kaccic cārān niśi śrutvā tat kāryam anucintya ca
c priyāṇy anubhavañ śeṣe viditvābhyantaraṃ janam
a kaccid dvau prathamau yāmau rātryāṃ suptvā viśāṃ pate
c saṃcintayasi dharmārthau yāma utthāya paścime
a kaccid darśayase nityaṃ manuṣyān samalaṃkṛtān
c utthāya kāle kālajñaḥ saha pāṇḍava mantribhiḥ
a kaccid raktāmbaradharāḥ khaḍgahastāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c abhitas tvām upāsante rakṣaṇārtham ariṃdama
a kaccid daṇḍyeṣu yamavat pūjyeṣu ca viśāṃ pate
c parīkṣya vartase samyag apriyeṣu priyeṣu ca
a kaccic chārīram ābādham auṣadhair niyamena vā
c mānasaṃ vṛddhasevābhiḥ sadā pārthāpakarṣasi
a kaccid vaidyāś cikitsāyām aṣṭāṅgāyāṃ viśāradāḥ
c suhṛdaś cānuraktāś ca śarīre te hitāḥ sadā
a kaccin na mānān mohād vā kāmād vāpi viśāṃ pate
c arthipratyarthinaḥ prāptān apāsyasi kathaṃ cana
a kaccin na lobhān mohād vā viśrambhāt praṇayena vā
c āśritānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vṛttiṃ tvaṃ saṃruṇatsi ca
d kaccid artheṣu saṃprauḍhān arthakarmavicakṣaṇān
d nāpakarṣasi karmabhyo hy arthayuktā itīva hi
a kaccit paurā na sahitā ye ca te rāṣṭravāsinaḥ
c tvayā saha virudhyante paraiḥ krītāḥ kathaṃ cana
a kaccit te durbalaḥ śatrur balenopanipīḍitaḥ
c mantreṇa balavān kaś cid ubhābhyāṃ vā yudhiṣṭhira
a kaccit sarve 'nuraktās tvāṃ bhūmipālāḥ pradhānataḥ
c kaccit prāṇāṃs tvadartheṣu saṃtyajanti tvayā hṛtāḥ
a kaccit te sarvavidyāsu guṇato 'rcā pravartate
c brāhmaṇānāṃ ca sādhūnāṃ tava niḥśreyase śubhā
d dakṣiṇās tvaṃ dadāsy eṣāṃ nityaṃ svargāpavargadāḥ
a kaccid dharme trayīmūle pūrvair ācarite janaiḥ
c vartamānas tathā kartuṃ tasmin karmaṇi vartase
a kaccit tava gṛhe 'nnāni svādūny aśnanti vai dvijāḥ
c guṇavanti guṇopetās tavādhyakṣaṃ sadakṣiṇam
a kaccit kratūn ekacitto vājapeyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
c puṇḍarīkāṃś ca kārtsnyena yatase kartum ātmavān
a kaccij jñātīn gurūn vṛddhān daivatāṃs tāpasān api
c caityāṃś ca vṛkṣān kalyāṇān brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyasi
d kaccic choko na manyur vā tvayā protpādyate 'nagha
d api maṅgalahastaś ca janaḥ pārśve 'nutiṣṭhati
a kaccid eṣā ca te buddhir vṛttir eṣā ca te 'nagha
c āyuṣyā ca yaśasyā ca dharmakāmārthadarśinī
a etayā vartamānasya buddhyā rāṣṭraṃ na sīdati
c vijitya ca mahīṃ rājā so 'tyantaṃ sukham edhate
a kaccid āryo viśuddhātmā kṣāritaś caurakarmaṇi
c adṛṣṭaśāstrakuśalair na lobhād vadhyate śuciḥ
a pṛṣṭo gṛhītas tatkārī tajjñair dṛṣṭaḥ sakāraṇaḥ
c kaccin na mucyate steno dravyalobhān nararṣabha
a vyutpanne kaccid āḍhyasya daridrasya ca bhārata
c arthān na mithyā paśyanti tavāmātyā hṛtā dhanaiḥ
a nāstikyam anṛtaṃ krodhaṃ pramādaṃ dīrghasūtratām
c adarśanaṃ jñānavatām ālasyaṃ kṣiptacittatām
a ekacintanam arthānām anarthajñaiś ca cintanam
c niścitānām anārambhaṃ mantrasyāparirakṣaṇam
a maṅgalyasyāprayogaṃ ca prasaṅgaṃ viṣayeṣu ca
c kaccit tvaṃ varjayasy etān rājadoṣāṃś caturdaśa
d prāyaśo yair vinaśyanti kṛtamūlāpi pārthivāḥ
a kaccit te saphalā vedāḥ kaccit te saphalaṃ dhanam
c kaccit te saphalā dārāḥ kaccit te saphalaṃ śrutam
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kathaṃ vai saphalā vedāḥ kathaṃ vai saphalaṃ dhanam
c kathaṃ vai saphalā dārāḥ kathaṃ vai saphalaṃ śrutam
d ity evaṃ bhāṣito rājñā sarvaśāstrārthatattvavit
d dharmarājaṃ mahātmānaṃ punar āha ca tattvataḥ
 nārada uvāca
a agnihotraphalā vedā dattabhuktaphalaṃ dhanam
c ratiputraphalā dārāḥ śīlavṛttaphalaṃ śrutam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etad ākhyāya sa munir nāradaḥ sumahātapāḥ
c papracchānantaram idaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
 nārada uvāca
a kaccid abhyāgatā dūrād vaṇijo lābhakāraṇāt
c yathoktam avahāryante śulkaṃ śulkopajīvibhiḥ
a kaccit te puruṣā rājan pure rāṣṭre ca mānitāḥ
c upānayanti paṇyāni upadhābhir avañcitāḥ
a kaccic chṛṇoṣi vṛddhānāṃ dharmārthasahitā giraḥ
c nityam arthavidāṃ tāta tathā dharmānudarśinām
a kaccit te kṛṣitantreṣu goṣu puṣpaphaleṣu ca
b niyuktāḥ kuśalās teṣu vibhāgajñāḥ kulocitāḥ
c dharmārthaṃ ca dvijātibhyo dīyate madhusarpiṣī
a dravyopakaraṇaṃ kaccit sarvadā sarvaśilpinām
c cāturmāsyāvaraṃ samyaṅ niyataṃ saṃprayacchasi
a kaccit kṛtaṃ vijānīṣe kartāraṃ ca praśaṃsasi
c satāṃ madhye mahārāja satkaroṣi ca pūjayan
a kaccit sūtrāṇi sarvāṇi gṛhṇāsi bharatarṣabha
c hastisūtrāśvasūtrāṇi rathasūtrāṇi cābhibho
a kaccid abhyasyate śaśvad gṛhe te bharatarṣabha
c dhanurvedasya sūtraṃ ca yantrasūtraṃ ca nāgaram
a kaccid astrāṇi sarvāṇi brahmadaṇḍaś ca te 'nagha
c viṣayogāś ca te sarve viditāḥ śatrunāśanāḥ
a kaccid agnibhayāc caiva sarpavyālabhayāt tathā
c rogarakṣobhayāc caiva rāṣṭraṃ svaṃ parirakṣasi
a kaccid andhāṃś ca mūkāṃś ca paṅgūn vyaṅgān abāndhavān
c piteva pāsi dharmajña tathā pravrajitān api
d ṣaḍanarthā mahārāja kaccit te pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtāḥ
d nidrālasyaṃ bhayaṃ krodho mārdavaṃ dīrghasūtratā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etāḥ kurūṇām ṛṣabho mahātmā
śrutvā giro brāhmaṇasattamasya
c praṇamya pādāv abhivādya hṛṣṭo
rājābravīn nāradaṃ devarūpam
a evaṃ kariṣyāmi yathā tvayoktaṃ
prajñā hi me bhūya evābhivṛddhā
c uktvā tathā caiva cakāra rājā
lebhe mahīṃ sāgaramekhalāṃ ca
 nārada uvāca
a evaṃ yo vartate rājā cāturvarṇyasya rakṣaṇe
c sa vihṛtyeha susukhī śakrasyaiti salokatām
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a saṃpūjyāthābhyanujñāto maharṣer vacanāt param
c pratyuvācānupūrvyeṇa dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a bhagavan nyāyyam āhaitaṃ yathāvad dharmaniścayam
c yathāśakti yathānyāyaṃ kriyate 'yaṃ vidhir mayā
a rājabhir yad yathā kāryaṃ purā tat tan na saṃśayaḥ
c yathānyāyopanītārthaṃ kṛtaṃ hetumad arthavat
a vayaṃ tu satpathaṃ teṣāṃ yātum icchāmahe prabho
c na tu śakyaṃ tathā gantuṃ yathā tair niyatātmabhiḥ
d taṃ tu viśrāntam āsīnaṃ devarṣim amitadyutim
a evam uktvā sa dharmātmā vākyaṃ tad abhipūjya ca
c muhūrtāt prāptakālaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā lokacaraṃ munim
a nāradaṃ svastham āsīnam upāsīno yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c apṛcchat pāṇḍavas tatra rājamadhye mahāmatiḥ
a bhavān saṃcarate lokān sadā nānāvidhān bahūn
c brahmaṇā nirmitān pūrvaṃ prekṣamāṇo manojavaḥ
a īdṛśī bhavatā kā cid dṛṣṭapūrvā sabhā kva cit
c ito vā śreyasī brahmaṃs tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
a tac chrutvā nāradas tasya dharmarājasya bhāṣitam
c pāṇḍavaṃ pratyuvācedaṃ smayan madhurayā girā
a mānuṣeṣu na me tāta dṛṣṭapūrvā na ca śrutā
c sabhā maṇimayī rājan yatheyaṃ tava bhārata
a sabhāṃ tu pitṛrājasya varuṇasya ca dhīmataḥ
c kathayiṣye tathendrasya kailāsanilayasya ca
a brahmaṇaś ca sabhāṃ divyāṃ kathayiṣye gataklamām
b divyāṃ divyair abhiprāyair upetāṃ viśvarūpiṇīm
b devaiḥ pitṛgaṇaiḥ sādhyair yajvabhir niyatātmabhiḥ
b juṣṭāṃ munigaṇaiḥ śāntair vedayajñaiḥ sadakṣiṇaiḥ
c yadi te śravaṇe buddhir vartate bharatarṣabha
a nāradenaivam uktas tu dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c prāñjalir bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ taiś ca sarvair nṛpair vṛtaḥ
a nāradaṃ pratyuvācedaṃ dharmarājo mahāmanāḥ
c sabhāḥ kathaya tāḥ sarvāḥ śrotum icchāmahe vayam
a kiṃdravyās tāḥ sabhā brahman kiṃvistārāḥ kimāyatāḥ
c pitāmahaṃ ca ke tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ paryupāsate
a vāsavaṃ devarājaṃ ca yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ ca ke
c varuṇaṃ ca kuberaṃ ca sabhāyāṃ paryupāsate
a etat sarvaṃ yathātattvaṃ devarṣe vadatas tava
c śrotum icchāma sahitāḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
a evam uktaḥ pāṇḍavena nāradaḥ pratyuvāca tam
c krameṇa rājan divyās tāḥ śrūyantām iha naḥ sabhāḥ
 nārada uvāca
a śakrasya tu sabhā divyā bhāsvarā karmabhir jitā
c svayaṃ śakreṇa kauravya nirmitārkasamaprabhā
a vistīrṇā yojanaśataṃ śatam adhyardham āyatā
c vaihāyasī kāmagamā pañcayojanam ucchritā
a jarāśokaklamāpetā nirātaṅkā śivā śubhā
c veśmāsanavatī ramyā divyapādapaśobhitā
a tasyāṃ deveśvaraḥ pārtha sabhāyāṃ paramāsane
c āste śacyā mahendrāṇyā śriyā lakṣmyā ca bhārata
a bibhrad vapur anirdeśyaṃ kirīṭī lohitāṅgadaḥ
c virajombaraś citramālyo hrīkīrtidyutibhiḥ saha
a tasyām upāsate nityaṃ mahātmānaṃ śatakratum
c marutaḥ sarvato rājan sarve ca gṛhamedhinaḥ
e siddhā devarṣayaś caiva sādhyā devagaṇās tathā
f marutvantaś ca sahitā bhāsvanto hemamālinaḥ
a ete sānucarāḥ sarve divyarūpāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c upāsate mahātmānaṃ devarājam ariṃdamam
a tathā devarṣayaḥ sarve pārtha śakram upāsate
c amalā dhūtapāpmāno dīpyamānā ivāgnayaḥ
e tejasvinaḥ somayujo vipāpā vigataklamāḥ
a parāśaraḥ parvataś ca tathā sāvarṇigālavau
b ekataś ca dvitaś caiva tritaś caiva mahāmuniḥ
c śaṅkhaś ca likhitaś caiva tathā gauraśirā muniḥ
a durvāsāś ca dīrghatapā yājñavalkyo 'tha bhālukiḥ
a   tathā dīrghatamā muniḥ
a pavitrapāṇiḥ sāvarṇiḥ
c uddālakaḥ śvetaketus tathā śāṭyāyanaḥ prabhuḥ
a haviṣmāṃś ca gaviṣṭhaś ca hariścandraś ca pārthivaḥ
c hṛdyaś codaraśāṇḍilyaḥ pārāśaryaḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ
da jābālir vāmadevaś ca śaktir gārgyasuvāmanau
a vātaskandho viśākhaś ca vidhātā kāla eva ca
c anantadantas tvaṣṭā ca viśvakarmā ca tumburuḥ
a ayonijā yonijāś ca vāyubhakṣā hutāśinaḥ
c īśānaṃ sarvalokasya vajriṇaṃ samupāsate
a sahadevaḥ sunīthaś ca vālmīkiś ca mahātapāḥ
c samīkaḥ satyavāṃś caiva pracetāḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ
a medhātithir vāmadevaḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
c maruttaś ca marīciś ca sthāṇuś cātrir mahātapāḥ
a kakṣīvān gautamas tārkṣyas tathā vaiśvānaro muniḥ
b ṣaḍartuḥ kavaṣo dhūmro raibhyo nalaparāvasū
b svastyātreyo jaratkāruḥ kahoḷaḥ kāśyapas tathā
b vibhaṇḍako ṛṣyaśṛṅga unmukho vimukhas tathā
c muniḥ kālakavṛkṣīya āśrāvyo 'tha hiraṇyadaḥ
e saṃvarto devahavyaś ca viṣvaksenaś ca vīryavān
f kaṇvaḥ kātyāyano rājan gārgyaḥ kauśika eva tu
a divyā āpas tathauṣadhyaḥ śraddhā medhā sarasvatī
c artho dharmaś ca kāmaś ca vidyutaś cāpi pāṇḍava
a jalavāhās tathā meghā vāyavaḥ stanayitnavaḥ
c prācī dig yajñavāhāś ca pāvakāḥ saptaviṃśatiḥ
a agnīṣomau tathendrāgnī mitro 'tha savitāryamā
c bhago viśve ca sādhyāś ca śukro manthī ca bhārata
d sarveṣāṃ marutāṃ mānyā guruḥ śukras tathaiva ca
d viśvāvasuś citrasenaḥ sumanas taruṇas tathā
a yajñāś ca dakṣiṇāś caiva grahāḥ stobhāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c yajñavāhāś ca ye mantrāḥ sarve tatra samāsate
a tathaivāpsaraso rājan gandharvāś ca manoramāḥ
a   rambhorvaśy atha menakā
a ghṛtācī pañcacūḍā ca vipracittipurogamāḥ
a viśvāvasuś citrasenaḥ parvatas tumburus tathā
a vidyādharās tu rājendra
c nṛtyavāditragītaiś ca hāsyaiś ca vividhair api
e ramayanti sma nṛpate devarājaṃ śatakratum
a stutibhir maṅgalaiś caiva stuvantaḥ karmabhis tathā
c vikramaiś ca mahātmānaṃ balavṛtraniṣūdanam
a brahmarājarṣayaḥ sarve sarve devarṣayas tathā
c vimānair vividhair divyair bhrājamānair ivāgnibhiḥ
a sragviṇo bhūṣitāś cānye yānti cāyānti cāpare
c bṛhaspatiś ca śukraś ca tasyām āyayatuḥ saha
a ete cānye ca bahavo yatātmāno yatavratāḥ
c vimānaiś candrasaṃkāśaiḥ somavat priyadarśanāḥ
e brahmaṇo vacanād rājan bhṛguḥ saptarṣayas tathā
a eṣā sabhā mayā rājan dṛṣṭā puṣkaramālinī
c śatakrator mahārāja yāmyāṃ śṛṇu mamānagha
 nārada uvāca
a kathayiṣye sabhāṃ divyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira nibodha tām
c vaivasvatasya yām arthe viśvakarmā cakāra ha
a taijasī sā sabhā rājan babhūva śatayojanā
c vistārāyāmasaṃpannā bhūyasī cāpi pāṇḍava
a arkaprakāśā bhrājiṣṇuḥ sarvataḥ kāmacāriṇī
c naivātiśītā nātyuṣṇā manasaś ca praharṣiṇī
a na śoko na jarā tasyāṃ kṣutpipāse na cāpriyam
c na ca dainyaṃ klamo vāpi pratikūlaṃ na cāpy uta
a sarve kāmāḥ sthitās tasyāṃ ye divyā ye ca mānuṣāḥ
c rasavac ca prabhūtaṃ ca bhakṣyabhojyam ariṃdama
d lehyaṃ coṣyaṃ ca peyaṃ ca hṛdyaṃ svādu manoharam

c rasavanti ca toyāni śītāny uṣṇāni caiva ha
d vṛkṣāś ca vividhās tatra nityapuṣpā manoramāḥ
d śītalāni ca ramyāṇi sukhoṣṇāni ca bhārata
a tasyāṃ rājarṣayaḥ puṇyās tathā brahmarṣayo 'malāḥ
c yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ tāta prahṛṣṭāḥ paryupāsate
a yayātir nahuṣaḥ pūrur māndhātā somako nṛgaḥ
c trasadasyuś ca turayaḥ kṛtavīryaḥ śrutaśravāḥ
a aripraṇut susiṃhaś ca kṛtavegaḥ kṛtir nimiḥ
c pratardanaḥ śibir matsyaḥ pṛthvakṣo 'tha bṛhadrathaḥ
a aiḍo maruttaḥ kuśikaḥ sāṃkāśyaḥ sāṃkṛtir bhavaḥ
c caturaśvaḥ sadaśvormiḥ kārtavīryaś ca pārthivaḥ
a bharatas tathā surathaḥ sunītho naiṣadho nalaḥ
b bharataḥ surathaś caiva tathā rājā taporathaḥ
b sunītho niśaṭho rājā nalo vai niṣadhādhipaḥ
c divodāso 'tha sumanā ambarīṣo bhagīrathaḥ
d lomapādo 'naraṇyaś ca lohitaḥ pūrur udvahaḥ
a vyaśvaḥ sadaśvo vadhryaśvaḥ pañcahastaḥ pṛthuśravāḥ
c ruṣadgur vṛṣasenaś ca kṣupaś ca sumahābalaḥ
a ruṣadaśvo vasumanāḥ purukutso dhvajī rathī
c ārṣṭiṣeṇo dilīpaś ca mahātmā cāpy uśīnaraḥ
a auśīnaraḥ puṇḍarīkaḥ śaryātiḥ śarabhaḥ śuciḥ
c aṅgo 'riṣṭaś ca venaś ca duḥṣantaḥ saṃjayo jayaḥ
a bhāṅgāsvariḥ sunīthaś ca niṣadho 'tha tviṣīrathaḥ
c karaṃdhamo bāhlikaś ca sudyumno balavān madhuḥ
d ailo maruttaś ca tathā balavān pṛthivīpatiḥ
a kapotaromā tṛṇakaḥ sahadevārjunau tathā
b vyaśvaḥ sāśvaḥ kṛśāśvaś ca śaśabinduś ca pārthivaḥ
b rājā daśarathaś caiva kakutstho 'tha pravardhanaḥ
c rāmo dāśarathiś caiva lakṣmaṇo 'tha pratardanaḥ
a alarkaḥ kakṣasenaś ca gayo gaurāśva eva ca
c jāmadagnyo 'tha rāmo 'tra nābhāgasagarau tathā
a bhūridyumno mahāśvaś ca pṛthvaśvo janakas tathā
c vainyo rājā vāriṣeṇaḥ purujo janamejayaḥ
a brahmadattas trigartaś ca rājoparicaras tathā
c indradyumno bhīmajānur gayaḥ pṛṣṭho nayo 'naghaḥ
a padmo 'tha mucukundaś ca bhūridyumnaḥ prasenajit
c ariṣṭanemiḥ pradyumnaḥ pṛthagaśvo 'jakas tathā
a śataṃ matsyā nṛpatayaḥ śataṃ nīpāḥ śataṃ hayāḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭrāś caikaśatam aśītir janamejayāḥ
a śataṃ ca brahmadattānām īriṇāṃ vairiṇāṃ śatam
b bhīṣmāṇāṃ dve śate 'py atra bhīmānāṃ tu tathā śatam
b śataṃ ca prativindhyānāṃ śataṃ nāgāḥ śataṃ hayāḥ
b palāśānāṃ śataṃ jñeyaṃ śataṃ kāśakuśādayaḥ
c śaṃtanuś caiva rājarṣiḥ pāṇḍuś caiva pitā tava
a uśadgavaḥ śataratho devarājo jayadrathaḥ
c vṛṣādarbhiś ca rājarṣir dhāmnā saha samantriṇā

c iṣṭvāśvamedhair bahubhir mahadbhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ

c yajvānaś caiva siddhāś ca ye ca yogaśarīriṇaḥ
a agniṣvāttāś ca pitaraḥ phenapāś coṣmapāś ca ye

a kālasya nayane yuktā yamasya puruṣāś ca ye

a ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pitṛrājasabhāsadaḥ

a prabhāsantī jvalantīva tejasā svena bhārata

a śāntāḥ saṃnyāsinaḥ siddhāḥ pūtāḥ puṇyena karmaṇā
c sarve bhāsvaradehāś ca sarve ca virajombarāḥ
a citrāṅgadāś citramālyāḥ sarve jvalitakuṇḍalāḥ
c sukṛtaiḥ karmabhiḥ puṇyaiḥ paribarhair vibhūṣitāḥ
a gandharvāś ca mahātmānaḥ śataśaś cāpsarogaṇāḥ
c vāditraṃ nṛttagītaṃ ca hāsyaṃ lāsyaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a puṇyāś ca gandhāḥ śabdāś ca tasyāṃ pārtha samantataḥ
c divyāni mālyāni ca tām upatiṣṭhanti sarvaśaḥ
a śataṃ śatasahasrāṇi dharmiṇāṃ taṃ prajeśvaram
c upāsate mahātmānaṃ rūpayuktā manasvinaḥ
a īdṛśī sā sabhā rājan pitṛrājño mahātmanaḥ
c varuṇasyāpi vakṣyāmi sabhāṃ puṣkaramālinīm
d tvam ekāgramanā rājann avadhāraya pārthiva
 nārada uvāca
a yudhiṣṭhira sabhā divyā varuṇasya sitaprabhā

d carmaṇvatī tathā caiva parṇāśā ca mahānadī
d sarayūr vāravatyātha lāṅgalī ca saridvarā
d karatoyā tathātreyī lauhityaś ca mahānadaḥ

d kambudā ca viśalyā ca kauśikī gomatī tathā
d devikā ca vipaṅkā ca tathā vaitaraṇī nadī
d tṛtīyā jyeṣṭhilā caiva śoṇaś caiva mahānadaḥ
d carmaṇvatī śvetanadī phalgunā ca mahānadī
d sarayūś cīravalkelā kuliś ca saritas tathā
d sutīrthā lokaviśrutāḥ
d saritaḥ sarvataś cānyās

a gītavāditravantaś ca gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ

a mahīdharā ratnavanto rasā yeṣu pratiṣṭhitāḥ

a sabhā vaiśravaṇī rājañ śatayojanam āyatā

a tapasā nirmitā rājan svayaṃ vaiśravaṇena sā

a guhyakair uhyamānā sā khe viṣakteva dṛśyate
c divyā hemamayair uccaiḥ pādapair upaśobhitā
a raśmivatī bhāsvarā ca divyagandhā manoramā

d saha patnyā mahārāja ṛddhyā saha virājate

d upāsate mahātmānaṃ tasyāṃ dhanadam īśvaram
