c ādityāḥ sādhirājāno nānādvaṃdvair udāhṛtāḥ
a maruto viśvakarmā ca vasavaś caiva bhārata
b sarve ca kāmapracurāḥ sabhāyāṃ tatra nityaśaḥ
c tathā pitṛgaṇāḥ sarve sarvāṇi ca havīṃṣy atha
a ṛgvedaḥ sāmavedaś ca yajurvedaś ca pāṇḍava
c atharvavedaś ca tathā parvāṇi ca viśāṃ pate
a itihāsopavedāś ca vedāṅgāni ca sarvaśaḥ
c grahā yajñāś ca somaś ca daivatāni ca sarvaśaḥ
a sāvitrī durgataraṇī vāṇī saptavidhā tathā
c medhā dhṛtiḥ śrutiś caiva prajñā buddhir yaśaḥ kṣamā
a sāmāni stutiśastrāṇi gāthāś ca vividhās tathā
c bhāṣyāṇi tarkayuktāni dehavanti viśāṃ pate
d nāṭakā vividhāḥ kāvyāḥ kathākhyāyikakārikāḥ
d tatra tiṣṭhanti te puṇyā ye cānye gurupūjakāḥ
a kṣaṇā lavā muhūrtāś ca divā rātris tathaiva ca
c ardhamāsāś ca māsāś ca ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ ca bhārata
a saṃvatsarāḥ pañcayugam ahorātrāś caturvidhāḥ
c kālacakraṃ ca yad divyaṃ nityam akṣayam avyayam
d dharmacakraṃ tathā cāpi nityam āste yudhiṣṭhira
a aditir ditir danuś caiva surasā vinatā irā
c kālakā surabhir devī saramā cātha gautamī
d prādhā kadrūś ca vai devyau devatānāṃ ca mātaraḥ
d rudrāṇī śrīś ca lakṣmīś ca bhadrā ṣaṣṭhī tathāparā
d pṛthivī gāṃ gatā devī hrīḥ svāhā kīrtir eva ca
d surā devī śacī caiva tathā puṣṭir arundhatī
d saṃvṛttir āśā niyatiḥ sṛṣṭir devī ratis tathā
d etāś cānyāś ca vai devya upatasthuḥ prajāpatim
a ādityā vasavo rudrā marutaś cāśvināv api
c viśvedevāś ca sādhyāś ca pitaraś ca manojavāḥ
d pitṝṇāṃ ca gaṇān viddhi saptaiva puruṣarṣabha
d catvāro mūrtimanto vai trayaś cāpy aśarīriṇaḥ
d vairājāś ca mahābhāgā agniṣvuāttāś ca bhārata
d gārhapatyā nākacarāḥ pitaro lokaviśrutāḥ
d somapā ekaśṛṅgāś ca caturvedāḥ kalās tathā
d ete caturṣu varṇeṣu pūjyante pitaro nṛpa
d etair āpyāyitaiḥ pūrvaṃ somaś cāpyāyyate punaḥ
d ta ete pitaraḥ sarve prajāpatim upasthitāḥ
d upāsate ca saṃhṛṣṭā brahmāṇam amitaujasam
a rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca dānavā guhyakās tathā
c suparṇanāgapaśavaḥ pitāmaham upāsate
d sthāvarā jaṅgamāś caiva mahābhūtās tathāpare
d puraṃdaraś ca devendro varuṇo dhanado yamaḥ
d mahādevaḥ sahomo 'tra sadāgacchati sarvaśaḥ
d mahāsenaś ca rājendra sadopāste pitāmaham
a devo nārāyaṇas tasyāṃ tathā devarṣayaś ca ye
c ṛṣayo vālakhilyāś ca yonijāyonijās tathā
a yac ca kiṃ cit triloke 'smin dṛśyate sthāṇujaṅgamam
c sarvaṃ tasyāṃ mayā dṛṣṭaṃ tad viddhi manujādhipa
a aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi yatīnām ūrdhvaretasām
c prajāvatāṃ ca pañcāśad ṛṣīṇām api pāṇḍava
a te sma tatra yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve divaukasaḥ
c praṇamya śirasā tasmai pratiyānti yathāgatam
a atithīn āgatān devān daityān nāgān munīṃs tathā
c yakṣān suparṇān kāleyān gandharvāpsarasas tathā
a mahābhāgān amitadhīr brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
c dayāvān sarvabhūteṣu yathārhaṃ pratipadyate
a pratigṛhya ca viśvātmā svayaṃbhūr amitaprabhaḥ
b madhureṇa sāmnā bhagavān pratigṛhṇāti nityaśaḥ
c sāntvamānārthasaṃbhogair yunakti manujādhipa
a tathā tair upayātaiś ca pratiyātaiś ca bhārata
c ākulā sā sabhā tāta bhavati sma sukhapradā
a sarvatejomayī divyā brahmarṣigaṇasevitā
c brāhmyā śriyā dīpyamānā śuśubhe vigataklamā
a sā sabhā tādṛśī dṛṣṭā sarvalokeṣu durlabhā
c sabheyaṃ rājaśārdūla manuṣyeṣu yathā tava
a etā mayā dṛṣṭapūrvāḥ sabhā deveṣu pāṇḍava
c taveyaṃ mānuṣe loke sarvaśreṣṭhatamā sabhā
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a prāyaśo rājalokas te kathito vadatāṃ vara
c vaivasvatasabhāyāṃ tu yathā vadasi vai prabho
a varuṇasya sabhāyāṃ tu nāgās te kathitā vibho
c daityendrāś caiva bhūyiṣṭhāḥ saritaḥ sāgarās tathā
a tathā dhanapater yakṣā guhyakā rākṣasās tathā
c gandharvāpsarasaś caiva bhagavāṃś ca vṛṣadhvajaḥ
a pitāmahasabhāyāṃ tu kathitās te maharṣayaḥ
c sarvadevanikāyāś ca sarvaśāstrāṇi caiva hi
a śatakratusabhāyāṃ tu devāḥ saṃkīrtitā mune
c uddeśataś ca gandharvā vividhāś ca maharṣayaḥ
a eka eva tu rājarṣir hariścandro mahāmune
c kathitas te sabhānityo devendrasya mahātmanaḥ
d kena karmavipākena hariścandro dvijarṣabha
d teṣu rājasahasreṣu prabhayāpy atirocate
a kiṃ karma tenācaritaṃ tapo vā niyatavratam
b kiṃ cid dattaṃ hutaṃ tena iṣṭaṃ vāpi mahāmune
c yenāsau saha śakreṇa spardhate sma mahāyaśāḥ
a pitṛlokagataś cāpi tvayā vipra pitā mama
c dṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍur mahābhāgaḥ kathaṃ cāsi samāgataḥ
a kim uktavāṃś ca bhagavann etad icchāmi veditum
b anāgatam atikrāntaṃ tat sarvaṃ tvayi niṣṭhitam
c tvattaḥ śrotum ahaṃ sarvaṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
 nārada uvāca
a yan māṃ pṛcchasi rājendra hariścandraṃ prati prabho
c tat te 'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi māhātmyaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
d ikṣvākūṇāṃ kule jātas triśaṅkur nāma pārthivaḥ
d ayodhyādhipatir vīro viśvāmitreṇa saṃsthitaḥ
d tasya satyavatī nāma patnī kekayavaṃśajā
d tasyāṃ garbhaḥ samabhavad dharmeṇa kurunandana
d sā ca kāle mahābhāgā janmamāsaṃ praviśya vai
d kumāraṃ janayām āsa hariścandram akalmaṣam
d sa vai rājā hariścandras traiśaṅkava iti smṛtaḥ
a sa rājā balavān āsīt samrāṭ sarvamahīkṣitām
c tasya sarve mahīpālāḥ śāsanāvanatāḥ sthitāḥ
a tenaikaṃ ratham āsthāya jaitraṃ hemavibhūṣitam
c śastrapratāpena jitā dvīpāḥ sapta nareśvara
a sa vijitya mahīṃ sarvāṃ saśailavanakānanām
c ājahāra mahārāja rājasūyaṃ mahākratum
a tasya sarve mahīpālā dhanāny ājahrur ājñayā
c dvijānāṃ pariveṣṭāras tasmin yajñe ca te 'bhavan
a prādāc ca draviṇaṃ prītyā yājakānāṃ nareśvaraḥ
c yathoktaṃ tatra tais tasmiṃs tataḥ pañcaguṇādhikam
a atarpayac ca vividhair vasubhir brāhmaṇāṃs tathā
c prāsarpakāle saṃprāpte nānādigbhyaḥ samāgatān
a bhakṣyair bhojyaiś ca vividhair yathākāmapuraskṛtaiḥ
c ratnaughatarpitais tuṣṭair dvijaiś ca samudāhṛtam
e tejasvī ca yaśasvī ca nṛpebhyo 'bhyadhiko 'bhavat
a etasmāt kāraṇāt pārtha hariścandro virājate
c tebhyo rājasahasrebhyas tad viddhi bharatarṣabha
a samāpya ca hariścandro mahāyajñaṃ pratāpavān
c abhiṣiktaḥ sa śuśubhe sāmrājyena narādhipa
d rājasūye 'bhiṣiktas tu samāptavaradakṣiṇe
a ye cānye 'pi mahīpālā rājasūyaṃ mahākratum
c yajante te mahendreṇa modante saha bhārata
a ye cāpi nidhanaṃ prāptāḥ saṃgrāmeṣv apalāyinaḥ
c te tatsadaḥ samāsādya modante bharatarṣabha
a tapasā ye ca tīvreṇa tyajantīha kalevaram
c te 'pi tat sthānam āsādya śrīmanto bhānti nityaśaḥ
a pitā ca tvāha kaunteya pāṇḍuḥ kauravanandanaḥ
c hariścandre śriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatau jātavismayaḥ
d vijñāya mānuṣaṃ lokam āyāntaṃ māṃ narādhipa
d provāca praṇato bhūtvā vadethās tvaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a samartho 'si mahīṃ jetuṃ bhrātaras te vaśe sthitāḥ
c rājasūyaṃ kratuśreṣṭham āharasveti bhārata
d tvayīṣṭavati putre 'haṃ hariścandravad āśu vai
d modiṣye bahulāḥ śaśvat samāḥ śakrasya saṃsadi
d evaṃ bhavatu vakṣye 'haṃ tava putraṃ narādhipam
d bhūrlokaṃ yadi gaccheyam iti pāṇḍum athābruvam
a tasya tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra saṃkalpaṃ kuru pāṇḍava
b gantāras te mahendrasya pūrve sarve pitāmahāḥ
b salokatāṃ surendrasya trailokyādhipater nṛpa
c gantāras te mahendrasya pūrvaiḥ saha salokatām
a bahuvighnaś ca nṛpate kratur eṣa smṛto mahān
c chidrāṇy atra hi vāñchanti yajñaghnā brahmarākṣasāḥ
a yuddhaṃ ca pṛṣṭhagamanaṃ pṛthivīkṣayakārakam
c kiṃ cid eva nimittaṃ ca bhavaty atra kṣayāvaham
d etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ karavāṇi te
a etat saṃcintya rājendra yat kṣamaṃ tat samācara
c apramattotthito nityaṃ cāturvarṇyasya rakṣaṇe
e bhava edhasva modasva dānais tarpaya ca dvijān
a etat te vistareṇoktaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
c āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi dāśārhanagarīṃ prati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam ākhyāya pārthebhyo nārado janamejaya
c jagāma tair vṛto rājann ṛṣibhir yaiḥ samāgataḥ
a gate tu nārade pārtho bhrātṛbhiḥ saha kaurava
c rājasūyaṃ kratuśreṣṭhaṃ cintayām āsa bhārata
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ṛṣes tad vacanaṃ śrutvā niśaśvāsa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c cintayan rājasūyāptiṃ na lebhe śarma bhārata
a rājarṣīṇāṃ hi taṃ śrutvā mahimānaṃ mahātmanām
c yajvanāṃ karmabhiḥ puṇyair lokaprāptiṃ samīkṣya ca
a hariścandraṃ ca rājarṣiṃ rocamānaṃ viśeṣataḥ
c yajvānaṃ yajñam āhartuṃ rājasūyam iyeṣa saḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiras tataḥ sarvān arcayitvā sabhāsadaḥ
c pratyarcitaś ca taiḥ sarvair yajñāyaiva mano dadhe
a sa rājasūyaṃ rājendra kurūṇām ṛṣabhaḥ kratum
c āhartuṃ pravaṇaṃ cakre manaḥ saṃcintya so 'sakṛt
a bhūyaś cādbhutavīryaujā dharmam evānupālayan
c kiṃ hitaṃ sarvalokānāṃ bhaved iti mano dadhe
a anugṛhṇan prajāḥ sarvāḥ sarvadharmavidāṃ varaḥ
c aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣāṃ hitaṃ cakre yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d sarveṣāṃ dīyatāṃ deyaṃ muṣṇan kopamadāv ubhau
d sādhu dharmeti dharmeti nānyac chrūyeta bhāṣitam
a evaṃ gate tatas tasmin pitarīvāśvasañ janāḥ
c na tasya vidyate dveṣṭā tato 'syājātaśatrutā
d parigrahān narendrasya bhīmasya paripālanāt
d śatrūṇāṃ kṣapaṇāc caiva bībhatsoḥ savyasācinaḥ
d dhīmataḥ sahadevasya dharmāṇām anuśāsanāt
d avigrahā vītabhayāḥ svakarmaniratāḥ sadā
d nikāmavarṣāḥ sphītāś ca āsañ janapadās tathā
d vārdhuṣī yajñasattvāni gorakṣaṃ karṣaṇaṃ vaṇik
d viśeṣāt sarvam evaitat saṃjajñe rājakarmaṇā
d anukarṣaṃ ca niṣkarṣaṃ vyādhipāvakamūrchanam
d sarvam eva na tatrāsīd dharmanitye yudhiṣṭhire
d dasyubhyo vañcakebhyaś ca rājñaḥ prati parasparam
d rājavallabhataś caiva nāśrūyata mṛṣākṛtam
d priyaṃ kartum upasthātuṃ balikarma svakarmajam
d abhihartuṃ nṛpāḥ ṣaṭsu pṛthak jātyaiś ca naigamaiḥ
d vavṛdhe viṣayas tatra dharmanitye yudhiṣṭhire
d kāmato 'py upayuñjānai rājasair lobhajair janaiḥ
d sarvavyāpī sarvaguṇī sarvasāhaḥ sa sarvarāṭ
d yasminn adhikṛtaḥ samrāḍ bhrājamāno mahāyaśāḥ
d yatra rājan daśa diśaḥ pitṛto mātṛtas tathā
d anuraktāḥ prajā āsann āgopālā dvijātayaḥ
a sa mantriṇaḥ samānāyya bhrātṝṃś ca vadatāṃ varaḥ
c rājasūyaṃ prati tadā punaḥ punar apṛcchata
a te pṛcchyamānāḥ sahitā vaco 'rthyaṃ mantriṇas tadā
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahāprājñaṃ yiyakṣum idam abruvan
a yenābhiṣikto nṛpatir vāruṇaṃ guṇam ṛcchati
c tena rājāpi san kṛtsnaṃ samrāḍguṇam abhīpsati
a tasya samrāḍguṇārhasya bhavataḥ kurunandana
c rājasūyasya samayaṃ manyante suhṛdas tava
a tasya yajñasya samayaḥ svādhīnaḥ kṣatrasaṃpadā
c sāmnā ṣaḍ agnayo yasmiṃś cīyante saṃśitavrataiḥ
a darvīhomān upādāya sarvān yaḥ prāpnute kratūn
c abhiṣekaṃ ca yajñānte sarvajit tena cocyate
a samartho 'si mahābāho sarve te vaśagā vayam
b acirāt tvaṃ mahārāja rājasūyam avāpsyasi
c avicārya mahārāja rājasūye manaḥ kuru
a ity evaṃ suhṛdaḥ sarve pṛthak ca saha cābruvan
c sa dharmyaṃ pāṇḍavas teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā viśāṃ pate
e dhṛṣṭam iṣṭaṃ variṣṭhaṃ ca jagrāha manasārihā
a śrutvā suhṛdvacas tac ca jānaṃś cāpy ātmanaḥ kṣamam
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b saṃpraśastaḥ kṣamārambhaḥ parīkṣām upacakrame
b caturbhir bhīmasenādyair bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitair hitam
b evam uktas tadā pārtho dharma eva mano dadhe
b sa rājasūyaṃ rājendraḥ kurūṇām ṛṣabhaḥ kratum
b jagāma manasā sadya āhariṣyan yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b bhūyas tv adbhutavīryaujā dharmam evānupālayan
c punaḥ punar mano dadhre rājasūyāya bhārata
a sa bhrātṛbhiḥ punar dhīmān ṛtvigbhiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
b mantribhiś cāpi sahito dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c dhaumyadvaipāyanādyaiś ca mantrayām āsa mantribhiḥ
d bhīmārjunayamaiḥ sārdhaṃ pārṣatena ca dhīmatā
d virāṭadrupadābhyāṃ ca sātyakena ca dhīmatā
d yudhāmanyūttamaujobhyāṃ saubhadreṇa ca dhīmatā
d draupadeyaiḥ paraṃ śūrair mantrayām āsa saṃvṛtaḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a iyaṃ yā rājasūyasya samrāḍarhasya sukratoḥ
c śraddadhānasya vadataḥ spṛhā me sā kathaṃ bhavet
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktās tu te tena rājñā rājīvalocana
c idam ūcur vacaḥ kāle dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
e arhas tvam asi dharmajña rājasūyaṃ mahākratum
a athaivam ukte nṛpatāv ṛtvigbhir ṛṣibhis tathā
c mantriṇo bhrātaraś cāsya tad vacaḥ pratyapūjayan
a sa tu rājā mahāprājñaḥ punar evātmanātmavān
c bhūyo vimamṛśe pārtho lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
a sāmarthyayogaṃ saṃprekṣya deśakālau vyayāgamau
c vimṛśya samyak ca dhiyā kurvan prājño na sīdati
d sarvais tair niścitamatiḥ kāla ity eva bhārata
a na hi yajñasamārambhaḥ kevalātmavipattaye
c bhavatīti samājñāya yatnataḥ kāryam udvahan
a sa niścayārthaṃ kāryasya kṛṣṇam eva janārdanam
c sarvalokāt paraṃ matvā jagāma manasā harim
a aprameyaṃ mahābāhuṃ kāmāj jātam ajaṃ nṛṣu
c pāṇḍavas tarkayām āsa karmabhir devasaṃmitaiḥ
a nāsya kiṃ cid avijñātaṃ nāsya kiṃ cid akarmajam
c na sa kiṃ cin na viṣahed iti kṛṣṇam amanyata
a sa tu tāṃ naiṣṭhikīṃ buddhiṃ kṛtvā pārtho yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c guruvad bhūtagurave prāhiṇod dūtam añjasā
a śīghragena rathenāśu sa dūtaḥ prāpya yādavān
c dvārakāvāsinaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dvāravatyāṃ samāsadat
d dūtaḥ
d sa prahvaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā vijñāpayata mādhavam
d dharmarājo hṛṣīkeśa dhaumyavyāsādibhiḥ saha
d pāñcālamātsyasahitair bhrātṛbhiś caiva sarvaśaḥ
d tvaddarśanaṃ mahābāho kāṅkṣate sa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d indrasenavacaḥ śrutvā yādavapravaro balī
a darśanākāṅkṣiṇaṃ pārthaṃ darśanākāṅkṣayācyutaḥ
b āmantrya vasudevaṃ ca baladevaṃ ca mādhavaḥ
c indrasenena sahita indraprasthaṃ yayau tadā
a vyatītya vividhān deśāṃs tvarāvān kṣipravāhanaḥ
c indraprasthagataṃ pārtham abhyagacchaj janārdanaḥ
a sa gṛhe bhrātṛvad bhrātrā dharmarājena pūjitaḥ
c bhīmena ca tato 'paśyat svasāraṃ prītimān pituḥ
a prītaḥ priyeṇa suhṛdā reme sa sahitas tadā
c arjunena yamābhyāṃ ca guruvat paryupasthitaḥ
a taṃ viśrāntaṃ śubhe deśe kṣaṇinaṃ kalyam acyutam
c dharmarājaḥ samāgamya jñāpayat svaṃ prayojanam
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a prārthito rājasūyo me na cāsau kevalepsayā
c prāpyate yena tat te ha viditaṃ kṛṣṇa sarvaśaḥ
a yasmin sarvaṃ saṃbhavati yaś ca sarvatra pūjyate
c yaś ca sarveśvaro rājā rājasūyaṃ sa vindati
a taṃ rājasūyaṃ suhṛdaḥ kāryam āhuḥ sametya me
c tatra me niścitatamaṃ tava kṛṣṇa girā bhavet
a ke cid dhi sauhṛdād eva doṣaṃ na paricakṣate
c arthahetos tathaivānye priyam eva vadanty uta
a priyam eva parīpsante ke cid ātmani yad dhitam
c evaṃprāyāś ca dṛśyante janavādāḥ prayojane
a tvaṃ tu hetūn atītyaitān kāmakrodhau vyatītya ca
c paramaṃ naḥ kṣamaṃ loke yathāvad vaktum arhasi
 śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca
a sarvair guṇair mahārāja rājasūyaṃ tvam arhasi
c jānatas tv eva te sarvaṃ kiṃ cid vakṣyāmi bhārata
a jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatraṃ yad avaśeṣitam
c tasmād avarajaṃ loke yad idaṃ kṣatrasaṃjñitam
a kṛto 'yaṃ kulasaṃkalpaḥ kṣatriyair vasudhādhipa
c nideśavāgbhis tat te ha viditaṃ bharatarṣabha
a ailasyekṣvākuvaṃśasya prakṛtiṃ paricakṣate
c rājānaḥ śreṇibaddhāś ca tato 'nye kṣatriyā bhuvi
a ailavaṃśyās tu ye rājaṃs tathaivekṣvākavo nṛpāḥ
c tāni caikaśataṃ viddhi kulāni bharatarṣabha
a yayātes tv eva bhojānāṃ vistaro 'tiguṇo mahān
c bhajate ca mahārāja vistaraḥ sa caturdiśam
a teṣāṃ tathaiva tāṃ lakṣmīṃ sarvakṣatram upāsate
b idānīm eva vai rājañ jarāsaṃdho mahīpatiḥ
b abhibhūya śriyaṃ teṣāṃ kulānām abhiṣecitaḥ
b sthito mūrdhni narendrāṇām ojasākramya sarvaśaḥ
c so 'vanīṃ madhyamāṃ bhuktvā mithobhedeṣv amanyata
a caturyus tv aparo rājā yasminn ekaśato 'bhavat
c sa sāmrājyaṃ jarāsaṃdhaḥ prāpto bhavati yonitaḥ
a taṃ sa rājā mahāprājña saṃśritya kila sarvaśaḥ
c rājan senāpatir jātaḥ śiśupālaḥ pratāpavān
a tam eva ca mahārāja śiṣyavat samupasthitaḥ
c vakraḥ karūṣādhipatir māyāyodhī mahābalaḥ
a aparau ca mahāvīryau mahātmānau samāśritau
c jarāsaṃdhaṃ mahāvīryaṃ tau haṃsaḍibhakāv ubhau
a dantavakraḥ karūṣaś ca kalabho meghavāhanaḥ
c mūrdhnā divyaṃ maṇiṃ bibhrad yaṃ taṃ bhūtamaṇiṃ viduḥ
a muraṃ ca narakaṃ caiva śāsti yo yavanādhipau
c aparyantabalo rājā pratīcyāṃ varuṇo yathā
a bhagadatto mahārāja vṛddhas tava pituḥ sakhā
c sa vācā praṇatas tasya karmaṇā caiva bhārata
a snehabaddhas tu pitṛvan manasā bhaktimāṃs tvayi
c pratīcyāṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cāntaṃ pṛthivyāḥ pāti yo nṛpaḥ
d te cāpi praṇatās tasya mahātmāno bhayārditāḥ
a mātulo bhavataḥ śūraḥ purujit kuntivardhanaḥ
c sa te saṃnatimān ekaḥ snehataḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
a jarāsaṃdhaṃ gatas tv evaṃ purā yo na mayā hataḥ
c puruṣottamavijñāto yo 'sau cediṣu durmatiḥ
a ātmānaṃ pratijānāti loke 'smin puruṣottamam
c ādatte satataṃ mohād yaḥ sa cihnaṃ ca māmakam
a vaṅgapuṇḍrakirāteṣu rājā balasamanvitaḥ
c pauṇḍrako vāsudeveti yo 'sau lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
a caturyuḥ sa mahārāja bhoja indrasakho balī
c vidyābalād yo vyajayat pāṇḍyakrathakakaiśikān
a bhrātā yasyāhṛtiḥ śūro jāmadagnyasamo yudhi
c sa bhakto māgadhaṃ rājā bhīṣmakaḥ paravīrahā
a priyāṇy ācarataḥ prahvān sadā saṃbandhinaḥ sataḥ
c bhajato na bhajaty asmān apriyeṣu vyavasthitaḥ
a na kulaṃ na balaṃ rājann abhijānaṃs tathātmanaḥ
c paśyamāno yaśo dīptaṃ jarāsaṃdham upāśritaḥ
a udīcyabhojāś ca tathā kulāny aṣṭādaśābhibho
c jarāsaṃdhabhayād eva pratīcīṃ diśam āśritāḥ
a śūrasenā bhadrakārā bodhāḥ śālvāḥ paṭaccarāḥ
c sustharāś ca sukuṭṭāś ca kuṇindāḥ kuntibhiḥ saha
a śālveyānāṃ ca rājānaḥ sodaryānucaraiḥ saha
c dakṣiṇā ye ca pāñcālāḥ pūrvāḥ kuntiṣu kośalāḥ
a tathottarāṃ diśaṃ cāpi parityajya bhayārditāḥ
c matsyāḥ saṃnyastapādāś ca dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āśritāḥ
a tathaiva sarvapāñcālā jarāsaṃdhabhayārditāḥ
c svarāṣṭraṃ saṃparityajya vidrutāḥ sarvatodiśam
d agrato hy asya pāñcālās tatrānīke mahātmanaḥ
d anirgate sārabale māgadhebhyo girivrajāt
a kasya cit tv atha kālasya kaṃso nirmathya bāndhavān
c bārhadrathasute devyāv upāgacchad vṛthāmatiḥ
a astiḥ prāptiś ca nāmnā te sahadevānuje 'bale
c balena tena sa jñātīn abhibhūya vṛthāmatiḥ
a śraiṣṭhyaṃ prāptaḥ sa tasyāsīd atīvāpanayo mahān
c bhojarājanyavṛddhais tu pīḍyamānair durātmanā
a jñātitrāṇam abhīpsadbhir asmatsaṃbhāvanā kṛtā
c dattvākrūrāya sutanuṃ tām āhukasutāṃ tadā
a saṃkarṣaṇadvitīyena jñātikāryaṃ mayā kṛtam
c hatau kaṃsasunāmānau mayā rāmeṇa cāpy uta
d hatvā kaṃsaṃ tathaivājau jarāsaṃdhasya bibhyatā
d mayā rāmeṇa cānyatra jñātayaḥ paripālitāḥ
a bhaye tu samupakrānte jarāsaṃdhe samudyate
c mantro 'yaṃ mantrito rājan kulair aṣṭādaśāvaraiḥ
a anāramanto nighnanto mahāstraiḥ śataghātibhiḥ
c na hanyāma vayaṃ tasya tribhir varṣaśatair balam
a tasya hy amarasaṃkāśau balena balināṃ varau
c nāmabhyāṃ haṃsaḍibhakāv ity āstāṃ yodhasattamau
a tāv ubhau sahitau vīrau jarāsaṃdhaś ca vīryavān
c trayas trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ paryāptā iti me matiḥ
a na hi kevalam asmākaṃ yāvanto 'nye ca pārthivāḥ
c tathaiva teṣām āsīc ca buddhir buddhimatāṃ vara
d aṣṭādaśa mayā tasya saṃgrāmā romaharṣaṇaḥ
d dattā na ca hato rājañ jarāsaṃdho mahābalaḥ
a atha haṃsa iti khyātaḥ kaś cid āsīn mahān nṛpaḥ
c sa cānyaiḥ sahito rājan saṃgrāme 'ṣṭādaśāvaraiḥ
a hato haṃsa iti proktam atha kenāpi bhārata
c tac chrutvā ḍibhako rājan yamunāmbhasy amajjata
a vinā haṃsena loke 'smin nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe
c ity etāṃ matim āsthāya ḍibhako nidhanaṃ gataḥ
a tathā tu ḍibhakaṃ śrutvā haṃsaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c prapede yamunām eva so 'pi tasyāṃ nyamajjata
a tau sa rājā jarāsaṃdhaḥ śrutvāpsu nidhanaṃ gatau
c svapuraṃ śūrasenānāṃ prayayau bharatarṣabha
a tato vayam amitraghna tasmin pratigate nṛpe
c punar ānanditāḥ sarve mathurāyāṃ vasāmahe
a yadā tv abhyetya pitaraṃ sā vai rājīvalocanā
c kaṃsabhāryā jarāsaṃdhaṃ duhitā māgadhaṃ nṛpam
a codayaty eva rājendra pativyasanaduḥkhitā
c patighnaṃ me jahīty evaṃ punaḥ punar ariṃdama
a tato vayaṃ mahārāja taṃ mantraṃ pūrvamantritam
c saṃsmaranto vimanaso vyapayātā narādhipa
a pṛthaktvena drutā rājan saṃkṣipya mahatīṃ śriyam
c prapatāmo bhayāt tasya sadhanajñātibāndhavāḥ
a iti saṃcintya sarve sma pratīcīṃ diśam āśritāḥ
c kuśasthalīṃ purīṃ ramyāṃ raivatenopaśobhitām
a punar niveśanaṃ tasyāṃ kṛtavanto vayaṃ nṛpa
c tathaiva durgasaṃskāraṃ devair api durāsadam
a striyo 'pi yasyāṃ yudhyeyuḥ kiṃ punar vṛṣṇipuṃgavāḥ
c tasyāṃ vayam amitraghna nivasāmo 'kutobhayāḥ
a ālokya girimukhyaṃ taṃ mādhavītīrtham eva ca
c mādhavāḥ kuruśārdūla parāṃ mudam avāpnuvan
a evaṃ vayaṃ jarāsaṃdhād āditaḥ kṛtakilbiṣāḥ
c sāmarthyavantaḥ saṃbandhād bhavantaṃ samupāśritāḥ
a triyojanāyataṃ sadma triskandhaṃ yojanād adhi
c yojanānte śatadvāraṃ vikramakramatoraṇam
e aṣṭādaśāvarair naddhaṃ kṣatriyair yuddhadurmadaiḥ
a aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi vrātānāṃ santi naḥ kule
c āhukasya śataṃ putrā ekaikas triśatāvaraḥ
a cārudeṣṇaḥ saha bhrātrā cakradevo 'tha sātyakiḥ
c ahaṃ ca rauhiṇeyaś ca sāmbaḥ śaurisamo yudhi
a evam ete rathāḥ sapta rājann anyān nibodha me
c kṛtavarmā anādhṛṣṭiḥ samīkaḥ samitiṃjayaḥ
a kahvaḥ śaṅkur nidāntaś ca saptaivaite mahārathāḥ
b pradyumnaś cāniruddhaś ca bhānur akrūrasāraṇau
b niśaṭhaś ca gadaś caiva sapta caite mahārathāḥ
b vitadrur jhallibabhrū ca uddhavo 'tha viḍūrathaḥ
b vasudevograsenau ca saptaite mantripuṃgavāḥ
b prasenajic ca yamalo rājarājaguṇānvitaḥ
b syamantako maṇir yasya rukmaṃ nisravate bahu
c putrau cāndhakabhojasya vṛddho rājā ca te daśa
a lokasaṃhananā vīrā vīryavanto mahābalāḥ
c smaranto madhyamaṃ deśaṃ vṛṣṇimadhye gatavyathāḥ
d śrībhagavān
d pāṇḍavaiś cāpi satataṃ nāthavanto vayaṃ nṛpa
a sa tvaṃ samrāḍguṇair yuktaḥ sadā bharatasattama
c kṣatre samrājam ātmānaṃ kartum arhasi bhārata
d duryodhanaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ droṇaṃ droṇāyaniṃ kṛpam
d karṇaṃ ca śiśupālaṃ ca rukmiṇaṃ ca dhanurdharam
d ekalavyaṃ drumaṃ śvetaṃ śalyaṃ śakunim eva ca
d etān ajitvā saṃgrāme kathaṃ śaknoṣi taṃ kratum
d athaite gauraveṇaiva na yotsyanti narādhipāḥ
d ekas tatra balonmattaḥ karṇo vaikartano vṛṣā
d yotsyate sa balāmarṣī divyāstrabalagarvitaḥ
a na tu śakyaṃ jarāsaṃdhe jīvamāne mahābale
c rājasūyas tvayā prāptum eṣā rājan matir mama
a tena ruddhā hi rājānaḥ sarve jitvā girivraje
c kandarāyāṃ girīndrasya siṃheneva mahādvipāḥ
a so 'pi rājā jarāsaṃdho yiyakṣur vasudhādhipaiḥ
b mahādevaṃ mahātmānam umāpatim ariṃdama
b abhiṣiktaiś ca rājanyaiḥ sahasrair uta cāṣṭabhiḥ
c ārādhya hi mahādevaṃ nirjitās tena pārthivāḥ
d pratijñāyāś ca pāraṃ sa gataḥ kṣatriyapuṃgavaḥ
a sa hi nirjitya nirjitya pārthivān pṛtanāgatān
c puram ānīya baddhvā ca cakāra puruṣavrajam
a vayaṃ caiva mahārāja jarāsaṃdhabhayāt tadā
c mathurāṃ saṃparityajya gatā dvāravatīṃ purīm
d nivasāma tathādyāpi sadhanajñātibāndhavāḥ
d kaṃsahetor hi yad vairaṃ māgadhasya mayā saha
d pāraṃ gatvā sa tasyājau yiyakṣur devam uttamam
a yadi tv enaṃ mahārāja yajñaṃ prāptum ihecchasi
c yatasva teṣāṃ mokṣāya jarāsaṃdhavadhāya ca
a samārambho hi śakyo 'yaṃ nānyathā kurunandana
c rājasūyasya kārtsnyena kartuṃ matimatāṃ vara
d jarāsaṃdhavadhopāyaś cintyatāṃ bharatarṣabha
d tasmiñ jite jitaṃ sarvaṃ sakalaṃ pārthivaṃ balam
a ity eṣā me matī rājan yathā vā manyase 'nagha
c evaṃ gate mamācakṣva svayaṃ niścitya hetubhiḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a uktaṃ tvayā buddhimatā yan nānyo vaktum arhati
c saṃśayānāṃ hi nirmoktā tvan nānyo vidyate bhuvi
a gṛhe gṛhe hi rājānaḥ svasya svasya priyaṃkarāḥ
c na ca sāmrājyam āptās te samrāṭśabdo hi kṛtsnabhāk
a kathaṃ parānubhāvajñaḥ svaṃ praśaṃsitum arhati
c pareṇa samavetas tu yaḥ praśastaḥ sa pūjyate
a viśālā bahulā bhūmir bahuratnasamācitā
c dūraṃ gatvā vijānāti śreyo vṛṣṇikulodvaha
a śamam eva paraṃ manye na tu mokṣād bhavec chamaḥ
c ārambhe pārameṣṭhyaṃ tu na prāpyam iti me matiḥ
a evam evābhijānanti kule jātā manasvinaḥ
c kaś cit kadā cid eteṣāṃ bhavec chreṣṭho janārdana
d vayaṃ caiva mahābhāga jarāsaṃdhabhayāt tadā
d śaṅkitāḥ sma mahābhāga daurātmyāt tasya cānagha
d ahaṃ hi tava durdharṣa bhujavīryāśrayaḥ prabho
d nātmānaṃ balinaṃ manye tvayi tasmād viśaṅkite
d tvatsakāśāc ca rāmāc ca bhīmasenāc ca mādhava
d arjunād vā mahābāho hantuṃ śakyo na veti vai
d evaṃ jānan hi vārṣṇeya vimṛśāmi punaḥ punaḥ
d tvaṃ me pramāṇabhūto 'si sarvakāryeṣu keśava
d tac chrutvā cābravīd bhīmo vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
 bhīma uvāca
a anārambhaparo rājā valmīka iva sīdati
c durbalaś cānupāyena balinaṃ yo 'dhitiṣṭhati
a atandritas tu prāyeṇa durbalo balinaṃ ripum
c jayet samyaṅ nayo rājan nītyārthān ātmano hitān
a kṛṣṇe nayo mayi balaṃ jayaḥ pārthe dhanaṃjaye
c māgadhaṃ sādhayiṣyāmo vayaṃ traya ivāgnayaḥ
d tvadbuddhibalam āśritya sarvaṃ prāpsyati dharmarāṭ
d jayo 'smākaṃ hi govinda yeṣāṃ nātho bhavān sadā
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a ādatte 'rthaparo bālo nānubandham avekṣate
c tasmād ariṃ na mṛṣyanti bālam arthaparāyaṇam
d sarvān vaṃśyān anumṛśann ekam eva satāṃ yuge
a hitvā karān yauvanāśvaḥ pālanāc ca bhagīrathaḥ
c kārtavīryas tapoyogād balāt tu bharato vibhuḥ
e ṛddhyā maruttas tān pañca samrāja iti śuśrumaḥ
f sāmrājyam icchatas te tu sarvākāraṃ yudhiṣṭhira
f sarvān vaṃśān anumṛśan naite santi yuge yuge
a nigrāhyalakṣaṇaṃ prāpto dharmārthanayalakṣaṇaiḥ
c bārhadratho jarāsaṃdhas tad viddhi bharatarṣabha
a na cainam anurudhyante kulāny ekaśataṃ nṛpāḥ
c tasmād etad balād eva sāmrājyaṃ kurute 'dya saḥ
a ratnabhājo hi rājāno jarāsaṃdham upāsate
c na ca tuṣyati tenāpi bālyād anayam āsthitaḥ
a mūrdhābhiṣiktaṃ nṛpatiṃ pradhānapuruṣaṃ balāt
c ādatte na ca no dṛṣṭo 'bhāgaḥ puruṣataḥ kva cit
a evaṃ sarvān vaśe cakre jarāsaṃdhaḥ śatāvarān
c taṃ durbalataro rājā kathaṃ pārtha upaiṣyati
d taṇḍulaprasthake rājā kapardinam upāsta saḥ
d kathaṃ jitvā punar yūyam asmān saṃpratiyāsyatha
a prokṣitānāṃ pramṛṣṭānāṃ rājñāṃ paśupater gṛhe
c paśūnām iva kā prītir jīvite bharatarṣabha
a kṣatriyaḥ śastramaraṇo yadā bhavati satkṛtaḥ
c nanu sma māgadhaṃ sarve pratibādhema yad vayam
a ṣaḍaśītiḥ samānītāḥ śeṣā rājaṃś caturdaśa
c jarāsaṃdhena rājānas tataḥ krūraṃ prapatsyate
a prāpnuyāt sa yaśo dīptaṃ tatra yo vighnam ācaret
c jayed yaś ca jarāsaṃdhaṃ sa samrāṇ niyataṃ bhavet
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a samrāḍguṇam abhīpsan vai yuṣmān svārthaparāyaṇaḥ
c kathaṃ prahiṇuyāṃ bhīmaṃ balāt kevalasāhasāt
a bhīmārjunāv ubhau netre mano manye janārdanam
c manaścakṣurvihīnasya kīdṛśaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet
a jarāsaṃdhabalaṃ prāpya duṣpāraṃ bhīmavikramam
c śramo hi vaḥ parājayyāt kim u tatra viceṣṭitam
a asminn arthāntare yuktam anarthaḥ pratipadyate
c yathāhaṃ vimṛśāmy ekas tat tāvac chrūyatāṃ mama
d tasmān na pratipattis tu kāryā yuktā matā mama
a saṃnyāsaṃ rocaye sādhu kāryasyāsya janārdana
c pratihanti mano me 'dya rājasūyo durāsadaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pārthaḥ prāpya dhanuḥśreṣṭham akṣayyau ca maheṣudhī
c rathaṃ dhvajaṃ sabhāṃ caiva yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣata
a dhanur astraṃ śarā vīryaṃ pakṣo bhūmir yaśo balam
c prāptam etan mayā rājan duṣprāpaṃ yad abhīpsitam
a kule janma praśaṃsanti vaidyāḥ sādhu suniṣṭhitāḥ
c balena sadṛśaṃ nāsti vīryaṃ tu mama rocate
a kṛtavīryakule jāto nirvīryaḥ kiṃ kariṣyati
b nirvīrye tu kule jāto vīryavāṃs tu viśiṣyate
c kṣatriyaḥ sarvaśo rājan yasya vṛttiḥ parājaye
a sarvair api guṇair hīno vīryavān hi tared ripūn
c sarvair api guṇair yukto nirvīryaḥ kiṃ kariṣyati
a dravyabhūtā guṇāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti hi parākrame
c jayasya hetuḥ siddhir hi karma daivaṃ ca saṃśritam
a saṃyukto hi balaiḥ kaś cit pramādān nopayujyate
c tena dvāreṇa śatrubhyaḥ kṣīyate sabalo ripuḥ
a dainyaṃ yathābalavati tathā moho balānvite
c tāv ubhau nāśakau hetū rājñā tyājyau jayārthinā
a jarāsaṃdhavināśaṃ ca rājñāṃ ca parimokṣaṇam
c yadi kuryāma yajñārthaṃ kiṃ tataḥ paramaṃ bhavet
a anārambhe tu niyato bhaved aguṇaniścayaḥ
c guṇān niḥsaṃśayād rājan nairguṇyaṃ manyase katham
a kāṣāyaṃ sulabhaṃ paścān munīnāṃ śamam icchatām
c sāmrājyaṃ tu tavecchanto vayaṃ yotsyāmahe paraiḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a jātasya bhārate vaṃśe tathā kuntyāḥ sutasya ca
c yā vai yuktā matiḥ seyam arjunena pradarśitā
a na mṛtyoḥ samayaṃ vidma rātrau vā yadi vā divā
c na cāpi kaṃ cid amaram ayuddhenāpi śuśrumaḥ
a etāvad eva puruṣaiḥ kāryaṃ hṛdayatoṣaṇam
c nayena vidhidṛṣṭena yad upakramate parān
a sunayasyānapāyasya saṃyuge paramaḥ kramaḥ
c saṃśayo jāyate sāmye sāmyaṃ ca na bhaved dvayoḥ
a te vayaṃ nayam āsthāya śatrudehasamīpagāḥ
c katham antaṃ na gacchema vṛkṣasyeva nadīrayāḥ
e pararandhre parākrāntāḥ svarandhrāvaraṇe sthitāḥ
a vyūḍhānīkair anubalair nopeyād balavattaram
c iti buddhimatāṃ nītis tan mamāpīha rocate
a anavadyā hy asaṃbuddhāḥ praviṣṭāḥ śatrusadma tat
c śatrudeham upākramya taṃ kāmaṃ prāpnuyāmahe
a eko hy eva śriyaṃ nityaṃ bibharti puruṣarṣabha
c antarātmeva bhūtānāṃ tatkṣaye vai balakṣayaḥ
d catuḥkikku sic
caturdaṃṣṭro dviśukto daśapadmavān
d ṣaḍ unnatair daśa bṛhat tribhir vyāptoti pārthivaḥ
a atha cet taṃ nihatyājau śeṣeṇābhisamāgatāḥ
c prāpnuyāma tataḥ svargaṃ jñātitrāṇaparāyaṇāḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kṛṣṇa ko 'yaṃ jarāsaṃdhaḥ kiṃvīryaḥ kiṃparākramaḥ
c yas tvāṃ spṛṣṭvāgnisadṛśaṃ na dagdhaḥ śalabho yathā
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a śṛṇu rājañ jarāsaṃdho yadvīryo yatparākramaḥ
c yathā copekṣito 'smābhir bahuśaḥ kṛtavipriyaḥ
a akṣauhiṇīnāṃ tisṛṇām āsīt samaradarpitaḥ
c rājā bṛhadratho nāma magadhādhipatiḥ patiḥ
a rūpavān vīryasaṃpannaḥ śrīmān atulavikramaḥ
b svarājyaṃ kārayām āsa magadheṣu girivraje
c nityaṃ dīkṣākṛśatanuḥ śatakratur ivāparaḥ
a tejasā sūryasadṛśaḥ kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥ
c yamāntakasamaḥ kope śriyā vaiśravaṇopamaḥ
a tasyābhijanasaṃyuktair guṇair bharatasattama
c vyāpteyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ
a sa kāśirājasya sute yamaje bharatarṣabha
c upayeme mahāvīryo rūpadraviṇasaṃmate
a tayoś cakāra samayaṃ mithaḥ sa puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c nātivartiṣya ity evaṃ patnībhyāṃ saṃnidhau tadā
a sa tābhyāṃ śuśubhe rājā patnībhyāṃ manujādhipa
c priyābhyām anurūpābhyāṃ kareṇubhyām iva dvipaḥ
a tayor madhyagataś cāpi rarāja vasudhādhipaḥ
c gaṅgāyamunayor madhye mūrtimān iva sāgaraḥ
a viṣayeṣu nimagnasya tasya yauvanam atyagāt
c na ca vaṃśakaraḥ putras tasyājāyata kaś cana
a maṅgalair bahubhir homaiḥ putrakāmābhir iṣṭibhiḥ
c nāsasāda nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ putraṃ kulavivardhanam
d sa bhāryābhyāṃ saha tadā nirvedam agamad bhṛśam
d rājyaṃ cāpi parityajya tapovanam athāśrayat
d vāryamāṇaḥ prakṛtibhir nṛpabhaktyā viśāṃ pate
a atha kākṣīvataḥ putraṃ gautamasya mahātmanaḥ
c śuśrāva tapasi śrāntam udāraṃ caṇḍakauśikam
a yadṛcchayāgataṃ taṃ tu vṛkṣamūlam upāśritam
c patnībhyāṃ sahito rājā sarvaratnair atoṣayat
d bṛhadrathaṃ ca sa ṛṣir yathāvat pratyanandata
d upaviṣṭaś ca tenātha anujñāto mahātmanā
d tam apṛcchat tadā vipraḥ kim āgamanam ity atha
d paurair anugatasyaiva patnībhyāṃ sahitasya ca
d sa uvāca muniṃ rājā bhagavan nāsti me sutaḥ
d aputrasya vṛthā janma ity āhur munisattamāḥ
d tādṛśasya hi rājyena vṛddhatve kiṃ prayojanam
d so 'haṃ tapaś cariṣyāmi patnībhyāṃ sahito vane
d nāprajasya mune kīrtiḥ svargaś caivākṣayo bhavet
d evam uktasya rājñā tu muneḥ kāruṇyam āgatam
a tam abravīt satyadhṛtiḥ satyavāg ṛṣisattamaḥ
c parituṣṭo 'smi te rājan varaṃ varaya suvrata
a tataḥ sabhāryaḥ praṇatas tam uvāca bṛhadrathaḥ
c putradarśananairāśyād bāṣpagadgadayā girā
 bṛhadratha uvāca
a bhagavan rājyam utsṛjya prasthitasya tapovanam
c kiṃ vareṇālpabhāgyasya kiṃ rājyenāprajasya me
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a etac chrutvā munir dhyānam agamat kṣubhitendriyaḥ
c tasyaiva cāmravṛkṣasya chāyāyāṃ samupāviśat
a tasyopaviṣṭasya muner utsaṅge nipapāta ha
c avātam aśukādaṣṭam ekam āmraphalaṃ kila
a tat pragṛhya muniśreṣṭho hṛdayenābhimantrya ca
c rājñe dadāv apratimaṃ putrasaṃprāptikārakam
a uvāca ca mahāprājñas taṃ rājānaṃ mahāmuniḥ
c gaccha rājan kṛtārtho 'si nivarta manujādhipa
d eṣa te tanayo rājan mā tapsīs tvaṃ tapo vane
d prajāḥ pālaya dharmeṇa eṣa dharmo mahīkṣitām
d yajasva vividhair yajñair indraṃ tarpaya cendunā
d putraṃ rājye pratiṣṭhāpya tata āśramam āvraja
d aṣṭau varān prayacchāmi tava putrasya pārthiva
d brahmaṇyatām ajeyatvaṃ yuddheṣu ca tathā ratim
d priyātitheyatāṃ caiva dīnānām anvavekṣaṇam
d tathā balaṃ ca sumahal loke kīrtiṃ ca śāśvatīm
d anurāgaṃ prajānāṃ ca dadau tasmai sa kauśikaḥ
d gaccha rājan kṛtārtho 'si nivartasva janādhipa
d anujñātaḥ sa ṛṣiṇā patnībhyāṃ sahito nṛpaḥ
d paurair anugataś cāpi viveśa svapuraṃ punaḥ
d etac chrutvā muner vākyaṃ śirasā praṇipatya ca
d muneḥ pādau mahāprājñaḥ sa nṛpaḥ svagṛhaṃ gataḥ
a yathāsamayam ājñāya tadā sa nṛpasattamaḥ
c dvābhyām ekaṃ phalaṃ prādāt patnībhyāṃ bharatarṣabha
d muneś ca bahumānena kālasya ca viparyayāt
a te tad āmraṃ dvidhā kṛtvā bhakṣayām āsatuḥ śubhe
c bhāvitvād api cārthasya satyavākyāt tathā muneḥ
a tayoḥ samabhavad garbhaḥ phalaprāśanasaṃbhavaḥ
c te ca dṛṣṭvā narapatiḥ parāṃ mudam avāpa ha
a atha kāle mahāprājña yathāsamayam āgate
c prajāyetām ubhe rājañ śarīraśakale tadā
a ekākṣibāhucaraṇe ardhodaramukhasphije
c dṛṣṭvā śarīraśakale pravepāte ubhe bhṛśam
a udvigne saha saṃmantrya te bhaginyau tadābale
c sajīve prāṇiśakale tatyajāte suduḥkhite
a tayor dhātryau susaṃvīte kṛtvā te garbhasaṃplave
c nirgamyāntaḥpuradvārāt samutsṛjyāśu jagmatuḥ
d dukūlābhyāṃ susaṃchanne pāṇḍarābhyām ubhe tadā
d ajñāte kasya cit te tu jahatus te catuṣpathe
d tato viviśatur dhātryau punar antaḥpuraṃ tadā
d kathayām āsatur ubhe devībhyāṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak
a te catuṣpathanikṣipte jarā nāmātha rākṣasī
c jagrāha manujavyāghra māṃsaśoṇitabhojanā
a kartukāmā sukhavahe śakale sā tu rākṣasī
c saṃghaṭṭayām āsa tadā vidhānabalacoditā
a te samānītamātre tu śakale puruṣarṣabha
c ekamūrtikṛte vīraḥ kumāraḥ samapadyata
a tataḥ sā rākṣasī rājan vismayotphullalocanā
c na śaśāka samudvoḍhuṃ vajrasāramayaṃ śiśum
a bālas tāmratalaṃ muṣṭiṃ kṛtvā cāsye nidhāya saḥ
c prākrośad atisaṃrambhāt satoya iva toyadaḥ
a tena śabdena saṃbhrāntaḥ sahasāntaḥpure janaḥ
c nirjagāma naravyāghra rājñā saha paraṃtapa
a te cābale pariglāne payaḥpūrṇapayodhare
c nirāśe putralābhāya sahasaivābhyagacchatām
a atha dṛṣṭvā tathābhūte rājānaṃ ceṣṭasaṃtatim
c taṃ ca bālaṃ subalinaṃ cintayām āsa rākṣasī
a nārhāmi viṣaye rājño vasantī putragṛddhinaḥ
b bālaṃ putram imaṃ hantuṃ dhārmikasya mahātmanaḥ
c bālaṃ putram upādātuṃ meghalekheva bhāskaram
a sā kṛtvā mānuṣaṃ rūpam uvāca manujādhipam
c bṛhadratha sutas te 'yaṃ maddattaḥ pratigṛhyatām
a tava patnīdvaye jāto dvijātivaraśāsanāt
c dhātrījanaparityakto mayāyaṃ parirakṣitaḥ
a tatas te bharataśreṣṭha kāśirājasute śubhe
c taṃ bālam abhipatyāśu prasnavair abhiṣiñcatām
a tataḥ sa rājā saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sarvaṃ tad upalabhya ca
c apṛcchan navahemābhāṃ rākṣasīṃ tām arākṣasīm
a kā tvaṃ kamalagarbhābhe mama putrapradāyinī
c kāmayā brūhi kalyāṇi devatā pratibhāsi me
 rākṣasy uvāca
a jarā nāmāsmi bhadraṃ te rākṣasī kāmarūpiṇī
c tava veśmani rājendra pūjitā nyavasaṃ sukham
d gṛhe gṛhe manuṣyāṇāṃ nityaṃ tiṣṭhati rākṣasī
d gṛhadevīti nāmnā vai purā sṛṣṭā svayaṃbhuvā
d dānavānāṃ vināśāya sthāpitā divyarūpiṇī
d yo māṃ bhaktyā likhet kuḍye saputrāṃ yauvanānvitām
d gṛhe tasya bhaved vṛddhir anyathā kṣayam āpnuyāt
d tvadgṛhe tiṣṭhamānā tu pūjitāhaṃ sadā vibho
d likhitā caiva kuḍyeṣu putrair bahubhir āvṛtā
d gandhapuṣpais tathā dhūpair bhakṣyair bhojyaiḥ supūjitā
a sāhaṃ pratyupakārārthaṃ cintayanty aniśaṃ nṛpa
c taveme putraśakale dṛṣṭavaty asmi dhārmika
a saṃśleṣite mayā daivāt kumāraḥ samapadyata
c tava bhāgyair mahārāja hetumātram ahaṃ tv iha
d meruṃ vā khādituṃ śaktā kiṃ punas tava bālakam
d gṛhasaṃpūjanāt tuṣṭyā mayā pratyarpitas tava
d tasya bālasya yat kṛtyaṃ tat kuruṣva narādhipa
d mama nāmnā ca loke 'smin khyāta eva bhaviṣyati
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a evam uktvā tu sā rājaṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata
c sa gṛhya ca kumāraṃ taṃ prāviśat svagṛhaṃ nṛpaḥ
a tasya bālasya yat kṛtyaṃ tac cakāra nṛpas tadā
c ājñāpayac ca rākṣasyā māgadheṣu mahotsavam
a tasya nāmākarot tatra prajāpatisamaḥ pitā
c jarayā saṃdhito yasmāj jarāsaṃdhas tato 'bhavat
a so 'vardhata mahātejā magadhādhipateḥ sutaḥ
c pramāṇabalasaṃpanno hutāhutir ivānalaḥ
d māgadho balasaṃpanno   hutīr ivānalaḥ
d mātāpitror nandikaraḥ śuklapakṣe yathā śaśī
d evaṃ sa vavṛdhe rājan kumāraḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
d kālena mahatā cāpi yauvanastho babhūva ha
a kasya cit tv atha kālasya punar eva mahātapāḥ
c magadhān upacakrāma bhagavāṃś caṇḍakauśikaḥ
a tasyāgamanasaṃhṛṣṭaḥ sāmātyaḥ sapuraḥsaraḥ
c sabhāryaḥ saha putreṇa nirjagāma bṛhadrathaḥ
a pādyārghyācamanīyais tam arcayām āsa bhārata
c sa nṛpo rājyasahitaṃ putraṃ cāsmai nyavedayat
a pratigṛhya tu tāṃ pūjāṃ pārthivād bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c uvāca māgadhaṃ rājan prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
a sarvam etan mayā rājan vijñātaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā
c putras tu śṛṇu rājendra yādṛśo 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati
d asya rūpaṃ ca sattvaṃ ca balam ūrjitam eva ca
d eṣa śriyā samuditaḥ putras tava na saṃśayaḥ
d prāpayiṣyati tat sarvaṃ vikrameṇa samanvitaḥ
a asya vīryavato vīryaṃ nānuyāsyanti pārthivāḥ
b patato vainateyasya gatim anye yathā khagāḥ
b vināśam upayāsyanti ye cāsya paripanthinaḥ
c devair api visṛṣṭāni śastrāṇy asya mahīpate
e na rujaṃ janayiṣyanti girer iva nadīrayāḥ
a sarvamūrdhābhiṣiktānām eṣa mūrdhni jvaliṣyati
c sarveṣāṃ niṣprabhakaro jyotiṣām iva bhāskaraḥ
a enam āsādya rājānaḥ samṛddhabalavāhanāḥ
c vināśam upayāsyanti śalabhā iva pāvakam
a eṣa śriyaṃ samuditāṃ sarvarājñāṃ grahīṣyati
c varṣāsv ivoddhatajalā nadīr nadanadīpatiḥ
a eṣa dhārayitā samyak cāturvarṇyaṃ mahābalaḥ
c śubhāśubham iva sphītā sarvasasyadharā dharā
d śriyaṃ samuditāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ
a asyājñāvaśagāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ
c sarvabhūtātmabhūtasya vāyor iva śarīriṇaḥ
a eṣa rudraṃ mahādevaṃ tripurāntakaraṃ haram
c sarvalokeṣv atibalaḥ svayaṃ drakṣyati māgadhaḥ
a evaṃ bruvann eva muniḥ svakāryārthaṃ vicintayan
c visarjayām āsa nṛpaṃ bṛhadratham athārihan
a praviśya nagaraṃ caiva jñātisaṃbandhibhir vṛtaḥ
c abhiṣicya jarāsaṃdhaṃ magadhādhipatis tadā
e bṛhadratho narapatiḥ parāṃ nirvṛtim āyayau
a abhiṣikte jarāsaṃdhe tadā rājā bṛhadrathaḥ
c patnīdvayenānugatas tapovanarato 'bhavat
a tapovanasthe pitari mātṛbhyāṃ saha bhārata
c jarāsaṃdhaḥ svavīryeṇa pārthivān akarod vaśe
a atha dīrghasya kālasya tapovanagato nṛpaḥ
c sabhāryaḥ svargam agamat tapas taptvā bṛhadrathaḥ
d jarāsaṃdho 'pi nṛpatir yathoktaṃ kauśikena tat
d varapradānam akhilaṃ prāpya rājyam apālayat
d nihate vāsudevena tadā kaṃse mahīpatau
d jāto vai vairanirbandhaḥ kṛṣṇena saha tasya vai
d bhrāmayitvā śataguṇam ekonaṃ yena bhārata
d gadā kṣiptā balavatā māgadhena girivrajāt
d tiṣṭhato mathurāyāṃ vai kṛṣṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ
d ekonayojanaśate sā papāta gadā śubhā
d dṛṣṭvā paurais tadā samyag gadā caiva niveditā
d gadāvasānaṃ tat khyātaṃ mathurāyāṃ samīpataḥ
a tasyāstāṃ haṃsaḍibhakāv aśastranidhanāv ubhau
c mantre matimatāṃ śreṣṭhau yuddhaśāstraviśāradau
d hate caiva mayā kaṃse sahaṃsaḍibhake tadā
d jarāsaṃdhasya duhitā rodate pārśvataḥ pituḥ
d tato vairaṃ vinirbaddhaṃ mayā tasya ca bhārata
a yau tau mayā te kathitau pūrvam eva mahābalau
c trayas trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ paryāptā iti me matiḥ
a evam eṣa tadā vīra balibhiḥ kukurāndhakaiḥ
c vṛṣṇibhiś ca mahārāja nītihetor upekṣitaḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a patitau haṃsaḍibhakau kaṃsāmātyau nipātitau
c jarāsaṃdhasya nidhane kālo 'yaṃ samupāgataḥ
a na sa śakyo raṇe jetuṃ sarvair api surāsuraiḥ
c prāṇayuddhena jetavyaḥ sa ity upalabhāmahe
a mayi nītir balaṃ bhīme rakṣitā cāvayorjunaḥ
c sādhayiṣyāma taṃ rājan vayaṃ traya ivāgnayaḥ
a tribhir āsādito 'smābhir vijane sa narādhipaḥ
c na saṃdeho yathā yuddham ekenābhyupayāsyati
a avamānāc ca lokasya vyāyatatvāc ca dharṣitaḥ
c bhīmasenena yuddhāya dhruvam abhyupayāsyati
a alaṃ tasya mahābāhur bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c lokasya samudīrṇasya nidhanāyāntako yathā
a yadi te hṛdayaṃ vetti yadi te pratyayo mayi
c bhīmasenārjunau śīghraṃ nyāsabhūtau prayaccha me
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam ukto bhagavatā pratyuvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmapārthau samālokya saṃprahṛṣṭamukhau sthitau
a acyutācyuta mā maivaṃ vyāharāmitrakarṣaṇa
c pāṇḍavānāṃ bhavān nātho bhavantaṃ cāśritā vayam
a yathā vadasi govinda sarvaṃ tad upapadyate
c na hi tvam agratas teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ lakṣmīḥ parāṅmukhī
d yeṣām abhimukhī lakṣmīs teṣāṃ kṛṣṇa tvam agrataḥ
a nihataś ca jarāsaṃdho mokṣitāś ca mahīkṣitaḥ
c rājasūyaś ca me labdho nideśe tava tiṣṭhataḥ
a kṣiprakārin yathā tv etat kāryaṃ samupapadyate
c mama kāryaṃ jagatkāryaṃ tathā kuru narottama
a tribhir bhavadbhir hi vinā nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe
c dharmakāmārtharahito rogārta iva durgataḥ
a na śauriṇā vinā pārtho na śauriḥ pāṇḍavaṃ vinā
c nājeyo 'sty anayor loke kṛṣṇayor iti me matiḥ
a ayaṃ ca balināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śrīmān api vṛkodaraḥ
c yuvābhyāṃ sahito vīraḥ kiṃ na kuryān mahāyaśāḥ
a supraṇīto balaugho hi kurute kāryam uttamam
c andhaṃ jaḍaṃ balaṃ prāhuḥ praṇetavyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ
a yato hi nimnaṃ bhavati nayantīha tato jalam
c yataś chidraṃ tataś cāpi nayante dhīdhanā balam
a tasmān nayavidhānajñaṃ puruṣaṃ lokaviśrutam
c vayam āśritya govindaṃ yatāmaḥ kāryasiddhaye
a evaṃ prajñānayabalaṃ kriyopāyasamanvitam
c puraskurvīta kāryeṣu kṛṣṇa kāryārthasiddhaye
a evam eva yaduśreṣṭhaṃ pārthaḥ kāryārthasiddhaye
c arjunaḥ kṛṣṇam anvetu bhīmo 'nvetu dhanaṃjayam
e nayo jayo balaṃ caiva vikrame siddhim eṣyati
a evam uktās tataḥ sarve bhrātaro vipulaujasaḥ
c vārṣṇeyaḥ pāṇḍaveyau ca pratasthur māgadhaṃ prati
a varcasvināṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ snātakānāṃ paricchadān
c ācchādya suhṛdāṃ vākyair manojñair abhinanditāḥ
d mādhavaḥ pāṇḍaveyau ca pratasthur vratadhāriṇaḥ
a amarṣād abhitaptānāṃ jñātyarthaṃ mukhyavāsasām
c ravisomāgnivapuṣāṃ bhīmam āsīt tadā vapuḥ
a hataṃ mene jarāsaṃdhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmapurogamau
c ekakāryasamudyuktau kṛṣṇau yuddhe 'parājitau
a īśau hi tau mahātmānau sarvakāryapravartane
c dharmārthakāmakāryāṇāṃ kāryāṇām iva nigrahe
a kurubhyaḥ prasthitās te tu madhyena kurujāṅgalam
c ramyaṃ padmasaro gatvā kālakūṭam atītya ca
a gaṇḍakīyāṃ tathā śoṇaṃ sadānīrāṃ tathaiva ca
c ekaparvatake nadyaḥ krameṇaitya vrajanti te
a saṃtīrya sarayūṃ ramyāṃ dṛṣṭvā pūrvāṃś ca kosalān
c atītya jagmur mithilāṃ mālāṃ carmaṇvatīṃ nadīm
a uttīrya gaṅgāṃ śoṇaṃ ca sarve te prāṅmukhās trayaḥ
c kuravoraśchadaṃ jagmur māgadhaṃ kṣetram acyutāḥ
a te śaśvad godhanākīrṇam ambumantaṃ śubhadrumam
c gorathaṃ girim āsādya dadṛśur māgadhaṃ puram
 vāsudeva uvāca
a eṣa pārtha mahān svāduḥ paśumān nityam ambumān
c nirāmayaḥ suveśmāḍhyo niveśo māgadhaḥ śubhaḥ
d puṣpauṣadhiphalopeto dhanadhānyasamṛddhimān
a vaihāro vipulaḥ śailo varāho vṛṣabhas tathā
c tathaivarṣigiris tāta śubhāś caityakapañcamāḥ
a ete pañca mahāśṛṅgāḥ parvatāḥ śītaladrumāḥ
c rakṣantīvābhisaṃhatya saṃhatāṅgā girivrajam
a puṣpaveṣṭitaśākhāgrair gandhavadbhir manoramaiḥ
c nigūḍhā iva lodhrāṇāṃ vanaiḥ kāmijanapriyaiḥ
d yatra dīrghatamā nāma ṛṣiḥ paramayantritaḥ
a śūdrāyāṃ gautamo yatra mahātmā saṃśitavrataḥ
c auśīnaryām ajanayat kākṣīvādīn sutān ṛṣiḥ
a gautamaḥ kṣayaṇād asmād athāsau tatra veśmani
c bhajate māgadhaṃ vaṃśaṃ sa nṛpāṇām anugrahāt
a aṅgavaṅgādayaś caiva rājānaḥ sumahābalāḥ
c gautamakṣayam abhyetya ramante sma purārjuna
a vanarājīs tu paśyemāḥ priyālānāṃ manoramāḥ
c lodhrāṇāṃ ca śubhāḥ pārtha gautamaukaḥsamīpajāḥ
c   rājan rājīvalocana
c puṃnāgānāṃ nagānāṃ ca
a arbudaḥ śakravāpī ca pannagau śatrutāpanau
c svastikasyālayaś cātra maṇināgasya cottamaḥ
a aparihāryā meghānāṃ māgadheyaṃ maṇeḥ kṛte
c kauśiko maṇimāṃś caiva vavṛdhāte hy anugraham
d evaṃ prāpya puraṃ ramyaṃ durādharṣaṃ samantataḥ
d pāṇḍare vipule caiva tathā vārāhake 'pi ca
d caityake ca giriśreṣṭhe mātaṅge ca śiloccaye
d eteṣu parvatendreṣu sarvasiddhisamālayāḥ
d yatīnām āśramāś caiva munīnāṃ ca mahātmanām
d vṛṣabhasya tamālasya mahāvīryasya vai tathā
d gandharvarakṣasāṃ caiva nāgānāṃ ca tathālayāḥ
d kakṣīvatas tapovīryāt tapodā iti viśrutāḥ
d puṇyatīrthāś ca te sarve siddhānāṃ caiva kīrtitāḥ
d maṇeś ca darśanād eva bhadraṃ hi śivam āpnuyāt
a arthasiddhiṃ tv anapagāṃ jarāsaṃdho 'bhimanyate
c vayam āsādane tasya darpam adya nihanma hi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā tataḥ sarve bhrātaro vipulaujasaḥ
c vārṣṇeyaḥ pāṇḍaveyau ca pratasthur māgadhaṃ puram
a tuṣṭapuṣṭajanopetaṃ cāturvarṇyajanākulam
c sphītotsavam anādhṛṣyam āseduś ca girivrajam
d puradvāram apāsya tvam advāreṇa praviśya te
a te 'tha dvāram anāsādya purasya girim ucchritam
c bārhadrathaiḥ pūjyamānaṃ tathā nagaravāsibhiḥ
a yatra māṣādam ṛṣabham āsasāda bṛhadrathaḥ
c taṃ hatvā māṣanālāś ca tisro bherīr akārayat
a ānahya carmaṇā tena sthāpayām āsa sve pure
c yatra tāḥ prāṇadan bheryo divyapuṣpāvacūrṇitāḥ
d bhaṅktvā bherītrayaṃ te 'pi caityaprākāram ādravan

a sthiraṃ suvipulaṃ śṛṅgaṃ sumahāntaṃ purātanam

c tatas te māgadhaṃ dṛṣṭvā puraṃ praviviśus tadā
d dṛṣṭvā tu durnimittaṃ tad brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
d śāntidānajapair homair devān aprīṇayaṃs tadā
a etasminn eva kāle tu jarāsaṃdhaṃ samarcayan
c paryagni kurvaṃś ca nṛpaṃ dviradasthaṃ purohitāḥ
d tatas tacchāntaye rājā jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān
d dīkṣito niyamastho 'sāv upavāsaparo 'bhavat
d nīrājayanti dīpais taṃ kālamṛtyuharair japaiḥ
d etasminn eva kāle tu kṛṣṇabhīmadhanaṃjayāḥ
a snātakavratinas te tu bāhuśastrā nirāyudhāḥ
b paśyantaḥ purasaubhāgyam ūrjitāṃ ca puraśriyam
c yuyutsavaḥ praviviśur jarāsaṃdhena bhārata
a bhakṣyamālyāpaṇānāṃ ca dadṛśuḥ śriyam uttamām
a   vipaṇiṃ ratnavāsasām
a divyanānāpaṇānāṃ ca
c sphītāṃ sarvaguṇopetāṃ sarvakāmasamṛddhinīm
a tāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā samṛddhiṃ te vīthyāṃ tasyāṃ narottamāḥ
c rājamārgeṇa gacchantaḥ kṛṣṇabhīmadhanaṃjayāḥ
a balād gṛhītvā mālyāni mālākārān mahābalāḥ
b karpūraśṛṅgaṃ koṣṭaṃ ca saphalaṃ cāntarāpaṇe
b vaiśyād balād gṛhītvā te vihṛtya ca mahārathāḥ
c virāgavasanāḥ sarve sragviṇo mṛṣṭakuṇḍalāḥ
a niveśanam athājagmur jarāsaṃdhasya dhīmataḥ
c govāsam iva vīkṣantaḥ siṃhā haimavatā yathā
a śailastambhanibhās teṣāṃ candanāgurubhūṣitāḥ
c aśobhanta mahārāja bāhavo bāhuśālinām
