c vyūḍhoraskān māgadhānāṃ vismayaḥ samajāyata
d advāreṇābhyavaskandya viviśur māgadhālayam
a te tv atītya janākīrṇās tisraḥ kakṣyā nararṣabhāḥ
c ahaṃkāreṇa rājānam upatasthur mahābalāḥ
d bhośabdenaiva rājānam ūcus te tu mahārathāḥ
d āyuṣmān bhava saumyeti vaded viprābhivādane
d vijayaṃ bāhujaṃ brūyād vaiśye naṣṭa itīrayet
d ārogyaṃ pādaje brūyāc chatrau nośabdam īrayet
d rājadatteṣv anarghyeṣu na niṣedus tadāsane
d pādenāsanam ākṛṣya tasminn upaviśed ripuḥ
d bhūtale vāpy anāstīrṇe śatruveśmany ayaṃ kramaḥ
a tān pādyamadhuparkārhān mānārhān satkṛtiṃ gatān
c pratyutthāya jarāsaṃdha upatasthe yathāvidhi
a uvāca caitān rājāsau svāgataṃ vo 'stv iti prabhuḥ
b maunam āsīt tadā pārthabhīmayor janamejaya
b teṣāṃ madhye mahābuddhiḥ kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīt
b vaktuṃ nāyāti rājendra etayor niyamasthayoḥ
b arvāṅ niśīthāt paratas tvayā sārdhaṃ vadiṣyataḥ
b yajñāgāre sthāpayitvā rājā rājagṛhaṃ gataḥ
b tato 'rdharātre saṃprāpte yāto yatra sthitā dvijāḥ
c tasya hy etad vrataṃ rājan babhūva bhuvi viśrutam
d bārhadratho vai rājendro mahābalaparākramaḥ
a snātakān brāhmaṇān prāptāñ śrutvā sa samitiṃjayaḥ
c apy ardharātre nṛpatiḥ pratyudgacchati bhārata
c   yoṣitsaṃghagato 'pi vā
c śrutvā samāgatān viprān
a tāṃs tv apūrveṇa veṣeṇa dṛṣṭvā nṛpatisattamaḥ
c upatasthe jarāsaṃdho vismitaś cābhavat tadā
a te tu dṛṣṭvaiva rājānaṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ nararṣabhāḥ
b satvaṃ tejo balaṃ dhairyaṃ gāmbhīryam iva mūrtimān
c idam ūcur amitraghnāḥ sarve bharatasattama
d rājan viddhy atithīn asmān arthino dūram āgatān
d tan naḥ prayaccha bhadraṃ te yad vayaṃ kāmayāmahe
d kiṃ durmarṣaṃ titikṣūṇāṃ kim akāryam asādhubhiḥ
d kim adeyaṃ vadānyānāṃ kaḥ paraḥ samadarśinām
d yo 'nityena śarīreṇa satāṃ geyaṃ yaśo dhruvam
d nācinoti svayaṃ kalpaḥ sa vācyaḥ śocya eva saḥ
d hariścandro rantideva uñchavṛttiḥ śibir baliḥ
d vyādhaḥ kapoto bahavo hy adhruveṇa dhruvaṃ gatāḥ
a svasty astu kuśalaṃ rājann iti sarve vyavasthitāḥ
c taṃ nṛpaṃ nṛpaśārdūla vipraikṣanta parasparam
a tān abravīj jarāsaṃdhas tadā yādavapāṇḍavān
c āsyatām iti rājendra brāhmaṇacchadmasaṃvṛtān
a athopaviviśuḥ sarve trayas te puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c saṃpradīptās trayo lakṣmyā mahādhvara ivāgnayaḥ
d svarair ākṛtibhis tāṃs tu prakoṣṭhair jyāhatair api
d rājanyabandhūn vijñāya dṛṣṭapūrvān acintayat
d rājanyabandhavo hy ete brahmaliṅgāni bibhrati
d dadāmi bhikṣitaṃ tebhya ātmānam api dustyajam
d baler na śrūyate kīrtir vitatā dikṣu sarvataḥ
d aiśvaryād bhraṃśitaś cāpi vipravyājena viṣṇunā
d śriyaṃ jihīrṣatendrasya viṣṇave dvijarūpiṇe
d jānann api mahīṃ prādād vāryamāṇo 'pi daityarāṭ
d vijitā brāhmaṇārthāya ko nv arthaḥ kṣatrabandhunā
d dehena tapamānena neheta vipulaṃ yaśaḥ
d ity udāramatiḥ prāha kṛṣṇārjunavṛkodarān
d he viprā vrīyatāṃ kāmo dadāmy ātmā śiro 'pi ca
a tān uvāca jarāsaṃdhaḥ satyasaṃdho narādhipaḥ
b harim indraṃ samīraṃ ca līlāmānuṣavigrahān
c vigarhamāṇaḥ kauravya veṣagrahaṇakāraṇāt
a na snātakavratā viprā bahirmālyānulepanāḥ
c bhavantīti nṛloke 'smin viditaṃ mama sarvaśaḥ
a te yūyaṃ puṣpavantaś ca bhujair jyāghātalakṣaṇaiḥ
b kṛtaśmaśrumukhā raktā raktatīkṣṇanakhāṅkurāḥ
b raktoṣṇīṣadharā raktadantapaṅktivirājitāḥ
c bibhrataḥ kṣātram ojaś ca brāhmaṇyaṃ pratijānatha
a evaṃ virāgavasanā bahirmālyānulepanāḥ
b kṣatriyā eva loke 'smin viditā mama sarvaśaḥ
c satyaṃ vadata ke yūyaṃ satyaṃ rājasu śobhate
d iyaṃ vasumatī satyaṃ satyarūpā mahīkṣitaḥ
d satye sthito vadet satyam anyathā vinaśiṣyati
a caityakaṃ ca gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ bhittvā kim iva sadma naḥ
c advāreṇa praviṣṭāḥ stha nirbhayā rājakilbiṣāt
c   praveṣṭavyaṃ ripor gṛham
c so 'haṃ na bhavatāṃ śatrur brāhmaṇā mama devatāḥ
c atāḍayata kiṃ bherīr yuddhasaṃnāhalakṣaṇāḥ
c yūyaṃ mayā na yoddhavyā
a karma caitad viliṅgasya kiṃ vādya prasamīkṣitam
c vadadhvaṃ vāci vīryaṃ ca brāhmaṇasya viśeṣataḥ
a evaṃ ca mām upasthāya kasmāc ca vidhinārhaṇām
c praṇītāṃ no na gṛhṇīta kāryaṃ kiṃ cāsmadāgame
a evam uktas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pratyuvāca mahāmanāḥ
c snigdhagambhīrayā vācā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
a snātakavratino rājan brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā viśaḥ
c viśeṣaniyamāś caiṣām aviśeṣāś ca santy uta
d snātakān brāhmaṇān rājan viddhy asmāṃs tvaṃ narādhipa
a viśeṣavāṃś ca satataṃ kṣatriyaḥ śriyam archati
c puṣpavatsu dhruvā śrīś ca puṣpavantas tato vayam
a kṣatriyo bāhuvīryas tu na tathā vākyavīryavān
c apragalbhaṃ vacas tasya tasmād bārhadrathe smṛtam
a svavīryaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca bāhvor dhātā nyaveśayat
c tad didṛkṣasi ced rājan draṣṭāsy adya na saṃśayaḥ
a advāreṇa ripor gehaṃ dvāreṇa suhṛdo gṛham
c praviśanti sadā santo dvāraṃ no varjitaṃ tataḥ
a kāryavanto gṛhān etya śatruto nārhaṇāṃ vayam
c pratigṛhṇīma tad viddhi etan naḥ śāśvataṃ vratam
 jarāsaṃdha uvāca
a na smareyaṃ kadā vairaṃ kṛtaṃ yuṣmābhir ity uta
c cintayaṃś ca na paśyāmi bhavatāṃ prati vaikṛtam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d evam ukto bhagavatā bṛhadrathasuto balī
d ātmany autsukam ālokya kṛṣṇam āha nṛpottamāḥ
a vaikṛte cāsati kathaṃ manyadhvaṃ mām anāgasam
c ariṃ vibrūta tad viprāḥ satāṃ samaya eṣa hi
a atha dharmopaghātād dhi manaḥ samupatapyate
c yo 'nāgasi prasṛjati kṣatriyo 'pi na saṃśayaḥ
d kṣatriyā eva loke 'smin viditaṃ mama sarvaśaḥ
a ato 'nyathācaraṃl loke dharmajñaḥ san mahāvrataḥ
c vṛjināṃ gatim āpnoti śreyaso 'py upahanti ca
a trailokye kṣatradharmād dhi śreyāṃsaṃ sādhucāriṇām
b nānyaṃ dharmaṃ praśaṃsanti ye ca dharmavido janāḥ
b tasya me 'dya sthitasyeha svadharme niyatātmanaḥ
c anāgasaṃ prajānānāḥ pramādād iva jalpatha
 vāsudeva uvāca
a kulakāryaṃ mahārāja kaś cid ekaḥ kulodvahaḥ
c vahate tanniyogād vai vayam abhyutthitās trayaḥ
a tvayā copahṛtā rājan kṣatriyā lokavāsinaḥ
c tad āgaḥ krūram utpādya manyase kiṃ tv anāgasam
a rājā rājñaḥ kathaṃ sādhūn hiṃsyān nṛpatisattama
c tad rājñaḥ saṃnigṛhya tvaṃ rudrāyopajihīrṣasi
a asmāṃs tad eno gaccheta tvayā bārhadrathe kṛtam
c vayaṃ hi śaktā dharmasya rakṣaṇe dharmacāriṇaḥ
d tasmād adyopagacchāmas tava bārhadrathe 'ntikam
a manuṣyāṇāṃ samālambho na ca dṛṣṭaḥ kadā cana
c sa kathaṃ mānuṣair devaṃ yaṣṭum icchasi śaṃkaram
a savarṇo hi savarṇānāṃ paśusaṃjñāṃ kariṣyati
c ko 'nya evaṃ yathā hi tvaṃ jarāsaṃdha vṛthāmatiḥ
d yasyāṃ yasyām avasthāyāṃ yad yat karma karoti yaḥ
d tasyāṃ tasyām avasthāyāṃ tat phalaṃ samavāpnuyāt
a te tvāṃ jñātikṣayakaraṃ vayam ārtānusāriṇaḥ
c jñātivṛddhinimittārthaṃ viniyantum ihāgatāḥ
a nāsti loke pumān anyaḥ kṣatriyeṣv iti caiva yat
c manyase sa ca te rājan sumahān buddhiviplavaḥ
a ko hi jānann abhijanam ātmanaḥ kṣatriyo nṛpa
c nāviśet svargam atulaṃ raṇānantaram avyayam
a svargaṃ hy eva samāsthāya raṇayajñeṣu dīkṣitāḥ
c yajante kṣatriyā lokāṃs tad viddhi magadhādhipa
a svargayonir jayo rājan svargayonir mahad yaśaḥ
c svargayonis tapo yuddhe mārgaḥ so 'vyabhicāravān
a eṣa hy aindro vaijayanto guṇo nityaṃ samāhitaḥ
c yenāsurān parājitya jagat pāti śatakratuḥ
d yena sarvān parājitya vijayas tv abhipāditaḥ
a svargam āsthāya kasya syād vigrahitvaṃ yathā tava
c māgadhair vipulaiḥ sainyair bāhulyabaladarpitaiḥ
a māvamaṃsthāḥ parān rājan nāsti vīryaṃ nare nare
c samaṃ tejas tvayā caiva kevalaṃ manujeśvara
a yāvad eva na saṃbuddhaṃ tāvad eva bhavet tava
c viṣahyam etad asmākam ato rājan bravīmi te
a jahi tvaṃ sadṛśeṣv eva mānaṃ darpaṃ ca māgadha
c mā gamaḥ sasutāmātyaḥ sabalaś ca yamakṣayam
a dambhodbhavaḥ kārtavīrya uttaraś ca bṛhadrathaḥ
c śreyaso hy avamanyeha vineśuḥ sabalā nṛpāḥ
a mumukṣamāṇās tvattaś ca na vayaṃ brāhmaṇabruvāḥ
c śaurir asmi hṛṣīkeśo nṛvīrau pāṇḍavāv imau
d anayor mātuleyaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ māṃ viddhi te ripum
a tvām āhvayāmahe rājan sthiro yudhyasva māgadha
c muñca vā nṛpatīn sarvān mā gamas tvaṃ yamakṣayam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d jarāsaṃdhaḥ
d etac chrutvā jarāsaṃdhaḥ kruddho vacanam abravīt
d nāhaṃ kaṃsaḥ pralambo vā na bāṇo na ca muṣṭikaḥ
d narako nendratapano na keśī na ca pūtanā
d na kālayavano vāpi ye tvayā nihatā yudhi
d tvaṃ tu gopakulotpanno jātiṃ vai pūrvikāṃ smara
d yo 'smadbhayād apakramya sāgarānūpam āśritaḥ
d janmabhūmiṃ parityajya madhurāṃ prākṛto yathā
d so 'dhunā katthase śaure śaradīva yathā ghanaḥ
d adyānṛṇyaṃ kariṣyāmi bhojarājasya dhīmataḥ
d jāmātur augrasenasya tvāṃ nihatyādya mādhava
d cirakāṅkṣito me saṃgrāmas tvāṃ hantuṃ sasuhṛdgaṇam
d diṣṭyā me saphalo yatnaḥ kṛto devaiḥ savāsavaiḥ
d klībāv imau ca govinda bhīmasenārjunāv ubhau
d hiṃsyāmi yudhi vikramya siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgān iva
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tasya roṣābhibhūtasya jarāsaṃdhasya garjataḥ
d śrībhagavān
d sarvabhūtāni vitresur ye tatrāsan samāgatāḥ
d kiṃ garjasi jarāsaṃdha karmaṇā tān samācara
d mama nirdeśakartṛbhyāṃ pāṇḍavābhyāṃ nṛpādhama
d sāmātyaṃ sasutaṃ cādya ghātayiṣyāmy ahaṃ raṇe
d na kathaṃ cana jīvan vai pravekṣyasi purottamam
 jarāsaṃdha uvāca
a nājitān vai narapatīn aham ādadmi kāṃś cana
c jitaḥ kaḥ paryavasthātā ko 'tra yo na mayā jitaḥ
a kṣatriyasyaitad evāhur dharmyaṃ kṛṣṇopajīvanam
c vikramya vaśam ānīya kāmato yat samācaret
a devatārtham upākṛtya rājñaḥ kṛṣṇa kathaṃ bhayāt
c aham adya vimuñceyaṃ kṣātraṃ vratam anusmaran
a sainyaṃ sainyena vyūḍhena eka ekena vā punaḥ
c dvābhyāṃ tribhir vā yotsye 'haṃ yugapat pṛthag eva vā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā jarāsaṃdhaḥ sahadevābhiṣecanam
c ājñāpayat tadā rājā yuyutsur bhīmakarmabhiḥ
a sa tu senāpatī rājā sasmāra bharatarṣabha
c kauśikaṃ citrasenaṃ ca tasmin yuddha upasthite
a yayos te nāmanī loke haṃseti ḍibhaketi ca
c pūrvaṃ saṃkathite pumbhir nṛloke lokasatkṛte
d niśaśvāsa jarāsaṃdho diṣṭaṃ saṃcintayaṃs tadā
a taṃ tu rājan vibhuḥ śaurī rājānaṃ balināṃ varam
c smṛtvā puruṣaśārdūla śārdūlasamavikramam
a satyasaṃdho jarāsaṃdhaṃ bhuvi bhīmaparākramam
c bhāgam anyasya nirdiṣṭaṃ vadhyaṃ bhūmibhṛd acyutaḥ
a nātmanātmavatāṃ mukhya iyeṣa madhusūdanaḥ
c brahmaṇo ''jñāṃ puraskṛtya hantuṃ haladharānujaḥ
d janamejayaḥ
d kimarthaṃ vairiṇāv āstām ubhau tau kṛṣṇamāgadhau
d kathaṃ ca nirjitaḥ saṃkhye jarāsaṃdhena mādhavaḥ
d kaś ca kaṃso māgadhasya yasya hetoḥ sa vairavān
d etad ācakṣva me sarvaṃ vaiśaṃpāyana tattvataḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d yādavānām anvavāye vasudevo mahāmatiḥ
d udapadyata vārṣṇeyo hy ugrasenasya mantrabhṛt
d ugrasenasya kaṃsas tu babhūva balavān sutaḥ
d jyeṣṭho bahūnāṃ kauravya sarvaśastraviśāradaḥ
d jarāsaṃdhasya duhitā tasya bhāryātiviśrutā
d rājyaśulkena dattā sā jarāsaṃdhena dhīmatā
d tadartham ugrasenasya madhurāyāṃ sutas tadā
d abhiṣiktas tadāmātyaiḥ sa vai tīvraparākramaḥ
d aiśvaryabalamattas tu sa tadā balamohitaḥ
d nigṛhya pitaraṃ bhuṅkte tad rājyaṃ mantribhiḥ saha
d vasudevasya tat kṛtyaṃ na śṛṇoti sa mandadhīḥ
d sa tena saha tad rājyaṃ dharmataḥ paryapālayat
d prītimān sa tu daityendro vasudevasya devakīm
d uvāha bhāryāṃ sa tadā duhitā devakasya yā
d tasyām udvāhyamānāyāṃ rathena janamejaya
d upāruroha vārṣṇeyaṃ kaṃso bhūmipatis tadā
d tato 'ntarikṣe vāg āsīd devadūtasya kasya cit
d vasudevaś ca śuśrāva tāṃ vācaṃ pārthivaś ca saḥ
d yām etāṃ vahamāno 'dya kaṃsodvahasi devakīm
d asyā yaś cāṣṭamo garbhaḥ sa te mṛtyur bhaviṣyati
d so 'vatīrya tato rājā khaḍgam uddhṛtya nirmalam
d iyeṣa tasyā mūrdhānaṃ chettuṃ paramadurmatiḥ
d sa sāntvayaṃs tadā kaṃsaṃ hasan krodhavaśānugam
d rājann anunayām āsa vasudevo mahāmatiḥ
d ahiṃsyāṃ pramadām āhuḥ sarvadharmeṣu pārthiva
d akasmād abalāṃ nārīṃ hantāsīmām anāgasīm
d yac ca te 'tra bhayaṃ rājañ śakyate bādhituṃ tvayā
d iyaṃ ca śakyā pālayituṃ samayaś caiva rakṣitum
d asyās tvam aṣṭamaṃ garbhaṃ jātamātraṃ mahīpate
d vidhvaṃsaya tadā prāptam evaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavet
d evaṃ sa rājā kathito vasudevena bhārata
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tasya tad vacanaṃ cakre śūrasenādhipas tadā
d tatas tasyāṃ saṃbabhūvuḥ kumārāḥ sūryavarcasaḥ
d jātāñ jātāṃs tu tān sarvāñ jaghāna madhureśvaraḥ
d atha tasyāṃ samabhavad baladevas tu saptamaḥ
d yāmyayā māyayā taṃ tu yamo rājā viśāṃ pate
d devakyā garbham atulaṃ rohiṇyā jaṭhare 'kṣipat
d ākṛṣya karṣaṇāt samyak saṃkarṣaṇa iti smṛtaḥ
d balaśreṣṭhatayā tasya baladeva iti smṛtaḥ
d punas tasyāṃ samabhavad aṣṭamo madhusūdanaḥ
d tasya garbhasya rakṣāṃ tu cakre so 'bhyadhikaṃ nṛpaḥ
d tataḥ kāle rakṣaṇārthaṃ vasudevasya sātvataḥ
d ugraḥ prayuktaḥ kaṃsena sacivaḥ krūrakarmakṛt
d vimūḍheṣu prabhāvena bālasyottīrya tatra vai
d upāgamya sa ghoṣe tu jagāma samahādyutiḥ
d jātamātraṃ vāsudevam athākṛṣya pitā tataḥ
d upajahre parikrītāṃ sutāṃ gopasya kasya cit
d mumukṣamāṇas taṃ śabdaṃ devadūtasya pārthiva
d jaghāna kaṃsas tāṃ kanyāṃ prahasantī jagāma sā
d āryeti vāśatī śabdaṃ tasmād āryeti kīrtitā
d evaṃ taṃ vañcayitvā ca rājānaṃ sa mahāmatiḥ
d vāsudevaṃ mahātmānaṃ vardhayām āsa gokule
d vāsudevo 'pi gopeṣu vavṛdhe 'bjam ivāmbhasi
d ajñāyamānaḥ kaṃsena gūḍho 'gnir iva dāruṣu
d vipracakre 'tha tān sarvān ballavān madhureśvaraḥ
d vardhamāno mahābāhus tejobalasamanvitaḥ
d tatas te kliśyamānās tu puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam
d bhayena kāmād apare gaṇaśaḥ paryavārayan
d sa tu labdhvā balaṃ rājann ugrasenasya saṃmataḥ
d vasudevātmajaḥ sarvabhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaṃ punaḥ
d nirjitya yudhi bhojendraṃ hatvā kaṃsaṃ mahābalaḥ
d abhyaṣiñcat tato rājya ugrasenaṃ viśāṃ pate
d tataḥ śrutvā jarāsaṃdho mādhavena hataṃ yudhi
d śūrasenādhipaṃ cakre kaṃsaputraṃ tadā nṛpa
d sa sainyaṃ mahad utthāpya vāsudevaṃ prasahya ca
d abhyaṣiñcat sutaṃ tatra sutāyā janamejaya
d ugrasenaṃ ca vṛṣṇīṃś ca mahābalasamanvitaḥ
d sa tatra viprakurute jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān
d etad vairaṃ kauraveya jarāsaṃdhasya mādhave
d āśāsitārtho rājendra saṃrurodha vinirjitān
d pārthivais tair nṛpatibhir yakṣyamāṇaḥ samṛddhimān
d devaśreṣṭhaṃ mahādevaṃ kṛttivāsaṃ triyambakam
d etat sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ kathitaṃ bharatarṣabha
d yathā tu sa hato rājā bhīmasenena tac chṛṇu
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tatas taṃ niścitātmānaṃ yuddhāya yadunandanaḥ
c uvāca vāgmī rājānaṃ jarāsaṃdham adhokṣajaḥ
a trayāṇāṃ kena te rājan yoddhuṃ vitarate manaḥ
c asmad anyatameneha sajjībhavatu ko yudhi
d tvayā māyāvinā kṛṣṇa na yotsye 'haṃ kadā cana
d bhayena me yojitānāṃ yadūnāṃ ca palāyataḥ
d arjuno na bhaved yoddhā na ca tulyabalo mama
d bhīmaḥ kṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇārdhaṃ vā kṣamaḥ syād iti me puraḥ
a evam uktaḥ sa kṛṣṇena yuddhaṃ vavre mahādyutiḥ
c jarāsaṃdhas tato rājan bhīmasenena māgadhaḥ
d na tvayā bhīruṇā yotsye yudhi viklavacetasā
d mathurāṃ svapurīṃ tyaktvā samudraṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
d ayaṃ tu vayasātulyo nātisattvo na me samaḥ
d arjuno no bhaved yoddhā bhīmas tulyabalo mama
d ity uktvā bhīmasenāya pradāya mahatīṃ gadām
d dvitīyāṃ svayam ādāya nirjagāma purād bahiḥ
d ādāya rocanāṃ mālāṃ māṅgalyāny aparāṇi ca
a dhārayann agadān mukhyān nirvṛtīr vedanāni ca
c upatasthe jarāsaṃdhaṃ yuyutsuṃ vai purohitaḥ
d arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca varjayām āsa māgadhaḥ
d matvā devaṃ gopa iti bālo 'rjunam iti sma ha
a kṛtasvastyayano vidvān brāhmaṇena yaśasvinā
c samanahyaj jarāsaṃdhaḥ kṣatradharmam anuvrataḥ
a avamucya kirīṭaṃ sa keśān samanumṛjya ca
c udatiṣṭhaj jarāsaṃdho velātiga ivārṇavaḥ
a uvāca matimān rājā bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
c bhīma yotsye tvayā sārdhaṃ śreyasā nirjitaṃ varam
d kṣetrodaye tataḥ kṛṣṇa bālo 'yam anujo 'rjunaḥ
a evam uktvā jarāsaṃdho bhīmasenam ariṃdamaḥ
c pratyudyayau mahātejāḥ śakraṃ balir ivāsuraḥ
a tataḥ saṃmantrya kṛṣṇena kṛtasvastyayano balī
c bhīmaseno jarāsaṃdham āsasāda yuyutsayā
a tatas tau naraśārdūlau bāhuśastrau samīyatuḥ
c vīrau paramasaṃhṛṣṭāv anyonyajayakāṅkṣiṇau
d karagrahaṇapūrvaṃ tu kṛtvā pādābhivandanam
d kakṣaiḥ kakṣāṃ vidhunvānāv āsphoṭaṃ tatra cakratuḥ
d skandhe dorbhyāṃ samāhatya nihatya ca muhur muhuḥ
d aṅgam aṅgaiḥ samāśliṣya punar āsphālanaṃ vibho
d citrahastādikaṃ kṛtvā kakṣābandhaṃ ca cakratuḥ
d galagaṇḍābhighātena sasphuliṅgena cāśanim
d bāhupāśādikaṃ kṛtvā pādāhataśirāv ubhau
d urohastaṃ tataś cakre pūrṇakumbhau prayujya tau
d karasaṃpīḍanaṃ kṛtvā garjantau vāraṇāv iva
d nardantau meghasaṃkāśau bāhupraharaṇāv ubhau
d talenāhanyamānau tu anyonyaṃ kṛtavīkṣaṇau
d siṃhāv iva susaṃskruddhāv ākṛṣyākṛṣya yudhyatām
d aṅgenāṅgaṃ samāpīḍya bāhubhyām ubhayor api
d āvṛtya bāhubhiś cāpi udaraṃ ca pracakratuḥ
d ubhau kaṭyāṃ supārśve tu takṣavantau ca śikṣitau
d adhohastaṃ svakaṇṭhe tūdarasyorasi cākṣipat
d sarvātikrāntamaryādaṃ pṛṣṭhabhaṅgaṃ ca cakratuḥ
d saṃpūrṇamūrchāṃ bāhubhyāṃ pūrṇakumbhaṃ pracakratuḥ
d tṛṇapīḍaṃ yathākāmaṃ pūrṇayogaṃ samuṣṭikam
d evamādīni yuddhāni prakurvantau parasparam
d tayor yuddhaṃ tato draṣṭuṃ sametāḥ puravāsinaḥ
d brāhmaṇā vaṇijaś caiva kṣatriyāś ca sahasraśaḥ
d śūdrāś ca naraśārdūla striyo vṛddhāś ca sarvaśaḥ
d nirantaram abhūt tatra janaughair abhisaṃvṛtam
a tayor atha bhujāghātān nigrahapragrahāt tathā
c āsīt subhīmasaṃhrādo vajraparvatayor iva
a ubhau paramasaṃhṛṣṭau balenātibalāv ubhau
b anyonyaṃ tau karatalair yodhayām āsatur bhṛśam
c anyonyasyāntaraṃ prepsū parasparajayaiṣiṇau
d śirobhir iva tau meṣau vṛkṣair iva niśācarau
d padair iva śubhāv aśvau tuṇḍābhyāṃ tittirāv iva
a tad bhīmam utsārya janaṃ yuddham āsīd upahvare
c balinoḥ saṃyuge rājan vṛtravāsavayor iva
a prakarṣaṇākarṣaṇābhyām abhyākarṣavikarṣaṇaiḥ
c ākarṣetāṃ tathānyonyaṃ jānubhiś cābhijaghnatuḥ
a tataḥ śabdena mahatā bhartsayantau parasparam
c pāṣāṇasaṃghātanibhaiḥ prahārair abhijaghnatuḥ
d tato bhīmaṃ jarāsaṃdho jaghānorasi muṣṭinā
d bhīmo 'pi taṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ vakṣasy abhijaghāna ha
a vyūḍhoraskau dīrghabhujau niyuddhakuśalāv ubhau
c bāhubhiḥ samasajjetām āyasaiḥ parighair iva
a kārttikasya tu māsasya pravṛttaṃ prathame 'hani
b tadā tad yuddham abhavad dināni daśa pañca ca
c anārataṃ divārātram aviśrāntam avartata
d ghoraṃ vismāpanakaram abhūt pañcadaśe 'hani
a tad vṛttaṃ tu trayodaśyāṃ samavetaṃ mahātmanoḥ
b gātraṃ gātreṇa saṃpīḍya viśrāmam agamad dvayoḥ
b vāyunā hy amṛtaśvāsād āpyāyata vṛkodaraḥ
c caturdaśyāṃ niśāyāṃ tu nivṛtto māgadhaḥ klamāt
a taṃ rājānaṃ tathā klāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājañ janārdanaḥ
c uvāca bhīmakarmāṇaṃ bhīmaṃ saṃbodhayann iva
d samayuddhe nṛṇāṃ madhyāt pāṭayan bodhayann iva
d śatror janmamṛtī vidvāñ jīvitaṃ ca jarākṛtam
d pārtham āpyāyayan svena tejasācintayad dhariḥ
d saṃcintyārivadhopāyaṃ bhīmasyāmoghadarśanaḥ
d darśayām āsa viṭapaṃ pāṭayann iva saṃjñayā
a klāntaḥ śatrur na kaunteya labhyaḥ pīḍayituṃ raṇe
c pīḍyamāno hi kārtsnyena jahyāj jīvitam ātmanaḥ
a tasmāt te naiva kaunteya pīḍanīyo narādhipaḥ
c samam etena yudhyasva bāhubhyāṃ bharatarṣabha
a evam uktaḥ sa kṛṣṇena pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahā
c jarāsaṃdhasya tad randhraṃ jñātvā cakre matiṃ vadhe
a tatas tam ajitaṃ jetuṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ vṛkodaraḥ
c saṃrabhya balināṃ mukhyo jagrāha kurunandanaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a bhīmasenas tataḥ kṛṣṇam uvāca yadunandanam
c buddhim āsthāya vipulāṃ jarāsaṃdhajighāṃsayā
a nāyaṃ pāpo mayā kṛṣṇa yuktaḥ syād anurodhitum
c prāṇena yaduśārdūla baddhavaṅkṣaṇavāsasā
a evam uktas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pratyuvāca vṛkodaram
c tvarayan puruṣavyāghro jarāsaṃdhavadhepsayā
a yat te daivaṃ paraṃ sattvaṃ yac ca te mātariśvanaḥ
c balaṃ bhīma jarāsaṃdhe darśayāśu tad adya naḥ
d bale tubhyaṃ mahābāho tam imaṃ jahi māgadham
d tavaiṣa vadhyo durbuddhir jarāsaṃdho mahārathaḥ
d ity antarikṣe tv aśrauṣaṃ yadā vāyur apohyate
d gomante parvataśreṣṭhe yenaiṣa parimokṣitaḥ
d baladevabhujaṃ prāpya ko 'nyo jīveta māgadhāt
d tad asya mṛtyur vihitas tvad ṛte na mahābala
d vāyuṃ cintya mahābāho jahi tvaṃ magadhādhipam
d evam uktas tadā bhīmo manasā cintya mārutam
d janārdanaṃ namasyaiva pariṣvajya ca phalgunam
a evam uktas tadā bhīmo jarāsaṃdham ariṃdamaḥ
c utkṣipya bhrāmayad rājan balavantaṃ mahābalaḥ
a bhrāmayitvā śataguṇaṃ bhujābhyāṃ bharatarṣabha
c babhañja pṛṣṭhe saṃkṣipya niṣpiṣya vinanāda ca
d kare gṛhītvā caraṇaṃ dvedhā cakre mahābalaḥ
a tasya niṣpiṣyamāṇasya pāṇḍavasya ca garjataḥ
c abhavat tumulo nādaḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraḥ
d sa vāmapādaṃ saṃkṛṣya gṛhītvā dakṣiṇe mahe
d dvidhā cakāra taṃ pārtho jarāsaṃdhaṃ mahābalam
a vitresur māgadhāḥ sarve strīṇāṃ garbhāś ca susruvuḥ
c bhīmasenasya nādena jarāsaṃdhasya caiva ha
a kiṃ nu svid dhimavān bhinnaḥ kiṃ nu svid dīryate mahī
c iti sma māgadhā jajñur bhīmasenasya nisvanāt
d gṛhītvā pādayoḥ śatruṃ pātayām āsa bhūtale
d ekaṃ pādaṃ padākramya dorbhyām anyaṃ pragṛhya ca
d gudataḥ pāṭayām āsa śākhām iva mahāgajaḥ
d ekapādoruvṛṣaṇakaṭihṛtpṛṣṭhanāsike
d ekabāhvakṣibhrūkarṇe śakale dadṛśuḥ prajāḥ
d vīkṣya bhīmaṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇo naḷaṃ jagrāha pāṇinā
d dvidhā vyatilikhat taṃ tu jarāsaṃdhavadhaṃ prati
d tatas tv ājñāya tasyai         
d         traṃ prākṣipad vinanāda ca
d punaḥ saṃdhāya tu tadā jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān
d bhīmena saha saṃgamya bāhuyuddhaṃ cakāra ha
d tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
d sarvalokakṣayakaraṃ sarva      
d             dya mādhavaḥ
d vyatyasya prākṣipat tat tu jarāsaṃdhavadhepsayā
d bhīmasenas tadājñātvā nirbibheda ca māgadham
d dvidhā vyatyasya pādena prākṣipac ca nanāda ha
d śuṣkamāṃsāsthimedosṛg bhinnamastakapiṇḍakaḥ
d śavabhūtas tadā rājan piṇḍīkṛta ivābabhau
a tato rājakuladvāri prasuptam iva taṃ nṛpam
c rātrau parāsum utsṛjya niścakramur ariṃdamāḥ
a jarāsaṃdharathaṃ kṛṣṇo yojayitvā patākinam
c āropya bhrātarau caiva mokṣayām āsa bāndhavān
a te vai ratnabhujaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ratnārhaṃ pṛthivīśvarāḥ
c rājānaś cakrur āsādya mokṣitā mahato bhayāt
a akṣataḥ śastrasaṃpanno jitāriḥ saha rājabhiḥ
c ratham āsthāya taṃ divyaṃ nirjagāma girivrajāt
d uṣṭrāṇāṃ śatasāhasraṃ vāhayitvā dhanaṃ bahu
d mahārhāṇi ca ratnāni rajataṃ kāñcanaṃ tathā
d sahadevaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya svādhīnaṃ ca girivraje
d caturaṅgabalaiḥ sārdhaṃ nirjagāma girivrajāt
a yaḥ sa sodaryavān nāma dviyodhaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c abhyāsaghātī saṃdṛśyo durjayaḥ sarvarājabhiḥ
a bhīmārjunābhyāṃ yodhābhyām āsthitaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c śuśubhe rathavaryo 'sau durjayaḥ sarvadhanvibhiḥ
a śakraviṣṇū hi saṃgrāme ceratus tārakāmaye
c rathena tena taṃ kṛṣṇa upāruhya yayau tadā
d evam etau mahābāhū tadā duṣkarakāriṇau
d kṛṣṇapraṇītau loke 'smin rathe ko draṣṭum arhati
d ity avocan vrajantaṃ taṃ jarāsaṃdhapurālayāḥ
d vāsudevaṃ naraśreṣṭhaṃ yuktaṃ vātajavair hayaiḥ
a taptacāmīkarābheṇa kiṅkiṇījālamālinā
c meghanirghoṣanādena jaitreṇāmitraghātinā
a yena śakro dānavānāṃ jaghāna navatīr nava
c taṃ prāpya samahṛṣyanta rathaṃ te puruṣarṣabhāḥ
a tataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ mahābāhuṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ sahitaṃ tadā
c rathasthaṃ māgadhā dṛṣṭvā samapadyanta vismitāḥ
a hayair divyaiḥ samāyukto ratho vāyusamo jave
c adhiṣṭhitaḥ sa śuśubhe kṛṣṇenātīva bhārata
a asaṅgī devavihitas tasmin rathavare dhvajaḥ
c yojanād dadṛśe śrīmān indrāyudhasamaprabhaḥ
a cintayām āsa kṛṣṇo 'tha garutmantaṃ sa cābhyayāt
c kṣaṇe tasmin sa tenāsīc caityayūpa ivocchritaḥ
a vyāditāsyair mahānādaiḥ saha bhūtair dhvajālayaiḥ
c tasthau rathavare tasmin garutmān pannagāśanaḥ
a durnirīkṣyo hi bhūtānāṃ tejasābhyadhikaṃ babhau
c āditya iva madhyāhne sahasrakiraṇāvṛtaḥ
a na sa sajjati vṛkṣeṣu śastraiś cāpi na riṣyate
c divyo dhvajavaro rājan dṛśyate devamānuṣaiḥ
a tam āsthāya rathaṃ divyaṃ parjanyasamanisvanam
c niryayau puruṣavyāghraḥ pāṇḍavābhyāṃ sahācyutaḥ
a yaṃ lebhe vāsavād rājā vasus tasmād bṛhadrathaḥ
c bṛhadrathāt krameṇaiva prāpto bārhadrathaṃ nṛpam
a sa niryayau mahābāhuḥ puṇḍarīkekṣaṇas tataḥ
c girivrajād bahis tasthau same deśe mahāyaśāḥ
a tatrainaṃ nāgarāḥ sarve satkāreṇābhyayus tadā
c brāhmaṇapramukhā rājan vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
a bandhanād vipramuktāś ca rājāno madhusūdanam
c pūjayām āsur ūcuś ca sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
a naitac citraṃ mahābāho tvayi devakinandana
c bhīmārjunabalopete dharmasya paripālanam
a jarāsaṃdhahrade ghore duḥkhapaṅke nimajjatām
c rājñāṃ samabhyuddharaṇaṃ yad idaṃ kṛtam adya te
a viṣṇo samavasannānāṃ giridurge sudāruṇe
c diṣṭyā mokṣād yaśo dīptam āptaṃ te puruṣottama
a kiṃ kurmaḥ puruṣavyāghra bravīhi puruṣarṣabha
c kṛtam ity eva taj jñeyaṃ nṛpair yady api duṣkaram
a tān uvāca hṛṣīkeśaḥ samāśvāsya mahāmanāḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiro rājasūyaṃ kratum āhartum icchati
a tasya dharmapravṛttasya pārthivatvaṃ cikīrṣataḥ
c sarvair bhavadbhir yajñārthe sāhāyyaṃ dīyatām iti
a tataḥ pratītamanasas te nṛpā bharatarṣabha
c tathety evābruvan sarve pratijajñuś ca tāṃ giram
a ratnabhājaṃ ca dāśārhaṃ cakrus te pṛthivīśvarāḥ
c kṛcchrāj jagrāha govindas teṣāṃ tadanukampayā
a jarāsaṃdhātmajaś caiva sahadevo mahārathaḥ
c niryayau sajanāmātyaḥ puraskṛtya purohitam
a sa nīcaiḥ praśrito bhūtvā bahuratnapurogamaḥ
c sahadevo nṛṇāṃ devaṃ vāsudevam upasthitaḥ
d sahadevaḥ
d yat kṛtaṃ puruṣavyāghra mama pitrā janārdana
d tat te hṛdi mahābāho na kāryaṃ puruṣottama
d tvāṃ prapanno 'smi govinda prasādaṃ kuru me prabho
d pitur icchāmi saṃskāraṃ kartuṃ devakinandana
d tvatto 'bhyanujñāṃ saṃprāpya bhīmasenāt tathārjunāt
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d nirbhayo vicariṣyāmi yathākāmaṃ yathāsukham
d evaṃ vijñāpyamānasya sahadevasya māriṣa
d prahṛṣṭo devakīputraḥ pāṇḍavau ca mahārathau
d kriyatāṃ saṃskriyā rājan pitus ta iti cābruvan
d tac chrutvā vāsudevasya pārthayoś ca māgadhaḥ
d praviśya nagaraṃ tūrṇaṃ saha mantribhir apy uta
d citāṃ candanakāṣṭhaiś ca kāleyasaralais tathā
d kālāgurusugandhaiś ca tailaiś ca vividhair api
d ghṛtadhārākṣataiś caiva sumanobhiś ca māgadham
d samantād avakīryanta dahyantaṃ magadhādhipam
d udakaṃ tasya cakre 'tha sahadevaḥ sahānujaḥ
d kṛtvā pituḥ svargagatiṃ niryayau yatra keśavaḥ
d pāṇḍavau ca mahābhāgau bhīmasenārjunāv ubhau
d sa prahvaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā vijñāpayata mādhavam
d ime ratnāni bhūrīṇi gojāvimahiṣādayaḥ
d hastino 'śvāś ca govinda vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca
d dīyatāṃ dharmarājāya yathā vā manyate bhavān
a bhayārtāya tatas tasmai kṛṣṇo dattvābhayaṃ tadā
b ādade 'sya mahārhāṇi ratnāni puruṣottamaḥ
b   sahadevaṃ janārdanaḥ
b magadhānāṃ mahīpālaṃ
c abhyaṣiñcata tatraiva jarāsaṃdhātmajaṃ tadā
a gatvaikatvaṃ ca kṛṣṇena pārthābhyāṃ caiva satkṛtaḥ
c viveśa rājā matimān punar bārhadrathaṃ puram
d abhiṣikto mahābāhur jārāsaṃdhir mahātmabhiḥ
d pārthābhyāṃ sahitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarvaiś ca vasudhādhipaiḥ
d yathāvayaḥ samāgamya visasarja narādhipān
d visṛjya sarvān nṛpatīn rājasūye mahātmabhiḥ
d āgantavyaṃ bhavadbhis tu dharmarājapriyepsubhiḥ
d evam uktvā mādhavena sarve te vasudhādhipāḥ
d evam astv iti cāpy uktvā sametāḥ parayā mudā
d bhīmārjunahṛṣīkeśāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ prayayuḥ saha
d ratnāny ādāya bhūrīṇi jvalanto ripusūdanāḥ
a kṛṣṇas tu saha pārthābhyāṃ śriyā paramayā jvalan
c ratnāny ādāya bhūrīṇi prayayau puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
a indraprastham upāgamya pāṇḍavābhyāṃ sahācyutaḥ
c sametya dharmarājānaṃ prīyamāṇo 'bhyabhāṣata
a diṣṭyā bhīmena balavāñ jarāsaṃdho nipātitaḥ
c rājāno mokṣitāś ceme bandhanān nṛpasattama
a diṣṭyā kuśalinau cemau bhīmasenadhanaṃjayau
c punaḥ svanagaraṃ prāptāv akṣatāv iti bhārata
a tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kṛṣṇaṃ pūjayitvā yathārhataḥ
c bhīmasenārjunau caiva prahṛṣṭaḥ pariṣasvaje
a tataḥ kṣīṇe jarāsaṃdhe bhrātṛbhyāṃ vihitaṃ jayam
c ajātaśatrur āsādya mumude bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
d hṛṣṭaś ca dharmarāḍ vākyaṃ janārdanam abhāṣata
d tvāṃ prāpya puruṣavyāghra bhīmasenena pātitaḥ
d māgadho 'sau balonmatto jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān
d rājasūyaṃ kratuśreṣṭhaṃ prāpsyāmi vigatajvaraḥ
d tvadbuddhibalam āśritya yāgārho 'smi janārdana
d pītaṃ pṛthivyāṃ kruddhena yaśas te puruṣottama
d jarāsaṃdhavadhenaiva prāptās te vipulāḥ śriyaḥ
d evaṃ saṃbhāṣya kaunteyaḥ prādād rathavaraṃ prabho
d pratigṛhya tu govindo jarāsaṃdhasya taṃ ratham
d prahṛṣṭas tasya mumude phalgunena janārdanaḥ
d prītimān abhavad rājan dharmarājapuraskṛtaḥ
a yathāvayaḥ samāgamya rājabhis taiś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c satkṛtya pūjayitvā ca visasarja narādhipān
a yudhiṣṭhirābhyanujñātās te nṛpā hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
c jagmuḥ svadeśāṃs tvaritā yānair uccāvacais tataḥ
a evaṃ puruṣaśārdūlo mahābuddhir janārdanaḥ
c pāṇḍavair ghātayām āsa jarāsaṃdham ariṃ tadā
a ghātayitvā jarāsaṃdhaṃ buddhipūrvam ariṃdamaḥ
c dharmarājam anujñāpya pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ ca bhārata
a subhadrāṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca phalgunaṃ yamajau tathā
c dhaumyam āmantrayitvā ca prayayau svāṃ purīṃ prati
d pāṇḍavair anudhāvadbhir yudhiṣṭhirapurogamaiḥ
d harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ prāpya cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥ
d jagāma hṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇas tu punar dvāravatīṃ purīm
a tenaiva rathamukhyena taruṇādityavarcasā
c dharmarājavisṛṣṭena divyenānādayan diśaḥ
a tato yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabha
c pradakṣiṇam akurvanta kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam
a tato gate bhagavati kṛṣṇe devakinandane
c jayaṃ labdhvā suvipulaṃ rājñām abhayadās tadā
a saṃvardhitaujaso bhūyaḥ karmaṇā tena bhārata
c draupadyāḥ pāṇḍavā rājan parāṃ prītim avardhayan
a tasmin kāle tu yad yuktaṃ dharmakāmārthasaṃhitam
c tad rājā dharmataś cakre rājyapālanakīrtimān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pārthaḥ prāpya dhanuḥśreṣṭham akṣayyau ca maheṣudhī
c rathaṃ dhvajaṃ sabhāṃ caiva yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣata
d ṛṣes tad vacanaṃ cintya niśaśvāsa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kartum icchan paraṃtapaḥ
d tasyeṅgitajño bībhatsuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d saṃvivartayiṣuḥ kāmaṃ pāvakāt pākaśāsaniḥ
a dhanur astraṃ śarā vīryaṃ pakṣo bhūmir yaśo balam
c prāptam etan mayā rājan duṣprāpaṃ yad abhīpsitam
d etac chrutvā kuruśreṣṭho dharmarājaḥ sahānujaḥ
d prahṛṣṭo mantribhiś caiva vyāsadhaumyādibhiḥ saha
d tato vyāso mahābuddhir uvācedaṃ vaco 'rjunam
d sādhu sādhv iti kaunteya diṣṭyā te buddhir īdṛśī
d pṛthivīm akhilāṃ jetum eko vyavasito bhavān
d dhanyaḥ pāṇḍur mahīpālo yasya putras tvam īdṛśaḥ
d sarvaṃ prāpsyati rājendro dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d tvadvīryeṇa sa dharmātmā sārvabhaumatvam eṣyati
d tvadbāhubalam āśritya rājasūyam avāpsyati
d sunayād vāsudevasya bhīmārjunabalena ca
d yamayoś caiva vīryeṇa sarvaṃ prāpsyati dharmarāṭ
d tasmād diśaṃ devaguptām udīcīṃ gaccha phalguna
d śakto bhavān surāñ jitvā ratnāny āhartum ojasā
d prācīṃ bhīmo balaślāghī prayātu bharatarṣabha
d yāmyāṃ tatra diśaṃ yātu sahadevo mahārathaḥ
d pratīcīṃ nakulo gantā varuṇenābhipālitām
d eṣā me naiṣṭhikī buddhiḥ kriyatāṃ bharatarṣabhāḥ
d śrutvā vyāsavaco hṛṣṭās tam ūcuḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ
d evam astu muniśreṣṭha yathājñāpayasi prabho
d te 'py anujñāpya rājānaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtāḥ
a tatra kṛtyam ahaṃ manye kośasyāsya vivardhanam
c karam āhārayiṣyāmi rājñaḥ sarvān nṛpottama
a vijayāya prayāsyāmi diśaṃ dhanadarakṣitām
b sarve vāyupravegāś ca sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ
c tithāv atha muhūrte ca nakṣatre ca tathā śive
a dhanaṃjayavacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c snigdhagambhīranādinyā taṃ girā pratyabhāṣata
a svasti vācyārhato viprān prayāhi bharatarṣabha
c durhṛdām apraharṣāya suhṛdāṃ nandanāya ca
e vijayas te dhruvaṃ pārtha priyaṃ kāmam avāpnuhi
a ity uktaḥ prayayau pārthaḥ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c agnidattena divyena rathenādbhutakarmaṇā
a tathaiva bhīmaseno 'pi yamau ca puruṣarṣabhau
c sasainyāḥ prayayuḥ sarve dharmarājābhipūjitāḥ
a diśaṃ dhanapater iṣṭām ajayat pākaśāsaniḥ
c bhīmasenas tathā prācīṃ sahadevas tu dakṣiṇām
a pratīcīṃ nakulo rājan diśaṃ vyajayad astravit
c khāṇḍavaprastham adhyāste dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d āsīt paramayā lakṣmyā suhṛdgaṇavṛtaḥ prabhuḥ
 janamejaya uvāca
a diśām abhijayaṃ brahman vistareṇānukīrtaya
c na hi tṛpyāmi pūrveṣāṃ śṛṇvānaś caritaṃ mahat
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a dhanaṃjayasya vakṣyāmi vijayaṃ pūrvam eva te
c yaugapadyena pārthair hi vijiteyaṃ vasuṃdharā
d avāpya rājā rājyārdhaṃ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d mahattve rājaśabdasya manaś cakre mahāmanāḥ
d tadā kṣatraṃ viditvāsya pṛthivīvijayaṃ prati
d amarṣāt pārthivendrās te taṃ sameyur yuyutsavaḥ
d tat sametya bhuvaḥ kṣatraṃ rathanāgāśvapattimat
d abhyayāt pārthivaṃ jiṣṇuṃ moghīkartuṃ janādhipa
d tat pārthaḥ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ yuyutsuḥ paramāhave
d pratyudyayau mahābāhus tarasā pākaśāsaniḥ
d tad bhagnaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ pārthenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
d vāyuneva ghanānīkaṃ moghībhūtaṃ yayau diśaḥ
d taj jitvā pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ samare paravīrahā
d yayau tadā vaśe kartum udīcīṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
a pūrvaṃ kuṇindaviṣaye vaśe cakre mahīpatīn
c dhanaṃjayo mahābāhur nātitīvreṇa karmaṇā
d tenaiva sahitaḥ prāyāj jiṣṇuḥ sālvapuraṃ prati
d sa sālvapuram āsādya sālvarājaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
d vikrameṇogradhanvānaṃ vaśe cakre mahāmanāḥ
d taṃ pārthaḥ sahasā jitvā dyumatsenaṃ dhaneśvaram
d kṛtvānusainikaṃ prāyāt kaṭadeśam ariṃdamaḥ
d tatra pāpajitaṃ jiṣṇuḥ sunābhaṃ vasudhādhipam
d vikrameṇa vaśe kṛtvā kṛtavān anusainikam
a ānartān kālakūṭāṃś ca kuṇindāṃś ca vijitya saḥ
c sumaṇḍalaṃ pāpajitaṃ kṛtavān anusainikam
a sa tena sahito rājan savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c vijigye sakalaṃ dvīpaṃ prativindhyaṃ ca pārthivam
a sakaladvīpavāsāṃś ca saptadvīpe ca ye nṛpāḥ
b tān sarvān ajayat pārtho dharmarājapriyepsayā
c arjunasya ca sainyānāṃ vigrahas tumulo 'bhavat
a sa tān api maheṣvāso vijitya bharatarṣabha
c tair eva sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ prāgjyotiṣam upādravat
a tatra rājā mahān āsīd bhagadatto viśāṃ pate
c tenāsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
a sa kirātaiś ca cīnaiś ca vṛtaḥ prāgjyotiṣo 'bhavat
c anyaiś ca bahubhir yodhaiḥ sāgarānūpavāsibhiḥ
a tataḥ sa divasān aṣṭau yodhayitvā dhanaṃjayam
b caturaṅgabalaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhagadattaḥ parājitaḥ
b pārthasāyakanunnas tu vihvalāṅgo bhṛśāturaḥ
c prahasann abravīd rājā saṃgrāme vigataklamaḥ
a upapannaṃ mahābāho tvayi pāṇḍavanandana
c pākaśāsanadāyāde vīryam āhavaśobhini
a ahaṃ sakhā surendrasya śakrād anavamo raṇe
c na ca śaknomi te tāta sthātuṃ pramukhato yudhi
a kim īpsitaṃ pāṇḍaveya brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
c yad vakṣyasi mahābāho tat kariṣyāmi putraka
 arjuna uvāca
a kurūṇām ṛṣabho rājā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ
c tasya pārthivatām īpse karas tasmai pradīyatām
a bhavān pitṛsakhā caiva prīyamāṇo mayāpi ca
c tato nājñāpayāmi tvāṃ prītipūrvaṃ pradīyatām
 bhagadatta uvāca
a kuntīmātar yathā me tvaṃ tathā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b sa tatra satkṛtas tena māsam uṣya dhanaṃjayaḥ
b udakprācyāṃ vinirjitya prāyād rāmagiriṃ prati
b tato rāmagiriṃ jitvā tathā bhuvanaparvatam
b anyān api vaśe cakre tarasā pākaśāsaniḥ
c sarvam etat kariṣyāmi kiṃ cānyat karavāṇi te
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a taṃ vijitya mahābāhuḥ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c prayayāv uttarāṃ tasmād diśaṃ dhanadapālitām
d evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca bhagadattaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
d anenaiva kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ bhaviṣyaty anujānatā
a antargiriṃ ca kaunteyas tathaiva ca bahirgirim
c tathoparigiriṃ caiva vijigye puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a vijitya parvatān sarvān ye ca tatra narādhipāḥ
c tān vaśe sthāpayitvā sa ratnāny ādāya sarvaśaḥ
a tair eva sahitaḥ sarvair anurajya ca tān nṛpān
c kulūtavāsinaṃ rājan bṛhantam upajagmivān
a mṛdaṅgavaranādena rathanemisvanena ca
c hastināṃ ca ninādena kampayan vasudhām imām
a tato bṛhantas taruṇo balena caturaṅgiṇā
c niṣkramya nagarāt tasmād yodhayām āsa pāṇḍavam
a sumahān saṃnipāto 'bhūd dhanaṃjayabṛhantayoḥ
c na śaśāka bṛhantas tu soḍhuṃ pāṇḍavavikramam
a so 'viṣahyatamaṃ jñātvā kaunteyaṃ parvateśvaraḥ
c upāvartata durmedhā ratnāny ādāya sarvaśaḥ
d upacāracchalenāsau pradadau saṃcitān vasūn
d arbudaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca nyarbudaṃ vājināṃ tathā
d tatas tenaiva sahitaḥ kaulūtena dhanaṃjayaḥ
a sa tad rājyam avasthāpya kulūtasahito yayau
c senābindum atho rājan rājyād āśu samākṣipat
a modāpuraṃ vāmadevaṃ sudāmānaṃ susaṃkulam
c kulūtān uttarāṃś caiva tāṃś ca rājñaḥ samānayat
a tatrasthaḥ puruṣair eva dharmarājasya śāsanāt
c vyajayad dhanaṃjayo rājan deśān pañca pramāṇataḥ
a sa divaḥprastham āsādya senābindoḥ puraṃ mahat
c balena caturaṅgeṇa niveśam akarot prabhuḥ
a sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvair viṣvagaśvaṃ narādhipam
c abhyagacchan mahātejāḥ pauravaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a vijitya cāhave śūrān pārvatīyān mahārathān
c dhvajinyā vyajayad rājan puraṃ pauravarakṣitam
d mahatā tatra sainyena pramathyat kurunandanaḥ
d urasāvalinaṃ caiva romāṇaṃ ca raṇe 'kṣipat
a pauravaṃ tu vinirjitya dasyūn parvatavāsinaḥ
a   senābinduṃ ca tatpure
a nyadhāpayad ameyātmā
c gaṇān utsavasaṃketān ajayat sapta pāṇḍavaḥ
a tataḥ kāśmīrakān vīrān kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ
c vyajayal lohitaṃ caiva maṇḍalair daśabhiḥ saha
a tatas trigartān kaunteyo dārvān kokanadāś ca ye
c kṣatriyā bahavo rājann upāvartanta sarvaśaḥ
a abhisārīṃ tato ramyāṃ vijigye kurunandanaḥ
c uraśāvāsinaṃ caiva rocamānaṃ raṇe 'jayat
a tataḥ siṃhapuraṃ ramyaṃ citrāyudhasurakṣitam
c prāmathad balam āsthāya pākaśāsanir āhave
a tataḥ suhmāṃś ca colāṃś ca kirīṭī pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
c sahitaḥ sarvasainyena prāmathat kurunandanaḥ
a tataḥ paramavikrānto bāhlīkān kurunandanaḥ
c mahatā parimardena vaśe cakre durāsadān
a gṛhītvā tu balaṃ sāraṃ phalgu cotsṛjya pāṇḍavaḥ
c daradān saha kāmbojair ajayat pākaśāsaniḥ
d yavanāṃś ca mahārāja śakāṃś ca vyajayad yudhi
d kirātān sabhayān kharvān khalān kācān bahuvṛtān
d nīrān utpāsikāṃś caiva mlecchāṃś cānyān sahasraśaḥ
d tān sarvān ajayat pārtho dharmarājapriyepsayā
a prāguttarāṃ diśaṃ ye ca vasanty āśritya dasyavaḥ
c nivasanti vane ye ca tān sarvān ajayat prabhuḥ
a lohān paramakāmbojān ṛṣikān uttarān api
c sahitāṃs tān mahārāja vyajayat pākaśāsaniḥ
a ṛṣikeṣu tu saṃgrāmo babhūvātibhayaṃkaraḥ
c tārakāmayasaṃkāśaḥ paramarṣikapārthayoḥ
a sa vijitya tato rājann ṛṣikān raṇamūrdhani
c śukodarasamaprakhyān hayān aṣṭau samānayat
e mayūrasadṛśān anyān ubhayān eva cāparān
f javanān āśugāṃś caiva karārthaṃ samupānayat
f tataḥ sa jitvā bībhatsur bhārataṃ varṣakaṃ tadā
f janamejayaḥ
f anyān vai divyavarṣāṃś ca jitavān kulaparvatān
f kathaṃ sa jitavān pārtho divyān varṣān saparvatān
f ānupūrvyāc ca me śaṃsa nāmabhiḥ saha vai dvija
f vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
f sa jitvā bhārataṃ varṣaṃ balād rājā dhanaṃjayaḥ
f dasyūṃś cāpy ajayat sarvān kukṣau himavato balāt
a sa vinirjitya saṃgrāme himavantaṃ saniṣkuṭam
c śvetaparvatam āsādya nyavasat puruṣarṣabhaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa śvetaparvataṃ vīraḥ samatikramya bhārata
c deśaṃ kiṃpuruṣāvāsaṃ drumaputreṇa rakṣitam
a mahatā saṃnipātena kṣatriyāntakareṇa ha
c vyajayat pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaḥ kare caiva nyaveśayat
a taṃ jitvā hāṭakaṃ nāma deśaṃ guhyakarakṣitam
c pākaśāsanir avyagraḥ sahasainyaḥ samāsadat
a tāṃs tu sāntvena nirjitya mānasaṃ sara uttamam
c ṛṣikulyāś ca tāḥ sarvā dadarśa kurunandanaḥ
a saro mānasam āsādya hāṭakān abhitaḥ prabhuḥ
c gandharvarakṣitaṃ deśaṃ vyajayat pāṇḍavas tataḥ
a tatra tittirikalmāṣān maṇḍūkākṣān hayottamān
c lebhe sa karam atyantaṃ gandharvanagarāt tadā
d hemakūṭam athāsādya nyaviśat phalgunas tadā
d taṃ hemakūṭaṃ rājendra samatikramya pāṇḍavaḥ
d harivarṣaṃ viveśātha sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
d tatra pārtho dadarśātha bahūṃś caiva manoramān
d nagarāṃś ca vanāṃś caiva nadīś ca vimalodakāḥ
d puruṣān devakalpāṃś ca nārīś ca priyadarśanāḥ
d tān sarvāṃs tatra dṛṣṭvātha mudā yukto dhanaṃjayaḥ
d vaśe cakre ca ratnāni lebhe ca subahūni ca
d tato niṣadham āsādya giristhān ajayat prabhuḥ
d atha rājann atikramya niṣadhaṃ śailam āyatam
d viveśa madhyamaṃ varṣaṃ pārtho divyam ilāvṛtam
d tatra devopamān divyān puruṣān devadarśanān
d adṛṣṭapūrvān subhagān sa dadarśa dhanaṃjayaḥ
d sadanāni ca śubhrāṇi nārīś cāpsarasaṃnibhāḥ
d dṛṣṭvā tān ajayad ramyān sa taiś ca dadṛśe tadā
d jitvā ca tān mahābhāgān kare ca viniveśya saḥ
d ratnāny ādāya divyāni bhūṣaṇair vasanaiḥ saha
d udīcīm atha rājendra yayau pārtho mudānvitaḥ
d sa dadarśa tato meruṃ śikharāṇāṃ prabhuṃ mahat
d taṃ kāñcanamayaṃ divyaṃ caturvarṇaṃ durāsadam
d āyataṃ śatasāhasraṃ yojanānāṃ tu susthitam
d jvalantam acalaṃ meruṃ tejorāśim anuttamam
d ākṣipantaṃ prabhāṃ bhānoḥ svaśṛṅgaiḥ kāñcanojjvalaiḥ
d kāñcanābharaṇaṃ divyaṃ devagandharvasevitam
d nityapuṣpaphalopetaṃ siddhacāraṇasevitam
d aprameyam anādhṛṣyam adharmabahulair janaiḥ
d vyālair ācaritaṃ ghorair divyauṣadhividīpitam
d svargam āvṛtya tiṣṭhantam ucchrayeṇa mahāgirim
d agamyaṃ manasāpy anyair nadīvṛkṣasamanvitam
d nānāvihagasaṃghaiś ca nāditaṃ sumanoharaiḥ
d taṃ dṛṣṭvā phalguno meruṃ prītimān abhavat tadā
d meror ilāvṛtaṃ varṣaṃ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalam
d meros tu dakṣiṇe pārśve jambūr nāma vanaspatiḥ
d nityapuṣpaphalopetaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ
d āsvargam ucchritā rājaṃs tasya śākhā vanaspateḥ
d yasya nāmnā tv idaṃ dvīpaṃ jambūdvīpam iti śrutam
d tāṃ ca jambūṃ dadarśātha savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
d tau dṛṣṭvāpratimau loke jambūṃ meruṃ ca saṃsthitau
d prītimān abhavad rājan sarvataḥ sa vilokayan
d tatra lebhe tato jiṣṇuḥ siddhair divyaiś ca cāraṇaiḥ
d ratnāni bahusāhasraṃ vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca
d anyāni ca mahārhāṇi tatra labdhvārjunas tadā
d āmantrayitvā tān sarvān yajñam uddiśya vai guroḥ
d athādāya bahūn ratnān gamanāyopacakrame
d meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā parvatapravaraṃ prabhuḥ
d yayau jambūnadītīre nadīṃ śreṣṭhāṃ vilokayan
d sa tāṃ manoramāṃ divyāṃ jambūsvādurasāvahām
d haimapakṣigaṇair juṣṭāṃ sauvarṇajalajākulām
d haimapaṅkāṃ haimajalāṃ śubhāṃ sauvarṇavālukām
d kva cit sauvarṇapadmaiś ca saṃkulāṃ haimapuṣpakaiḥ
d kva cit supuṣpitaiḥ kīrṇāṃ suvarṇakumudotpalaiḥ
d kva cit tīraruhaiḥ kīrṇāṃ haimavṛkṣaiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ
d tīrthaiś ca rukmasopānaiḥ sarvataḥ saṃkulāṃ śubhām
d vimalair maṇijālaiś ca nṛttagītaravair yutām
d dīptair hemavitānaś ca samantāc chobhitāṃ śubhām
d tathāvidhāṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthas tāṃ praśaśaṃsa ha
d adṛṣṭapūrvāṃ rājendra dṛṣṭvā harṣam avāpa ca
d darśanīyān nadītīre puruṣān sumanoharān
d tān nadīsalilāhārān sadārān amaropamān
d nityaṃ sukhamudā yuktān sarvālaṃkāraśobhitān
d tebhyo bahūni ratnāni tadā lebhe dhanaṃjayaḥ
d divyajāmbūnadaṃ haimaṃ bhūṣaṇāni ca peśalam
d labdhvā tān durlabhān pārthaḥ pratīcīṃ prayayau diśam
d nāgānāṃ rakṣitaṃ deśam ajayac cārjunas tataḥ
d tato gatvā mahārāja vāruṇīṃ pākaśāsaniḥ
d gandhamādanam āsādya tatrasthān ajayat prabhuḥ
d taṃ gandhamādanaṃ rājann atikramya tato 'rjunaḥ
d ketumālaṃ viveśātha varṣaṃ ratnasamanvitam
d sevitaṃ devakalpaiś ca nārībhiḥ priyadarśanaiḥ
d taṃ jitvā cārjuno rājan kare ca viniveśya ca
d āhṛtya tatra ratnāni durlabhāni tathārjunaḥ
d punaś ca parivṛtyātha madhyaṃ deśam ilāvṛtam
d gatvā prācīṃ diśaṃ rājan savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
d merumandarayor madhye śailodām abhito nadīm
d ye te kīcakaveṇūnāṃ chāyāṃ ramyām upāsate
d khaṣāñ jhaṣāṃś ca nadyotān praghasān dīrghaveṇikān
d paśupāṃś ca kuṇindāṃś ca ṭaṅkaṇān paraṭaṅkaṇān
d etān samastāñ jitvā ca kare ca viniveśya ca
d ratnāny ādāya sarvebhyo mālyavantaṃ tato yayau
d taṃ mālyavantaṃ śailendraṃ samatikramya pāṇḍavaḥ
d bhadrāśvaṃ praviveśātha varṣaṃ svargopamaṃ śubham
d tatrāmaropamān ramyān puruṣān sukhasaṃyutān
d jitvā tān svavaśe kṛtvā kare ca viniveśya ca
d āhṛtya sarvaratnāni asaṃkhyāni tatas tataḥ
d nīlaṃ nāma giriṃ gatvā tatrasthān ajayat prabhuḥ
d tato jiṣṇur atikramya parvataṃ nīlam āyatam
d viveśa ramyakaṃ varṣaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ mithunaiḥ śubhaiḥ
d taṃ deśam atha jitvā sa kare ca viniveśya ca
d ajayac cāpi bībhatsur deśaṃ guhyakarakṣitam
d tatra lebhe ca rājendra sauvarṇān mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
d agṛhṇad yajñabhūtyarthaṃ ramaṇīyān manoramān
d anyāni labdhvā ratnāni pāṇḍavo 'tha mahābalaḥ
d gandharvarakṣitaṃ deśam ajayat sagaṇaṃ tadā
d tatra ratnāni divyāni labdhvā rājann athārjunaḥ
d śvetaparvatam āsādya jitvā parvatavāsinaḥ
d sa śvetaṃ parvataṃ rājan samatikramya pāṇḍavaḥ
d varṣaṃ hiraṇyakaṃ nāma viveśātha mahīpate
d sa tu deśeṣu ramyeṣu gantuṃ tatropacakrame
d madhye prāsādavṛndeṣu nakṣatrāṇāṃ śaśī yathā
d mahāpatheṣu rājendra sarvato yāntam arjunam
d prāsādavaraśṛṅgasthāḥ parayā vīryaśobhayā
d dadṛśus tāḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ pārtham ātmayaśaskaram
d taṃ kalāpadharaṃ śūraṃ sarathaṃ sānugaṃ prabhum
d savarmaṃ sakirīṭaṃ vai saṃnaddhaṃ saparicchadam
d sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ tejorāśim anuttamam
d śakropamam amitraghnaṃ paravāraṇavāraṇam
d paśyantaḥ strīgaṇās tatra śaktipāṇiṃ sma menire
d ayaṃ sa puruṣavyāghro raṇe 'dbhutaparākramaḥ
d asya bāhubalaṃ prāpya na bhavanty asuhṛdgaṇāḥ
d iti vāco bruvantyas tāḥ striyaḥ premṇā dhanaṃjayam
d tuṣṭuvuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca sasṛjus tasya mūrdhani
d dṛṣṭvā te tu mudā yuktāḥ kautūhalasamanvitāḥ
d ratnair vibhūṣaṇaiś caiva abhyavarṣanta pāṇḍavam
d atha jitvā samastāṃs tān kare ca viniveśya ca
d maṇihemapravālāni vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d etāni labdhvā pārtho 'pi śṛṅgavantaṃ giriṃ yayau
d śṛṅgavantaṃ ca kaunteyaḥ samatikramya phalgunaḥ
a uttaraṃ harivarṣaṃ tu samāsādya sa pāṇḍavaḥ
b vidyādharagaṇāṃś caiva yakṣendrāṃś ca vinirjayan
b tatra lebhe mahātmā vai vāso divyam anuttamam
b kiṃnaradrumapatrāṃś ca tatra kṛṣṇājinān bahūn
b yājñīyāṃs tāṃs tadā divyāṃs tatra lebhe dhanaṃjayaḥ
c iyeṣa jetuṃ taṃ deśaṃ pākaśāsananandanaḥ
a tata enaṃ mahākāyā mahāvīryā mahābalāḥ
c dvārapālāḥ samāsādya hṛṣṭā vacanam abruvan
a pārtha nedaṃ tvayā śakyaṃ puraṃ jetuṃ kathaṃ cana
c upāvartasva kalyāṇa paryāptam idam acyuta
a idaṃ puraṃ yaḥ praviśed dhruvaṃ sa na bhaven naraḥ
c prīyāmahe tvayā vīra paryāpto vijayas tava
a na cāpi kiṃ cij jetavyam arjunātra pradṛśyate
c uttarāḥ kuravo hy ete nātra yuddhaṃ pravartate
a praviṣṭaś cāpi kaunteya neha drakṣyasi kiṃ cana
c na hi mānuṣadehena śakyam atrābhivīkṣitum
a atheha puruṣavyāghra kiṃ cid anyac cikīrṣasi
c tad bravīhi kariṣyāmo vacanāt tava bhārata
a tatas tān abravīd rājann arjunaḥ pākaśāsaniḥ
c pārthivatvaṃ cikīrṣāmi dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
d kṛṣṇasya śāsanāc caiva pārthivatvaṃ cikīrṣati
a na pravekṣyāmi vo deśaṃ bādhyatvaṃ yadi mānuṣaiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirāya yat kiṃ cit karavan naḥ pradīyatām
d no cet kṛṣṇena sahito yodhayiṣyāmi pālakāḥ
a tato divyāni vastrāṇi divyāny ābharaṇāni ca
c mokājināni divyāni tasmai te pradaduḥ karam
a evaṃ sa puruṣavyāghro vijigye diśam uttarām
b sudarśanadvīpam idaṃ kārtsnyena bharatarṣabhaḥ
c saṃgrāmān subahūn kṛtvā kṣatriyair dasyubhis tathā
a sa vinirjitya rājñas tān kare ca viniveśya ha
c dhanāny ādāya sarvebhyo ratnāni vividhāni ca
a hayāṃs tittirikalmāṣāñ śukapatranibhān api
c mayūrasadṛśāṃś cānyān sarvān anilaraṃhasaḥ
a vṛtaḥ sumahatā rājan balena caturaṅgiṇā
c ājagāma punar vīraḥ śakraprasthaṃ purottamam
d dharmarājāya tat pārtho dhanaṃ sarvaṃ savāhanam
d nyavedayad anujñātas tena rājñā gṛhān yayau
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etasminn eva kāle tu bhīmaseno 'pi vīryavān
c dharmarājam anujñāpya yayau prācīṃ diśaṃ prati
a mahatā balacakreṇa pararāṣṭrāvamardinā
b hastyaśvarathapūrṇena daṃśitena pratāpavān
c vṛto bharataśārdūlo dviṣacchokavivardhanaḥ
a sa gatvā rājaśārdūlaḥ pāñcālānāṃ puraṃ mahat
c pāñcālān vividhopāyaiḥ sāntvayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
d kiṃ cit karaṃ samādāya videhānāṃ puraṃ yayau
a tataḥ sa gaṇḍakīṃ śūro videhāṃś ca nararṣabhaḥ
c vijityālpena kālena daśārṇān agamat prabhuḥ
a tatra dāśārṇako rājā sudharmā lomaharṣaṇam
c kṛtavān karma bhīmena mahad yuddhaṃ nirāyudham
a bhīmasenas tu tad dṛṣṭvā tasya karma paraṃtapaḥ
b balaṃ sarvam avaṣṭabhya paricakrāma maṇḍalam
b pothayitvā puraṃ sarvaṃ suvarmāṇaṃ tato 'jayat
c adhisenāpatiṃ cakre sudharmāṇaṃ mahābalam
a tataḥ prācīṃ diśaṃ bhīmo yayau bhīmaparākramaḥ
c sainyena mahatā rājan kampayann iva medinīm
a so 'śvamedheśvaraṃ rājan rocamānaṃ sahānujam
c jigāya samare vīro balena balināṃ varaḥ
a sa taṃ nirjitya kaunteyo nātitīvreṇa karmaṇā
c pūrvadeśaṃ mahāvīryo vijigye kurunandanaḥ
a tato dakṣiṇam āgamya pulindanagaraṃ mahat
c sukumāraṃ vaśe cakre sumitraṃ ca narādhipam
a tatas tu dharmarājasya śāsanād bharatarṣabhaḥ
c śiśupālaṃ mahāvīryam abhyayāj janamejaya
a cedirājo 'pi tac chrutvā pāṇḍavasya cikīrṣitam
c upaniṣkramya nagarāt pratyagṛhṇāt paraṃtapaḥ
a tau sametya mahārāja kurucedivṛṣau tadā
c ubhayor ātmakulayoḥ kauśalyaṃ paryapṛcchatām
a tato nivedya tad rāṣṭraṃ cedirājo viśāṃ pate
c uvāca bhīmaṃ prahasan kim idaṃ kuruṣe 'nagha
a tasya bhīmas tadācakhyau dharmarājacikīrṣitam
c sa ca tat pratigṛhyaiva tathā cakre narādhipaḥ
a tato bhīmas tatra rājann uṣitvā tridaśāḥ kṣapāḥ
c satkṛtaḥ śiśupālena yayau sabalavāhanaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ kumāraviṣaye śreṇimantam athājayat
c kosalādhipatiṃ caiva bṛhadbalam ariṃdamaḥ
a ayodhyāyāṃ tu dharmajñaṃ dīrghaprajñaṃ mahābalam
c ajayat pāṇḍavaśreṣṭho nātitīvreṇa karmaṇā
a tato gopālakacchaṃ ca sottamān api cottarān
c mallānām adhipaṃ caiva pārthivaṃ vyajayat prabhuḥ
a tato himavataḥ pārśve samabhyetya jaradgavam
c sarvam alpena kālena deśaṃ cakre vaśe balī
a evaṃ bahuvidhān deśān vijitya puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c unnāṭam abhito jigye kukṣimantaṃ ca parvatam
e pāṇḍavaḥ sumahāvīryo balena balināṃ varaḥ
a sa kāśirājaṃ samare subandhum anivartinam
c vaśe cakre mahābāhur bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
a tataḥ supārśvam abhitas tathā rājapatiṃ kratham
c yudhyamānaṃ balāt saṃkhye vijigye pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
a tato matsyān mahātejā malayāṃś ca mahābalān
c anavadyān gayāṃś caiva paśubhūmiṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a nivṛtya ca mahābāhur madarvīkaṃ mahīdharam
c sopadeśaṃ vinirjitya prayayāv uttarāmukhaḥ
e vatsabhūmiṃ ca kaunteyo vijigye balavān balāt
a bhargāṇām adhipaṃ caiva niṣādādhipatiṃ tathā
c vijigye bhūmipālāṃś ca maṇimatpramukhān bahūn
a tato dakṣiṇamallāṃś ca bhogavantaṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c tarasaivājayad bhīmo nātitīvreṇa karmaṇā
a śarmakān varmakāṃś caiva sāntvenaivājayat prabhuḥ
c vaidehakaṃ ca rājānaṃ janakaṃ jagatīpatim
e vijigye puruṣavyāghro nātitīvreṇa karmaṇā
f śakāṃś ca barbarāṃś caiva ajayac chadmapūrvakam
a vaidehasthas tu kaunteya indraparvatam antikāt
c kirātānām adhipatīn vyajayat sapta pāṇḍavaḥ
a tataḥ suhmān prācyasuhmān samakṣāṃś caiva vīryavān
c vijitya yudhi kaunteyo māgadhān upayād balī
a daṇḍaṃ ca daṇḍadhāraṃ ca vijitya pṛthivīpatīn
c tair eva sahitaḥ sarvair girivrajam upādravat
a jārāsaṃdhiṃ sāntvayitvā kare ca viniveśya ha
c tair eva sahito rājan karṇam abhyadravad balī
a sa kampayann iva mahīṃ balena caturaṅgiṇā
c yuyudhe pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaḥ karṇenāmitraghātinā
d tair eva sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ karṇaṃ cāpy ajayat prabhuḥ
d śiśupālena sahitas taṃ vinirjitya pāṇḍavaḥ
a sa karṇaṃ yudhi nirjitya vaśe kṛtvā ca bhārata
c tato vijigye balavān rājñaḥ parvatavāsinaḥ
a atha modāgiriṃ caiva rājānaṃ balavattaram
c pāṇḍavo bāhuvīryeṇa nijaghāna mahāmṛdhe
a tataḥ pauṇḍrādhipaṃ vīraṃ vāsudevaṃ mahābalam
b idānīṃ vṛṣṇivīryeṇa na yotsyāmīti pauṇḍrakaḥ
b kṛṣṇasya bhujasaṃtrāsāt karam āśu dadau nṛpaḥ
c kauśikīkacchanilayaṃ rājānaṃ ca mahaujasam
a ubhau balavṛtau vīrāv ubhau tīvraparākramau
c nirjityājau mahārāja vaṅgarājam upādravat
a samudrasenaṃ nirjitya candrasenaṃ ca pārthivam
c tāmraliptaṃ ca rājānaṃ kācaṃ vaṅgādhipaṃ tathā
d aṅgānām adhipaṃ caiva kāliṅgānām atheśvaram
a suhmānām adhipaṃ caiva ye ca sāgaravāsinaḥ
c sarvān mlecchagaṇāṃś caiva vijigye bharatarṣabhaḥ
d kirātān puruṣādāṃś ca karṇapravaraṇān api
d ye ca kākamukhā nāma nararākṣasayonayaḥ
d kirātāṃs tṛṇamūlāṃś ca kirātān oṣṭhakarṇikān
a evaṃ bahuvidhān deśān vijitya pavanātmajaḥ
c vasu tebhya upādāya lauhityam agamad balī
a sa sarvān mlecchanṛpatīn sāgaradvīpavāsinaḥ
c karam āhārayām āsa ratnāni vividhāni ca
a candanāguruvastrāṇi maṇimuktam anuttamam
c kāñcanaṃ rajataṃ vajraṃ vidrumaṃ ca mahādhanam
a sa koṭiśatasaṃkhyena dhanena mahatā tadā
c abhyavarṣad ameyātmā dhanavarṣeṇa pāṇḍavam
a indraprastham athāgamya bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
c nivedayām āsa tadā dharmarājāya tad dhanam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathaiva sahadevo 'pi dharmarājena pūjitaḥ
c mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ prayayau dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
a sa śūrasenān kārtsnyena pūrvam evājayat prabhuḥ
c matsyarājaṃ ca kauravyo vaśe cakre balād balī
a adhirājādhipaṃ caiva dantavakraṃ mahāhave
c jigāya karadaṃ caiva svarājye saṃnyaveśayat
a sukumāraṃ vaśe cakre sumitraṃ ca narādhipam
c tathaivāparamatsyāṃś ca vyajayat sa paṭaccarān
c śreṇim antam atho jitvā gośṛṅge 'tha paṭaccarān
a niṣādabhūmiṃ gośṛṅgaṃ parvatapravaraṃ tathā
c tarasā vyajayad dhīmāñ śreṇimantaṃ ca pārthivam
a navarāṣṭraṃ vinirjitya kuntibhojam upādravat
c prītipūrvaṃ ca tasyāsau pratijagrāha śāsanam
a tataś carmaṇvatīkūle jambhakasyātmajaṃ nṛpam
c dadarśa vāsudevena śeṣitaṃ pūrvavairiṇā
a cakre tatra sa saṃgrāmaṃ saha bhojena bhārata
c sa tam ājau vinirjitya dakṣiṇābhimukho yayau
d bhagadattaṃ mahābāhuḥ kṣatriyaṃ narakātmajam
d arjunāya karaṃ dattaṃ śrutvā tatra nyavartata
d sekān aparasekāṃś ca vyajayat sumahābalaḥ
a karāṃs tebhya upādāya ratnāni vividhāni ca
c tatas tair eva sahito narmadām abhito yayau
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau sainyena mahatā vṛtau
c jigāya samare vīrāv āśvineyaḥ pratāpavān
d tato ratnāny upādāya puraṃ bhojakaṭaṃ yayau
d tatra yuddham abhūd rājan divasadvayam acyuta
d sa vijitya durādharṣaṃ bhīṣmakaṃ mādrinandanaḥ
d kośalādhipatiṃ caiva tathā veṇātaṭādhipam
d kāntārakāṃś ca samare tathā prākoṭakān nṛpān
d nāṭakeyāṃś ca samare tathā herambakān yudhi
d mārudhaṃ ca vinirjitya ramyagrāmam atho balāt
d nācīnān arbukāṃś caiva rājānaś ca sahasraśaḥ
d tāṃs tān āṭavikān sarvān ajayat pāṇḍunandanaḥ
d vātādhipaṃ ca nṛpatiṃ vaśe cakre mahābalaḥ
d pulindāṃś ca raṇe jitvā yayau dakṣiṇataḥ punaḥ
d yuyudhe pāṇḍyarājena divasaṃ nakulānujaḥ
d taṃ jitvā sa mahābāhuḥ prayayau dakṣiṇāpatham
d guhām āsādayām āsa kiṣkindhāṃ lokaviśrutām
d tatra vānararājābhyāṃ maindena dvividena ca
d yuyudhe divasān sapta na ca tau vikṛtiṃ gatau
d tatas tuṣṭau mahātmānau sahadevāya vānarau
d ūcatuś caiva saṃhṛṣṭau prītipūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
d gaccha pāṇḍavaśārdūla ratnāny ādāya sarvaśaḥ
d avighnam astu kāryāya dharmarājāya dhīmate
a tato ratnāny upādāya purīṃ māhiṣmatīṃ yayau
c tatra nīlena rājñā sa cakre yuddhaṃ nararṣabhaḥ
a pāṇḍavaḥ paravīraghnaḥ sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
c tato 'sya sumahad yuddham āsīd bhīrubhayaṃkaram
a sainyakṣayakaraṃ caiva prāṇānāṃ saṃśayāya ca
c cakre tasya hi sāhāyyaṃ bhagavān havyavāhanaḥ
d cakre bhārataśārdūla bahurūpatvam āsthitaḥ
a tato hayā rathā nāgāḥ puruṣāḥ kavacāni ca
c pradīptāni vyadṛśyanta sahadevabale tadā
a tataḥ susaṃbhrāntamanā babhūva kurunandanaḥ
c nottaraṃ prativaktuṃ ca śakto 'bhūj janamejaya
 janamejaya uvāca
a kimarthaṃ bhagavān agniḥ pratyamitro 'bhavad yudhi
c sahadevasya yajñārthaṃ ghaṭamānasya vai dvija
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tatra māhiṣmatīvāsī bhagavān havyavāhanaḥ
c śrūyate nigṛhīto vai purastāt pāradārikaḥ
d nīlasya rājño duhitā babhūvātīva śobhanā
d sāgnihotram upātiṣṭhad bodhanāya pituḥ sadā
d vyajanair dhūyamāno 'pi tāvat prajvalate na saḥ
d yāvac cārupuṭauṣṭhena vāyunā na vidhūyate
d tataḥ sa bhagavān agniś cakame tāṃ sudarśanām
a nīlasya rājñaḥ pūrveṣām upanītaś ca so 'bhavat
c tadā brāhmaṇarūpeṇa caramāṇo yadṛcchayā
d cakame tāṃ varārohāṃ kanyām utpalalocanām
a taṃ tu rājā yathāśāstram anvaśād dhārmikas tadā
c prajajvāla tataḥ kopād bhagavān havyavāhanaḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismito rājā jagāma śirasā kavim
b tataḥ kālena tāṃ kanyāṃ tathaiva hi tadā nṛpaḥ
b pradadau viprarūpāya vahnaye śirasā nataḥ
b pratigṛhya ca tāṃ subhrūṃ nīlarājñaḥ sutāṃ tadā
c cakre prasādaṃ ca tadā tasya rājño vibhāvasuḥ
a vareṇa chandayām āsa taṃ nṛpaṃ sviṣṭakṛttamaḥ
c abhayaṃ ca sa jagrāha svasainye vai mahīpatiḥ
a tataḥ prabhṛti ye ke cid ajñānāt tāṃ purīṃ nṛpāḥ
c jigīṣanti balād rājaṃs te dahyantīha vahninā
a tasyāṃ puryāṃ tadā caiva māhiṣmatyāṃ kurūdvaha
c babhūvur anabhigrāhyā yoṣitaś chandataḥ kila
a evam agnir varaṃ prādāt strīṇām aprativāraṇe
c svairiṇyas tatra nāryo hi yatheṣṭaṃ pracaranty uta
a varjayanti ca rājānas tad rāṣṭraṃ puruṣottama
c bhayād agner mahārāja tadā prabhṛti sarvadā
a sahadevas tu dharmātmā sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayārditam
c parītam agninā rājann ākampata yathā giriḥ
a upaspṛśya śucir bhūtvā so 'bravīt pāvakaṃ tataḥ
c tvadartho 'yaṃ samārambhaḥ kṛṣṇavartman namo 'stu te
a mukhaṃ tvam asi devānāṃ yajñas tvam asi pāvaka
c pāvanāt pāvakaś cāsi vahanād dhavyavāhanaḥ
a vedās tvadarthaṃ jātāś ca jātavedās tato hy asi
b citrabhānuḥ sureśaś ca analas tvaṃ vibhāvasuḥ
b agnir duḥsparśanaś cāsi hutāśo jvalanaḥ śikhī
b vaiśvānaras tvaṃ piṅgeśa bhūritejāḥ plavaṃgamaḥ
b kumārasūnur bhagavān rukmagarbho hiraṇyakṛt
b citrabhānuḥ sureśaś ca analas tvaṃ vibhāvaso
b svargadvāraspṛśaś cāsi hutāśo jvalanaḥ śikhī
b vaiśvānaras tvaṃ piṅgeśaḥ plavaṃgo bhūritejasaḥ
b kumārasūs tvaṃ bhagavān rudradharmo hiraṇyakṛt
b agnir dadātu me tejo vāyuḥ prāṇaṃ dadātu me
b pṛthivī balam ādadhyāc chivaṃ cāpo diśantu me
b apāṃ garbha mahāsattva jātavedaḥ sureśvara
b devānāṃ mukham agne tvaṃ satyena vipunīhi mām
b ṛṣibhir brāhmaṇaiś caiva daivatair asurair api
b nityaṃ suhuta yajñeṣu satyena vipunīhi mām
b dhūmaketuḥ śikhī ca tvaṃ pāpahānilasaṃbhavaḥ
b sarvaprāṇiṣu nityasthaḥ satyena vipunīhi mām
b evaṃ stuto 'si bhagavan prītena śucinā mayā
b vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
b tuṣṭiṃ puṣṭiṃ smṛtiṃ caiva prītiṃ cāgne prayaccha me
b ity evaṃ mantram āgneyaṃ paṭhan yo juhuyād vibhum
b ṛddhimān satataṃ dāntaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
c yajñavighnam imaṃ kartuṃ nārhas tvaṃ havyavāhana
a evam uktvā tu mādreyaḥ kuśair āstīrya medinīm
c vidhivat puruṣavyāghraḥ pāvakaṃ pratyupāviśat
a pramukhe sarvasainyasya bhītodvignasya bhārata
c na cainam atyagād vahnir velām iva mahodadhiḥ
a tam abhyetya śanair vahnir uvāca kurunandanam
c sahadevaṃ nṛṇāṃ devaṃ sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
a uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha kauravya jijñāseyaṃ kṛtā mayā
b devadevasya kṛṣṇasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ
b bhujam āśritya yajñaṃ taṃ cikīrṣuṃ pāṇḍunandanam
b jānāmi sahadevādya kṛtārtho yāhi sāṃpratam
c vedmi sarvam abhiprāyaṃ tava dharmasutasya ca
a mayā tu rakṣitavyeyaṃ purī bharatasattama
c yāvad rājño 'sya nīlasya kulavaṃśadharā iti
e īpsitaṃ tu kariṣyāmi manasas tava pāṇḍava
a tata utthāya hṛṣṭātmā prāñjaliḥ śirasānataḥ
c pūjayām āsa mādreyaḥ pāvakaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a pāvake vinivṛtte tu nīlo rājābhyayāt tadā
b pāvakasyājñayā cainam arcayām āsa pārthivaḥ
c satkāreṇa naravyāghraṃ sahadevaṃ yudhāṃ patim
a pratigṛhya ca tāṃ pūjāṃ kare ca viniveśya tam
c mādrīsutas tataḥ prāyād vijayī dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
a traipuraṃ sa vaśe kṛtvā rājānam amitaujasam
c nijagrāha mahābāhus tarasā potaneśvaram
a āhṛtiṃ kauśikācāryaṃ yatnena mahatā tataḥ
c vaśe cakre mahābāhuḥ surāṣṭrādhipatiṃ tathā
a surāṣṭraviṣayasthaś ca preṣayām āsa rukmiṇe
c rājñe bhojakaṭasthāya mahāmātrāya dhīmate
a bhīṣmakāya sa dharmātmā sākṣād indrasakhāya vai
c sa cāsya sasuto rājan pratijagrāha śāsanam
a prītipūrvaṃ mahābāhur vāsudevam avekṣya ca
c tataḥ sa ratnāny ādāya punaḥ prāyād yudhāṃ patiḥ
a tataḥ śūrpārakaṃ caiva gaṇaṃ copakṛtāhvayam
c vaśe cakre mahātejā daṇḍakāṃś ca mahābalaḥ
a sāgaradvīpavāsāṃś ca nṛpatīn mlecchayonijān
c niṣādān puruṣādāṃś ca karṇaprāvaraṇān api
d niṣādān ajayat tatra sāgaramlecchayonijān
a ye ca kālamukhā nāma narā rākṣasayonayaḥ
b ye caikapādā manujā vṛkṣakoṭaraśāyinaḥ
c kṛtsnaṃ kollagiriṃ caiva muracīpattanaṃ tathā
a dvīpaṃ tāmrāhvayaṃ caiva parvataṃ rāmakaṃ tathā
c timiṃgilaṃ ca nṛpatiṃ vaśe cakre mahāmatiḥ
a ekapādāṃś ca puruṣān kevalān vanavāsinaḥ
c nagarīṃ saṃjayantīṃ ca picchaṇḍaṃ karahāṭakam
e dūtair eva vaśe cakre karaṃ cainān adāpayat
f bhṛgukacchaṃ gato dhīmān daṇḍenāmitrakarśanaḥ
f barbarān pāraśān anyān dvīpavāsān vaśe vaśī
f tūlakān daradāṃś cānyān sindhurān vanavāsinaḥ
f aśmakān mūlakāṃś caiva vidarbhāṃś ca mahābalān
f dūtair eva vaśe cakre kare ca viniveśya saḥ
f tataḥ kusṛtivītajñān dakṣiṇāpathavāsinaḥ
f ajayat saṃyuge tatra dharmamārgeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ
a pāṇḍyāṃś ca draviḍāṃś caiva sahitāṃś coḍrakeralaiḥ
b siṃhaladvīpakān anyān dūtaiś cakre vaśe balāt
b ghaṭotkacaṃ mahābāhuṃ rākṣasaṃ ghoradarśanam
b āgamyatām iti prāha dharmarājasya śāsanāt
b sarvasvaṃ karam ādāya tair eva sahito nṛpaḥ
b uttaraṃ tīram āsādya sāgarasyormimālinaḥ
b sa rākṣasaparīvāras taṃ praṇamyāśu saṃsthitaḥ
c andhrāṃs talavanāṃś caiva kaliṅgān oṣṭrakarṇikān
a antākhīṃ caiva romāṃ ca yavanānāṃ puraṃ tathā
c dūtair eva vaśe cakre karaṃ cainān adāpayat
d kānanadvīpakāṃś caiva tarasātītya cāhave
d tāmraparṇīṃ tato gatvā kanyātīrtham atītya ca
d dakṣiṇāṃ ca diśaṃ sarvāṃ vijitya kurunandana
d sahadevas tato rājan mantribhiḥ saha tatra vai
d saṃpradhārya mahābāhuḥ sacivair buddhimattaraiḥ
d cintayām āsa kauravyo bhrātṛputraṃ ghaṭotkacam
d tataś cintitamātras tu rākṣasaḥ pratyadṛśyata
d atidīrgho mahābāhuḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
d abhivādya tato rājan sahadevaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥ
d prahvaḥ kṛtāñjalis tasthau kiṃ kāryam iti cābravīt
d taṃ meruśikharākāram āgataṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
a bharukacchaṃ gato dhīmān dūtān mādravatīsutaḥ
c preṣayām āsa rājendra paulastyāya mahātmane
e vibhīṣaṇāya dharmātmā prītipūrvam ariṃdamaḥ
a sa cāsya pratijagrāha śāsanaṃ prītipūrvakam
c tac ca kālakṛtaṃ dhīmān anvamanyata sa prabhuḥ
d bibhīṣaṇo mahātman yad īpsitaṃ karavāṇy aham
a tataḥ saṃpreṣayām āsa ratnāni vividhāni ca
c candanāgurumukhyāni divyāny ābharaṇāni ca
a vāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi maṇīṃś caiva mahādhanān
b prītimān abhavad dṛṣṭvā ratnaughaṃ taṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
b janamejayaḥ
b icchāmy āgamanaṃ śrotuṃ haiḍimbasya dvijottama
b laṅkāyāṃ ca gatiṃ brahman paulastyasya ca darśanam
b kāverīdarśanaṃ caiva rājānaḥ sarva eva tān
b ānupūrvyāc ca me śaṃsa sarvaṃ brāhmaṇapuṃgava
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b śṛṇu rājan purā vṛttaṃ sahadevasya sāhasam
b kānanadvīpakāṃś caiva tarasā jitya cāhave
b dakṣiṇāṃ ca diśaṃ jitvā colasya viṣayaṃ yayau
b dadarśa puṇyatoyāṃ vai kāverīṃ saritāṃ varām
b nānāpakṣigaṇair juṣṭāṃ tāpasair upaśobhitām
b sālalodhrārjunair bilvair jambūśalmalikiṃśukaiḥ
b kadambaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca kāśmaryāmalakair vṛtām
b nyagrodhaiś ca mahāśākhaiḥ plakṣair audumbarair api
b śamīpalāśavṛkṣaiś ca aśvatthaiḥ khadirair vṛtām
b badarībhiś ca saṃpannām aśvakarṇaiś ca śobhitām
b karañjatintriṇīkaiś ca tālavrātair alaṃkṛtām
b śirīṣaiḥ kuṭajair nimbair madhūkaiḥ kṣīrakair vṛtām
b puṃnāgair bakulaiḥ kundaiś campakaiḥ sarvato vṛtām
b priyaṅgvaśokatilakair atimuktaiś ca śobhitām
b asanaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca nāgavṛkṣair alaṃkṛtām
b ketakībhiḥ kurabakair jātiyūthikakundalaiḥ
b aṅkolaiḥ karavīraiś ca puṃnāgaiḥ pāṭalair vṛtām
b kramukair nālikeraiś ca panasāmraiś ca śobhitām
b cūtaiḥ puṇḍrakapatraiś ca kadalyāḍhakasaṃvṛtām
b nīpaiś ca vetasaiḥ kīrṇāṃ nālakundakuśair vṛtām
b evaṃ bahuvidhair vṛkṣair divyair anyaiś ca śobhitām
b haṃsakāraṇḍavaiḥ kīrṇāṃ kuraraiḥ sārasaiḥ śukaiḥ
b cakravākagaṇair juṣṭāṃ plavaiś ca jalavāyasaiḥ
b samudrakākaiḥ krauñcaiś ca nāditāṃ jalakukkuṭaiḥ
b evaṃ khagaiś ca bahubhiḥ saṃghuṣṭāṃ jalacāribhiḥ
b āśramair bahubhir yuktāṃ caityavṛkṣaiś ca śobhitām
b sevitāṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ śubhrair vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ
b kva cit tīraruhair vṛkṣair mālābhir iva śobhitām
b puṣpagulmalatopetām aṅganām iva bhūṣaṇaiḥ
b kva cit patracitaiḥ padmaiḥ kva cit saugandhikotpalaiḥ
b kahlārakumudaiḥ phullaiḥ kamalair upaśobhitām
b nānāpuṣparajodhvastāṃ pramadām iva bhūṣitām
b ramaṇīyāṃ tathā hṛdyāṃ vihṛtām apsarogaṇaiḥ
b mṛṣṭatīrthām akaluṣāṃ prāṇināṃ jīvanīṃ śubhām
b apārāṃ svādutoyāṃ vai pulinadvīpaśobhitām
b kāverīṃ tādṛśīṃ dṛṣṭvā prītimān pāṇḍavo 'bravīt
b asmadrāṣṭre yathā gaṅgā kāverī ca tathā iha
b sahadevas tu tāṃ tīrtvā nadīm anucaraiḥ saha
b dakṣiṇaṃ tīram āsādya gamanāyopacakrame
b āgataṃ pāṇḍavaṃ tatra śrutvā viṣayavāsinaḥ
b darśanārthaṃ yayus te tu kautūhalasamanvitāḥ
b dramiḷāḥ puruṣā rājan striyaś ca priyadarśanāḥ
b gatvā pāṇḍusutaṃ tatra dadṛśus te mudānvitāḥ
b sukumāraṃ viśālākṣaṃ vrajantaṃ tridaśopamam
b darśanīyatamaṃ loke netrair animiṣair iva
b āścaryabhūtaṃ dadṛśur dramiḷās te samāhitāḥ
b mahāsenopamaṃ dṛṣṭvā pūjāṃ cakruś ca tasya vai
b ratnaiś ca vividhair iṣṭair bhogair anyaiś ca saṃmataiḥ
b gītamaṅgalayuktābhiḥ stuvanto nakulānujam
b sahadevas tu tān dṛṣṭvā dramilān āgatāṃs tadā
b visṛjya tān mahārāja prasthito dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
b dūtena tarasā colaṃ vijitya dramiḷeśvaram
b tato ratnāny upādāya pāṇḍyasya viṣayaṃ yayau
b darśane sahadevasya na ca tṛptā narāḥ pare
b gacchantam anugacchantaḥ prītyā kautūhalānvitāḥ
b tato mādrīsuto rājan mṛgavrātān vyalokayat
b gajān vanacarān anyān vyāghrān kṛṣṇamṛgān bahūn
b śukān mayūrān dṛṣṭvā tu gṛdhrān āraṇyakukkuṭān
b tato deśaṃ samāsādya śvaśurasya mahīpateḥ
b preṣayām āsa mādreyo dūtān pāṇḍyāya vai tadā
b pratijagrāha tasyājñāṃ saṃprītyā malayadhvajaḥ
b bhāryā rūpavatī jiṣṇoḥ pāṇḍyasya tanayā śubhā
b citrāṅgadeti vikhyātā dramilā yoṣitāṃ varā
b āgataṃ sahadevaṃ tu sā śrutvāntaḥpure pituḥ
b preṣayām āsa saṃprītyā pūjāṃ ratnāni vai bahu
b pāṇḍyo 'pi bahuratnāni dūtaiḥ saha mumoca ha
b maṇimuktāpravālāṃś ca śaṅkhaśuktiyutān bahūn
b tāṃ dṛṣṭvā prītimān pūjāṃ pāṇḍavo 'tha mudā nṛpa
b bhrātuḥ putre bahūn ratnān adadād babhruvāhane
b pāṇḍyaṃ dramiḷarājānaṃ śvaśuraṃ malayadhvajam
b sa dūtais taṃ vaśe kṛtvā maṇalūreśvaraṃ tadā
b tato ratnāny upādāya dramiḷair āvṛto yayau
b agastyasyālayaṃ divyaṃ devalokasamaṃ girim
b sa taṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā malayaṃ bharatarṣabha
b laṅghayitvā tu mādreyas tāmraparṇīṃ nadīṃ śubhām
b prasannasalilāṃ divyāṃ suśītāṃ candanodvahām
b samudratīram āsādya nyaviśat pāṇḍunandanaḥ
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b sahadevas tato rājan mantribhiḥ saha bhārata
b saṃpradhārya mahābāhuḥ sacivair buddhimattaraiḥ
b anumānya sa tāṃ rājan sahadevas tvarānvitaḥ
b cintayām āsa rājendra bhrātuḥ putraṃ ghaṭotkacam
b tataś cintitamātre tu rākṣasaḥ pratyadṛśyata
b atidīrgho mahākāyaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
b nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśas taptakāñcanakuṇḍalaḥ
b vicitrahārakeyūraḥ kiṅkiṇīmaṇibhūṣitaḥ
b hemamālī mahādaṃṣṭraḥ kirīṭī kukṣibandhanaḥ
b tāmrakeśo hariśmaśrur bhīmākṣaḥ kanakāṅgadaḥ
b raktacandanadigdhāṅgaḥ sūkṣmāmbaradharo balī
b javena sa yayau tatra cālayann iva medinīm
b tato dṛṣṭvā janā rājann āyāntaṃ parvatopamam
b bhayād dhi dudruvuḥ sarve siṃhāt kṣudramṛgā yathā
b āsasāda ca mādreyaṃ pulastyaṃ rāvaṇo yathā
b abhivādya tato rājan sahadevaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥ
b prahvaḥ kṛtāñjalis tasthau kiṃ kāryam iti cābravīt
b taṃ meruśikharākāram āgataṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
b taṃ pariṣvajya bāhubhyāṃ mūrdhny upāghrāya cāsakṛt
b sahadevaḥ
b pūjayitvā sahāmātyaḥ prīto vākyam uvāca ha
b gaccha laṅkāṃ purīṃ vatsa karārthaṃ mama śāsanāt
b tatra dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ rākṣasendraṃ vibhīṣaṇam
b ratnāni rājasūyārthaṃ vividhāni bahūni ca
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b upādāya ca sarvāṇi pratyāgaccha mahābala
b pāṇḍavenaivam uktas tu mudā yukto ghaṭotkacaḥ
b tathety uktvā mahārāja pratasthe dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
b yayau pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā sahadevaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥ
b laṅkām abhimukho rājan samudram avalokayat
b kūrmagrāhajhaṣākīrṇaṃ mīnair nakrais tathākulam
b śuktivrātaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ śaṅkhānāṃ nicayākulam
b sa dṛṣṭvā rāmasetuṃ ca cintayan rāmavikramam
b praṇamya tam atikramya yāmyāṃ velām alokayat
b gatvā pāraṃ samudrasya dakṣiṇaṃ sa ghaṭotkacaḥ
b dadarśa laṅkāṃ rājendra nākapṛṣṭhopamāṃ śubhām
b prākāreṇāvṛtāṃ ramyāṃ śubhadvāraiś ca śobhitām
b prāsādair bahusāhasraiḥ śvetaraktaiś ca saṃkulām
b tāpanīyagavākṣeṇa muktājālāntarāṇi ca
b haimarājatajālena dāntajālaiś ca śobhitām
b harmyagopurasaṃbādhāṃ rukmatoraṇasaṃkulām
b divyadundubhinirhrādām udyānavanaśobhitām
b sarvakālaphalair vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpitair upaśobhitām
b puṣpagandhaiś ca saṃkīrṇāṃ ramaṇīyamahāpathām
b nānāratnaiś ca saṃpūrṇām indrasyevāmarāvatīm
b viveśa sa purīṃ laṅkāṃ rākṣasaiś ca niṣevitām
b dadarśa rākṣasavrātāñ śūlaprāsadharān bahūn
b nānāveṣadharān dakṣān nārīś ca priyadarśanāḥ
b divyamālyāmbaradharā divyabhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥ
b madaraktāntanayanāḥ pīnaśroṇipayodharāḥ
b bhaimaseniṃ tato dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭās te vismayaṃ gatāḥ
b āsasāda gṛhaṃ rājña indrasya sadanopamam
b ghaṭotkacaḥ
b sa dvārapālam āsādya vākyam etad uvāca ha
b kurūṇām ṛṣabho rājā pāṇḍur nāma mahābalaḥ
b kanīyāṃs tasya dāyādaḥ sahadeva iti śrutaḥ
b kṛṣṇamitrasya tu guro rājasūyārtham udyataḥ
b tenāhaṃ preṣito dūtaḥ karārthaṃ kauravasya ca
b draṣṭum icchāmi rājendraṃ tvaṃ kṣipraṃ māṃ nivedaya
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā dvārapālo mahīpateḥ
b tathety uktvā viveśātha bhavanaṃ sa nivedakaḥ
b sāñjaliḥ sa samācaṣṭa sarvāṃ dūtagiraṃ tadā
b dvārapālavacaḥ śrutvā rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
b uvāca vākyaṃ dharmātmā samīpaṃ me praveśyatām
b evam uktas tu rājendra dharmajñena mahātmanā
b atha niṣkramya saṃbhrānto dvāḥstho haiḍimbam abravīt
b ehi dūta nṛpaṃ draṣṭuṃ kṣipraṃ praviśa ca svayam
b dvārapālavacaḥ śrutvā praviveśa ghaṭotkacaḥ
b sa praviśya dadarśātha rākṣasendrasya mandiram
b tataḥ kailāsasaṃkāśaṃ taptakāñcanatoraṇam
b prākāreṇa parikṣiptaṃ gopuraiś cāpi śobhitam
b harmyaprāsādasaṃbādhaṃ nānāratnasamanvitam
b kāñcanais tāpanīyaiś ca sphāṭikai rājatair api
b vajravaiḍūryagarbhaiś ca stambhair dṛṣṭimanoharaiḥ
b nānādhvajapatākābhir yuktaṃ maṇivicitritam
b citramālyāvṛtaṃ ramyaṃ taptakāñcanavedikam
b tān dṛṣṭvā tatra sarvān sa bhaimasenir manoramān
b praviśann eva haiḍimbaḥ śuśrāva muravasvanam
b tantrīgītasamākīrṇaṃ samatālamitākṣaram
b divyadundubhinirhrādaṃ vāditraśatasaṃkulam
b sa śrutvā madhuraṃ śabdaṃ prītimān abhavat tadā
b tato vigāhya haiḍimbo bahukakṣyāṃ manoramām
b sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ dvāḥsthena saha bhārata
b taṃ vibhīṣaṇam āsīnaṃ kāñcane paramāsane
b divye bhāskarasaṃkāśe muktāmaṇivibhūṣite
b divyābharaṇacitrāṅgaṃ divyarūpadharaṃ vibhum
b divyamālyāmbaradharaṃ divyagandhokṣitaṃ śubham
b vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā sūryavaiśvānaraprabham
b upopaviṣṭaṃ sacivair devair iva śatakratum
b yakṣair mahārathair divyair nārībhiḥ priyadarśanaiḥ
b gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhiḥ pūjyamānaṃ yathāvidhi
b cāmare vyajane cāgrye hemadaṇḍe mahādhane
b gṛhīte varanārībhyāṃ dhūyamāne ca mūrdhani
b arciṣmantaṃ śriyā juṣṭaṃ kuberavaruṇopamam
b dharme caiva sthitaṃ nityam adbhutaṃ rākṣaseśvaram
b dṛṣṭvā ghaṭotkaco rājan vavande taṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
b prahvas tasthau mahāvīryaḥ śakraṃ citraratho yathā
b taṃ dūtam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
b vibhīṣaṇaḥ
b pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ sāntvapūrvaṃ vaco 'bravīt
b kasya vaṃśe nu saṃjātaḥ karam icchan mahīpatiḥ
b tasyānujān samastāṃś ca puraṃ deśaṃ ca tasya vai
b tvāṃ ca kāryaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b vistareṇa mama brūhi sarvān etān pṛthak pṛthak
b evam uktas tu haiḍimbaḥ paulastyena mahātmanā
b ghaṭotkacaḥ
b kṛtāñjalir uvācātha sāntvayan rākṣasādhipam
b somasya vaṃśe rājāsīt pāṇḍur nāma mahābalaḥ
b pāṇḍoḥ putrāś ca pañcāsañ śakratulyaparākramāḥ
b teṣāṃ jyeṣṭhas tu nāmnābhūd dharmaputra iti śrutaḥ
b ajātaśatrur dharmātmā dharmo vigrahavān iva
b tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā prāpya rājyam akārayat
b gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe tīre nagare nāgasāhvaye
b tad datvā dhṛtarāṣṭrāya śakraprasthaṃ yayau tataḥ
b bhrātṛbhiḥ saha rājendra śakraprasthe pramodate
b gaṅgāyamunayor madhye tāv ubhau nagarottamau
b nityaṃ dharme sthito rājā śakraprasthe praśāsati
b tasyānujo mahābāhur bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
b mahātejā mahāvīryaḥ siṃhatulyaḥ sa pāṇḍavaḥ
b daśanāgasahasrāṇāṃ bale tulyaḥ sa pāṇḍavaḥ
b tasyānujo 'rjuno nāma mahāvīryaparākramaḥ
b sukumāro mahāsattvo loke vīryeṇa viśrutaḥ
b kārtavīryasamo vīrye sāgarapratimo bale
b jāmadagnyasamo hy astre saṃkhye rāmasamo 'rjunaḥ
b rūpe śakrasamaḥ pārthas tejasā bhāskaropamaḥ
b devadānavagandharvaiḥ piśācoragarākṣasaiḥ
b mānuṣaiś ca samastaiś ca ajeyaḥ phalguno raṇe
b tena tat khāṇḍavaṃ dāvaṃ tarpitaṃ jātavedase
b tarasā tarpayitvā taṃ śakraṃ devagaṇaiḥ saha
b labdhāny astrāṇi divyāni tarpayitvā hutāśanam
b tena labdhā mahārāja durlabhā daivatair api
b vāsudevasya bhaginī subhadrā nāma viśrutā
b arjunasyānujo rājan nakulaś ceti viśrutaḥ
b darśanīyatamo loke mūrtimān iva manmathaḥ
b tasyānujo mahātejāḥ sahadeva iti śrutaḥ
b tenāhaṃ preṣito rājan sahadevena māriṣa
b ahaṃ ghaṭotkaco nāma bhīmasenasuto balī
b mama mātā mahābhāgā hiḍimbā nāma rākṣasī
b pārthānām upakārārthaṃ carāmi pṛthivīm imām
b āsīt pṛthivyāḥ sarvasyā mahīpālo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b rājasūyaṃ kratuśreṣṭham āhartum upacakrame
b saṃdideśa ca sa bhrātṝn karārthaṃ sarvatodiśam
b udīcīm arjunas tūrṇaṃ karārthaṃ samupāyayau
b gatvā śatasahasrāṇi yojanāni mahābalaḥ
b jitvā sarvān nṛpān yuddhe hatvā ca tarasā vaśī
b svargadvāram upāgamya ratnāny ādāya vai bhṛśam
b aśvāṃś ca vividhān divyān sarvān ādāya phalgunaḥ
b dhanaṃ bahuvidhaṃ rājan dharmaputrāya vai dadau
b bhīmaseno hi rājendra jitvā prācīṃ diśaṃ balāt
b vaśe kṛtvā mahīpālān pāṇḍavāya dhanaṃ dadau
b diśaṃ pratīcīṃ nakulaḥ karārthaṃ prayayau tathā
b sahadevo diśaṃ yāmyāṃ jitvā sarvān mahīkṣitaḥ
b māṃ saṃdideśa rājendra karārtham iha satkṛtaḥ
b pārthānāṃ caritaṃ tubhyaṃ saṃkṣepāt samudāhṛtam
b tam avekṣya mahārāja dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
b pāvakaṃ rājasūyaṃ ca bhagavantaṃ hariṃ prabhum
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b etān avekṣya dharmajña karaṃ tvaṃ dātum arhasi
b tena tad bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
b prītimān abhavad rājan dharmātmā sacivaiḥ saha
b sa cāsya pratijagrāha śāsanaṃ prītipūrvakam
b tac ca kālakṛtaṃ dhīmān ity amanyata sa prabhuḥ
b tato dadau vicitrāṇi kambalāni kuthāni ca
b dāntakāñcanaparyaṅkān maṇihemavicitritān
b bhūṣaṇāni vicitrāṇi mahārhāṇi bahūni ca
b pravālāni ca śubhrāṇi maṇīṃś ca vividhān bahūn
b kāñcanāni ca bhāṇḍāni kalaśāni ghaṭāni ca
b rājatāni ca bhāṇḍāni citrāṇi ca bahūni ca
b śastrāṇi rukmacitrāṇi maṇimuktair vicitritān
b yajñasya toraṇe yuktān dadau tālāṃś caturdaśa
b rukmapaṅkajapuṣpāṇi śibikā maṇibhūṣitāḥ
b mukuṭāni mahārhāṇi hemavarṇāṃś ca kuṇḍalān
b hemapuṣpāṇi vividhān rukmamālyāni cāparān
b śaṅkhāṃś ca candrasaṃkāśāñ śatāvartān vicitriṇaḥ
b candanāni ca mukhyāni rukmaratnāny anekaśaḥ
b vāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi kambalāni bahūny api
b anyāṃś ca vividhān rājan ratnāni ca bahūni ca
b sa dadau sahadevāya tadā rājā vibhīṣaṇaḥ
b vibhīṣaṇaṃ ca rājānam abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ
b pradakṣiṇaṃ parītyaiva nirjagāma ghaṭotkacaḥ
b tāni sarvāṇi ratnāni aṣṭāśītir niśācarāḥ
b ājahruḥ samudā rājan haiḍimbena tadā saha
b ratnāny ādāya sarvāṇi pratasthe sa ghaṭotkacaḥ
b tato ratnāny upādāya haiḍimbo rākṣasaiḥ saha
b jagāma tūrṇaṃ laṅkāyāḥ sahadevapadaṃ prati
b āseduḥ pāṇḍavaṃ sarve laṅghayitvā mahodadhim
b sahadevo dadarśātha ratnāhārān niśācarān
b āgatān bhīmasaṃkāśān haiḍimbaṃ ca tathā nṛpa
b dramilā nairṛtān dṛṣṭvā dudruvus te bhayārditāḥ
b bhaimasenis tato gatvā mādreyaṃ prāñjaliḥ sthitaḥ
b prītimān abhavad dṛṣṭvā ratnaughaṃ taṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
b visṛjya dramilān sarvān gamanāyopacakrame
c nyavartata tato dhīmān sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
a evaṃ nirjitya tarasā sāntvena vijayena ca
c karadān pārthivān kṛtvā pratyāgacchad ariṃdamaḥ
d ratnasāram upādāya yayau saha niśācaraiḥ
d indraprasthaṃ viveśātha kampayann iva medinīm
d dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraṃ rājan sahadevaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
d prahvo 'bhivādya tasthau sa pūjitaś caiva tena vai
d laṅkāprāptān dhanaughāṃś ca dṛṣṭvā tān durlabhān bahūn
d prītimān abhavad rājā vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayau
a dharmarājāya tat sarvaṃ nivedya bharatarṣabha
b koṭīsahasram adhikaṃ hiraṇyasya mahātmanaḥ
b vicitrāṃs tu maṇīn ratnān gojāvimahiṣāṃs tathā
c kṛtakarmā sukhaṃ rājann uvāsa janamejaya
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a nakulasya tu vakṣyāmi karmāṇi vijayaṃ tathā
c vāsudevajitām āśāṃ yathāsau vyajayat prabhuḥ
a niryāya khāṇḍavaprasthāt pratīcīm abhito diśam
c uddiśya matimān prāyān mahatyā senayā saha
a siṃhanādena mahatā yodhānāṃ garjitena ca
c rathanemininādaiś ca kampayan vasudhām imām
a tato bahudhanaṃ ramyaṃ gavāśvadhanadhānyavat
c kārttikeyasya dayitaṃ rohītakam upādravat
a tatra yuddhaṃ mahad vṛttaṃ śūrair mattamayūrakaiḥ
c marubhūmiṃ ca kārtsnyena tathaiva bahudhānyakam
a śairīṣakaṃ mahecchaṃ ca vaśe cakre mahādyutiḥ
b ākrośaṃ caiva rājarṣiṃ tena yuddham abhūn mahat
b tān daśārṇān sa jitvā ca pratasthe pāṇḍunandanaḥ
b liliṭān pāṭanāṃś caiva dūtair eva jigāya tān
c śibīṃs trigartān ambaṣṭhān mālavān pañcakarpaṭān
a tathā madhyamikāyāṃś ca vāṭadhānān dvijān atha
c punaś ca parivṛtyātha puṣkarāraṇyavāsinaḥ
a gaṇān utsavasaṃketān vyajayat puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c sindhukūlāśritā ye ca grāmaṇeyā mahābalāḥ
a śūdrābhīragaṇāś caiva ye cāśritya sarasvatīm
c vartayanti ca ye matsyair ye ca parvatavāsinaḥ
a kṛtsnaṃ pañcanadaṃ caiva tathaivāparaparyaṭam
b ratnākaram amitraghnaṃ tathā vellātaṭaṃ punaḥ
b tathā siṃhanadaṃ caiva tathaivāparapattanān
b dūtair eva vaśe cakre nakulaḥ kulanandanaḥ
c uttarajyotikaṃ caiva tathā vṛndāṭakaṃ puram
e dvārapālaṃ ca tarasā vaśe cakre mahādyutiḥ
a ramaṭhān hārahūṇāṃś ca pratīcyāś caiva ye nṛpāḥ
c tān sarvān sa vaśe cakre śāsanād eva pāṇḍavaḥ
d araṇaṃ caiva romaṃ ca yavanānāṃ purāṇi ca
d lambānudeśajāṃś caiva bandhakāṃś ca narottama
d dūtair eva vaśe cakre karaṃ cainān adāpayat
a tatrasthaḥ preṣayām āsa vāsudevāya cābhibhuḥ
b dūtaṃ dharmavidaṃ śāntaṃ vāgminaṃ śucim uttamam
b sa cāpi yojayām āsa vāsudevāya bhārata
c sa cāsya daśabhī rājyaiḥ pratijagrāha śāsanam
a tataḥ śākalam abhyetya madrāṇāṃ puṭabhedanam
c mātulaṃ prītipūrveṇa śalyaṃ cakre vaśe balī
a sa tasmin satkṛto rājñā satkārārho viśāṃ pate
c ratnāni bhūrīṇy ādāya saṃpratasthe yudhāṃ patiḥ
a tataḥ sāgarakukṣisthān mlecchān paramadāruṇān
c pahlavān barbarāṃś caiva tān sarvān anayad vaśam
a tato ratnāny upādāya vaśe kṛtvā ca pārthivān
c nyavartata naraśreṣṭho nakulaś citramārgavit
a karabhāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi kośaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ

a indraprasthagataṃ vīram abhyetya sa yudhiṣṭhiram

 sarvam ānaya naḥ kṣipraṃ sahadeva yathātatham
 indraseno viśokaś ca rukmaś cārjunasārathiḥ
 annādye vyāpṛtāḥ santu sahadeva tavājñayā
 upārjitān sarvakāmān sugandharasamiśritān
 manoharān prītikarān annādye 'rthe susaṃskṛtān
 samīko dhvajasenaś ca pañcasārathipuṃgavāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pitāmahaṃ guruṃ caiva pratyudgamya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c abhivādya tato rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīt
e bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ drauṇiṃ duryodhanaviviṃśatī
a asmin yajñe bhavanto mām anugṛhṇantu sarvaśaḥ
c idaṃ vaḥ svam ahaṃ caiva yad ihāsti dhanaṃ mama
e prīṇayantu bhavanto māṃ yatheṣṭam aniyantritāḥ
a evam uktvā sa tān sarvān dīkṣitaḥ pāṇḍavāgrajaḥ
c yuyoja ha yathāyogam adhikāreṣv anantaram
a bhakṣyabhojyādhikāreṣu duḥśāsanam ayojayat
a   yuyutsuṃ samayojayat
a paṅktyāropaṇakārye tu ucchiṣṭāpanaye punaḥ
a bhojanāvekṣaṇe caiva
c parigrahe brāhmaṇānām aśvatthāmānam uktavān
a rājñāṃ tu pratipūjārthaṃ saṃjayaṃ saṃnyayojayat
c kṛtākṛtaparijñāne bhīṣmadroṇau mahāmatī
d tatrānvatiṣṭhatāṃ rājā vṛddhau paramasaṃmatau
a hiraṇyasya suvarṇasya ratnānāṃ cānvavekṣaṇe
c dakṣiṇānāṃ ca vai dāne kṛpaṃ rājā nyayojayat
e tathānyān puruṣavyāghrāṃs tasmiṃs tasmin nyayojayat
a bāhliko dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca somadatto jayadrathaḥ
c nakulena samānītāḥ svāmivat tatra remire
a kṣattā vyayakaras tv āsīd viduraḥ sarvadharmavit
c duryodhanas tv arhaṇāni pratijagrāha sarvaśaḥ
d kuntī mādrī ca gāndhārī strīṇāṃ kurvantu cārcanam
d anyāḥ sarvāḥ snuṣās tāsāṃ saṃdeśaṃ yāntu mā ciram
d tiṣṭhet kṛṣṇāntike so 'yam arjunaḥ kāryasiddhaye
d caraṇakṣālane kṛṣṇo brāhmaṇānāṃ svayaṃ hy abhūt
d karṇaḥ kośagṛhādhīśaś cāyavyayasamīkṣakaḥ
a sarvalokaḥ samāvṛttaḥ piprīṣuḥ phalam uttamam
c draṣṭukāmaḥ sabhāṃ caiva dharmarājaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
a na kaś cid āharat tatra sahasrāvaram arhaṇam
c ratnaiś ca bahubhis tatra dharmarājam avardhayan
a kathaṃ nu mama kauravyo ratnadānaiḥ samāpnuyāt
c yajñam ity eva rājānaḥ spardhamānā dadur dhanam
a bhavanaiḥ savimānāgraiḥ sodarkair balasaṃvṛtaiḥ
c lokarājavimānaiś ca brāhmaṇāvasathaiḥ saha
a kṛtair āvasathair divyair vimānapratimais tathā
c vicitrai ratnavadbhiś ca ṛddhyā paramayā yutaiḥ
a rājabhiś ca samāvṛttair atīvaśrīsamṛddhibhiḥ
c aśobhata sado rājan kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥ
a ṛddhyā ca varuṇaṃ devaṃ spardhamāno yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c ṣaḍagninātha yajñena so 'yajad dakṣiṇāvatā
e sarvāñ janān sarvakāmaiḥ samṛddhaiḥ samatarpayat
a annavān bahubhakṣyaś ca bhuktavajjanasaṃvṛtaḥ
c ratnopahārakarmaṇyo babhūva sa samāgamaḥ
a iḍājyahomāhutibhir mantraśikṣāsamanvitaiḥ
c tasmin hi tatṛpur devās tate yajñe maharṣibhiḥ
a yathā devās tathā viprā dakṣiṇānnamahādhanaiḥ
c tatṛpuḥ sarvavarṇāś ca tasmin yajñe mudānvitāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato 'bhiṣecanīye 'hni brāhmaṇā rājabhiḥ saha
c antarvedīṃ praviviśuḥ satkārārthaṃ maharṣayaḥ
a nāradapramukhās tasyām antarvedyāṃ mahātmanaḥ
c samāsīnāḥ śuśubhire saha rājarṣibhis tadā
a sametā brahmabhavane devā devarṣayo yathā
c karmāntaram upāsanto jajalpur amitaujasaḥ
a idam evaṃ na cāpy evam evam etan na cānyathā
c ity ūcur bahavas tatra vitaṇḍānāḥ parasparam
a kṛśān arthāṃs tathā ke cid akṛśāṃs tatra kurvate
c akṛśāṃś ca kṛśāṃś cakrur hetubhiḥ śāstraniścitaiḥ
a tatra medhāvinaḥ ke cid artham anyaiḥ prapūritam
c vicikṣipur yathā śyenā nabhogatam ivāmiṣam
a ke cid dharmārthasaṃyuktāḥ kathās tatra mahāvratāḥ
c remire kathayantaś ca sarvavedavidāṃ varāḥ
a sā vedir vedasaṃpannair devadvijamaharṣibhiḥ
c ābabhāse samākīrṇā nakṣatrair dyaur ivāmalā
a na tasyāṃ saṃnidhau śūdraḥ kaś cid āsīn na cāvrataḥ
c antarvedyāṃ tadā rājan yudhiṣṭhiraniveśane
a tāṃ tu lakṣmīvato lakṣmīṃ tadā yajñavidhānajām
c tutoṣa nāradaḥ paśyan dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
a atha cintāṃ samāpede sa munir manujādhipa
c nāradas taṃ tadā paśyan sarvakṣatrasamāgamam
a sasmāra ca purāvṛttāṃ kathāṃ tāṃ bharatarṣabha
c aṃśāvataraṇe yāsau brahmaṇo bhavane 'bhavat
a devānāṃ saṃgamaṃ taṃ tu vijñāya kurunandana
c nāradaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sasmāra manasā harim
a sākṣāt sa vibudhārighnaḥ kṣatre nārāyaṇo vibhuḥ
c pratijñāṃ pālayan dhīmāñ jātaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a saṃdideśa purā yo 'sau vibudhān bhūtakṛt svayam
c anyonyam abhinighnantaḥ punar lokān avāpsyatha
a iti nārāyaṇaḥ śaṃbhur bhagavāñ jagataḥ prabhuḥ
c ādiśya vibudhān sarvān ajāyata yadukṣaye
a kṣitāv andhakavṛṣṇīnāṃ vaṃśe vaṃśabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c parayā śuśubhe lakṣmyā nakṣatrāṇām ivoḍurāṭ
a yasya bāhubalaṃ sendrāḥ surāḥ sarva upāsate
c so 'yaṃ mānuṣavan nāma harir āste 'rimardanaḥ
a aho bata mahad bhūtaṃ svayaṃbhūr yad idaṃ svayam
c ādāsyati punaḥ kṣatram evaṃ balasamanvitam
a ity etāṃ nāradaś cintāṃ cintayām āsa dharmavit
c hariṃ nārāyaṇaṃ jñātvā yajñair īḍyaṃ tam īśvaram
a tasmin dharmavidāṃ śreṣṭho dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
c mahādhvare mahābuddhis tasthau sa bahumānataḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tataḥ samuditā mukhyair guṇair guṇavatāṃ varāḥ
d bahavo bhāvitātmānaḥ pṛthak pṛthag ariṃdamāḥ
d ātmakṛtyam iti jñātvā pāñcālās tatra sarvaśaḥ
d samīyur vṛṣṇayaś caiva tadānīkāgrahāriṇaḥ
d sadārāḥ sajanāmātyā vahanto ratnasaṃcayān
d vikṛṣṭatvāc ca deśasya gurubhāratayā ca te
d yayuḥ pramuditāḥ paścād rājabhir na samaṃ yayuḥ
d balaśeṣaṃ samuditaṃ parigṛhya samantataḥ
d rājñāṃ cakrāyudhaḥ śaurir amitragaṇamardanaḥ
d balādhikāre nikṣiptaṃ saṃmānyānakadundubhim
d saṃprāyād yādavaśreṣṭho yajamāne yudhiṣṭhire
d uccāvacam upādāya dharmarājāya mādhavaḥ
d dhanaughaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā khāṇḍavaprastham āyayau
d tatra yajñāgatān sarvāṃś caidyavakrapurogamān
d bhūmipālagaṇān sarvān saprabhān iva toyadān
d meghakāyān niḥśvasato yūthapān iva yūthapaḥ
d balinaḥ siṃhasaṃkāśān mahīm āvṛtya tiṣṭhataḥ
d tato janaughasaṃbādhaṃ rājasāgaram avyayam
d nādayan rathaghoṣeṇābhyupāyān madhusūdanaḥ
d asūryam iva sūryeṇa nivātam iva vāyunā
d kṛṣṇena samupetena jaharṣe bhārataṃ puram
d brāhmaṇakṣatriyāṇāṃ hi pūjārthaṃ sarvadharmavit
d sahadevo viśeṣajño mādrīputraḥ kṛto 'bhavat
d prabhavantaṃ tu bhūtānāṃ bhāsvantam iva tejasā
d praviśantaṃ yajñabhūmiṃ sitasyāvarajaṃ vibhum
d tejorāśim ṛṣiṃ vipram adṛśyam avijānatām
d vayodhikānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ mārgam ātmani tiṣṭhatām
d jagatas tasthuṣaś caiva prabhavāpyayam acyutam
d anantam antaṃ śatrūṇām amitragaṇamardanam
d prabhavaṃ sarvabhūtānām āpatsv abhayam acyutam
d bhaviṣyaṃ bhāvanaṃ bhūtaṃ dvāravatyām ariṃdamam
d sa dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam āyāntaṃ pratipūjyāmitaujasam
d yathārhaṃ keśave vṛttiṃ pratyapadyata pāṇḍavaḥ
d jyaiṣṭhyakāniṣṭhyasaṃyogaṃ saṃpradhārya guṇāguṇaiḥ
d ārirādhayiṣur dharmaḥ pūjayitvā dvijottamān
