d mahad ādityasaṃkāśam āsanaṃ ca jagatpateḥ
d dadau nāsāditaṃ kaiś cit tasminn upaviveśa saḥ
a tato bhīṣmo 'bravīd rājan dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c kriyatām arhaṇaṃ rājñāṃ yathārham iti bhārata
a ācāryam ṛtvijaṃ caiva saṃyuktaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
c snātakaṃ ca priyaṃ cāhuḥ ṣaḍ arghyārhān nṛpaṃ tathā
a etān arhān abhigatān āhuḥ saṃvatsaroṣitān
c ta ime kālapūgasya mahato 'smān upāgatāḥ
a eṣām ekaikaśo rājann arghyam ānīyatām iti
c atha caiṣāṃ variṣṭhāya samarthāyopanīyatām
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kasmai bhavān manyate 'rgham ekasmai kurunandana
c upanīyamānaṃ yuktaṃ ca tan me brūhi pitāmaha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo buddhyā niścitya bhārata
c vārṣṇeyaṃ manyate kṛṣṇam arhaṇīyatamaṃ bhuvi
a eṣa hy eṣāṃ sametānāṃ tejobalaparākramaiḥ
c madhye tapann ivābhāti jyotiṣām iva bhāskaraḥ
a asūryam iva sūryeṇa nivātam iva vāyunā
c bhāsitaṃ hlāditaṃ caiva kṛṣṇenedaṃ sado hi naḥ
a tasmai bhīṣmābhyanujñātaḥ sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
c upajahre 'tha vidhivad vārṣṇeyāyārghyam uttamam
d gām arghyaṃ madhuparkaṃ cāpy ānīyāpāharat tadā
d caraṇāv aspṛśac chaureḥ sahadevo viśāṃ pate
d keśavaś cāpy upāghrāya mūrdhni śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d sahadevam athovāca kaccid vaḥ kuśalaṃ gṛhe
d so 'pi taṃ tu tathety āha sarvaṃ nanu tavājñayā
d etasminn antare rājann idam āsīd athādbhutam
d tāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣatriyāḥ sarve pūjāṃ kṛṣṇasya bhūyasīm
d saṃprekṣyānyonyam āsīnā hṛdayais tām adhārayan
a pratijagrāha tat kṛṣṇaḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā
c śiśupālas tu tāṃ pūjāṃ vāsudeve na cakṣame
a sa upālabhya bhīṣmaṃ ca dharmarājaṃ ca saṃsadi
c apākṣipad vāsudevaṃ cedirājo mahābalaḥ
d teṣām ākārabhāvajñaḥ sahadevo na cakṣame
d mānināṃ balināṃ rājñāṃ puraḥ saṃdarśite pade
d puṣpavṛṣṭir mahaty āsīt sahadevasya mūrdhani
d janmaprabhṛti vṛṣṇīnāṃ sunīthaḥ śatrur abravīt
d praṣṭā viyonijo rājā prativaktā nadīsutaḥ
d pratigrahītā gopālaḥ pradātā ca viyonijaḥ
d sadasyā mūkavat sarve āsate 'tra kim ucyate
d ity uktvā sa vihasyāśu pāṇḍavaṃ punar abravīt
d atipaśyasi vā sarvān na vā paśyasi pāṇḍava
d tiṣṭhatsv anyeṣu pūjyeṣu gopam arcitavān asi
d ete caivobhaye tāta kāryasya tu vināśake
d atidṛṣṭir adṛṣṭir vā tayoḥ kiṃ tvaṃ samāsthitaḥ
 śiśupāla uvāca
a nāyam arhati vārṣṇeyas tiṣṭhatsv iha mahātmasu
c mahīpatiṣu kauravya rājavat pārthivārhaṇam
a nāyaṃ yuktaḥ samācāraḥ pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
c yat kāmāt puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ pāṇḍavārcitavān asi
a bālā yūyaṃ na jānīdhvaṃ dharmaḥ sūkṣmo hi pāṇḍavāḥ
c ayaṃ tatrābhyatikrānta āpageyo 'lpadarśanaḥ
a tvādṛśo dharmayukto hi kurvāṇaḥ priyakāmyayā
c bhavaty abhyadhikaṃ bhīṣmo lokeṣv avamataḥ satām
a kathaṃ hy arājā dāśārho madhye sarvamahīkṣitām
c arhaṇām arhati tathā yathā yuṣmābhir arcitaḥ
a atha vā manyase kṛṣṇaṃ sthaviraṃ bharatarṣabha
c vasudeve sthite vṛddhe katham arhati tatsutaḥ
a atha vā vāsudevo 'pi priyakāmo 'nuvṛttavān
c drupade tiṣṭhati kathaṃ mādhavo 'rhati pūjanam
a ācāryaṃ manyase kṛṣṇam atha vā kurupuṃgava
c droṇe tiṣṭhati vārṣṇeyaṃ kasmād arcitavān asi
a ṛtvijaṃ manyase kṛṣṇam atha vā kurunandana
c dvaipāyane sthite vipre kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d bhīṣme śāṃtanave rājan sthite puruṣasattame
d svacchandamṛtyuke rājan kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d aśvatthāmni sthite vīre sarvaśāstraviśārade
d kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayā rājann arcitaḥ kurunandana
d duryodhane ca rājendre sthite puruṣasattame
d kṛpe ca bhāratācārye kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d drumaṃ kiṃpuruṣācāryam atikramya tathārcitaḥ
d bhīṣmake ca durādharṣe pāṇḍye ca kṛtalakṣaṇe
d nṛpe ca rukmiṇi śreṣṭhe ekalavye tathaiva ca
d śalye madrādhipe caiva kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d ayaṃ ca sarvarājñāṃ yo balaślāghī mahārathaḥ
d jāmadagnyasya dayitaḥ śiṣyo viprasya bhārata
d yenātmabalam āśritya rājāno yudhi nirjitāḥ
d taṃ ca karṇam atikramya kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d bhīṣme śāṃtanave rājan sthite puruṣasattame
d svacchandamṛtyuke tasmin kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d kṛpe ca bhāratācārye kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d aśvatthāmni sthite vīre sarvaśastraviśārade
d kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayā rājann arcito yadunandanaḥ
d drume kiṃpuruṣācārye kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d ayaṃ pārthād anavamo dhanurvede parākrame
d ekalavye sthite rājan kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d bhagadatte mahāvīrye jayatsene ca māgadhe
d kāliṅge ca sthite rājan kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d pūrvadeśādhipe vīre kausalendre bṛhadbale
d virāṭe ca sthite vīre kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d bhīṣmake ca durādharṣe pāṇḍye ca kṛtadhanvani
d nṛpe rukmiṇi ca śreṣṭhe dantavakre ca pārthive
d śalye madrādhipe caiva kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d surāṣṭrādhipatau vīre mālave ca sthite nṛpe
d kṛtakṣaṇe ca vaidehe kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d ayaṃ ca sarvarājñāṃ yo balaślāghī mahārathaḥ
d jāmadagnyasya dayitaḥ śiṣyo viprasya bhārata
d yenātmabalam āśritya jarāsaṃdho yudhā jitaḥ
d taṃ karṇaṃ samatikramya kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbhojaṃ ca sudakṣiṇam
d sthite sālve ca rājendre kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
d asmin pārthasakhe rājan gandharvāṇāṃ mahīpatau
d sthite citrarathe vīre kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥ
d bāhlīkaṃ sthaviraṃ vīraṃ kauravāṇāṃ mahāratham
d saumadattiṃ mahāvīryaṃ somadattaṃ mahāratham
d śakuniṃ saubalaṃ caiva sindhurājaṃ mahābalam
d etān avamatān kṛtvā kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
a naiva ṛtviṅ na cācāryo na rājā madhusūdanaḥ
b na snātako na jāmātā kathaṃ kṛṣṇo 'rcitas tvayā
c arcitaś ca kuruśreṣṭha kim anyat priyakāmyayā
a atha vāpy arcanīyo 'yaṃ yuṣmākaṃ madhusūdanaḥ
c kiṃ rājabhir ihānītair avamānāya bhārata
a vayaṃ tu na bhayād asya kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥ
c prayacchāmaḥ karān sarve na lobhān na ca sāntvanāt
a asya dharmapravṛttasya pārthivatvaṃ cikīrṣataḥ
c karān asmai prayacchāmaḥ so 'yam asmān na manyate
a kim anyad avamānād dhi yad imaṃ rājasaṃsadi
c aprāptalakṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇam arghyeṇārcitavān asi
a akasmād dharmaputrasya dharmātmeti yaśo gatam
c ko hi dharmacyute pūjām evaṃ yuktāṃ prayojayet
e yo 'yaṃ vṛṣṇikule jāto rājānaṃ hatavān purā
f jarāsaṃdhaṃ mahātmānam anyāyena durātmavān
a adya dharmātmatā caiva vyapakṛṣṭā yudhiṣṭhirāt
c kṛpaṇatvaṃ niviṣṭaṃ ca kṛṣṇe 'rghyasya nivedanāt
a yadi bhītāś ca kaunteyāḥ kṛpaṇāś ca tapasvinaḥ
b rājñāṃ tu madhye pūjāṃ te kṛtavanto garīyasīm
c nanu tvayāpi boddhavyaṃ yāṃ pūjāṃ mādhavo 'rhati
a atha vā kṛpaṇair etām upanītāṃ janārdana
c pūjām anarhaḥ kasmāt tvam abhyanujñātavān asi
a ayuktām ātmanaḥ pūjāṃ tvaṃ punar bahu manyase
c haviṣaḥ prāpya niṣyandaṃ prāśituṃ śveva nirjane
a na tv ayaṃ pārthivendrāṇām avamānaḥ prayujyate
c tvām eva kuravo vyaktaṃ pralambhante janārdana
a klībe dārakriyā yādṛg andhe vā rūpadarśanam
c arājño rājavat pūjā tathā te madhusūdana
a dṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhiro rājā dṛṣṭo bhīṣmaś ca yādṛśaḥ
c vāsudevo 'py ayaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ sarvam etad yathātatham
a ity uktvā śiśupālas tān utthāya paramāsanāt
c niryayau sadasas tasmāt sahito rājabhis tadā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā śiśupālam upādravat
c uvāca cainaṃ madhuraṃ sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
a nedaṃ yuktaṃ mahīpāla yādṛśaṃ vai tvam uktavān
c adharmaś ca paro rājan pāruṣyaṃ ca nirarthakam
a na hi dharmaṃ paraṃ jātu nāvabudhyeta pārthiva
c bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tv enaṃ māvamaṃsthā ato 'nyathā
a paśya cemān mahīpālāṃs tvatto vṛddhatamān bahūn
c mṛṣyante cārhaṇāṃ kṛṣṇe tadvat tvaṃ kṣantum arhasi
a veda tattvena kṛṣṇaṃ hi bhīṣmaś cedipate bhṛśam
c na hy enaṃ tvaṃ tathā vettha yathainaṃ veda kauravaḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a nāsmā anunayo deyo nāyam arhati sāntvanam
c lokavṛddhatame kṛṣṇe yo 'rhaṇāṃ nānumanyate
a kṣatriyaḥ kṣatriyaṃ jitvā raṇe raṇakṛtāṃ varaḥ
c yo muñcati vaśe kṛtvā gurur bhavati tasya saḥ
a asyāṃ ca samitau rājñām ekam apy ajitaṃ yudhi
c na paśyāmi mahīpālaṃ sātvatīputratejasā
a na hi kevalam asmākam ayam arcyatamo 'cyutaḥ
c trayāṇām api lokānām arcanīyo janārdanaḥ
a kṛṣṇena hi jitā yuddhe bahavaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
c jagat sarvaṃ ca vārṣṇeye nikhilena pratiṣṭhitam
a tasmāt satsv api vṛddheṣu kṛṣṇam arcāma netarān
c evaṃ vaktuṃ na cārhas tvaṃ mā bhūt te buddhir īdṛśī
a jñānavṛddhā mayā rājan bahavaḥ paryupāsitāḥ
b yasya rājan prabhāvajñāḥ purā sarve ca rakṣitāḥ
c teṣāṃ kathayatāṃ śaurer ahaṃ guṇavato guṇān
e samāgatānām aśrauṣaṃ bahūn bahumatān satām
a karmāṇy api ca yāny asya janmaprabhṛti dhīmataḥ
c bahuśaḥ kathyamānāni narair bhūyaḥ śrutāni me
a na kevalaṃ vayaṃ kāmāc cedirāja janārdanam
c na saṃbandhaṃ puraskṛtya kṛtārthaṃ vā kathaṃ cana
a arcāmahe 'rcitaṃ sadbhir bhuvi bhaumasukhāvaham
c yaśaḥ śauryaṃ jayaṃ cāsya vijñāyārcāṃ prayujmahe
a na hi kaś cid ihāsmābhiḥ subālo 'py aparīkṣitaḥ
c guṇair vṛddhān atikramya harir arcyatamo mataḥ
a jñānavṛddho dvijātīnāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ balādhikaḥ
b vaiśyānāṃ dhānyadhanavāñ śūdrāṇām eva janmataḥ
c pūjye tāv iha govinde hetū dvāv api saṃsthitau
a vedavedāṅgavijñānaṃ balaṃ cāpy amitaṃ tathā
c nṛṇāṃ hi loke kasyāsti viśiṣṭaṃ keśavād ṛte
a dānaṃ dākṣyaṃ śrutaṃ śauryaṃ hrīḥ kīrtir buddhir uttamā
c saṃnatiḥ śrīr dhṛtis tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiś ca niyatācyute
a tam imaṃ sarvasaṃpannam ācāryaṃ pitaraṃ gurum
c arcyam arcitam arcārhaṃ sarve saṃmantum arhatha
a ṛtvig gurur vivāhyaś ca snātako nṛpatiḥ priyaḥ
c sarvam etad dhṛṣīkeśe tasmād abhyarcito 'cyutaḥ
a kṛṣṇa eva hi lokānām utpattir api cāpyayaḥ
c kṛṣṇasya hi kṛte bhūtam idaṃ viśvaṃ samarpitam
a eṣa prakṛtir avyaktā kartā caiva sanātanaḥ
c paraś ca sarvabhūtebhyas tasmād vṛddhatamo 'cyutaḥ
a buddhir mano mahān vāyus tejo 'mbhaḥ khaṃ mahī ca yā
c caturvidhaṃ ca yad bhūtaṃ sarvaṃ kṛṣṇe pratiṣṭhitam
a ādityaś candramāś caiva nakṣatrāṇi grahāś ca ye
c diśaś copadiśaś caiva sarvaṃ kṛṣṇe pratiṣṭhitam
d agnihotramukhā vedā gāyatrī chandasāṃ mukham
d rājā mukhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ nadīnāṃ sāgaro mukham
d nakṣatrāṇāṃ mukhaṃ candra ādityas tejasāṃ mukham
d parvatānāṃ mukhaṃ merur garuḍaḥ patatāṃ mukham
d ūrdhvaṃ tiryag adhaś caiva yāvatī jagato gatiḥ
d sadevakeṣu lokeṣu bhagavān keśavo mukham
d eṣa rudraś ca sarvātmā brahmā caiṣa sanātanaḥ
d akṣaraḥ kṣararūpeṇa mānuṣatvam upāgataḥ
a ayaṃ tu puruṣo bālaḥ śiśupālo na budhyate
c sarvatra sarvadā kṛṣṇaṃ tasmād evaṃ prabhāṣate
a yo hi dharmaṃ vicinuyād utkṛṣṭaṃ matimān naraḥ
c sa vai paśyed yathādharmaṃ na tathā cedirāḍ ayam
a savṛddhabāleṣv atha vā pārthiveṣu mahātmasu
c ko nārhaṃ manyate kṛṣṇaṃ ko vāpy enaṃ na pūjayet
a athemāṃ duṣkṛtāṃ pūjāṃ śiśupālo vyavasyati
c duṣkṛtāyāṃ yathānyāyaṃ tathāyaṃ kartum arhati
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d evam ukte tu gāṅgeye śiśupālaś cukopa ha
d sahadevaḥ
d kruddhaṃ sunīthaṃ dṛṣṭvātha sahadevo 'bravīt tadā
d nītipūrvam idaṃ sarvaṃ cedirāja mayā kṛtam
d na me vimatir astīha kāraṇaṃ cātra me śṛṇu
d sa pārthivānāṃ sarveṣāṃ guruḥ kṛṣṇo balena vai
d tasmād abhyarcito 'rghyārhaḥ sarve saṃmantum arhatha
d yo vā na sahate rājñāṃ kaś cit sabalavāhanaḥ
d kṣipraṃ yuddhāya niryātu śaktaś ced atra me yudhi
d tasya mūrdhni susaṃnyastaṃ rājñaḥ savyaṃ padaṃ mayā
d evam ukto mayā hetur uttaraṃ prabravītu me
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tato na vyājahāraiṣāṃ kaś cid buddhimatāṃ satām
d mānināṃ balināṃ rājñāṃ madhye saṃdarśite pade
d puṣpavṛṣṭir mahaty āsīt sahadevasya mūrdhani
d evam ukte sunīthasya sahadevena keśave
d svabhāvarakte nayane bhūyo rakte babhūvatuḥ
d tasya kopaṃ samudbhūtaṃ jñātvā bhīṣmaḥ pratāpavān
d ācacakṣe punas tasmai kṛṣṇasyaivottamān guṇān
d sa sunīthaṃ samāmantrya tāṃś ca sarvān mahīkṣitaḥ
d uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭha idaṃ matimatāṃ varaḥ
d sahadevena rājāno yad uktaṃ keśavaṃ prati
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tat tatheti vijānīdhvaṃ bhūyaś cātra nibodhata
d tato bhīṣmasya tac chrutvā vacaḥ kāle yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d uvāca matimān bhīṣmaṃ tataḥ kauravanandanaḥ
d vistareṇāsya devasya karmāṇīcchāmi sarvaśaḥ
d śrotuṃ bhagavatas tāni prabravīhi pitāmaha
d karmaṇām ānupūrvyaṃ ca prādurbhāvāṃś ca me vibhoḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d yathā ca prakṛtiḥ kṛṣṇe tan me brūhi pitāmaha
d evam uktas tadā bhīṣmaḥ provāca puruṣarṣabham
d yudhiṣṭhiram amitraghnaṃ tasmin kṣatrasamāgame
d samakṣaṃ vāsudevasya devasyeva śatakratoḥ
d karmāṇy asukarāṇy anyair ācacakṣe janādhipa
d śṛṇvatāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca dharmarājasya cāntike
d idaṃ matimatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ prati viśāṃ pate
d sāmnaivāmantrya rājendraṃ cedirājam ariṃdamam
d bhīmakarmā tato bhīṣmo bhūyaḥ sa idam abravīt
d bhīṣmaḥ
d kurūṇāṃ cāpi rājānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram uvāca ha
d vartamānām atītāṃ ca śṛṇu rājan yudhiṣṭhira
d īśvarasyottamasyaināṃ karmaṇāṃ gahanāṃ gatim
d avyakto vyaktaliṅgastho ya eṣa bhagavān prabhuḥ
d purā nārāyaṇo devaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ prapitāmahaḥ
d sahasraśīrṣaḥ puruṣo dhruvo 'vyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ
d sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrāsyaḥ sahasracaraṇo vibhuḥ
d sahasrabāhuḥ sāhasro devo nāmasahasravān
d sahasramukuṭo devo viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥ
d anekavarṇo devādir avyaktād vai pare sthitaḥ
d asṛjat salilaṃ pūrvaṃ sa ca nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
d tatas tu bhagavāṃs toye brahmāṇam asṛjat svayam
d brahmā caturmukho lokān sarvāṃs tān asṛjat svayam
d ādikāle purā hy evaṃ sarvalokasya codbhavaḥ
d purātha pralaye prāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame
d brahmādiṣu pralīneṣu naṣṭe loke carācare
d ābhūtasaṃplave prāpte pralīne prakṛtau mahān
d ekas tiṣṭhati sarvātmā sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
d nārāyaṇasya cāṅgāni sarvadaivāni bhārata
d śiras tasya divaṃ rājan nābhiḥ khaṃ caraṇau mahī
d aśvinau karṇayor devau cakṣuṣī śaśibhāskarau
d indravaiśvānarau devau mukhaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ
d anyāni sarvadaivāni tasyāṅgāni mahātmanaḥ
d sarvaṃ vyāpya haris tasthau sūtraṃ maṇigaṇān iva
d ābhūtasaṃplavānte 'tha dṛṣṭvā sarvaṃ tamonvitam
d nārāyaṇo mahāyogī sarvajñaḥ paramātmavān
d brahmabhūtas tadātmānaṃ brahmāṇam asṛjat svayam
d so 'dhyakṣaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhūtaḥ prabhavo 'cyutaḥ
d sanatkumāraṃ rudraṃ ca manuṃ caiva tapodhanān
d sarvam evāsṛjad brahmā tato lokān prajās tathā
d tena tad vyasṛjat tatra prāpte kāle yudhiṣṭhira
d tebhyo 'bhavan mahātmabhyo bahudhā brahma śāśvatam
d kalpānāṃ bahukoṭyaś ca samatītā hi bhārata
d ābhūtasaṃplavāś caiva bahukoṭyo 'ticakramuḥ
d manvantarayuge 'jasraṃ saṃkalpā bhūtasaṃplavāḥ
d cakravat parivartante sarvaṃ viṣṇumayaṃ jagat
d sṛṣṭvā caturmukhaṃ devaṃ devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
d sa lokānāṃ hitārthāya kṣīrode vasati prabhuḥ
d brahmā tu sarvabhūtānāṃ lokasya ca pitāmahaḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d tato nārāyaṇo devaḥ sarvasya prapitāmahaḥ
d avyakto vyaktaliṅgastho ya eṣa bhagavān prabhuḥ
d nārāyaṇo jagac cakre prabhavāpyayasaṃhitaḥ
d eṣa nārāyaṇo bhūtvā harir āsīd yudhiṣṭhira
d brahmāṇaṃ śaśisūryau ca dharmaṃ caivāsṛjat svayam
d bahuśaḥ sarvabhūtātmā prādurbhavati kāryataḥ
d prādurbhāvāṃs tu vakṣyāmi divyān devagaṇair yutān
d suptvā yugasahasraṃ sa prādurbhavati kāryavān
d pūrṇe yugasahasre 'tha devadevo jagatpatiḥ
d brahmāṇaṃ kapilaṃ caiva parameṣṭhiṃ tathaiva ca
d devān saptaṛṣīṃś caiva śaṃkaraṃ ca mahāyaśāḥ
d sanatkumāraṃ bhagavān manuṃ caiva prajāpatim
d purā cakre 'tha devādiḥ pradīptāgnisamaprabhaḥ
d yena cārṇavamadhyasthau naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame
d naṣṭadevāsuranare praṇaṣṭoragarākṣase
d yoddhukāmau sudurdharṣau bhrātarau madhukaiṭabhau
d hatau prabhavatā tena tayor dattvā vṛtaṃ varam
d bhūmiṃ baddhvā kṛtau pūrvaṃ mṛnmayau dvau mahāsurau
d karṇasrotodbhavau tau tu viṣṇos tasya mahātmanaḥ
d mahārṇave prasvapataḥ śailarājasamau sthitau
d tau viveśa svayaṃ vāyur brahmaṇā sādhu coditaḥ
d tau divaṃ chādayitvā tu vavṛdhāte mahāsurau
d vāyuprāṇau tu tau dṛṣṭvā brahmā paryāmṛśac chanaiḥ
d ekaṃ mṛdutaraṃ viddhi kaṭhinaṃ viddhi cāparam
d nāmanī tu tayoś cakre sa vibhuḥ salilodbhavaḥ
d mṛdus tv ayaṃ madhur nāma kaṭhinaḥ kaiṭabhaḥ svayam
d tau daityau kṛtanāmānau ceratur balagarvitau
d tau purātha divaṃ sarvāṃ prāptau rājan mahāsurau
d pracchādyātha divaṃ sarvāṃ ceratur madhukaiṭabhau
d sarvam ekārṇavaṃ lokaṃ yoddhukāmau sunirbhayau
d tau gatāv asurau dṛṣṭvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
d ekārṇavāmbunicaye tatraivāntaradhīyata
d sa padme padmanābhasya nābhideśāt samutthite
d āsīd ādau svayaṃ janma tat paṅkajam apaṅkajam
d pūjayām āsa vasatiṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
d tāv ubhau jalagarbhasthau nārāyaṇacaturmukhau
d bahūn varṣāyutān apsu śayānau na cakampatuḥ
d atha dīrghasya kālasya tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau
d ājagmatus tam uddeśaṃ yatra brahmā vyavasthitaḥ
d tau dṛṣṭvā lokanāthas tu kopāt saṃraktalocanaḥ
d utpapātātha śayanāt padmanābho mahādyutiḥ
d tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ tayos tasya ca vai tadā
d ekārṇave tadā ghore trailokye jalatāṃ gate
d tad abhūt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ varṣasaṃghān sahasraśaḥ
d na ca tāv asurau yuddhe tadā śramam avāpatuḥ
d atha dīrghasya kālasya tau daityau yuddhadurmadau
d ūcatuḥ prītamanasau devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
d prītau svas tava yuddhena ślāghyas tvaṃ mṛtyur āvayoḥ
d āvāṃ jahi na yatrorvī salilena pariplutā
d hatau ca tava putratvaṃ prāpnuyāva surottama
d yo hy āvāṃ yudhi nirjetā tasyāvāṃ vihitau sutau
d tayoḥ sa vacanaṃ śrutvā tadā nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
d tau pragṛhya mṛdhe daityau dorbhyāṃ tau samapīḍayat
d ūrubhyāṃ nidhanaṃ cakre tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau
d tau hatau cāplutau toye vapurbhyām ekatāṃ gatau
d medo mumucatur daityau mathyamānau jalormibhiḥ
d medasā taj jalaṃ vyāptaṃ tābhyām antardadhe tadā
d nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān asṛjad vividhāḥ prajāḥ
d daityayor medasā channā sarvā rājan vasuṃdharā
d tadā prabhṛti kaunteya medinīti smṛtā mahī
d prabhāvāt padmanābhasya śāśvatī ca kṛtā nṛṇām
d bhīṣmaḥ
d prādurbhāvasahasrāṇi samatītāny anekaśaḥ
d yathāśakti tu vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tān kurunandana
d purā kamalanābhasya svapataḥ sāgarāmbhasi
d puṣkare yatra saṃbhūtā devā ṛṣigaṇaiḥ saha
d eṣa pauṣkariko nāma prādurbhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
d purāṇaḥ kathyate yatra vedaśrutisamāhitaḥ
d vārāhas tu śrutimukhaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
d yatra viṣṇuḥ suraśreṣṭho vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ
d ujjahāra mahīṃ toyāt saśailavanakānanām
d vedapādo yūpadaṃṣṭraḥ kratudantaś citīmukhaḥ
d agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ
d ahorātrekṣaṇo divyo vedāṅgaḥ śrutibhūṣaṇaḥ
d ājyanāsaḥ snuvatuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvano mahān
d dharmasatyamayaḥ śrīmān karmavikramasatkṛtaḥ
d prāyaścittamayo dhīraḥ paśujānur mahāvṛṣaḥ
d udgātṛhomaliṅgo 'sau paśubījamahauṣadhiḥ
d bāhyāntarātmā mantrāsthivikṛtaḥ saumyadarśanaḥ
d vedaskandho havirgandho havyakavyādivegavān
d prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhir ācitaḥ
d dakṣiṇāhṛdayo yogī mahāsatramayo mahān
d upākarmoṣṭharucakaḥ pravargyāvartabhūṣaṇaḥ
d chāyāpatnīsahāyo vai maṇiśṛṅga ivocchritaḥ
d evaṃ yajñavarāho vai bhūtvā viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ
d mahīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ saśailavanakānanām
d ekārṇavajale bhraṣṭām ekārṇavagataḥ prabhuḥ
d majjitāṃ salile tasmin svadevīṃ pṛthivīṃ tadā
d ujjahāra viṣāṇena mārkaṇḍeyasya paśyataḥ
d śṛṅgeṇemāṃ samuddhṛtya lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
d sahasraśīrṣo deveśo nirmame jagatīṃ prabhuḥ
d evaṃ yajñavarāheṇa bhūtabhavyabhavātmanā
d uddhṛtā pṛthivī devī sāgarāmbudharā purā
d nihatā dānavāḥ sarve devadevena viṣṇunā
d vārāhaḥ kathito hy eṣa nārasiṃham atho śṛṇu
d yatra bhūtvā mṛgendreṇa hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d daityendro balavān rājan surārir balagarvitaḥ
d hiraṇyakaśipur nāma āsīt trailokyakaṇṭakaḥ
d daityānām ādipuruṣo vīryavān dhṛtimān balī
d sa praviśya vanaṃ rājaṃś cakāra tapa uttamam
d daśa varṣasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca
d japopavāsas tasyāsīt sthāṇur maunavrato dṛḍhaḥ
d tato damaśamābhyāṃ ca brahmacaryeṇa cānagha
d brahmā prītamanās tasya tapasā niyamena ca
d tataḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān svayam āgamya bhūpate
d vimānenārkavarṇena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatā
d ādityair vasubhiḥ sādhyair marudbhir daivataiḥ saha
d radrair viśvasahāyaiś ca yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ
d diśābhir vidiśābhiś ca nadībhiḥ sāgarais tathā
d nakṣatraiś ca muhūrtaiś ca khecaraiś cāparair grahaiḥ
d devarṣibhis tapoyuktaiḥ siddhaiḥ saptarṣibhis tathā
d rājarṣibhiḥ puṇyatamair gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ
d carācaraguruḥ śrīmān vṛtaḥ sarvasurais tathā
d brahmā
d brahmā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho daityam āgamya cābravīt
d prīto 'smi tava bhaktasya tapasānena suvrata
d varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhi
d hiraṇyakaśipuḥ
d na devāsuragandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
d na mānuṣāḥ piśācāś ca hanyur māṃ devasattama
d ṛṣayo vā na māṃ śāpaiḥ kruddhā lokapitāmaha
d śapeyus tapasā yuktā vara eṣa vṛto mayā
d na śastreṇa na cāstreṇa giriṇā pādapena ca
d na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa syān na cānyena me vadhaḥ
d nākāśe vā na bhūmau vā rātrau vā divase 'pi vā
d nāntar vā na bahir vāpi syād vadho me pitāmaha
d paśubhir vā mṛgair na syāt pakṣibhir vā sarīsṛpaiḥ
d brahmā
d dadāsi ced varān etān devadeva vṛṇomy aham
d ete divyā varās tāta mayā dattās tavādbhutāḥ
d sarvakāmān varāṃs tāta prāpsyase tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
d evam uktvā sa bhagavān ākāśena jagāma ha
d rarāja brahmaloke sa brahmarṣigaṇasevitaḥ
d tato devāś ca nāgāś ca gandharvā munayas tathā
d varapradānaṃ śrutvā te brahmāṇam upatasthire
d devāḥ
d vareṇānena bhagavan bādhiṣyati sa no 'suraḥ
d tat prasīdasva bhagavan vadho 'sya pravicintyatām
d bhagavan sarvabhūtānāṃ svayaṃbhūr ādikṛd vibhuḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d sraṣṭā ca havyakavyānām avyaktaprakṛtir dhruvaḥ
d tato lokahitaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā devaḥ prajāpatiḥ
d provāca bhagavān vākyaṃ sarvadevagaṇāṃs tadā
d avaśyaṃ tridaśās tena prāptavyaṃ tapasaḥ phalam
d tapaso 'nte 'sya bhagavān vadhaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kariṣyati
d etac chrutvā surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā tasya vai vadham
d svāni sthānāni divyāni jagmus te vai mudānvitāḥ
d labdhamātre vare cāpi sarvās tā bādhate prajāḥ
d hiraṇyakaśipur daityo varadānena darpitaḥ
d rājyaṃ cakāra daityendro daityasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
d sapta dvīpān vaśe cakre lokālokāntaraṃ balāt
d divyalokān samastān vai bhogān divyān avāpa saḥ
d devāṃs tribhuvanasthāṃs tān parājitya mahāsuraḥ
d trailokyaṃ vaśam ānīya svarge vasati dānavaḥ
d yadā varamadonmatto nyavasad dānavo divi
d atha lokān samastāṃś ca vijitya sa mahābalaḥ
d bhaveyam aham evendraḥ somo 'gnir māruto raviḥ
d salilaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca nakṣatrāṇi diśo daśa
d ahaṃ krodhaś ca kāmaś ca varuṇo vāsavo yamaḥ
d dhanadaś ca dhanādhyakṣo yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣādhipaḥ
d ete bhaveyam ity uktvā svayaṃ bhūtvā balāt sa ca
d teṣāṃ gṛhītvā sthānāni teṣāṃ kāryāṇy avāpa saḥ
d īḍyaś cāsmin makhavarair devakiṃnarasattamaiḥ
d narakasthān samānīya svargasthāṃs tāṃś cakāra saḥ
d evamādīni karmāṇi kṛtvā daityapatir balī
d āśrameṣu mahābhāgān munīn vai saṃśitavratān
d satyadharmaratān dāntān purā dharṣitavāṃś ca saḥ
d yajñīyān kṛtavān daityān ayajñīyāś ca devatāḥ
d yatra yatra surā jagmus tatra tatra vrajanty uta
d sthānāni devatānāṃ tu hṛtvā rājyam apālayat
d pañca koṭyaś ca varṣāṇi niyutāny ekaṣaṣṭi ca
d ṣaṣṭiś caiva sahasrāṇāṃ jagmus tasya durātmanaḥ
d etad varṣaṃ sa daityendro bhogaiśvaryam avāpa saḥ
d tenāti bādhyamānās te daityendreṇa balīyasā
d brahmalokaṃ surā jagmuḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥ
d devāḥ
d pitāmahaṃ samāsādya khinnāḥ prāñjalayo 'bruvan
d bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa nas trāyasva ihāgatān
d bhayaṃ ditisutād ghoraṃ bhavaty adya divāniśam
d bhagavan sarvabhūtānāṃ svayaṃbhūr ādikṛd vibhuḥ
d brahmā
d sraṣṭā tvaṃ havyakavyānām avyaktaḥ prakṛtir dhruvaḥ
d śrūyatām āpad evaṃ hi durvijñeyaṃ mayāpi ca
d nārāyaṇas tu puruṣo viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥ
d avyaktaḥ sarvabhūtānām acintyo vibhur avyayaḥ
d mamāpi sa tu yuṣmākaṃ vyasane paramā gatiḥ
d nārāyaṇaḥ paro 'vyaktād aham avyaktasaṃbhavaḥ
d matto jajñuḥ prajā lokāḥ sarvadevāsurāś ca te
d devā yathāhaṃ yuṣmākaṃ tathā nārāyaṇo mama
d pitāmaho 'haṃ sarvasya sa viṣṇuḥ prapitāmahaḥ
d niścitaṃ vibudhā daityaṃ sa viṣṇus taṃ haniṣyati
d bhīṣmaḥ
d tasya nāsti hy aśakyaṃ ca tasmād vrajata māciram
d pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te bharatarṣabha
d vibudhā brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ jagmuḥ kṣīrodadhiṃ prati
d ādityā vasavaḥ sādhyā viśve ca marutas tathā
d rudrā maharṣayaś caiva aśvinau ca surūpiṇau
d anye ca divyā ye rājaṃs te sarve sagaṇāḥ surāḥ
d caturmukhaṃ puraskṛtya śvetadvīpam upasthitāḥ
d gatvā kṣīrasamudre taṃ śāśvatīṃ paramāṃ gatim
d anantaśayanaṃ devam anantaṃ dīptatejasam
d śaraṇyaṃ tridaśā viṣṇum upatasthuḥ sanātanam
d devaṃ brahmamayaṃ yajñaṃ brahmadevaṃ mahābalam
d bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca prabhuṃ lokanamaskṛtam
d devāḥ
d nārāyaṇaṃ vibhuṃ devaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
d trāyasva no 'dya deveśa hiraṇyakaśipor vadhāt
d tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo dhātā brahmādīnāṃ surottama
d utphullāmalapatrākṣa śatrupakṣabhayaṃkara
d kṣayāya ditivaṃśasya śaraṇaṃ tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
d bhīṣmaḥ
d devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā tadā viṣṇuḥ śuciśravāḥ
d viṣṇuḥ
d adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vaktum evopacakrame
d bhayaṃ tyajadhvam amarā abhayaṃ vo dadāmy aham
d tad evaṃ tridivaṃ devāḥ pratipadyata māciram
d eṣo 'haṃ sagaṇaṃ daityaṃ varadānena darpitam
d brahmā
d avadhyam amarendrāṇāṃ dānavendraṃ nihanmy aham
d bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa khinnā hy ete bhṛśaṃ surāḥ
d viṣṇuḥ
d tasmāt tvaṃ jahi daityendraṃ kṣipraṃ kālo 'sya mā ciram
d kṣipraṃ devāḥ kariṣyāmi tvarayā daityanāśanam
d tasmāt tvaṃ vibudhāś caiva pratipadyata vai divam
d bhīṣmaḥ
d evam uktvā tu bhagavān visṛjya tridiveśvarān
d narasyārdhatanuṃ kṛtvā siṃhasyārdhatanuṃ tathā
d nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇiṃ niṣpiṣya pāṇinā
d bhīmarūpo mahātejā vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
d hiraṇyakaśipuṃ rājañ jagāma harir īśvaraḥ
d daityās tam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā nārasiṃhaṃ mahābalam
d vavarṣuḥ śastravarṣais te susaṃkruddhās tadā harim
d tair visṛṣṭāni śastrāṇi bhakṣayām āsa vai hariḥ
d jaghāna ca raṇe daityān sahasrāṇi bahūny api
d tān nihatya ca daityendrān sarvān kruddhān mahābalān
d abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddho daityendraṃ balagarvitam
d jīmūtaghanasaṃkāśo jīmūtaghananisvanaḥ
d jīmūta iva dīptaujā jīmūta iva vegavān
d devārir ditijo duṣṭo nṛsiṃhaṃ samupādravat
d daityaṃ so 'tibalaṃ dṛṣṭvā kruddhaśārdūlavikramam
d dṛptair daityagaṇair guptaṃ kharair nakhamukhair uta
d tataḥ kṛtvā tu yuddhaṃ vai tena daityena vai hariḥ
d saṃdhyākāle mahātejā bhavanānte tvarānvitaḥ
d ūrau nidhāya daityendraṃ nirbibheda nakhair hi tam
d mahābalaṃ mahāvīryaṃ varadānena darpitam
d daityaśreṣṭhaṃ suraśreṣṭho jaghāna tarasā hariḥ
d hiraṇyakaśipuṃ hatvā sarvān daityāṃś ca vai tadā
d vibudhānāṃ prajānāṃ ca hitaṃ kṛtvā mahādyutiḥ
d pramumoda harir devaḥ prāpya dharmaṃ tadā bhuvi
d eṣa te nārasiṃho 'tra kathitaḥ pāṇḍunandana
d bhīṣmaḥ
d śṛṇu tvaṃ vāmanaṃ nāma prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
d purā tretāyuge rājan balir vairocano 'bhavat
d daityānāṃ pārthivo vīro balenāpratimo balī
d tadā balir mahārāja daityasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
d vijitya tarasā śakram indrasthānam avāpa saḥ
d tena vitrāsitā devā balinākhaṇḍalādayaḥ
d brahmāṇaṃ vai puraskṛtya gatvā kṣīrodadhiṃ tadā
d tuṣṭuvuḥ sahitāḥ sarve devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
d teṣāṃ prasādaṃ cakre 'tha vibudhānāṃ haris tadā
d prasādajaṃ tasya vibhor adityāṃ janma ucyate
d aditer api putratvam etya yādavanandanaḥ
d eṣa viṣṇur iti khyāta indrasyāvarajo 'bhavat
d tasminn eva tu kāle tu daityendro vīryavān balī
d aśvamedhaṃ kratuśreṣṭham āhartum upacakrame
d vartamāne tadā yajñe daityendrasya yudhiṣṭhira
d sa viṣṇur vāmano bhūtvā pracchanno brahmaveṣadhṛk
d muṇḍo yajñopavītī ca kṛṣṇājinadharaḥ śikhī
d palāśadaṇḍaṃ saṃgṛhya vāmano 'dbhutadarśanaḥ
d praviśya sa baler yajñe vartamāne tu dakṣiṇām
d dehīty uvāca daityendraṃ vikramāṃs trīn mamaiva ha
d dīyatāṃ tripadīmātram ity avocan mahāsuram
d sa tatheti pratiśrutya pradadau viṣṇave tadā
d tena labdhvā harir bhūmiṃ jṛmbhayām āsa vai bhṛśam
d sa śiśuḥ sadivaṃ khaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca viśāṃ pate
d tribhir vikramaṇair etat sarvam ākramatābhibhūḥ
d baler balavato yajñe balinā viṣṇunā purā
d vikramais tribhir akṣobhyāḥ kṣobhitās te mahāsurāḥ
d vipracittimukhāḥ kruddhā daityasaṃghā mahābalāḥ
d nānāvaktrā mahākāyā nānāveṣadharā nṛpa
d nānāpraharaṇā raudrā nānāmālyānulepanāḥ
d svāny āyudhāni saṃgṛhya pradīptā iva tejasā
d kramamāṇaṃ hariṃ tatra upāvartanta bhārata
d pramathya sarvān daiteyān pādahastatalais tu tān
d rūpaṃ kṛtvā mahābhīmaṃ jahārāśu sa medinīm
d saṃprāpya divam ākāśam ādityasadane sthitaḥ
d atyarocata bhūtātmā bhāskaraṃ svena tejasā
d prakāśayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradiśaś ca mahābalaḥ
d śuśubhe sa mahābāhuḥ sarvalokān prakāśayan
d tasya vikramato bhūmiṃ candrādityau stanāntare
d nabhaḥ prakramamāṇasya nābhyāṃ kila tadā sthitau
d param ākramamāṇasya jānubhyāṃ tau vyavasthitau
d viṣṇor amitavīryasya vadanty evaṃ dvijātayaḥ
d athāsādya kapālaṃ sa aṇḍasya tu yudhiṣṭhira
d tacchidrāt syandinī tasya pādād bhraṣṭātha nimnagā
d sasāra sāgaraṃ sāśu pāvanī sāgaraṃgamā
d jahāra medinīṃ sarvāṃ hatvā dānavapuṃgavān
d āsurīṃ śriyam āhṛtya trīṃl lokān sa janārdanaḥ
d saputradārān asurān pātāle vinyapātayat
d namuciḥ śambaraś caiva prahlādaś ca mahāmanāḥ
d pādapātābhinirdhūtāḥ pātāle vinipātitāḥ
d mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā saviśeṣāṇi vai hariḥ
d kālaṃ ca sakalaṃ rājan gātrabhūtāny adarśayat
d tasya gātre jagat sarvam ānītam iva dṛśyate
d na kiṃ cid asti lokeṣu yad anāptaṃ mahātmanā
d tad dhi rūpam upendrasya devadānavamānavāḥ
d dṛṣṭvā taṃ mumuhuḥ sarve viṣṇutejobhipīḍitāḥ
d balir baddho 'bhimānī ca yajñavāṭe mahātmanā
d virocanakulaṃ sarvaṃ pātāle vinipātitam
d evaṃvidhāni karmāṇi kṛtvā garuḍavāhanaḥ
d na vismayam upāgacchat pārameṣṭhyena tejasā
d sa sarvam amaraiśvaryaṃ saṃpradāya śacīpateḥ
d trailokyaṃ ca dadau śakre viṣṇur dānavasūdanaḥ
d eṣa te vāmano nāma prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
d vedavidbhir dvijair etat kathyate vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d mānuṣeṣu yathā viṣṇoḥ prādurbhāvaṃ tathā śṛṇu
d viṣṇoḥ punar mahārāja prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
d dattātreya iti khyāta ṛṣir āsīn mahāyaśāḥ
d tena naṣṭeṣu vedeṣu kriyāsu ca makheṣu ca
d cāturvarṇye ca saṃkīrṇe dharme śithilatāṃ gate
d abhivardhati cādharme satye naṣṭe sthite 'nṛte
d prajāsu kṣīyamāṇāsu dharme cākulatāṃ gate
d sayajñāḥ sakriyā vedāḥ pratyānītāś ca tena vai
d cāturvarṇyam asaṃkīrṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tena mahātmanā
d sa eṣa vai yadā prādād dhehayādhipater varam
d taṃ hehayānām adhipas tv arjuno 'bhiprasādayan
d vane paryacarat samyak śuśrūṣur anasūyakaḥ
d nirmamo nirahaṃkāro dīrghakālam atoṣayat
d ārādhya dattātreyaṃ hi agṛhṇāt sa varān imān
d āptād āptatarād viprād vidvān vidvanniṣevitān
d ṛte 'maratvād vipreṇa dattātreyeṇa dhīmatā
d varaiś caturbhiḥ pravṛta imāṃs tatrābhyanandata
d śrīmān manasvī balavān satyavāg anasūyakaḥ
d sahasrabāhur bhūyāsam eṣa me prathamo varaḥ
d jarāyujāṇḍajaṃ sarvaṃ sarvaṃ caiva carācaram
d prāśāstum icche dharmeṇa dvitīyas tv eṣa me varaḥ
d pitṝn devān ṛṣīn viprān yajeyaṃ vipulair makhaiḥ
d amitrān niśitair bāṇair ghātayeyaṃ raṇājire
d dattātreyeha bhagavaṃs tṛtīyo vara eṣa me
d yasya nāsīn na bhavitā na cāsti sadṛśaḥ pumān
d iha vā divi vā loke sa me hantā bhaved iti
d so 'rjunaḥ kṛtavīryasya varaḥ putro 'bhavad yudhi
d sa sahasraṃ sahasrāṇāṃ māhiṣmatyām avardhata
d sa bhūmim akhilāṃ jitvā dvīpāṃś cāpi samudriṇaḥ
d nabhasīva jvalan sūryaḥ puṇyaiḥ karmabhir arjunaḥ
d indradvīpaṃ kaśeruṃ ca tāmradvīpaṃ gabhastimat
d gāndharvaṃ vāruṇaṃ dvīpaṃ saumyārṣam iti ca prabhuḥ
d pūrvair ajitapūrvāṃś ca dvīpān ajayad arjunaḥ
d sauvarṇaṃ sarvam apy āsīd vimānavaram uttamam
d caturdhā vyabhajad rāṣṭraṃ tad vibhajyānvapālayat
d ekāṃśenāharat senām ekāṃśenāvasad gṛhān
d yas tu tasya tṛtīyāṃśo rājāsīj janasaṃgrahe
d āptaḥ paramakalyāṇas tena yajñān akalpayat
d ye dasyavo grāmacarā araṇye ca vasanti ye
d caturthena ca so 'ṃśena tān sarvān pratyaṣedhayat
d sarvebhyaś cāntavāsibhyaḥ kārtavīryo 'harad balim
d āhṛtaṃ svabalair yat tad arjunasyāvamanyate
d kāko vā mūṣiko vāpi taṃ tam eva nyabarhayat
d dvārāṇi nāpidhīyante rāṣṭreṣu nagareṣu ca
d sa eva rāṣṭrapālo 'bhūt strīpālo 'bhavad arjunaḥ
d sa evāsīd ajāpālaḥ sa gopālo viśāṃ pate
d sarvāṇy eva manuṣyāṇāṃ rājā kṣetrāṇi rakṣati
d idaṃ tu kārtavīryasya babhūvāsadṛśaṃ janaiḥ
d na pūrve nāpare tasya gamiṣyanti gatiṃ nṛpāḥ
d yad arṇave prayātasya vastraṃ na pariṣicyate
d śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇām anuśiṣyārjuno mahīm
d dattātreyaprasādena evaṃ rājyaṃ cakāra saḥ
d evaṃ bahūni karmāṇi cakre lokahitāya saḥ
d dattātreya iti khyātaḥ prādurbhāvas tu vaiṣṇavaḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d kathito bharataśreṣṭha śṛṇu bhūyo mahātmanaḥ
d yadā bhṛgukule janma yadarthaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
d jāmadagnya iti khyātaḥ prādurbhāvas tu vaiṣṇavaḥ
d jamadagneḥ suto rājan rāmo nāma sa vīryavān
d hehayāntakaro rājan sa rāmo balināṃ varaḥ
d kārtavīryo mahāvīryo balenāpratimas tathā
d rāmeṇa jāmadagnyena hato viṣamam ācaran
d taṃ kārtavīryaṃ rājānaṃ hehayānām ariṃdamam
d rathasthaṃ pārthivaṃ rāmaḥ pātayitvāvadhīd raṇe
d jambhasya yajñahantā sa ṛtvijaṃ caiva saṃstare
d jambhasya mūrdhni bhettā ca hantā ca śatadundubheḥ
d sa eṣa kṛṣṇo govindo jāto bhṛguṣu vīryavān
d sahasrabāhum uddhartuṃ sahasrajitam āhave
d kṣatriyāṇāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭim ayutāni mahāyaśāḥ
d sarasvatyāṃ sametāni eṣa vai dhanuṣājayat
d brahmadviṣāṃ vadhe tasmin sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
d punar jagrāha śūrāṇām antaṃ cakre nararṣabhaḥ
d tato daśasahasrasya bhaṅktvā pūrvam ariṃdamaḥ
d sahasraṃ musalenāghnan sahasram udakṛntata
d caturdaśa sahasrāṇi kaṇadhūmam apāyayat
d śiṣṭān brahmadviṣo jitvā tato 'snāyata bhārgavaḥ
d rāma rāmety abhikruṣṭo brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyārditaiḥ
d nyaghnad daśa sahasrāṇi rāmaḥ paraśunābhibhūḥ
d na hy amṛṣyata tāṃ vācam ārtair bhṛśam udīritām
d bhṛgo rāmābhidhāveti yadākrandan dvijātayaḥ
d kāśmīrān daradān kuntīn kṣudrakān mālavāñ śakān
d cedikāśikarūśāṃś ca ṛṣīkān krathakaiśikān
d aṅgān vaṅgān kaliṅgāṃś ca māgadhān kāśikosalān
d rātrāyaṇān vītihotrān kirātān mārttikāvatān
d etān anyāṃś ca rājendrān deśe deśe sahasraśaḥ
d nikṛtya niśitair bāṇaiḥ saṃpradāya vivasvate
d kīrṇā kṣatriyakoṭībhir merumandarabhūṣaṇā
d triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivī tena niḥkṣatriyā kṛtā
d kṛtvā niḥkṣatriyāṃ caiva bhārgavaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ
d indragopakavarṇasya jīvaṃjīvanibhasya ca
d pūrayām āsa saritaḥ kṣatajasya sarāṃsi ca
d cakāra tarpaṇaṃ vīraḥ pitṝṇāṃ tāsu teṣu ca
d sarvān aṣṭādaśa dvīpān vaśam ānīya bhārgavaḥ
d so 'śvamedhasahasrāṇi naramedhaśatāni ca
d iṣṭvā sāgaraparyantāṃ kāśyapāya mahīṃ dadau
d tasyāgreṇānuparyeti bhūmiṃ kṛtvā vipāṃsulām
d tataḥ kālakṛtāṃ satyāṃ bhārgavāya mahātmane
d gāthām apy atra gāyanti ye purāṇavido janāḥ
d vedim aṣṭādaśotsedhāṃ hiraṇyasyātipauruṣīm
d rāmasya jāmadagnyasya pratijagrāha kāśyapaḥ
d evam iṣṭvā mahābāhuḥ kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
d anyad varṣaśataṃ rāmaḥ saubhe sālvam ayodhayat
d tataḥ sa bhṛguśārdūlas taṃ saubhaṃ yodhayan prabhuḥ
d subandhuraṃ rathaṃ rājann āsthāya bharatarṣabha
d nagnikānāṃ kumārīṇāṃ gāyantīnām upāśṛṇot
d rāma rāma mahābāho bhṛgūṇāṃ kīrtivardhana
d tyaja śastrāṇi sarvāṇi na tvaṃ saubhaṃ vadhiṣyasi
d cakrahasto gadāpāṇir bhītānām abhayaṃkaraḥ
d yudhi pradyumnasāmbābhyāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saubhaṃ vadhiṣyati
d tac chrutvā puruṣavyāghras tata eva vanaṃ yayau
d nyasya sarvāṇi śastrāṇi kālakāṅkṣī mahāyaśāḥ
d rathaṃ varmāyudhaṃ caiva śarān paraśum eva ca
d dhanūṃṣy apsu pratiṣṭhāpya rāmas tepe paraṃ tapaḥ
d hriyaṃ prajñāṃ śriyaṃ kīrtiṃ lakṣmīṃ cāmitrakarśanaḥ
d pañcādhiṣṭhāya dharmātmā taṃ rathaṃ visasarja ha
d ādikāle pravṛttaṃ hi vibhajan kālam īśvaraḥ
d nāhanac chraddhayā saubhaṃ na hy aśakto mahāyaśāḥ
d jāmadagnya iti khyāto yas tv asau bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d so 'sya bhāgas tapas tepe bhārgavo lokaviśrutaḥ
d śṛṇu rājaṃs tathā viṣṇoḥ prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
d caturviṃśe yuge cāpi mārkaṇḍeyapuraḥsaraḥ
d tithau nāvamike jajñe tathā daśarathād api
d kṛtvātmānaṃ mahābāhuś caturdhā viṣṇur avyayaḥ
d loke rāma iti khyātas tejasā bhāskaropamaḥ
d prasādhanārthaṃ lokasya viṣṇus tasya sanātanaḥ
d dharmārtham eva kaunteya jajñe tatra mahāyaśāḥ
d tam apy āhur manuṣyendraṃ sarvabhūtapates tanum
d yajñavighnaṃ tadā kṛtvā viśvāmitrasya bhārata
d subāhur nihatahas tena mārīcas tāḍito bhṛśam
d tasmai dattāni śastrāṇi viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā
d vadhārthaṃ devaśatrūṇāṃ durvārāṇi surair api
d vartamāne tadā yajñe janakasya mahātmanaḥ
d bhagnaṃ māheśvaraṃ cāpaṃ krīḍatā līlayā param
d tato vivāhaṃ sītāyāḥ kṛtvā sa raghuvallabhaḥ
d nagarīṃ punar āsādya mumude tatra sītayā
d kasya cit tv atha kālasya pitrā tatrābhicoditaḥ
d kaikeyyāḥ priyam anvicchan vanam abhyavapadyata
d yaḥ samāḥ sarvadharmajñaś caturdaśa vane vasan
d lakṣmaṇānucaro rāmaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
d caturdaśa vane taptvā tapo varṣāṇi bhārata
d rūpiṇī yasya pārśvasthā sītety abhihitā janaiḥ
d pūrvocitatvāt sā lakṣmīr bhartāram anugacchati
d janasthāne vasan kāryaṃ tridaśānāṃ cakāra saḥ
d mārīcaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ hatvā kharaṃ triśirasaṃ tathā
d caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ ghorakarmaṇām
d jaghāna rāmo dharmātmā prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā
d virādhaṃ ca kabandhaṃ ca rākṣasau krūrakarmiṇau
d jaghāna ca tadā rāmo gandharvau śāpavikṣatau
d sa rāvaṇasya bhaginīnāsācchedaṃ ca kārayat
d bhāryāviyogaṃ taṃ prāpya mṛgayan vyacarad vanam
d tatas tam ṛśyamūkaṃ sa gatvā pampām atītya ca
d sugrīvaṃ mārutiṃ dṛṣṭvā cakre maitrīṃ tayoḥ sa vai
d atha gatvā sa kiṣkindhāṃ sugrīveṇa tadā saha
d nihatya vālinaṃ yuddhe vānarendraṃ mahābalam
d abhyaṣiñcat tadā rāmaḥ sugrīvaṃ vānareśvaram
d tataḥ sa vīryavān rājaṃs tvarayan vai samutsukaḥ
d vicitya vāyuputreṇa laṅkādeśaṃ niveditam
d setuṃ baddhvā samudrasya vānaraiḥ sahitas tadā
d sītāyāḥ padam anvicchan rāmo laṅkāṃ viveśa ha
d devoragagaṇānāṃ hi yakṣarākṣasapakṣiṇām
d tatrāvadhyaṃ rākṣasendraṃ rāvaṇaṃ yudhi durjayam
d yuktaṃ rākṣasakoṭībhir bhinnāñjanacayopamam
d durnirīkṣyaṃ suragaṇair varadānena darpitam
d jaghāna sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ sānvayaṃ rāvaṇaṃ raṇe
d trailokyakaṇṭakaṃ vīraṃ mahākāyaṃ mahābalam
d rāvaṇaṃ sagaṇaṃ hatvā rāmo bhūtapatiḥ purā
d laṅkāyāṃ taṃ mahātmānaṃ rākṣasendraṃ vibhīṣaṇam
d abhiṣicya ca tatraiva amaratvaṃ dadau tadā
d āruhya puṣpakaṃ rāmaḥ sītām ādāya pāṇḍava
d sabalaḥ svapuraṃ gatvā dharmarājyam apālayat
d dānavo lavaṇo nāma madhoḥ putro mahābalaḥ
d śatrughnena hato rājaṃs tato rāmasya śāsanāt
d evaṃ bahūni karmāṇi kṛtvā lokahitāya saḥ
d rājyaṃ cakāra vidhivad rāmo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d daśāśvamedhān ājahre jyotirukthyān ahargaṇān
d nāśrūyantāśubhā vāco nātyayaḥ prāṇināṃ tadā
d na vittajaṃ bhayaṃ cāsīd rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d prāṇināṃ ca bhayaṃ nāsīj jalānalavidhānajam
d paryadevan na vidhavā nānāthāḥ kāś canābhavan
d sarvam āsīt tadā tṛptaṃ rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d na saṃkarakarā varṇā na kṛṣṭakarakṛj janaḥ
d na ca sma vṛddhā bālānāṃ pretakāryāṇi kurvate
d viśaḥ paryacaran kṣatraṃ kṣatraṃ nāpīḍayad viśaḥ
d narā nātyacaran bhāryā bhāryā nātyacaran patīn
d nāsīd alpakṛṣir loke rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d āsan varṣasahasrāṇi tathā putrasahasriṇaḥ
d arogāḥ prāṇino 'py āsan rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d ṛṣīṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ tathaiva ca
d pṛthivyāṃ sahavāso 'bhūd rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d sarve hy āsaṃs tṛptarūpās tadā tasmin viśāṃ pate
d dharmeṇa pṛthivīṃ sarvām anuśāsati bhūmipe
d tapasy evābhavan sarve sarve dharmam anuvratāḥ
d pṛthivyāṃ dhārmike tasmin rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d nādharmiṣṭho naraḥ kaś cid babhūva prāṇināṃ kva cit
d prāṇāpānau samāv āstāṃ rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d gāthām apy atra gāyanti ye purāṇavido janāḥ
d śyāmo yuvā lohitākṣo mātaṅgānām ivarṣabhaḥ
d ājānubāhuḥ sumukhaḥ siṃhaskandho mahābalaḥ
d daśa varṣasahasrāṇi daśa varṣaśatāni ca
d rājyaṃ bhogaṃ ca saṃprāpya śaśāsa pṛthivīm imām
d rāmo rāmo rāma iti prajānām abhavan kathāḥ
d rāmabhūtaṃ jagad idaṃ rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati
d ṛgyajuḥsāmahīnāś ca na tadāsan dvijātayaḥ
d uṣitvā daṇḍake kāryaṃ tridaśānāṃ cakāra saḥ
d pūrvāpakāriṇaṃ saṃkhye paulastyaṃ manujarṣabhaḥ
d devagandharvanāgānām ariṃ sa nijaghāna ha
d sattvavān guṇasaṃpanno dīpyamānaḥ svatejasā
d evam eva mahābāhur ikṣvākukulavardhanaḥ
d rāvaṇaṃ sagaṇaṃ hatvā divam ākramatābhibhūḥ
d iti dāśaratheḥ khyātaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
d tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahābāhur bhītānām abhayaṃkaraḥ
d aṣṭāviṃśe yuge rājañ jajñe śrīvatsalakṣaṇaḥ
d peśalaś ca vadānyaś ca loke bahumato nṛṣu
d smṛtimān deśakālajñaḥ śaṅkhacakragadāsidhṛk
d vāsudeva iti khyāto lokānāṃ hitakṛt sadā
d vṛṣṇīnāṃ ca kule jāto bhūmeḥ priyacikīrṣayā
d sa nṛṇām abhayaṃ dātā madhuheti sa viśrutaḥ
d sa śakrārjunarāmāṇāṃ kila sthānāny asūdayat
d kaṃsādīn nijaghānājau daityān mānuṣavigrahān
d ayaṃ lokahitārthāya prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
d kalkī viṣṇuyaśā nāma bhūyaś cotpatsyate hariḥ
d kaler yugānte saṃprāpte dharme śithilatāṃ gate
d pāṣaṇḍināṃ gaṇānāṃ hi vadhārthaṃ bharatarṣabha
d dharmasya ca vivṛddhyarthaṃ viprāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
d ete cānye ca bahavo divyā devagaṇair yutāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d prādurbhāvāḥ purāṇeṣu gīyante brahmavādibhiḥ
d evam ukto 'tha kaunteyas tataḥ pauravanandanaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d ābabhāṣe punar bhīṣmaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d bhūya eva manuṣyendra upendrasya yaśasvinaḥ
d janma vṛṣṇiṣu vijñātum icchāmi vadatāṃ vara
d yathaiva bhagavāñ jātaḥ kṣitāv iha janārdanaḥ
d mādhaveṣu mahābuddhis tan me brūhi pitāmaha
d yadarthaṃ ca mahātejā gās tu govṛṣabhekṣaṇaḥ
d rarakṣa kaṃsasya vadhāl lokānām abhirakṣitā
d krīḍatā caiva yad bālye govindena viceṣṭitam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tadā matimatāṃ śreṣṭha tan me brūhi pitāmaha
d evam uktas tato bhīṣmaḥ keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d mādhaveṣu tadā janma kathayām āsa vīryavān
d hanta te kathayiṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhira yathātatham
d yato nārāyaṇasyeha janma vṛṣṇiṣu kaurava
d purā loke mahārāja vartamāne kṛte yuge
d āsīt trailokyavikhyātaḥ saṃgrāmas tārakāmayaḥ
d virocano mayas tāro varāhaḥ śveta eva ca
d lambaḥ kiśoraḥ svarbhānur ariṣṭo 'tha kṣaraś ca vai
d vipracittiḥ pralambaś ca vṛtrajambhabalādayaḥ
d namuciḥ kālanemiś ca prahlāda iti viśrutaḥ
d ete cānye ca bahavo daityasaṃghāḥ sahasraśaḥ
d nānāśastradharā rājan nānābhūṣaṇavāhanāḥ
d devatānām abhimukhās tasthur daiteyadānavāḥ
d devās tu yudhyamānās te dānavān abhyayū raṇe
d ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyā viśve marudgaṇāḥ
d indro yamaś ca candraś ca varuṇo 'tha dhaneśvaraḥ
d aśvinau ca mahāvīryau ye cānye devatāgaṇāḥ
d cakrur yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ dānavaiś ca yathākramam
d yudhyamānāḥ sameyuś ca devā daiteyadānavaiḥ
d tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ devadānavasaṃkulam
d tābhyāṃ balābhyāṃ saṃjajñe tumulo vigrahas tadā
d tīkṣṇaiḥ śastraiḥ kiranto 'tha abhyayur devadānavāḥ
d aghnan devān sagandharvān sayakṣoragacāraṇān
d te vadhyamānā daiteyair devasaṃghās tadā raṇe
d dudruvuḥ saṃpariśrāntāḥ kṣīṇapraharaṇā raṇe
d trātāraṃ manasā jagmur devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
d etasminn antare tatra jagāma harir īśvaraḥ
d dīpayañ jyotiṣā bhūmiṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
d tam āgataṃ suparṇasthaṃ viṣṇuṃ lokanamaskṛtam
d dṛṣṭvā mudā yutāḥ sarve bhayaṃ tyaktvā raṇe surāḥ
d cakrur yuddhaṃ punaḥ sarve devā daiteyadānavaiḥ
d tad yuddham abhavad ghoram acintyaṃ romaharṣaṇam
d jaghnur daityān raṇe devāḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥ
d te vadhyamānā vibudhair dudruvur daityadānavāḥ
d vidrutān dānavān dṛṣṭvā tadā bhārata saṃyuge
d kālanemir iti khyāto dānavaḥ pratyadṛśyata
d śatapraharaṇo ghoraḥ śatabāhuḥ śatānanaḥ
d śataśīrṣaḥ sthitaḥ śrīmāñ śataśṛṅga ivācalaḥ
d bhāskarākāramukuṭaḥ śiñjitābharaṇāṅgadaḥ
d dhūmrakeśo hariśmaśrur nirdaṣṭhoṣṭhapuṭānanaḥ
d trailokyāntaravistāraṃ dhārayan vipulaṃ vapuḥ
d tarjayan vai raṇe devāñ chādayan sa diśo daśa
d abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddho vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
d tataḥ śastraprapātaiś ca devān dharṣitavān raṇe
d athābhyayuḥ surān sarvān punas te daityadānavāḥ
d āpīḍayan raṇe kruddhās tato devān yudhiṣṭhira
d te vadhyamānā vibudhāḥ samare kālaneminā
d daityaiś caiva mahārāja dudruvuḥ sahitā diśaḥ
d vidrutān vibudhān dṛṣṭvā kālanemir mahāsuraḥ
d indraṃ yamāgnivaruṇān vāyuṃ ca dhanadaṃ ravim
d etāṃś cānyān balāj jitvā teṣāṃ kāryāṇy avāpa saḥ
d tān sarvāṃs tarasā jitvā kālanemir mahāsuraḥ
d dadarśa gagane viṣṇuṃ suparṇasthaṃ mahādyutim
d taṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhatāmrākṣas tarjayann abhyayāt tadā
d sa bāhuśatam udyamya sarvāstragrahaṇaṃ raṇe
d roṣād bhārata daityendro viṣṇor urasi pātayat
d daityāś ca dānavāś caiva sarve mayapurogamāḥ
d svāny āyudhāni saṃgṛhya sarve viṣṇum atāḍayan
d sa tāḍyamāno 'tibalair daityaiḥ sarvāyudhodyataiḥ
d na cacāla harir yuddhe 'kampyamāna ivācalaḥ
d punar udyamya saṃkruddhaḥ kālanemir dṛḍhāṃ gadām
d jaghāna saṃyuge rājan sa viṣṇuṃ garuḍaṃ ca vai
d sa dṛṣṭvā garuḍaṃ śrāntaṃ cakram udyamya vai hariḥ
d śataṃ śirāṃsi bāhūṃś ca so 'cchinat kālaneminaḥ
d jaghānānyāṃś ca tān sarvān samare daityadānavān
d tasmin rājan raṇe daityās traya eva viniḥsṛtāḥ
d virocano mayaś caiva svarbhānuś ca mahāsuraḥ
d sarvān aśeṣān hatvā tu viṣṇur vai daityadānavān
d vibudhānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca svāni sthānāni vai dadau
d dattvā surāṇāṃ suprītiṃ prāpya sarvāṇi bhārata
d jagāma brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ brahmalokaṃ tadā hariḥ
d brahmalokaṃ praviśyātha tatra nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
d paurāṇāṃ guhyasadanaṃ divyaṃ nārāyaṇāśramam
d saṃpraviśya tadā devaḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
d sahasraśīrṣo bhūtvātha śayanāyopacakrame
d ādidevaḥ purāṇātmā nidrāvaśam upāgataḥ
d śete sukhaṃ sadā viṣṇur mohayañ jagad avyayaḥ
d jagmus tasyātha varṣāṇi śayānasya mahātmanaḥ
d ṣaṭtriṃśacchatasāhasraṃ mānuṣeṇeha saṃkhyayā
d tataḥ kṛtayugatretādvāparānte bubodha saḥ
d brahmādibhiḥ suraiś cāpi stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
d utplutya śayanād viṣṇur brahmaṇā vibudhaiḥ saha
d devānāṃ ca hitārthāya yayau devasabhāṃ prati
d meroḥ śikharavinyastāṃ jvalantīṃ tāṃ śubhāṃ sabhām
d viviśus tāṃ surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā saha bhārata
d jagmus tatra niṣedus te sā niḥśabdam abhūt tadā
d bhūmiḥ
d tatra bhūmir uvācātha khedāt karuṇabhāṣiṇī
d rājñāṃ balair balavatāṃ khinnāsmi bhṛśapīḍitā
d nityaṃ bhārapariśrāntā duḥkhāj jīvāmi vai surāḥ
d pure pure ca nṛpatiḥ koṭisaṃkhyair balair vṛtaḥ
d rāṣṭre rāṣṭre ca śataśo grāmāḥ kulasahasriṇaḥ
d bhūmipānāṃ sahasraiś ca teṣāṃ ca balināṃ balaiḥ
d grāmāyutaiś ca rāṣṭraiś ca ahaṃ nirvivarīkṛtā
d ke cid daityeṣu cotpannā ke cid rākṣasayonayaḥ
d tasmād dhārayituṃ śaktā na śakṣyāmi janān aham
d daityeśair bādhyamānās tāḥ prajā nityaṃ durātmabhiḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d bhūmes tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devo nārāyaṇas tadā
d bhīṣmaḥ
d vyādiśya tān surān sarvān kṣitau vastuṃ mano dadhe
d yac cakre bhagavān viṣṇur vasudevakulodbhavaḥ
d tat te 'haṃ nṛpa vakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣataḥ
d vāsudevasya māhātmyaṃ caritaṃ ca mahādyuteḥ
d hitārthaṃ suramartyānāṃ lokānāṃ hi hitāya ca
d yadā divi vibhus tāta na reme bhagavān asau
d tato vyādiśya bhūtāni bhuvi bhaumasukhāvahaḥ
d nigrahārthāya daityānāṃ codayām āsa vai tadā
d marutaś ca vasūṃś caiva sūryācandramasāv ubhau
d gandharvāpsarasaś caiva rudrādityāṃs tathāśvinau
d jāyadhvaṃ mānuṣe loke sarvabhūtamaheśvarāḥ
d jaṅgamāni viśālākṣo hy ātmānaṃ hy ātmanāsṛjat
d jāyatām iti govindas tiryagyonigatair api
d tāni sarvāṇi sarvajñaḥ sasurāṇi sureśvaraḥ
d ta evam uktāḥ kṛṣṇena sarva eva divaukasaḥ
d daityadānavahantāraḥ saṃbhūtā bhuvaneśvarāḥ
d yayātivaṃśajasyātha vasudevasya dhīmataḥ
d kule puṇyayaśaḥkarmā bheje nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
d ājñāpayitvā ratyartham ajāyata yadoḥ kule
d ātmānam ātmanā tāta kṛtvā bahuvidhaṃ hariḥ
d ratyartham eva gāvas tā rarakṣa puruṣottamaḥ
d ajātaśatro jātas tu yathaiṣa bhuvi bhūmipa
d bhīṣmaḥ
d kīrtyamānaṃ mayā tāta nibodha bharatarṣabha
d sāgarāḥ samakampanta mudā celuś ca parvatāḥ
d jajvaluś cāgnayaḥ śāntā jāyamāne janārdane
d śivāḥ saṃpravavur vātāḥ praśāntam abhavad rajaḥ
d jyotīṃṣi saṃprakāśante jāyamāne janārdane
d devadundubhayaś cāpi sasvanur bhṛśam ambare
d abhyavarṣat tadāgamya nāradaḥ puṣpavṛṣṭibhiḥ
d gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhir astuvan madhusūdanam
d upatasthus tadā prītāḥ prādurbhāve maharṣayaḥ
d tatas tān abhisaṃprekṣya nāradapramukhān ṛṣīn
d upānṛtyann upajagur gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d upatasthe ca govindaṃ sahasrākṣaḥ śacīpatiḥ
d abhyabhāṣata tejasvī maharṣīn pūjayaṃs tadā
d kṛtyāni devakāryāṇi kṛtvā lokahitāya ca
d svaṃ lokaṃ lokakṛd devaḥ punar gacchati tejasā
d ity uktvā munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ jagāma tridiveśvaraḥ
d abhyanujñāya tān sarvāñ chādayan prakṛtiṃ parām
d nandagopakule kṛṣṇa uṣitvā bahulāḥ samāḥ
d vasudevas tato jātaṃ bālam ādityasaṃnibham
d nandagopakule rājan bhayāt pracchādayad dharim
d tataḥ kadācit suptaṃ taṃ śakaṭasya tv adhaḥ śiśum
d yaśodā saṃparityajya jagāma yamunāṃ nadīm
d śiśulīlāṃ tataḥ kurvan svahastacaraṇau kṣipan
d ruroda madhuraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pādāv ūrdhvaṃ prasārayan
d pādāṅguṣṭhena śakaṭaṃ dhārayann atha keśavaḥ
d tatrāthaikena pādena pātayitvā tadā śiśuḥ
d nyubjaṃ payodharākāṅkṣī cakāra ca ruroda ca
d pātitaṃ śakaṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhinnabhāṇḍaghaṭīghaṭam
d janās te śiśunā tena vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ
d pratyakṣaṃ śūrasenānāṃ dṛśyate mahad adbhutam
d śayānena hataḥ pakṣī śiśunā tigmatejasā
d pūtanā cāpi nihatā mahākāyā mahāstanī
d paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ vāsudevena bhārata
d tataḥ kāle mahārāja saṃsaktau rāmakeśavau
d kṛṣṇaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaś cobhau riṅkhiṇau samapadyatām
d anyonyakiraṇagrastau candrasūryāv ivāmbare
d visarpayetāṃ sarvatra sarpabhogabhujau tadā
d rejatuḥ pāṃsudigdhāṅgau rāmakṛṣṇau tadā nṛpa
d kva cic ca jānubhiḥ spṛṣṭau krīḍamānau kva cid vane
d pibantau dadhikulyāś ca mathyamāne ca bhārata
d tataḥ sa bālo govindo navanītaṃ tadākṣayam
d grasamānas tu tatrātha gopībhir dadṛśe 'tha vai
d dāmnātholūkhale kṛṣṇo gopastrībhiś ca bandhitaḥ
d tadātha śiśunā tena rājaṃs tāv arjunāv ubhau
d samūlaviṭapau bhagnau tad adbhutam ivābhavat
d tatas tau bālyam uttīrṇau kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāv ubhau
d tasminn eva vrajasthāne saptavarṣau babhūvatuḥ
d nīlapītāmbaradharau pītaśvetānulepanau
d babhūvatur vatsapālau kākapakṣadharāv ubhau
d parṇavādyaṃ śrutisukhaṃ vādayantau varānanau
d śuśubhāte vanagatāv udīrṇāv iva pannagau
d mayūrāṅgajakarṇau tau pallavāpīḍadhāriṇau
d vanamālāparikṣiptau sālapotāv ivodgatau
d aravindakṛtāpīḍau rajjuyajñopavītinau
d śikyatumbadharau vīrau gopaveṇupravādakau
d kva cid dhasantāv anyonyaṃ krīḍamānau kva cid vane
d parṇaśayyāsu saṃsuptau kva cin nidrāntaraiṣiṇau
d tau vatsān pālayantau hi śobhayantau mahad vanam
d cañcūryantau ramantau sma rājann evaṃ tadā śubhau
d tato vṛndāvanaṃ gatvā vasudevasutāv ubhau
d bhīṣmaḥ
d govrajaṃ tatra kaunteya cārayantau vijahratuḥ
d tataḥ kadā cid govindo jyeṣṭhaṃ saṃkarṣaṇaṃ vinā
d cacāra tad vanaṃ ramyaṃ ramyarūpo varānanaḥ
d kākapakṣadharaḥ śrīmāñ śyāmaḥ padmanibhekṣaṇaḥ
d śrīvatsenorasā yuktaḥ śaśāṅka iva lakṣmaṇā
d rajjuyajñopavītī sa pītāmbaradharo yuvā
d śvetagandhena liptāṅgo nīlakuñcitamūrdhajaḥ
d rājatā barhipatreṇa mandamārutakampinā
d kva cid gāyan kva cit krīḍan kva cin nṛtyan kva cid dhasan
d gopaveṇuṃ sa madhuraṃ kāmaṃ tad api vādayan
d prahlādanārthaṃ tu gavāṃ kva cid vanagato yuvā
d gokule meghakāle tu cacāra dyutimān prabhuḥ
d bahuramyeṣu deśeṣu vanasya vanarājiṣu
d tāsu kṛṣṇo mudaṃ lebhe krīḍayā bharatarṣabha
d sa kadā cid vane tasmin gobhiḥ saha parivrajan
d bhāṇḍīraṃ nāma dṛṣṭvātha nyagrodhaṃ keśavo mahān
d tasya chāyānivāsāya matiṃ cakre tadā prabhuḥ
d sa tatra vayasā tulyair vatsapālaiḥ sahānagha
d reme sa divasān kṛṣṇaḥ purā svargapure yathā
d taṃ krīḍamānaṃ gopālāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ bhāṇḍīravāsinaḥ
d ramayanti sma bahavo mānyaiḥ krīḍanakais tadā
d anye sma parigāyanti gopā muditamānasāḥ
d gopālāḥ kṛṣṇam evānye gāyanti sma vanapriyāḥ
d teṣāṃ sa gāyatām eva vādayām āsa keśavaḥ
d parṇavādyāntare veṇuṃ tumbavīṇāṃ ca tatra vai
d evaṃ krīḍāntaraiḥ kṛṣṇo gopālair vijahāra saḥ
d tena bālena kaunteya kṛtaṃ lokahitaṃ tadā
d paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vāsudevena bhārata
d hrade nīpavane tatra krīḍitaṃ nāgamūrdhani
d śāsayitvā tu kālīyaṃ sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
d vijahāra tataḥ kṛṣṇo baladevasahāyavān
d dhenuko dāruṇo daityo rājan rāsabhavigrahaḥ
d tadā tālavane rājan baladevena vai hataḥ
d tataḥ kadā cit kaunteya rāmakṛṣṇau vanaṃ gatau
d cārayantau pravṛddhāni godhanāni śubhānanau
d viharantau mudā yuktau vīkṣamāṇau vanāni vai
d kṣvelayantau pragāyantau vicinvantau ca pādapān
d nāmabhir vyāharantau ca vatsān gāś ca paraṃtapau
d ceratur lokasiddhābhiḥ krīḍābhir aparājitau
d tau devau mānuṣīṃ dīkṣāṃ vahantau surapūjitau
d tajjātiguṇayuktābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vanam
d tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahātejās tadā gatvā tu govrajam
d giriyajñaṃ tam evaiṣa prakṛtaṃ gopadārakaiḥ
d bubhuje pāyasaṃ śaurir īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtakṛt
d taṃ dṛṣṭvā gopakāḥ sarve kṛṣṇam eva samarcayan
d pūjyamānas tato gopair divyaṃ vapur adhārayat
d dhṛto govardhano nāma saptāhaṃ parvatas tadā
d śiśunā vāsudevena gavārtham arimardana
d krīḍamānas tadā kṛṣṇaḥ kṛtavān karma duṣkaram
d tad adbhutam ivātrāsīt sarvalokasya bhārata
d devadevaḥ kṣitiṃ gatvā kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mudānvitaḥ
d govinda iti taṃ hy uktvā hy abhyaṣiñcat puraṃdaraḥ
d ity uktvāśliṣya govindaṃ puruhūto 'bhyayād divam
d athāriṣṭa iti khyātaṃ daityaṃ vṛṣabhavigraham
d jaghāna tarasā kṛṣṇaḥ paśūnāṃ hitakāmyayā
d keśinaṃ nāma daiteyaṃ rājan vai hayavigraham
d tathā vanagataṃ pārtha gajāyutabalaṃ hayam
d pragṛhya bhojaputrasya jaghāna puruṣottamaḥ
d āndhraṃ mallaṃ ca cāṇūraṃ nijaghāna mahāsuram
d sunāmānam amitraghnaḥ sarvasainyapuraskṛtam
d mṛgarūpeṇa govindaṃ trāsayām āsa bhārata
d baladevena cāyatnāt samāje muṣṭiko hataḥ
d trāsitaś ca tadā kaṃsaḥ sa hi kṛṣṇena bhārata
d airāvataṃ yuyutsantaṃ mātaṅgānām ivarṣabham
d kṛṣṇaḥ kuvalayāpīḍaṃ hatavāṃs tasya paśyataḥ
d hatvā kaṃsam amitraghnaḥ sarveṣāṃ paśyatāṃ tadā
d abhiṣicyograsenaṃ taṃ pitroḥ pādam avandata
d evamādīni karmāṇi kṛtavān vai janārdanaḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d evaṃ bālye 'pi gopālaiḥ krīḍābhis tau vijahratuḥ
d tatas tau jagmatus tāta guruṃ sāndīpaniṃ punaḥ
d guruśuśrūṣayā yuktau dharmajñau dharmacāriṇau
d vratam ugraṃ mahātmānau vicarantāv avantiṣu
d ahorātraiś catuḥṣaṣṭyā ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vedam āpatuḥ
d lekhyaṃ ca gaṇitaṃ cobhau prāpnutāṃ yadunandanau
d gāndharvavedaṃ citraṃ ca sakalaṃ samavāpatuḥ
d hastiśikṣāśvaśikṣāṃ ca dvādaśāhena cāpatuḥ
d tāv ubhau jagmatur vīrau guruṃ sāndīpaniṃ punaḥ
d dhanurvedacikīrṣārthaṃ dharmajñau dharmacāriṇau
d tāv iṣvastravarācāryam abhigamya praṇamya ca
d tena tau satkṛtau rājan vicarantāv avantiṣu
d pañcāśadbhir ahorātrair daśāṅgaṃ supratiṣṭhitam
d sarahasyaṃ dhanurvedaṃ sakalaṃ tāv avāpatuḥ
d dṛṣṭvā kṛtārthau viprendro gurvarthe tāv acodayat
d ayācatārthaṃ govindaṃ tataḥ sāndīpanir vibhuḥ
d mama putraḥ samudre 'smiṃs timinā cāpavāhitaḥ
d putram ānaya bhadraṃ te bhakṣitaṃ timinā mama
d ārtāya gurave tatra pratiśuśrāva duṣkaram
d aśakyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kartum anyena kena cit
d yaś ca sāndīpaneḥ putraṃ jaghāna bharatarṣabha
d so 'suraḥ samare tābhyāṃ samudre vinipātitaḥ
d tataḥ sāndīpaneḥ putraḥ prasādād amitaujasaḥ
d dīrghakālaṃ gataḥ pretaḥ punar āsīc charīravān
d tad aśakyam acintyaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sumahad adbhutam
d sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ vismayaḥ samajāyata
d aiśvaryāṇi ca sarvāṇi gavāśvaṃ ca dhanāni ca
d sarvaṃ tad upajahrāte gurave rāmakeśavau
d gadāparighayuddheṣu sarvāstreṣu ca keśavaḥ
d paramāṃ mukhyatāṃ prāptaḥ sarvalokeṣu viśrutaḥ
d kaś ca nārāyaṇād anyaḥ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam
d ratham ādityasaṃkāśam ātiṣṭheta śacīpateḥ
d tasya cāpratimo yantā vajrapāṇeḥ priyaḥ sakhā
d mātaliḥ saṃgṛhītā syād anyatra puruṣottamāt
d bhojarājatanūjo 'pi kaṃsas tāta yudhiṣṭhira
d astrajñāne bale vīrye kārtavīryasamo 'bhavat
d tasya bhojapateḥ putrād bhojarājanyavardhanāt
d udvijante sma rājānaḥ suparṇād iva pannagāḥ
d citrakārmukanistriṃśavimalaprāsayodhinaḥ
d śataṃ śatasahasrāṇi pādātās tasya bhārata
d aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi śūrāṇām anivartinām
d abhavan bhojarājasya jāmbūnadamayadhvajāḥ
d rukmakāñcanakakṣyās tu gajās tasya yudhiṣṭhira
d tāvanty eva sahasrāṇi gajānām anivartinām
d te ca parvatasaṃkāśāś citradhvajapatākinaḥ
d babhūvur bhojarājasya nityaṃ pramuditā gajāḥ
d svalaṃkṛtānāṃ śīghrāṇāṃ kareṇūnāṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d abhavad bhojarājasya dvis tāvad dhi mahad balam
d ṣoḍaśāśvasahasrāṇi kiṃśukābhāni tasya vai
d aparas tu mahāvyūhaḥ kiśorāṇāṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d ārohavarasaṃpanno durdharṣaḥ kena cid balāt
d sa ca ṣoḍaśasāhasraḥ kaṃsabhrātṛpuraḥsaraḥ
d sunāmā sarvatas tv enaṃ sa kaṃsaṃ paryapālayat
d ya āsan sarvavarṇās tu hayās tasya yudhiṣṭhira
d sa gaṇo miśrako nāma ṣaṣṭisāhasra ucyate
d kaṃsaroṣamahāvegāṃ dhvajānūpamahādrumām
d mattadvipamahāgrāhāṃ vaivasvatavaśānugām
d śastrajālamahāphenāṃ sādivegamahājalām
d gadāparighapāṭhīnāṃ nānākavacaśaivalām
d rathanāgamahāvartāṃ nānārudhirakardamām
d citrakārmukanistriṃśāṃ rathāśvakalilahradām
d mahāmṛdhanadīṃ ghorāṃ yudhāvartananisvanām
d ko vā nārāyaṇād ekaḥ kaṃsahantā yudhiṣṭhira
d eṣa śakrarathe tiṣṭhaṃs tāny anīkāni bhārata
d vyadhamad bhojaputrasya mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ
d taṃ sabhāsthaṃ sahāmātyaṃ hatvā kaṃsaṃ sahānvayam
d mānayām āsa mānārhāṃ devakīṃ sasuhṛdgaṇām
d yaśodāṃ rohiṇīṃ caiva abhivādya punaḥ punaḥ
d ugrasenaṃ ca rājānam abhiṣicya janārdanaḥ
d arcito yadumukhyais tu bhagavān vāsavānujaḥ
d tataḥ pārthivam āyāntaṃ sahitaṃ sarvarājabhiḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d sarasvatyāṃ jarāsaṃdham ajayat puruṣottamaḥ
d śūrasenapuraṃ tyaktvā sarvayādavanandanaḥ
d dvārakāṃ bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ pratyapadyata keśavaḥ
d pratyapadyata yānāni ratnāni ca bahūni ca
d yathārhaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo nairṛtān pratyapadyata
d tatra vighnaṃ caranti sma daiteyāḥ saha dānavaiḥ
d tāñ jaghāna mahābāhur varadattān mahāsurān
d sa vighnam akarot tatra narako nāma nairṛtaḥ
d trāsanaḥ surasaṃghānāṃ vidito vaḥ prabhāvataḥ
d sa bhūmyāṃ mūrtiliṅgasthaḥ sarvadevāsurāntakaḥ
d mānuṣāṇām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pratīpam akarot tadā
d tvaṣṭur duhitaraṃ bhaumaḥ kaśerum agamat tadā
d gajarūpeṇa jagrāha rucirāṅgīṃ caturdaśīm
d pramathya ca jahāraināṃ hṛtvā ca narako 'bravīt
d narakaḥ
d naṣṭaśokabhayābādhaḥ prāgjyotiṣapatis tadā
d yāni devamanuṣyeṣu ratnāni vividhāni ca
d bibharti ca mahī kṛtsnā sāgareṣu ca yad vasu
d adyaprabhṛti tad devi sahitāḥ sarvanairṛtāḥ
d tavaivopahariṣyanti daityāś ca saha dānavaiḥ
d evam uttamaratnāni bahūni vividhāni ca
d sa jahāra tadā bhaumaḥ strīratnāni ca bhārata
d gandharvāṇāṃ ca yāḥ kanyā jahāra narako balāt
d yāś ca devamanuṣyāṇāṃ sapta cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d caturdaśasahasrāṇām ekaviṃśacchatāni ca
d ekaveṇīdharāḥ sarvāḥ satāṃ mārgam anuvratāḥ
d tāsām antaḥpuraṃ bhaumo 'kārayan maṇiparvate
d audakāyām adīnātmā murasya viṣayaṃ prati
d tāś ca prāgjyotiṣo rājā murasya daśa cātmajāḥ
d nairṛtāś ca yathā mukhyāḥ pālayanta upāsate
d sa eṣa tapasaḥ pāre varadatto mahīsutaḥ
d aditiṃ dharṣayām āsa kuṇḍalārthaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d na cāsuragaṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ sahitaiḥ karma tat purā
d kṛtapūrvaṃ mahāghoraṃ yad akārṣīn mahāsuraḥ
d yaṃ mahī suṣuve devī yasya prāgjyotiṣaṃ puram
d viṣayāntapālāś catvāro yasyāsan yuddhadurmadāḥ
d ādevayānam āvṛtya panthānaṃ paryavasthitāḥ
d trāsanāḥ surasaṃghānāṃ virūpai rākṣasaiḥ saha
d hayagrīvo nisumbhaś ca ghoraḥ pañcajanas tathā
d muraḥ putrasahasraiś ca varadatto mahāsuraḥ
d tadvadhārthaṃ mahābāhur eṣa cakragadāsidhṛk
d jāto vṛṣṇiṣu devakyāṃ vāsudevo janārdanaḥ
d tasyāsya puruṣendrasya lokaprathitatejasaḥ
d nivāso dvārakā tāta vidito vaḥ pradhānataḥ
d atīva hi purī ramyā dvārakā vāsavakṣayāt
d ati vai rājate pṛthvyāṃ pratyakṣaṃ te yudhiṣṭhira
d tasmin devapuraprakhye sā sabhā vṛṣṇyupāśrayā
d yā dāśārhīti vikhyātā yojanāyatavistṛtā
d tatra vṛṣṇyandhakāḥ sarve rāmakṛṣṇapurogamāḥ
d lokayātrām imāṃ kṛtsnāṃ parirakṣanta āsate
d tatrāsīneṣu sarveṣu kadā cid bharatarṣabha
d divyagandhā vavur vātāḥ kusumānāṃ ca vṛṣṭayaḥ
d tataḥ sūryasahasrābhas tejorāśir mahādbhutaḥ
d muhūrtam antarikṣe 'bhūt tato bhūmau pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d madhye tu tejasas tasya pāṇḍaraṃ gajam āsthitaḥ
d vṛto devagaṇaiḥ sarvair vāsavaḥ pratyadṛśyata
d rāmakṛṣṇau ca rājā ca vṛṣṇyandhakagaṇaiḥ saha
d utpatya sahasā tasmai namaskāram akurvata
d so 'vatīrya gajāt tūrṇaṃ pariṣvajya janārdanam
d sasvaje baladevaṃ ca rājānaṃ ca tam āhukam
d uddhavaṃ vasudevaṃ ca vikadruṃ ca mahāmatim
d pradyumnasāmbaniśaṭhān aniruddhaṃ sasātyakim
d gadaṃ sāraṇam akrūraṃ bhānujhilliviḍūrathān
d kṛtavarmācārudeṣṇau dāśārhāṇāṃ purogamān
d pariṣvajya ca dṛṣṭvā ca bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
d vṛṣṇyandhakamahāmātrān pariṣvajyātha vāsavaḥ
d pragṛhya pūjāṃ tair dattāṃ bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥ
d so 'diter vacanāt tāta kuṇḍalārthe janārdana
d uvāca paramaprīto jahi bhaumam iti prabho
d bhīṣmaḥ
d tam uvāca mahābāhuḥ priyamāṇo janārdanaḥ
d nihatya narakaṃ bhaumam āhariṣyāmi kuṇḍale
d evam uktvā tu govindo rāmam evābhyabhāṣata
d pradyumnam aniruddhaṃ ca sāmbaṃ cāpratimaṃ bale
d etāṃś coktvā tadā tatra vāsudevo mahāyaśāḥ
d athāruhya suparṇaṃ vai śaṅkhacakragadāsidhṛt
d yayau tadā hṛṣīkeśo devānāṃ hitakāmyayā
d taṃ prayāntam amitraghnaṃ devāḥ sahapuraṃdarāḥ
d pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayuḥ prītāḥ stuvanto viṣṇum acyutam
d ugrān rakṣogaṇān hatvā narakasya mahāsurān
d kṣurāntān mauravān pāśān ṣaṭsahasraṃ dadarśa saḥ
d saṃchidya pāśāñ śastreṇa muraṃ hatvā sahānvayam
d śilāsaṃghān atikramya niśumbham avapothayat
d yaḥ sahasrasamas tv ekaḥ sarvān devān ayodhayat
d taṃ jaghāna mahāvīryaṃ hayagrīvaṃ mahābalam
d apāratejā durdharṣaḥ sarvayādavanandanaḥ
d madhye lohitagaṅgāyāṃ bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
d audakāyāṃ virūpākṣaṃ jaghāna madhusūdanaḥ
d pañca pañcajanān ghorān narakasya mahāsurān
d tataḥ prāgjyotiṣaṃ nāma dīpyamānam iva śriyā
d puram āsādayām āsa tatra yuddham avartata
d mahad devāsuraṃ yuddhaṃ yad vṛttaṃ bharatarṣabha
d yuddhaṃ na syāt samaṃ tena lokavismayakārakam
d cakralāṅgalasaṃchinnāḥ śaktikhaḍgahatās tadā
d nipetur dānavās tatra samāsādya janārdanam
d aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi dānavānāṃ paraṃtapa
d nihatya puruṣavyāghraḥ pātālavivaraṃ yayau
d trāsanaṃ surasaṃghānāṃ narakaṃ puruṣottamaḥ
d yodhayaty atitejasvī madhuvan madhusūdanaḥ
d tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ tena bhaumena bhārata
d kuṇḍalārthe sureśasya narakeṇa mahātmanā
d muhūrtaṃ lālayitvātha narakaṃ madhusūdanaḥ
d pravṛttacakraṃ cakreṇa pramamātha balād balī
d cakrapramathitaṃ tasya papāta sahasā bhuvi
d uttamāṅgaṃ hatāṅgasya vṛtre vajrahate yathā
d bhūmis tu patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā te vai prādāc ca kuṇḍale
d pradāya ca mahābāhum idaṃ vacanam abravīt
d sṛṣṭas tvayaiva madhuhaṃs tvayaiva nihataḥ prabho
d yathecchasi tathā krīḍan prajās tasyānupālaya
d vāsudevaḥ
d devānāṃ ca munīnāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
d udvejanīyo bhūtānāṃ brahmadviṭ puruṣādhamaḥ
d lokadviṣṭaḥ sutas tubhyaṃ devārir lokakaṇṭakaḥ
d sarvalokanamaskāryām aditiṃ bādhate balī
d kuṇḍale darpasaṃpūrṇas tato me nihato 'suraḥ
d naiva manyus tvayā kāryo yat kṛtaṃ mayi bhāmini
d matprabhāvāc ca te putro labdhavān gatim uttamām
d tasmād gaccha mahābhāge bhārāvataraṇaṃ kṛtam
d bhīṣmaḥ
d nihatya narakaṃ bhaumaṃ satyabhāmāsahāyavān
d sahito lokapālaiś ca dadarśa narakālayam
d athāsya gṛham āsādya narakasya yaśasvinaḥ
d dadarśa dhanam akṣayyaṃ ratnāni vividhāni ca
d maṇimuktāpravālāni vaiḍūryavikṛtāni ca
d aśmasārān arkamaṇīn vimalān sphāṭikān api
d jāmbūnadamayāny eva śātakumbhamayāni ca
d pradīptajvalanābhāni śītaraśmiprabhāṇi ca
d hiraṇyavarṇaṃ ruciraṃ śvetam abhyantaraṃ gṛham
d yat tad arthaṃ gṛhe dṛṣṭaṃ narakasya dhanaṃ bahu
d na hi rājñaḥ kuberasya tāvad dhanasamucchrayaḥ
d dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ purā sākṣān mahendrasadaneṣv api
d hate bhaume nisumbhe ca vāsavaḥ sagaṇo 'bravīt
d dāśārhapatim āsīnam āhṛtya maṇikuṇḍale
d imāni maṇiratnāni vividhāni vasūni ca
d hemasūtrā mahākakṣyās tomarair vīryaśālinaḥ
d bhīmarūpāś ca mātaṅgāḥ pravālavikṛtāḥ kuthāḥ
d vimalāni patākāni vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca
d te ca viṃśatisāhasrā dvis tāvatyaḥ kareṇavaḥ
d aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi deśajāś cottamā hayāḥ
d gobhiś cāvikṛtair yānaiḥ kāmaṃ tava janārdana
d etat te prāpayiṣyāmi vṛṣṇyāvāsam ariṃdama
d āvikāni ca sūkṣmāṇi śayanāny āsanāni ca
d kāmavyāhāriṇaś cāpi pakṣiṇaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
d candanāgarumiśrāṇi yānāni vividhāni ca
d tac ca te prāpayiṣyāmi vṛṣṇyāvāsam ariṃdama
d vasu yat triṣu lokeṣu dharmeṇaivārjitaṃ tvayā
d devagandharvaratnāni daiteyāsurajāni ca
d yāni santīha ratnāni narakasya niveśane
d etat tu garuḍe sarvaṃ kṣipram āropya vāsavaḥ
d dāśārhapatinā sārdham upāyān maṇiparvatam
d tatra puṇyā vavur vātāḥ prabhāś citrāḥ samujjvalāḥ
d prekṣatāṃ surasaṃghānāṃ vismayaḥ samapadyata
d tridaśā ṛṣayaś caiva candrādityau tathā divi
d prabhayā tasya śailasya nirviśeṣam ivābhavat
d anujñātas tu rāmeṇa vāsavena ca keśavaḥ
d prīyamāṇo mahābāhur viveśa maṇiparvatam
d tatra vaiḍūryavarṇāni dadarśa madhusūdanaḥ
d satoraṇapatākāni dvārāṇi śaraṇāni ca
d citragrathitameghābhaḥ prababhau maṇiparvataḥ
d hemacitrapatākaiś ca prāsādair upaśobhitaḥ
d harmyāṇi ca viśālāni maṇisopānavanti ca
d tatrasthā varavarṇābhā dadarśa madhusūdanaḥ
d gandharvāsuramukhyānāṃ priyā duhitaras tadā
d triviṣṭapasame deśe tiṣṭhantam aparājitam
d parivavrur mahābāhum ekaveṇīdharāḥ striyaḥ
d sarvāḥ kāṣāyavāsinyaḥ sarvāś ca niyatendriyāḥ
d vratasaṃtāpajaḥ śoko nātra kāś cid apīḍayat
d arajāṃsi ca vāsāṃsi bibhratyaḥ kauśikāny api
d sametya yadusiṃhasya cakrur asyāñjaliṃ striyaḥ
d ūcuś cainaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ sarvās tāḥ kamalekṣaṇāḥ
d nāradena samākhyātam asmākaṃ puruṣottama
d āgamiṣyati govindaḥ surakāryārthasiddhaye
d so 'suraṃ narakaṃ hatvā nisumbhaṃ muram eva ca
d bhaumaṃ ca saparīvāraṃ hayagrīvaṃ ca dānavam
d tathā pañcajanaṃ caiva prāpsyate dhanam akṣayam
d so 'cireṇaiva kālena yuṣmadbhartā bhaviṣyati
d evam uktvāgamad dhīmān devarṣir nāradas tadā
d tvāṃ cintayānāḥ satataṃ tapo ghoram upāsmahe
d kāle 'tīte mahābāhuṃ kadā drakṣyāma mādhavam
d ity evaṃ hṛdi saṃkalpaṃ kṛtvā puruṣasattama
d tapaś carāma satataṃ rakṣyamāṇā hi dānavaiḥ
d gāndharveṇa vivāhena vivāhaṃ kuru naḥ priyam
d tato 'smatpriyakāmārthaṃ bhagavān mārutaḥ svayam
d yathoktaṃ nāradenātha nacirāt tad bhaviṣyati
d tāsāṃ paramanārīṇām ṛṣabhākṣaṃ puraskṛtam
d dadṛśur devagandharvā gṛṣṭīnām iva gopatim
d tasya candropamaṃ vaktram udīkṣya muditendriyāḥ
d saṃprahṛṣṭā mahābāhum idaṃ vacanam abruvan
d satyaṃ bata purā vāyur idam asmān ihābravīt
d sarvabhūtakṛtajñaś ca maharṣir api nāradaḥ
d viṣṇur nārāyaṇo devaḥ śaṅkhacakragadāsidhṛk
d sa bhaumaṃ narakaṃ hatvā bhartā vo bhavitā hi saḥ
d diṣṭyā tasyarṣimukhyasya nāradasya mahātmanaḥ
d vacanaṃ darśanād eva satyaṃ bhavitum arhati
d yat priyaṃ bata paśyāma vaktraṃ candropamaṃ tu te
d darśanena kṛtārthāḥ sma vayam adya mahātmanaḥ
d uvāca sa yaduśreṣṭhaḥ sarvās tā jātamanmathāḥ
d yathā brūta viśālākṣyas tat sarvaṃ vo bhaviṣyati
d tāni sarvāṇi ratnāni gamayitvātha kiṃkaraiḥ
d striyaś ca gamayitvātha devarṣinṛpakanyakāḥ
d vainateyabhuje kṛṣṇo maṇiparvatam uttamam
d kṣipram āropayāṃ cakre bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
d sapakṣigaṇamātaṅgaṃ savyālamṛgapannagam
d śākhāmṛgagaṇair juṣṭaṃ saprastaraśilātalam
d nyaṅkubhiś ca varāhaiś ca rurubhiś ca niṣevitam
d saprapātamahāsānuṃ vicitraśikhisaṃkulam
d taṃ mahendrānujaḥ śauriś cakāra garuḍopari
d paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānām utpāṭya maṇiparvatam
d upendraṃ baladevaṃ ca vāsavaṃ ca mahābalam
d taṃ ca ratnaugham atulaṃ parvataṃ ca mahābalaḥ
d varuṇasyāmṛtaṃ divyaṃ chatraṃ candropamaṃ śubham
d svapakṣabalavikṣepair mahādriśikharopamaḥ
d dikṣu sarvāsu saṃrāvaṃ sa cakre garuḍo vahan
d ārujan parvatāgrāṇi pādapāṃś ca samutkṣipan
d saṃjahāra mahābhrāṇi vaiśvānarapathaṃ gataḥ
d grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ saptarṣigaṇatejasām
d prabhājālam atikramya candrasūryapathaṃ yayau
d meroḥ śikharam āsādya madhyamaṃ madhusūdanaḥ
d devasthānāni sarvāṇi dadarśa bharatarṣabha
d viśveṣāṃ marutāṃ caiva sādhyānāṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
d bhrājamānāny atikramya aśvinoś ca paraṃtapa
d prāpya puṇyatamaṃ sthānaṃ devalokam ariṃdamaḥ
d śakrasadma samāsādya avaruhya janārdanaḥ
d so 'bhivādya diteḥ pādāv arcitaḥ sarvadaivataiḥ
d brahmadakṣapurogaiś ca prajāpatibhir eva ca
d aditeḥ kuṇḍale divye dadāvātha tadā vibhuḥ
d ratnāni ca parārdhyāṇi rāmeṇa saha keśavaḥ
d pratigṛhya ca tat sarvam aditir vāsavānujam
d pūjayām āsa dāśārhaṃ rāmaṃ ca vigatajvarā
d śacī mahendramahiṣī kṛṣṇasya mahiṣīṃ tadā
d satyabhāmāṃ tu saṃgṛhya adityai vai nyavedayat
d sā tasyāḥ satyabhāmāyāḥ kṛṣṇapriyacikīrṣayā
d aditiḥ
d varaṃ prādād devamātā satyāyai vigatajvarā
d jarāṃ na yāsyasi śubhe yāvad vai kṛṣṇamānuṣam
d bhīṣmaḥ
d sarvagandhaguṇopetā bhaviṣyasi varānane
d vihṛtya satyabhāmā vai saha śacyā sumadhyamā
d śacyāpi samanujñātā yayau kṛṣṇaniveśanam
d saṃpūjyamānas tridaśair maharṣigaṇasevitaḥ
d dvārakāṃ prayayau kṛṣṇo devalokād ariṃdamaḥ
d so 'tipatya mahābāhur dīrgham adhvānam acyutaḥ
d vardhamānapuradvāram āsasāda purottamam
d bhīṣmaḥ
d tāṃ purīṃ dvārakāṃ dṛṣṭvā vibhur nārāyaṇo hariḥ
d hṛṣṭaḥ sarvārthasaṃpannāṃ praveṣṭum upacakrame
d so 'paśyad vṛkṣaṣaṇḍāṃś ca ramyān ārāmajān bahūn
d samantato dvāravatyāṃ nānāpuṣpaphalānvitān
d arkacandrapratīkāśair merukūṭanibhair gṛhaiḥ
d dvārakā racitā ramyaiḥ sukṛtā viśvakarmaṇā
d padmaṣaṇḍākulābhiś ca haṃsasevitavāribhiḥ
d gaṅgāsindhuprakāśābhiḥ parighābhir alaṃkṛtā
d prākāreṇārkavarṇena pāṇḍareṇa virājatā
d viyanmūrdhni niviṣṭena dyaur ivābhraparicchadā
d nandanapratimaiś cāpi miśrakapratimair vanaiḥ
d bhāti caitrarathaṃ divyaṃ pitāmahavanaṃ yathā
d vaibhrājapratimaiś caiva sarvartukusumotkaṭaiḥ
d bhāti tārāparikṣiptā dvārakā dyaur ivāmbare
d bhāti raivatakaḥ śailo ramyasānur mahājiraḥ
d pūrvasyāṃ diśi ramyāyāṃ dvārakāyāṃ vibhūṣaṇam
d dakṣiṇasyāṃ latāveṣṭaḥ pañcavarṇo virājate
d indraketupratīkāśaḥ paścimāṃ diśam āśritaḥ
d sukakṣo rājataḥ śailaś citrapuṣpamahāvanaḥ
d uttarasyāṃ diśi tathā veṇumanto virājate
d mandarādripratīkāśaḥ pāṇḍaraḥ pāṇḍavarṣabha
d citrakambalavarṇābhaṃ pāñcajanyavanaṃ tathā
d sarvartukavanaṃ caiva bhāti raivatakaṃ prati
d latāveṣṭaṃ samantāt tu meruprabhavanaṃ mahat
d bhāti tālavanaṃ caiva puṣpakaṃ puṇḍarīki ca
d sukakṣaṃ parivāryainaṃ citrapuṣpaṃ mahāvanam
d śatapatravanaṃ caiva karavīrakusumbhi ca
d bhāti caitrarathaṃ caiva nandanaṃ ca mahāvanam
d ramaṇaṃ bhāvanaṃ caiva veṇumantaṃ samantataḥ
d bhāti puṣkariṇī ramyā pūrvasyāṃ diśi bhārata
d dhanuḥśataparīṇāhā keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
d mahāpurīṃ dvāravatīṃ pañcāśadbhir mukhair yutām
d praviṣṭo dvārakāṃ ramyāṃ bhāsayantīṃ samantataḥ
d aprameyāṃ mahotsedhāṃ mahāgādhapariplavām
d prāsādavarasaṃpannāṃ śvetaprāsādaśālinīm
d tīkṣṇayantraśataghnībhir yantrajālaiḥ samanvitām
d āyasaiś ca mahācakrair dadarśa dvārakāṃ purīm
d aṣṭau rathasahasrāṇi prākāre kiṅkiṇīkinaḥ
d samucchritapatākāni yathā devapure tathā
d aṣṭayojanavistīrṇām acalāṃ dvādaśāyatām
d dviguṇopaniveśāṃ ca dadarśa dvārakāṃ purīm
d aṣṭamārgāṃ mahākakṣyāṃ mahāṣoḍaśacatvarām
d evaṃ mārgaparikṣiptāṃ sākṣād uśanasā kṛtām
d vyūhānām antarā mārgāḥ sapta caiva mahāpathāḥ
d tatra sā vihitā sākṣān nagarī viśvakarmaṇā
d kāñcanair maṇisopānair upetā janaharṣiṇī
d gītaghoṣamahāghoṣaiḥ prāsādapravaraiḥ śubhā
d tasmin puravaraśreṣṭhe dāśārhāṇāṃ yaśasvinām
d veśmāni jahṛṣe dṛṣṭvā bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥ
d samucchritapatākāni pāriplavanibhāni ca
d kāñcanāgrāṇi bhāsvanti merukūṭanibhāni ca
d sudhāpāṇḍaraśṛṅgaiś ca śātakumbhaparicchadaiḥ
d ratnasānuguhāśṛṅgaiḥ sarvaratnavibhūṣitaiḥ
d saharmyaiḥ sārdhacandraiś ca saniryūhaiḥ sapañjaraiḥ
d sayantragṛhasaṃbādhaiḥ sadhātubhir ivādribhiḥ
d maṇikāñcanabhaumaiś ca sudhāmṛṣṭatalais tathā
d jāmbūnadamayair dvārair vaiḍūryavikṛtārgalaiḥ
d sarvartusukhasaṃsparśair mahādhanaparicchadaiḥ
d ramyasānuguhāśṛṅgair vicitrair iva parvataiḥ
d pañcavarṇasuvarṇaiś ca puṣpavṛṣṭisamaprabhaiḥ
d tulyaiḥ parjanyanirghoṣair nānāvarṇair ivāmbudaiḥ
d mahendraśikharaprakhyair vihitair viśvakarmaṇā
d ālikhadbhir ivākāśam aticandrārkabhāsvaraiḥ
d tair dāśārhamahānāgair babhāse bhavanahradaiḥ
d caṇḍanāgākulair ghorair hradair bhogavatī yathā
d kṛṣṇadhvajopavāhyaiś ca dāśārhāyudharohitaiḥ
d vṛṣṇimattamayūraiś ca strīsahasraprajākulaiḥ
d vāsudevendraparjanyair gṛhameghair alaṃkṛtā
d dadṛśe dvārakātīva meghair dyaur iva saṃvṛtā
d sākṣād bhagavato veśma vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
d dadṛśur devadevasya caturyojanam āyatam
d tāvad eva ca vistīrṇam aprameyaṃ mahādhanaiḥ
d prāsādavarasaṃpannaṃ yuktaṃ jagatiparvataiḥ
d yaṃ cakāra mahābāhus tvaṣṭā vāsavacoditaḥ
d prāsādaṃ padmanābhasya sarvato yojanāyatam
d meror iva gireḥ śṛṅgam ucchritaṃ kāñcanāyutam
d rukmiṇyāḥ pravaro vāso vihitaḥ sa mahātmanā
d satyabhāmā punar veśma sadā vasati pāṇḍaram
d vicitramaṇisopānaṃ yaṃ viduḥ śītavān iti
d vimalādityavarṇābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtam
d vyaktabaddhaṃ vanoddeśaiś caturdiśi mahādhvajam
d sa ca prāsādamukhyo 'tra jāmbavatyā vibhūṣitaḥ
d prabhayā bhūṣaṇaiś citrais trailokyam iva bhāsayan
d yas tu pāṇḍaravarṇābhas tayor antaram āśritaḥ
d viśvakarmākarod enaṃ kailāsaśikharopamam
d jāmbūnadapradīptāgraḥ pradīptajvalanopamaḥ
d sāgarapratimo 'tiṣṭhan merur ity abhiviśrutaḥ
d tasmin gāndhārarājasya duhitā kulaśālinī
d sukeśī nāma vikhyātā keśavena niveśitā
d padmakūṭa iti khyātaḥ padmavarṇo mahāprabhaḥ
d suprabhāyā mahābāho nivāsaḥ paramārcitaḥ
d yas tu sūryaprabho nāma prāsādavara ucyate
d lakṣmaṇāyāḥ kuruśreṣṭha sa dattaḥ śārṅgadhanvanā
d vaiḍūryavaravarṇābhaḥ prāsādo haritaprabhaḥ
d setujālāni yatraiva tatraiva ca niveśitaḥ
d yaṃ viduḥ sarvabhūtāni harir ity eva bhārata
d sa mitravindayā vāso devarṣigaṇapūjitaḥ
d mahiṣyā vāsudevasya bhūṣaṇaṃ sarvaveśmanām
d yas tu prāsādamukhyo 'tra vihitaḥ sarvaśilpibhiḥ
d atīva ramyaḥ so 'py atra prahasann iva tiṣṭhati
d sudattāyāḥ suvāsas tu pūjitaḥ sarvaśilpibhiḥ
d mahiṣyā vāsudevasya ketumān iti viśrutaḥ
d prāsādo virajo nāma virajasko mahātmanaḥ
d upasthānagṛhaṃ tāta keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
d yas tu prāsādamukhyo 'tra yaṃ tvaṣṭā vyadadhāt svayam
d yojanāyataviṣkambhaṃ sarvaratnamayaṃ vibhoḥ
d teṣāṃ tu vihitāḥ sarve rukmadaṇḍāḥ patākinaḥ
d sadane vāsudevasya mārgasaṃjananā dhvajāḥ
d ghaṇṭājālāni tatraiva sarveṣāṃ ca niveśane
d āhṛtya yadusiṃhena vaijayanty acalo mahān
d haṃsakūṭasya yac chṛṅgam indradyumnasaro mahat
d ṣaṣṭitālasamutsedham ardhayojanavistṛtam
d sakiṃnaramahānādaṃ tad apy amitatejasaḥ
d paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam
d ādityapathagaṃ yat tan meroḥ śikharam uttamam
d jāmbūnadamayaṃ divyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam
d tad apy utpāṭya kṛṣṇena svaṃ niveśanam āhṛtam
d bhrājamānaṃ purā tatra sarvauṣadhivibhūṣitam
d yam indrabhavanāc chaurir ājahāra paraṃtapaḥ
d pārijātaḥ sa tatraiva keśavena niveśitaḥ
d lepahastaśatair juṣṭo vimānaiś ca hiraṇmayaiḥ
d vihitā vāsudevena brahmasthalamahādrumāḥ
d padmākulajalopetā ratnasaugandhikotpalāḥ
d maṇimauktikavālūkāḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ sarāṃsi ca
d tāsāṃ paramakūlāni śobhayanti mahādrumāḥ
d sālatālāśvakarṇāś ca śataśākhāś ca rohiṇaḥ
d bhallātakāḥ kapitthāś ca candravṛkṣāś ca campakāḥ
d kharjūrāḥ ketakāś caiva samantāt pariropitāḥ
d ye ca haimavatā vṛkṣā ye ca nandanajās tathā
d āhṛtya yadusiṃhena te 'pi tatra niveśitāḥ
d raktapītāruṇaprakhyāḥ sitapuṣpāś ca pādapāḥ
d sarvartuphalapūrṇās te teṣu kānanasaṃdhiṣu
d sahasrapatrapadmāś ca mandārāś ca sahasraśaḥ
d aśokāḥ karṇikārāś ca tilakā nāgamallikāḥ
d kuravā nāgapuṣpāś ca campakās tṛṇagulmakāḥ
d saptaparṇāḥ kadambāś ca nīpāḥ kuravakās tathā
d ketakyaḥ kesarāś caiva hintālatalatāṭakāḥ
d tālāḥ priyaṅguvakulāḥ piṇḍikā bījapūrakāḥ
d drākṣāmalakakharjūrā mṛdvīkā jambukās tathā
d āmrāḥ panasavṛkṣāś ca aṅkolās tilatindukāḥ
d likucāmrātakāś caiva kṣīrikā kaṇṭakīs tathā
d nālikereṅgudāś caiva utkrośakavanāni ca
d vanāni ca kadalyāś ca jātimallikapāṭalāḥ
d kumudotpalapūrṇāś ca vāpyaḥ kūpāḥ sahasraśaḥ
d bhallātakakapitthāś ca taitabhā bandhujīvakāḥ
d priyaṅgvaśokakāśmaryaḥ prācīnāś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
d priyaṅgubadarībhiś ca yavaiḥ spandanacandanaiḥ
d śamībilvapalāśaiś ca pālāśavaṭapippalaiḥ
d udumbaraiś ca bilvaiś ca pālāśaiḥ pāribhadrakaiḥ
d indravṛkṣārjunaiś caiva aśvatthaiś ciribilvakaiḥ
d saubhañjanakavṛkṣaiś ca bhallaṭair aśvasāhvayaiḥ
d sarjais tāmbūlavallībhir lavaṅgaiḥ kramukais tathā
d vaṃśaiś ca vividhais tatra samantāt pariropitaiḥ
d ye ca nandanajā vṛkṣā ye ca caitrarathe vane
d sarve te yadunāthena samantāt pariropitāḥ
d samākulā mahāvāpyaḥ pītā lohitavālukāḥ
d tasmin gṛhavare nadyaḥ prasannasalilā hradāḥ
d phullotpalajalopetā nānādrumasamākulāḥ
d tasmin gṛhavare nadyo maṇiśarkaravālukāḥ
d mattabarhiṇasaṃghāś ca kokilāś ca madodvahāḥ
d babhūvuḥ paramopetāḥ sarve jagatiparvatāḥ
d tatraiva gajayūthāni tatra gomahiṣās tathā
d nivāsāś ca kṛtās tatra varāhamṛgapakṣiṇām
d viśvakarmakṛtaḥ śailaḥ prākāras tasya veśmanaḥ
d vyaktaṃ kiṣkuśatodyāmaḥ sudhākarasamaprabhaḥ
d tena te ca mahāśailāḥ saritaś ca sarāṃsi ca
d parikṣiptāni harmyasya vanāny upavanāni ca
d bhīṣmaḥ
d evam ālokayāṃ cakrur dvārakām ṛṣabhās trayaḥ
d upendrabaladevau ca vāsavaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
d tatas taṃ pāṇḍaraṃ śaurir mūrdhni tiṣṭhan garutmataḥ
d prītaḥ śaṅkham upādadhmau vidviṣāṃ romaharṣaṇam
d tasya śaṅkhasya śabdena sāgaraś cukṣubhe bhṛśam
d rarāsa ca nabhaḥ sarvaṃ tac citram abhavat tadā
d pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaṃ niśamya kukurāndhakāḥ
d viśokāḥ samapadyanta garuḍasya ca darśanāt
d śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ suparṇaśirasi sthitam
d dṛṣṭvā jahṛṣire kṛṣṇaṃ bhāskarodayatejasam
d tatas tūryapraṇādaś ca bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaḥ
d siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe sarveṣāṃ puravāsinām
d tatas te sarvadāśārhāḥ sarve ca kukurāndhakāḥ
d prīyamāṇāḥ samājagmur ālokya madhusūdanam
d vāsudevaṃ puraskṛtya veṇuśaṅkharavaiḥ saha
d ugraseno yayau rājā vāsudevaniveśanam
d ānandituṃ paryacaran sveṣu veśmasu devakī
d rohiṇī ca yathoddeśam āhukasya ca yā striyaḥ
d hatā brahmadviṣaḥ sarve jayanty andhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
d evam uktaḥ saha strībhir akṣatair madhusūdanaḥ
d tataḥ śauriḥ suparṇena svaṃ niveśanam abhyayāt
d cakārātha yathoddeśam īśvaro maṇiparvatam
d tato dhanāni ratnāni sabhāyāṃ madhusūdanaḥ
d nidhāya puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ pitur darśanalālasaḥ
d tataḥ sāndīpiniṃ pūrvam upaspṛṣṭvā mahāyaśāḥ
d vavande pṛthutāmrākṣaḥ prīyamāṇo mahābhujaḥ
d tathāśruparipūrṇākṣam ānandagatacetasam
d vavande saha rāmeṇa pitaraṃ vāsavānujaḥ
d tābhyāṃ ca mūrdhny upāghrātaḥ keśavaḥ paravīrahā
d yathāśreṣṭham upāgamya sātvatān yadunandanaḥ
d sarveṣāṃ nāma jagrāha dāśārhāṇām adhokṣajaḥ
d tataḥ sarvāṇi vittāni sarvaratnamayāni ca
d bhīṣmaḥ
d vyabhajat tāni tebhyo 'tha sarvebhyo yadunandanaḥ
d sā keśavamahāmātrair mahendrapramukhaiḥ saha
d śuśubhe vṛṣṇiśārdūlaiḥ siṃhair iva girer guhā
d athāsanagatān sarvān uvāca vibudhādhipaḥ
d śubhayā harṣayan vācā mahendras tān mahāyaśāḥ
d kukurāndhakamukhyāṃś ca taṃ ca rājānam āhukam
d yadarthaṃ janma kṛṣṇasya mānuṣeṣu mahātmanaḥ
d yat kṛtaṃ vāsudevena tad vakṣyāmi samāsataḥ
d ayaṃ śatasahasrāṇi dānavānām ariṃdamaḥ
d nihatya puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ pātālavivaraṃ yayau
d yac ca nādhigataṃ pūrvaiḥ prahlādabaliśambaraiḥ
d tad idaṃ śauriṇā vittaṃ prāpitaṃ bhavatām iha
d sapāśaṃ muram ākramya pāñcajanyaṃ ca dhīmatā
d śilāsaṃghān atikramya nisumbhaḥ sagaṇo hataḥ
d hayagrīvaś ca vikrānto dānavo nihato balī
d mathitaś ca mṛdhe bhaumaḥ kuṇḍale cāhṛte punaḥ
d prāptaṃ ca divi deveṣu keśavena mahad yaśaḥ
d vītaśokabhayābādhāḥ kṛṣṇabāhubalāśrayāḥ
d yajanto vividhaiḥ somair makhair andhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
d punar bāṇavadhe śaurim ādityā vasubhiḥ saha
d manmukhābhigamiṣyanti sādhyāś ca madhusūdanam
d evam uktvā tataḥ sarvān āmantrya kukurāndhakān
d sasvaje rāmakṛṣṇau ca vasudevaṃ ca vāsavaḥ
d pradyumnasāmbaniśaṭhān aniruddhaṃ ca sāraṇam
d babhruṃ jhilliṃ gadaṃ bhānuṃ cārudeṣṇaṃ ca vṛtrahā
d satkṛtya sāraṇākrūrau punar ābhāṣya sātyakim
d sasvaje vṛṣṇirājānam āhukaṃ kukurādhipam
d bhojaṃ ca kṛtavarmāṇam anyāṃś cāndhakavṛṣṇiṣu
d āmantrya devapravaro vāsavo vāsavānujam
d tataḥ śvetācalaprakhyaṃ gajam airāvataṃ prabhuḥ
d paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānām āruroha śacīpatiḥ
d pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca divaṃ ca varavāraṇam
d mukhāḍambaranirghoṣaiḥ pūrayantam ivāsakṛt
d haimayantramahākakṣyaṃ hiraṇmayaviṣāṇinam
d manoharakuthāstīrṇaṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam
d anekaśataratnābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtam
d nityasrutamadāsrāvaṃ kṣarantam iva toyadam
d diśāgajaṃ mahāmātraṃ kāñcanasrajam āsthitaḥ
d prababhau mandarāgrasthaḥ pratapan bhānumān iva
d tato vajramayaṃ bhīmaṃ pragṛhya paramāṅkuśam
d yayau balavatā sārdhaṃ pāvakena śacīpatiḥ
d taṃ kareṇugajavrātair vimānaiś ca marudgaṇāḥ
d pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayuḥ prītāḥ kuberavaruṇagrahāḥ
d sa vāyupatham āsthāya vaiśvānarapathaṃ gataḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d prāpya sūryapathaṃ devas tatraivāntaradhīyata
d tataḥ sarvadaśārhāṇām āhukasya ca yāḥ striyaḥ
d nandagopasya mahiṣī yaśodā lokaviśrutā
d revatī ca mahābhāgā rukmiṇī ca pativratā
d satyā jāmbavatī cobhe gāndhārī śiṃśumāpi ca
d viśokā lakṣmaṇā sādhvī sumitrā ketumā tathā
d vāsudevamahiṣyo 'nyāḥ śriyā sārdhaṃ yayus tadā
d vibhūtiṃ draṣṭumanasaḥ keśavasya varāṅganāḥ
d prīyamāṇāḥ sabhāṃ jagmur ālokayitum acyutam
d devakī sarvadevīnāṃ rohiṇī ca puraskṛtā
d dadṛśur devam āsīnaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ halabhṛtā saha
d tau tu pūrvam upakramya rohiṇīm abhivādya ca
d abhyavādayatāṃ devau devakīṃ rāmakeśavau
d devakīṃ saptadevīnāṃ yathāśreṣṭhaṃ ca mātaraḥ
d vavande saha rāmeṇa bhagavān vāsavānujaḥ
d athāsanavaraṃ prāpya vṛṣṇidārapuraskṛtā
d ubhāv aṅkagatau cakre devakī rāmakeśavau
d sā tābhyām ṛṣabhākṣābhyāṃ putrābhyāṃ śuśubhe tadā
d devakī devamāteva mitreṇa varuṇena ca
d tataḥ prāptā yaśodāyā duhitā vai kṣaṇena hi
d jājvalyamānā vapuṣā prabhayātīva bhārata
d ekānaṅgeti yām āhuḥ kanyāṃ tāṃ kāmarūpiṇīm
d yatkṛte sagaṇaṃ kaṃsaṃ jaghāna puruṣottamaḥ
d tataḥ sa bhagavān rāmas tām upākramya bhāminīm
d mūrdhny upāghrāya savyena parijagrāha pāṇinā
d tāṃ ca tatropasaṃgṛhya priyām iva sakhīṃ samām
d dakṣiṇena karāgreṇa parijagrāha mādhavaḥ
d dadṛśus tāṃ sabhāmadhye bhaginīṃ rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
d rukmapadmaśayāṃ padmāṃ śrīm ivottamanāgayoḥ
d athākṣatamahāvṛṣṭyā lājapuṣpaghṛtair api
d vṛṣṇayo 'vākiran prītāḥ saṃkarṣaṇajanārdanau
d sabālāḥ sahavṛddhāś ca sajñātikulabāndhavāḥ
d upopaviviśuḥ prītā vṛṣṇayo madhusūdanam
d pūjyamāno mahābāhuḥ paurāṇāṃ rativardhanaḥ
d viveśa puruṣavyāghraḥ svaveśma madhusūdanaḥ
d rukmiṇyā sahito devyā pramumoda sukhī sukham
d tadanantaraṃ ca satyāyā jāmbavatyāś ca bhārata
d sarvāsāṃ ca yaduśreṣṭhaḥ sarvakālavihāravān
d jagāma ca hṛṣīkeśo rukmiṇyāḥ sa niveśanam
d eṣa tāta mahābāho vijayaḥ śārṅgadhanvanaḥ
d etadarthaṃ ca janmāhur mānuṣeṣu mahātmanaḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ
d dvārakāyāṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ svadāreṣu divāniśam
d sukhaṃ labdhvā mahārāja pramumoda mahāyaśāḥ
d pautrasya kāraṇāc cakre vibudhānāṃ hitaṃ tadā
d savāsavaiḥ suraiḥ sarvair dustaraṃ bharatarṣabha
d bāṇo nāmābhavad rājā baler jyeṣṭhasuto balī
d vīryavān bharataśreṣṭha sa ca bāhusahasravān
d tataś cakre tapas tīvraṃ satyena manasā nṛpa
d rudram ārādhayām āsa sa ca bāṇaḥ samā bahu
d tasmai bahuvarā dattāḥ śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā
d tasmāl labdhvā varān bāṇo durlabhān asurair bhuvi
d sa śoṇitapure rājyaṃ cakārāpratimo bale
d trāsitāś ca surāḥ sarve tena bāṇena pāṇḍava
d vijitya vibudhān sarvān sendrān bāṇaḥ samā bahu
d aśāsata mahad rājyaṃ kubera iva bhārata
d ṛddhyarthaṃ kurute yatnaṃ tasya caivośanā kaviḥ
d tato rājann uṣā nāma bāṇasya duhitā tathā
d rūpeṇāpratimā loke menakāyāḥ sutā yathā
d athopāyena kaunteya aniruddho mahādyutiḥ
d prādyumnis tām uṣāṃ prāpya pracchannaḥ pramumoda ha
d atha bāṇo mahātejās tadā tatra yudhiṣṭhira
d taṃ guhyanilayaṃ jñātvā prādyumniṃ sutayā saha
d gṛhītvā kārayām āsa vastuṃ kārāgṛhe balāt
d sukumāraḥ sukhārho 'tha tadā duḥkham avāpa saḥ
d bāṇena khedito rājann aniruddho mumoha ca
d etasminn eva kāle tu nārado munipuṅgavaḥ
d dvārakāṃ prāpya kaunteya kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaco 'bravīt
d kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābāho yadūnāṃ kīrtivardhana
d tvatpautro bādhyamāno 'tha bāṇenāmitatejasā
d kṛcchraṃ prāpto 'niruddho vai śete kanyāgṛhe sadā
d evam uktvā surarṣir vai bāṇasyātha puraṃ yayau
d nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā tato rājañ janārdanaḥ
d āhūya baladevaṃ vai pradyumnaṃ ca mahādyutim
d āruroha garutmantaṃ tābhyāṃ saha janārdanaḥ
