d tataḥ suparṇam āruhya trayas te puruṣarṣabhāḥ
d jagmuḥ kruddhā mahāvīryā bāṇasya nagaraṃ prati
d athāsādya mahārāja tat puraṃ dadṛśuś ca te
d tāmraprākārasaṃvītāṃ rūpyadvāraiś ca śobhitām
d hemaprāsādasaṃbādhāṃ muktāmaṇivicitritām
d udyānavanasaṃpannāṃ nṛttagītaiś ca śobhitām
d toraṇaiḥ pakṣibhiḥ kīrṇāṃ puṣkariṇyaiś ca śobhitām
d tāṃ purīṃ svargasaṃkāśāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām
d dṛṣṭvā mudā yutāṃ haimāṃ vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ
d tasya bāṇapurasyāsan dvārasthā devatāḥ sadā
d maheśvaro guhaś caiva bhadrakālī ca pāvakaḥ
d etā vai devatā rājan rarakṣus tāṃ purīṃ sadā
d atha kṛṣṇo balāj jitvā dvārapālān yudhiṣṭhira
d susaṃkruddho mahātejāḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
d āsasādottaradvāraṃ śaṃkareṇābhipālitam
d tatra tasthau mahātejāḥ śūlapāṇir maheśvaraḥ
d pinākaṃ saśaraṃ gṛhya bāṇasya hitakāmyayā
d jñātvā tam āgataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
d tatas tau cakratur yuddhaṃ vāsudevamaheśvarau
d tad yuddham abhavad ghoram acintyaṃ romaharṣaṇam
d anyonyaṃ tau tatakṣetām anyonyajayakāṅkṣiṇau
d divyāstrāṇi ca tau devau kruddhau mumucatuś ca tau
d tataḥ kṛṣṇo raṇaṃ kṛtvā muhūrtaṃ śūlapāṇinā
d vijitya taṃ mahādevaṃ tato yuddhe janārdanaḥ
d anyāṃś ca jitvā dvārasthān praviveśa purottamam
d praviśya bāṇam āsādya sa tatrātha janārdanaḥ
d cakre yuddhaṃ mahat kruddhas tena bāṇena pāṇḍava
d bāṇo 'pi sarvaśastrāṇi śitāni bharatarṣabha
d susaṃkruddhas tadā yuddhe pātayām āsa keśave
d punar udyamya śastrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ sarvabāhubhiḥ
d mumoca bāṇaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ prati raṇājire
d tataḥ kṛṣṇas tadā chitvā sarvaśastrāṇi bhārata
d kṛtvā muhūrtaṃ bāṇena yuddhaṃ rājann adhokṣajaḥ
d cakram udyamya rājan vai divyaṃ śastrottamaṃ tataḥ
d sahasrabāhūṃś ciccheda bāṇasyāmitatejasaḥ
d tato bāṇo mahārāja kṛṣṇena bhṛśapīḍitaḥ
d chinnabāhuḥ papātāśu viśākha iva pādapaḥ
d sa pātayitvā bāleyaṃ bāṇaṃ kṛṣṇas tvarānvitaḥ
d prādyumniṃ mokṣayām āsa kṣiptaṃ rājagṛhe tadā
d mokṣayitvātha govindaḥ prādyumniṃ saha bhāryayā
d bāṇasya sarvaratnāni asaṃkhyāni jahāra saḥ
d godhanāny atha sarvasvaṃ sa bāṇasyālaye balāt
d jahāra ca hṛṣīkeśo yadūnāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥ
d tataḥ sa sarvaratnāni cāhṛtya madhusūdanaḥ
d kṣipram āropayāṃ cakre sarvasvaṃ garuḍopari
d tvarayātha sa kaunteya baladevaṃ mahābalam
d pradyumnaṃ ca mahāvīryam aniruddhaṃ mahādyutim
d uṣāṃ ca sundarīṃ rājan bhṛtyadāsīgaṇaiḥ saha
d sarvān etān samāropya ratnāni vividhāni ca
d mudā yukto mahātejāḥ pītāmbaradharo balī
d divyābharaṇacitrāṅgaḥ śaṅkhacakragadāsidhṛk
d āruroha garutmantam udayaṃ bhāskaro yathā
d athāruhya suparṇaṃ sa prayayau dvārakāṃ prati
d praviśya svapuraṃ kṛṣṇo yādavaiḥ sahitas tadā
d bhīṣmaḥ
d pramumoda tadā rājan svargastho vāsavo yathā
d sūditā mauravāḥ pāśā niśumbhanarakau hatau
d kṛtakṣemaḥ punaḥ panthāḥ puraṃ prāgjyotiṣaṃ prati
d śauriṇā pṛthivīpālās trāsitā bharatarṣabha
d dhanuṣaś ca praṇādena pāñcajanyasvanena ca
d meghaprakhyair anīkaiś ca dākṣiṇātyābhisaṃvṛtam
d rukmiṇaṃ trāsayām āsa keśavo bharatarṣabha
d tataḥ parjanyaghoṣeṇa rathenādityavarcasā
d uvāha mahiṣīṃ bhojyām eṣa cakragadādharaḥ
d jārūthyām āhṛtiḥ krāthaḥ śiśupālaś ca nirjitaḥ
d vakraś ca saha śaibyena śatadhanvā ca kṣatriyaḥ
d indradyumno hataḥ kopād yavanaś ca kaśerumān
d hataḥ saubhapatiḥ sālvaḥ sahaiva krathadhanvanā
d parvatānāṃ sahasraṃ ca cakreṇa puruṣottamaḥ
d vibhidya puṇḍarīkākṣo dyumatsenam ayodhayat
d mahendraśikhare caiva nimeṣāntaracāriṇau
d jagrāha bharataśreṣṭha varuṇasyābhitaś carau
d irāvatyām ubhau caitāv agnisūryasamau bale
d gopatis tālaketuś ca nihatau śārṅgadhanvanā
d akṣaprapatane caiva nemihaṃsapatheṣu ca
d ubhau tāv api kṛṣṇena surāṣṭrau vinipātitau
d dagdhā vārāṇasī tāta keśavena mahātmanā
d sānubandhaḥ sarāṣṭraś ca kāśīnām ṛṣabho hataḥ
d prāgjyotiṣaṃ puraśreṣṭham asurair bahubhir vṛtam
d prāpya lohitakūṭāni kṛṣṇena varuṇo jitaḥ
d ajeyo duṣpradharṣaś ca lokapālo mahādyutiḥ
d indradvīpo mahendreṇa gupto maghavatā svayam
d pārijāto hṛtaḥ pārtha keśavena balīyasā
d pāṇḍyaṃ pauṇḍraṃ ca mātsyaṃ ca kaliṅgaṃ ca janārdanaḥ
d jaghāna sahitān sarvān aṅgarājaṃ ca mādhavaḥ
d eṣa caikaśataṃ hatvā rathena kṣatrapuṃgavān
d gāndhārīm avahat kṛṣṇo mahiṣīṃ yādavarṣabhaḥ
d atha gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ krīḍārthaṃ madhusūdanaḥ
d jigāya bharataśreṣṭha kuntyāś ca pramukhe vibhuḥ
d droṇaṃ drauṇiṃ kṛpaṃ karṇaṃ bhīmasenaṃ suyodhanam
d vakrānuyāne sahitāñ jigāya bharatarṣabha
d babhroś ca priyam anvicchann eṣa cakragadādharaḥ
d veṇudārivṛtāṃ bhāryām unmamātha yudhiṣṭhira
d paryāptāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sāśvāṃ sarathakuñjarām
d veṇudārivaśe yuktāṃ jigāya madhusūdanaḥ
d avāpya tapasā vīryaṃ balam ojaś ca bhārata
d trāsitāḥ sagaṇāḥ sarve bāṇena vibudhādhipāḥ
d vajrāśanigadāpāśais trāsayadbhir anekaśaḥ
d tasya nāsīd raṇe mṛtyur devair api savāsavaiḥ
d so 'bhibhūtaś ca kṛṣṇena nihataś ca mahātmanā
d chittvā bāhusahasraṃ tad govindena mahātmanā
d eṣa pīṭhaṃ mahābāhuḥ kaṃsaṃ ca madhusūdanaḥ
d paiṭhakaṃ cātilomānaṃ nijaghāna janārdanaḥ
d jambham airāvataṃ caiva virūpaṃ ca mahāyaśāḥ
d jaghāna bharataśreṣṭha śambaraṃ cārimardanam
d eṣa bhogavatīṃ gatvā vāsukiṃ bharatarṣabha
d nirjitya puṇḍarīkākṣo rauhiṇeyam amocayat
d evaṃ bahūni karmāṇi śiśur eva janārdanaḥ
d kṛtavān puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ saṃkarṣaṇasahāyavān
d evam eṣo 'surāṇāṃ ca surāṇāṃ cāpi sarvaśaḥ
d bhayābhayakaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarvalokeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
d evam eṣa mahābāhuḥ śāstā sarvadurātmanām
d kṛtvā devārtham amitaṃ svasthānaṃ pratipatsyate
d eṣa bhogavatīṃ ramyām ṛṣīkāntāṃ mahāyaśāḥ
d dvārakām ātmasāt kṛtvā sāgaraṃ gamayiṣyati
d bahupuṇyavatīṃ ramyāṃ caityayūpavatīṃ śubhām
d dvārakāṃ varuṇāvāsaṃ pravekṣyati sakānanām
d tāṃ sūryasadanaprakhyāṃ manojñāṃ śārṅgadhanvanaḥ
d visṛṣṭāṃ vāsudevena sāgaraḥ plāvayiṣyati
d surāsuramanuṣyeṣu nāsīn na bhavitā kva cit
d yas tām adhyavasad rājā anyatra madhusūdanāt
d bhrājamānās tu śiśavo vṛṣṇyandhakamahārathāḥ
d taj juṣṭaṃ pratipatsyante nākapṛṣṭhaṃ gatāsavaḥ
d evam eṣa daśārhāṇāṃ vidhāya vidhinā vidhim
d viṣṇur nārāyaṇaḥ somaḥ sūryaś ca bhavitā svayam
d aprameyo 'niyojyaś ca yatrakāmagamo vaśī
d modate bhagavān bhūtair bālaḥ krīḍanakair iva
d naiṣa garbhatvam āpede na yonyām āvasat prabhuḥ
d ātmanas tejasā kṛṣṇaḥ sarveṣāṃ kurute gatim
d yathā budbuda utthāya tatraiva tu nilīyate
d carācarāṇi bhūtāni tathā nārāyaṇe sadā
d na pramātuṃ mahābāhuḥ śakyo bhārata keśavaḥ
d paraṃ hy aparam etad viśvarūpān na vidyate
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā tato bhīṣmo virarāma mahāyaśāḥ
c vyājahārottaraṃ tatra sahadevo 'rthavad vacaḥ
a keśavaṃ keśihantāram aprameyaparākramam
b sarvalokeśvaraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vijñāya puruṣottamam
c pūjyamānaṃ mayā yo vaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ na sahate nṛpāḥ
d kṣipraṃ yuddhāya niryātu śaktaś ced atra me yudhi
a sarveṣāṃ balināṃ mūrdhni mayedaṃ nihitaṃ padam
c evam ukte mayā samyag uttaraṃ prabravītu saḥ
d sa eva hi mayā vadhyo bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a matimantas tu ye ke cid ācāryaṃ pitaraṃ gurum
c arcyam arcitam arcārham anujānantu te nṛpāḥ
a tato na vyājahāraiṣāṃ kaś cid buddhimatāṃ satām
c mānināṃ balināṃ rājñāṃ madhye saṃdarśite pade
a tato 'patat puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ sahadevasya mūrdhani
c adṛśyarūpā vācaś cāpy abruvan sādhu sādhv iti
a āvidhyad ajinaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ bhaviṣyadbhūtajalpakaḥ
c sarvasaṃśayanirmoktā nāradaḥ sarvalokavit
d uvācākhilabhūtānāṃ madhye spaṣṭataraṃ vacaḥ
d kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ nārcayiṣyanti ye narāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d jīvanmṛtās tu te jñeyā na saṃbhāṣyāḥ kadā cana
a tatrāhūtāgatāḥ sarve sunīthapramukhā gaṇāḥ
c saṃprādṛśyanta saṃkruddhā vivarṇavadanās tathā
a yudhiṣṭhirābhiṣekaṃ ca vāsudevasya cārhaṇam
b na syād yathā tathā kāryam evaṃ sarve tadābruvan
b niṣkarṣān niścayāt sarve rājānaḥ krodhamūrchitāḥ
c abruvaṃs tatra rājāno nirvedād ātmaniścayāt
a suhṛdbhir vāryamāṇānāṃ teṣāṃ hi vapur ābabhau
c āmiṣād apakṛṣṭānāṃ siṃhānām iva garjatām
a taṃ balaugham aparyantaṃ rājasāgaram akṣayam
c kurvāṇaṃ samayaṃ kṛṣṇo yuddhāya bubudhe tadā
a pūjayitvā tu pūjārhaṃ brahmakṣatraṃ viśeṣataḥ
c sahadevo nṛṇāṃ devaḥ samāpayata karma tat
a tasminn abhyarcite kṛṣṇe sunīthaḥ śatrukarṣaṇaḥ
c atitāmrekṣaṇaḥ kopād uvāca manujādhipān
a sthitaḥ senāpatir vo 'haṃ manyadhvaṃ kiṃ nu sāṃpratam
c yudhi tiṣṭhāma saṃnahya sametān vṛṣṇipāṇḍavān
a iti sarvān samutsāhya rājñas tāṃś cedipuṃgavaḥ
c yajñopaghātāya tataḥ so 'mantrayata rājabhiḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ sāgarasaṃkāśaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatisāgaram
b saṃvartavātābhihataṃ bhīmaṃ kṣubdham ivārṇavam
c roṣāt pracalitaṃ sarvam idam āha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a bhīṣmaṃ matimatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vṛddhaṃ kurupitāmaham
c bṛhaspatiṃ bṛhattejāḥ puruhūta ivārihā
a asau roṣāt pracalito mahān nṛpatisāgaraḥ
c atra yat pratipattavyaṃ tan me brūhi pitāmaha
a yajñasya ca na vighnaḥ syāt prajānāṃ ca śivaṃ bhavet
c yathā sarvatra tat sarvaṃ brūhi me 'dya pitāmaha
a ity uktavati dharmajñe dharmarāje yudhiṣṭhire
c uvācedaṃ vaco bhīṣmas tataḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
a mā bhais tvaṃ kuruśārdūla śvā siṃhaṃ hantum arhati
c śivaḥ panthāḥ sunīto 'tra mayā pūrvataraṃ vṛtaḥ
a prasupte hi yathā siṃhe śvānas tatra samāgatāḥ
c bhaṣeyuḥ sahitāḥ sarve tatheme vasudhādhipāḥ
a vṛṣṇisiṃhasya suptasya tatheme pramukhe sthitāḥ
c bhaṣante tāta saṃkruddhāḥ śvānaḥ siṃhasya saṃnidhau
a na hi saṃbudhyate tāvat suptaḥ siṃha ivācyutaḥ
b tad idaṃ jñātapūrvaṃ hi tava saṃstotum icchataḥ
c tena siṃhīkaroty etān nṛsiṃhaś cedipuṃgavaḥ
a pārthivān pārthivaśreṣṭha śiśupālo 'lpacetanaḥ
c sarvān sarvātmanā tāta netukāmo yamakṣayam
a nūnam etat samādātuṃ punar icchaty adhokṣajaḥ
c yad asya śiśupālasthaṃ tejas tiṣṭhati bhārata
a viplutā cāsya bhadraṃ te buddhir buddhimatāṃ vara
c cedirājasya kaunteya sarveṣāṃ ca mahīkṣitām
a ādātuṃ hi naravyāghro yaṃ yam icchaty ayaṃ yadā
c tasya viplavate buddhir evaṃ cedipater yathā
a caturvidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ triṣu lokeṣu mādhavaḥ
c prabhavaś caiva sarveṣāṃ nidhanaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
a iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā tataś cedipatir nṛpaḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ rūkṣākṣarā vācaḥ śrāvayām āsa bhārata
 śiśupāla uvāca
a vibhīṣikābhir bahvībhir bhīṣayan sarvapārthivān
c na vyapatrapase kasmād vṛddhaḥ san kulapāṃsanaḥ
a yuktam etat tṛtīyāyāṃ prakṛtau vartatā tvayā
c vaktuṃ dharmād apetārthaṃ tvaṃ hi sarvakurūttamaḥ
a nāvi naur iva saṃbaddhā yathāndho vāndham anviyāt
c tathābhūtā hi kauravyā bhīṣma yeṣāṃ tvam agraṇīḥ
a pūtanāghātapūrvāṇi karmāṇy asya viśeṣataḥ
c tvayā kīrtayatāsmākaṃ bhūyaḥ pracyāvitaṃ manaḥ
a avaliptasya mūrkhasya keśavaṃ stotum icchataḥ
c kathaṃ bhīṣma na te jihvā śatadheyaṃ vidīryate
a yatra kutsā prayoktavyā bhīṣma bālatarair naraiḥ
c tam imaṃ jñānavṛddhaḥ san gopaṃ saṃstotum icchasi
a yady anena hatā bālye śakuniś citram atra kim
c tau vāśvavṛṣabhau bhīṣma yau na yuddhaviśāradau
a cetanārahitaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ yady anena nipātitam
c pādena śakaṭaṃ bhīṣma tatra kiṃ kṛtam adbhutam
d arkapramāṇau tau vṛkṣau yady anena nipātitau
d nāgaś ca pātito yena tatra kiṃ vismayaṃ kṛtam
a valmīkamātraḥ saptāhaṃ yady anena dhṛto 'calaḥ
c tadā govardhano bhīṣma na tac citraṃ mataṃ mama
a bhuktam etena bahv annaṃ krīḍatā nagamūrdhani
c iti te bhīṣma śṛṇvānāḥ paraṃ vismayam āgatāḥ
d matimanto na śaṃsanti sajjanā dharmiṇaḥ sadā
a yasya cānena dharmajña bhuktam annaṃ balīyasaḥ
c sa cānena hataḥ kaṃsa ity etan na mahādbhutam
d kāgahā bagahā vatsasarpahā kharahā tathā
d agnipo māyika iva kathaṃ nārho 'grapūjane
a na te śrutam idaṃ bhīṣma nūnaṃ kathayatāṃ satām
c yad vakṣye tvām adharmajña vākyaṃ kurukulādhama
a strīṣu goṣu na śastrāṇi pātayed brāhmaṇeṣu ca
c yasya cānnāni bhuñjīta yaś ca syāc charaṇāgataḥ
a iti santo 'nuśāsanti sajjanā dharmiṇaḥ sadā
c bhīṣma loke hi tat sarvaṃ vitathaṃ tvayi dṛśyate
a jñānavṛddhaṃ ca vṛddhaṃ ca bhūyāṃsaṃ keśavaṃ mama
c ajānata ivākhyāsi saṃstuvan kurusattama
e goghnaḥ strīghnaś ca san bhīṣma kathaṃ saṃstavam arhati
e   tvadvākyād yadi pūjyate
e evaṃbhūtaś ca yo bhīṣma
a asau matimatāṃ śreṣṭho ya eṣa jagataḥ prabhuḥ
c saṃbhāvayati yady evaṃ tvadvākyāc ca janārdanaḥ
e evam etat sarvam iti sarvaṃ tad vitathaṃ dhruvam
a na gāthā gāthinaṃ śāsti bahu ced api gāyati
c prakṛtiṃ yānti bhūtāni bhūliṅgaśakunir yathā
a nūnaṃ prakṛtir eṣā te jaghanyā nātra saṃśayaḥ
b nadīsutatvāt te cittaṃ cañcalaṃ na sthiraṃ smṛtam
c ataḥ pāpīyasī caiṣāṃ pāṇḍavānām apīṣyate
a yeṣām arcyatamaḥ kṛṣṇas tvaṃ ca yeṣāṃ pradarśakaḥ
c dharmavāk tvam adharmajñaḥ satāṃ mārgād avaplutaḥ
a ko hi dharmiṇam ātmānaṃ jānañ jñānavatāṃ varaḥ
c kuryād yathā tvayā bhīṣma kṛtaṃ dharmam avekṣatā
d cet tvaṃ dharmaṃ vijānāsi yadi prājñā matis tava
a anyakāmā hi dharmajña kanyakā prājñamāninā
b gṛhītā pāṇidharmeṇa rājñā sālvena dhīmatā
c ambā nāmeti bhadraṃ te kathaṃ sāpahṛtā tvayā
a yāṃ tvayāpahṛtāṃ bhīṣma kanyāṃ naiṣitavān nṛpaḥ
c bhrātā vicitravīryas te satāṃ vṛttam anuṣṭhitaḥ
a dārayor yasya cānyena miṣataḥ prājñamāninaḥ
c tava jātāny apatyāni sajjanācarite pathi
a na hi dharmo 'sti te bhīṣma brahmacaryam idaṃ vṛthā
c yad dhārayasi mohād vā klībatvād vā na saṃśayaḥ
a na tv ahaṃ tava dharmajña paśyāmy upacayaṃ kva cit
c na hi te sevitā vṛddhā ya evaṃ dharmam abruvan
a iṣṭaṃ dattam adhītaṃ ca yajñāś ca bahudakṣiṇāḥ
c sarvam etad apatyasya kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm
a vratopavāsair bahubhiḥ kṛtaṃ bhavati bhīṣma yat
c sarvaṃ tad anapatyasya moghaṃ bhavati niścayāt
a so 'napatyaś ca vṛddhaś ca mithyādharmānuśāsanāt
c haṃsavat tvam apīdānīṃ jñātibhyaḥ prāpnuyā vadham
a evaṃ hi kathayanty anye narā jñānavidaḥ purā
c bhīṣma yat tad ahaṃ samyag vakṣyāmi tava śṛṇvataḥ
a vṛddhaḥ kila samudrānte kaś cid dhaṃso 'bhavat purā
c dharmavāg anyathāvṛttaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ so 'nuśāsti ha
a dharmaṃ carata mādharmam iti tasya vacaḥ kila
b ghorāṃ māyāṃ praviṣṭāḥ stha tasmāj jāgrata jāgrata
b ahiṃsā paramo dharma iti tasya vacaḥ kila
c pakṣiṇaḥ śuśruvur bhīṣma satataṃ dharmavādinaḥ
d haṃsasya tad vacaḥ śrutvā muditāḥ sarvapakṣiṇaḥ
d pakṣiṇaḥ
d ūcuś cainaṃ khagā haṃsaṃ parivārya ca sarvaśaḥ
d kathayasva bhavān dharmaṃ pakṣiṇāṃ tat samāsataḥ
d ko hi nāma dvijaśreṣṭha brūhi no dharmam uttamam
d haṃsaḥ
d prajāsv ahiṃsā dharmo vai hiṃsādharmaḥ khagavrajāḥ
d etad evānuboddhavyaṃ dharmādharmaḥ samāsataḥ
d vṛddhahaṃsavacaḥ śrutvā pakṣiṇas te susaṃhitāḥ
d pakṣiṇaḥ
d ūcuś ca dharmalubdhās te smayamānā ivāṇḍajāḥ
d dharmaṃ yaḥ kurute nityaṃ loke dhīrataro 'ṇḍajaḥ
d haṃsaḥ
d sa yatra gacched dharmātmā tan no brūhīha tattvataḥ
d dharmaṃ yaḥ kurute nityaṃ loke sadvṛttim āsthitaḥ
d pakṣiṇaḥ
d sa gacchet sarvalokān vai tathā vai niyataṃ khagāḥ
d jñātvā hi dharmādharmaṃ ca nityaṃ loke dvijottama
d haṃsaḥ
d durlabhaṃ svargalokaṃ tu taṃ kasmāt tvaṃ na gacchasi
d bālā yūyaṃ na jānīdhvaṃ dharmasūkṣmaṃ vihaṃgamāḥ
d dharmaṃ yaḥ kurute loke satataṃ śubhabuddhinā
d sa cāyuṣo 'nte svaṃ dehaṃ tyaktvā svargaṃ tu gacchati
d sa cāham api ca tyaktvā kāle deham imaṃ dvijāḥ
d śiśupālaḥ
d svargalokaṃ gamiṣyāmi iyaṃ dharmasya vai gatiḥ
d evaṃ dharmakathāṃ cakre sa haṃsaḥ pakṣiṇāṃ bhṛśam
d pakṣiṇaḥ śuśruvur bhīṣma satataṃ dharmam eva te
a athāsya bhakṣyam ājahruḥ samudrajalacāriṇaḥ
c aṇḍajā bhīṣma tasyānye dharmārtham iti śuśruma
a tasya caiva samabhyāśe nikṣipyāṇḍāni sarvaśaḥ
c samudrāmbhasy amodanta caranto bhīṣma pakṣiṇaḥ
a teṣām aṇḍāni sarveṣāṃ bhakṣayām āsa pāpakṛt
c sa haṃsaḥ saṃpramattānām apramattaḥ svakarmaṇi
a tataḥ prakṣīyamāṇeṣu teṣv aṇḍeṣv aṇḍajo 'paraḥ
c aśaṅkata mahāprājñas taṃ kadā cid dadarśa ha
c   karmāsyedaṃ bhaved iti
c tato gateṣu haṃseṣu sarveṣu carituṃ tadā
c sthita ātmānam āvṛtya
d tato gateṣu haṃseṣu sarveṣu caritaṃ tadā
d sthita ātmānam āvṛtya taṃ kadā cid dadarśa ha
a tataḥ sa kathayām āsa dṛṣṭvā haṃsasya kilbiṣam
c teṣāṃ paramaduḥkhārtaḥ sa pakṣī sarvapakṣiṇām
a tataḥ pratyakṣato dṛṣṭvā pakṣiṇas te samāgatāḥ
c nijaghnus taṃ tadā haṃsaṃ mithyāvṛttaṃ kurūdvaha
d haṃsavat tvam apīdānīṃ jñātibhyo vadham āpnuyāḥ
d vṛddhahaṃso hatas tatra mithyāvṛtto durātmavān
a te tvāṃ haṃsasadharmāṇam apīme vasudhādhipāḥ
c nihanyur bhīṣma saṃkruddhāḥ pakṣiṇas tam ivāṇḍajam
a gāthām apy atra gāyanti ye purāṇavido janāḥ
c bhīṣma yāṃ tāṃ ca te samyak kathayiṣyāmi bhārata
a antarātmani vinihite
rauṣi patraratha vitatham
c aṇḍabhakṣaṇam aśuci te
karma vācam atiśayate
 śiśupāla uvāca
a sa me bahumato rājā jarāsaṃdho mahābalaḥ
c yo 'nena yuddhaṃ neyeṣa dāso 'yam iti saṃyuge
a keśavena kṛtaṃ yat tu jarāsaṃdhavadhe tadā
c bhīmasenārjunābhyāṃ ca kas tat sādhv iti manyate
a advāreṇa praviṣṭena chadmanā brahmavādinā
c dṛṣṭaḥ prabhāvaḥ kṛṣṇena jarāsaṃdhasya dhīmataḥ
a yena dharmātmanātmānaṃ brahmaṇyam abhijānatā
c naiṣitaṃ pādyam asmai tad dātum agre durātmane
a bhujyatām iti tenoktāḥ kṛṣṇabhīmadhanaṃjayāḥ
c jarāsaṃdhena kauravya kṛṣṇena vikṛtaṃ kṛtam
a yady ayaṃ jagataḥ kartā yathainaṃ mūrkha manyase
c kasmān na brāhmaṇaṃ samyag ātmānam avagacchati
a idaṃ tv āścaryabhūtaṃ me yad ime pāṇḍavās tvayā
c apakṛṣṭāḥ satāṃ mārgān manyante tac ca sādhv iti
a atha vā naitad āścaryaṃ yeṣāṃ tvam asi bhārata
c strīsadharmā ca vṛddhaś ca sarvārthānāṃ pradarśakaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā rūkṣaṃ rūkṣākṣaraṃ bahu
c cukopa balināṃ śreṣṭho bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
a tasya padmapratīkāśe svabhāvāyatavistṛte
c bhūyaḥ krodhābhitāmrānte rakte netre babhūvatuḥ
a triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ cāsya dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
c lalāṭasthāṃ trikūṭasthāṃ gaṅgāṃ tripathagām iva
a dantān saṃdaśatas tasya kopād dadṛśur ānanam
c yugānte sarvabhūtāni kālasyeva didhakṣataḥ
a utpatantaṃ tu vegena jagrāhainaṃ manasvinam
c bhīṣma eva mahābāhur mahāsenam iveśvaraḥ
a tasya bhīmasya bhīṣmeṇa vāryamāṇasya bhārata
c guruṇā vividhair vākyaiḥ krodhaḥ praśamam āgataḥ
a nāticakrāma bhīṣmasya sa hi vākyam ariṃdamaḥ
c samuddhūto ghanāpāye velām iva mahodadhiḥ
a śiśupālas tu saṃkruddhe bhīmasene narādhipa
c nākampata tadā vīraḥ pauruṣe sve vyavasthitaḥ
a utpatantaṃ tu vegena punaḥ punar ariṃdamaḥ
c na sa taṃ cintayām āsa siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā
a prahasaṃś cābravīd vākyaṃ cedirājaḥ pratāpavān
c bhīmasenam atikruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaparākramam
a muñcainaṃ bhīṣma paśyantu yāvad enaṃ narādhipāḥ
c matpratāpāgninirdagdhaṃ pataṃgam iva vahninā
a tataś cedipater vākyaṃ tac chrutvā kurusattamaḥ
c bhīmasenam uvācedaṃ bhīṣmo matimatāṃ varaḥ
d naiṣā cedipater buddhir yayā tv āhvayate 'cyutam
d bhīmasena mahābāho kṛṣṇe 'sya vadhaniścayaḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a cedirājakule jātas tryakṣa eṣa caturbhujaḥ
c rāsabhārāvasadṛśaṃ rurāva ca nanāda ca
a tenāsya mātāpitarau tresatus tau sabāndhavau
c vaikṛtaṃ tac ca tau dṛṣṭvā tyāgāya kurutāṃ matim
a tataḥ sabhāryaṃ nṛpatiṃ sāmātyaṃ sapurohitam
c cintāsaṃmūḍhahṛdayaṃ vāg uvācāśarīriṇī
a eṣa te nṛpate putraḥ śrīmāñ jāto mahābalaḥ
c tasmād asmān na bhetavyam avyagraḥ pāhi vai śiśum
a na caivaitasya mṛtyus tvaṃ na kālaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ
c mṛtyur hantāsya śastreṇa sa cotpanno narādhipa
a saṃśrutyodāhṛtaṃ vākyaṃ bhūtam antarhitaṃ tataḥ
c putrasnehābhisaṃtaptā jananī vākyam abravīt
a yenedam īritaṃ vākyaṃ mamaiva tanayaṃ prati
c prāñjalis taṃ namasyāmi bravītu sa punar vacaḥ
d yāthātathyena bhagavān devo vā yadi vetaraḥ
d mahad balaṃ mahad bhūtam ity uktvā punar uttaram
a śrotum icchāmi putrasya ko 'sya mṛtyur bhaviṣyati
c antarhitaṃ tato bhūtam uvācedaṃ punar vacaḥ
a yenotsaṅge gṛhītasya bhujāv abhyadhikāv ubhau
c patiṣyataḥ kṣititale pañcaśīrṣāv ivoragau
a tṛtīyam etad bālasya lalāṭasthaṃ ca locanam
c nimajjiṣyati yaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'sya mṛtyur bhaviṣyati
a tryakṣaṃ caturbhujaṃ śrutvā tathā ca samudāhṛtam
c dharaṇyāṃ pārthivāḥ sarve abhyagacchan didṛkṣavaḥ
a tān pūjayitvā saṃprāptān yathārhaṃ sa mahīpatiḥ
c ekaikasya nṛpasyāṅke putram āropayat tadā
a evaṃ rājasahasrāṇāṃ pṛthaktvena yathākramam
c śiśur aṅke samārūḍho na tat prāpa nidarśanam
d etad eva tu saṃśrutya dvāravatyāṃ mahābalau
a tataś cedipuraṃ prāptau saṃkarṣaṇajanārdanau
c yādavau yādavīṃ draṣṭuṃ svasāraṃ tāṃ pitus tadā
d pitṛsvasāraṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā samāśvāsya mahābhujau
d tau dāmaghoṣaṃ rājānam abhivādya yathākramam
a abhivādya yathānyāyaṃ yathājyeṣṭhaṃ nṛpāṃś ca tān
c kuśalānāmayaṃ pṛṣṭvā niṣaṇṇau rāmakeśavau
a abhyarcitau tadā vīrau prītyā cābhyadhikaṃ tataḥ
c putraṃ dāmodarotsaṅge devī saṃnyadadhāt svayam
a nyastamātrasya tasyāṅke bhujāv abhyadhikāv ubhau
c petatus tac ca nayanaṃ nimamajja lalāṭajam
a tad dṛṣṭvā vyathitā trastā varaṃ kṛṣṇam ayācata
c dadasva me varaṃ kṛṣṇa bhayārtāyā mahābhuja
a tvaṃ hy ārtānāṃ samāśvāso bhītānām abhayaṃkaraḥ
b evam uktas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ provāca yadunandanaḥ
b sa taṃ dvyakṣaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā samāśvāsya mahābhujaḥ
b śrutvā pitṛṣvasur vākyaṃ bhaktānām abhayapradaḥ
c pitṛṣvasāraṃ mā bhaiṣīr ity uvāca janārdanaḥ
a dadāni kaṃ varaṃ kiṃ vā karavāṇi pitṛṣvasaḥ
c śakyaṃ vā yadi vāśakyaṃ kariṣyāmi vacas tava
a evam uktā tataḥ kṛṣṇam abravīd yadunandanam
c śiśupālasyāparādhān kṣamethās tvaṃ mahābala
d matkṛte yaduśārdūla viddhy enaṃ me varaṃ prabho
d ity uktaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ pratyuvāca mahābalaḥ
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a aparādhaśataṃ kṣāmyaṃ mayā hy asya pitṛṣvasaḥ
c putrasya te vadhārhāṇāṃ mā tvaṃ śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
d evam etat purāvṛttaṃ śiśāv asmin vṛkodara
d sa jānann ātmano mṛtyuṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yadusukhāvaham
 bhīṣma uvāca
a evam eṣa nṛpaḥ pāpaḥ śiśupālaḥ sumandadhīḥ
c tvāṃ samāhvayate vīra govindavaradarpitaḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a naiṣā cedipater buddhir yayā tvāhvayate 'cyutam
c nūnam eṣa jagadbhartuḥ kṛṣṇasyaiva viniścayaḥ
a ko hi māṃ bhīmasenādya kṣitāv arhati pārthivaḥ
c kṣeptuṃ daivaparītātmā yathaiṣa kulapāṃsanaḥ
a eṣa hy asya mahābāho tejoṃśaś ca harer dhruvam
c tam eva punar ādātum icchat pṛthuyaśā hariḥ
a yenaiṣa kuruśārdūla śārdūla iva cedirāṭ
c garjaty atīva durbuddhiḥ sarvān asmān acintayan
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato na mamṛṣe caidyas tad bhīṣmavacanaṃ tadā
c uvāca cainaṃ saṃkruddhaḥ punar bhīṣmam athottaram
 śiśupāla uvāca
a dviṣatāṃ no 'stu bhīṣmaiṣa prabhāvaḥ keśavasya yaḥ
c yasya saṃstavavaktā tvaṃ bandivat satatotthitaḥ
a saṃstavāya mano bhīṣma pareṣāṃ ramate sadā
c yadi saṃstauṣi rājñas tvam imaṃ hitvā janārdanam
a daradaṃ stuhi bāhlīkam imaṃ pārthivasattamam
c jāyamānena yeneyam abhavad dāritā mahī
a vaṅgāṅgaviṣayādhyakṣaṃ sahasrākṣasamaṃ bale
c stuhi karṇam imaṃ bhīṣma mahācāpavikarṣaṇam
d yasyeme kuṇḍale divye sahaje devanirmite
d kavacaṃ ca mahābāho bālārkasadṛśaprabham
d vāsavapratimo yena jarāsaṃdho 'tidurjayaḥ
d vijito bāhuyuddhena dehabhedaṃ ca lambhitaḥ
d stuhi bhīṣmabāhūru vīrau ca bhuvi viśrutau
a droṇaṃ drauṇiṃ ca sādhu tvaṃ pitāputrau mahārathau
c stuhi stutyāv imau bhīṣma satataṃ dvijasattamau
a yayor anyataro bhīṣma saṃkruddhaḥ sacarācarām
c imāṃ vasumatīṃ kuryād aśeṣām iti me matiḥ
a droṇasya hi samaṃ yuddhe na paśyāmi narādhipam
c aśvatthāmnas tathā bhīṣma na caitau stotum icchasi
a śalyādīn api kasmāt tvaṃ na stauṣi vasudhādhipān
c stavāya yadi te buddhir vartate bhīṣma sarvadā
a kiṃ hi śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ yad vṛddhānāṃ tvayā nṛpa
c purā kathayatāṃ nūnaṃ na śrutaṃ dharmavādinām
a ātmanindātmapūjā ca paranindā parastavaḥ
c anācaritam āryāṇāṃ vṛttam etac caturvidham
a yad astavyam imaṃ śaśvan mohāt saṃstauṣi bhaktitaḥ
c keśavaṃ tac ca te bhīṣma na kaś cid anumanyate
a kathaṃ bhojasya puruṣe vargapāle durātmani
c samāveśayase sarvaṃ jagat kevalakāmyayā
a atha vaiṣā na te bhaktiḥ pakṛtiṃ yāti bhārata
c mayaiva kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ bhūliṅgaśakunir yathā
a bhūliṅgaśakunir nāma pārśve himavataḥ pare
c bhīṣma tasyāḥ sadā vācaḥ śrūyante 'rthavigarhitāḥ
a mā sāhasam itīdaṃ sā satataṃ vāśate kila
c sāhasaṃ cātmanātīva carantī nāvabudhyate
a sā hi māṃsārgalaṃ bhīṣma mukhāt siṃhasya khādataḥ
c dantāntaravilagnaṃ yat tad ādatte 'lpacetanā
a icchataḥ sā hi siṃhasya bhīṣma jīvaty asaṃśayam
c tadvat tvam apy adharmajña sadā vācaḥ prabhāṣase
a icchatāṃ pārthivendrāṇāṃ bhīṣma jīvasy asaṃśayam
c lokavidviṣṭakarmā hi nānyo 'sti bhavatā samaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataś cedipateḥ śrutvā bhīṣmaḥ sa kaṭukaṃ vacaḥ
c uvācedaṃ vaco rājaṃś cedirājasya śṛṇvataḥ
a icchatāṃ kila nāmāhaṃ jīvāmy eṣāṃ mahīkṣitām
c yo 'haṃ na gaṇayāmy etāṃs tṛṇānīva narādhipān
a evam ukte tu bhīṣmeṇa tataḥ saṃcukrudhur nṛpāḥ
c ke cij jahṛṣire tatra ke cid bhīṣmaṃ jagarhire
a ke cid ūcur maheṣvāsāḥ śrutvā bhīṣmasya tad vacaḥ
c pāpo 'valipto vṛddhaś ca nāyaṃ bhīṣmo 'rhati kṣamām
a hanyatāṃ durmatir bhīṣmaḥ paśuvat sādhv ayaṃ nṛpaiḥ
c sarvaiḥ sametya saṃrabdhair dahyatāṃ vā kaṭāgninā
a iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā tataḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
c uvāca matimān bhīṣmas tān eva vasudhādhipān
a uktasyoktasya nehāntam ahaṃ samupalakṣaye
c yat tu vakṣyāmi tat sarvaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ vasudhādhipāḥ
a paśuvad ghātanaṃ vā me dahanaṃ vā kaṭāgninā
b etac chrutvā tato bhīṣmas teṣāṃ pārthivasaṃsadi
b uvāca vākyaṃ dharmātmā bhīṣmas tān kṣatriyāṃs tataḥ
c kriyatāṃ mūrdhni vo nyastaṃ mayedaṃ sakalaṃ padam
a eṣa tiṣṭhati govindaḥ pūjito 'smābhir acyutaḥ
c yasya vas tvarate buddhir maraṇāya sa mādhavam
a kṛṣṇam āhvayatām adya yuddhe śārṅgagadādharam
c yāvad asyaiva devasya dehaṃ viśatu pātitaḥ
d pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ yo vai pratisamo bhavet
d duryodhanaṃ ca rājendram atikramya mahābhujam
d jayadrathaṃ ca rājānaṃ kṛtāsraṃ dṛḍhavikramam
d drumaṃ kiṃpuruṣācāryaṃ loke prathitavikramam
d atikramya mahāvīryaṃ kiṃ praśaṃsasi keśavam
d vṛddhaṃ ca bhāratācāryaṃ tathā śāradvataṃ kṛpam
d atikramya mahāvīryaṃ kiṃ praśaṃsasi keśavam
d dhanurdharāṇāṃ pravaraṃ rukmiṇaṃ puruṣottamam
d atikramya mahāvīryaṃ kiṃ praśaṃsasi keśavam
d bhīṣmakaṃ ca mahāvīryaṃ dantavakraṃ ca bhūmipam
d bhagadattaṃ yūpaketuṃ jayatsenaṃ ca māgadham
d virāṭadrupadau cobhau śakuniṃ ca bṛhadbalam
d vindānuvindāv āvantyau pāṇḍyaṃ śvetam athottamam
d śaṅkhaṃ ca sumahābhāgaṃ vṛṣasenaṃ ca māninam
d ekalavyaṃ ca vikrāntaṃ kāliṅgaṃ ca mahāratham
d atikramya mahāvīryaṃ kiṃ praśaṃsasi keśavam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ śrutvaiva bhīṣmasya cedirāḍ uruvikramaḥ
c yuyutsur vāsudevena vāsudevam uvāca ha
a āhvaye tvāṃ raṇaṃ gaccha mayā sārdhaṃ janārdana
c yāvad adya nihanmi tvāṃ sahitaṃ sarvapāṇḍavaiḥ
a saha tvayā hi me vadhyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇa sarvathā
c nṛpatīn samatikramya yair arājā tvam arcitaḥ
a ye tvāṃ dāsam arājānaṃ bālyād arcanti durmatim
c anarham arhavat kṛṣṇa vadhyās ta iti me matiḥ
e ity uktvā rājaśārdūlas tasthau garjann amarṣaṇaḥ
f paśyatāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ śiśupālaḥ pratāpavān
f sa raṇāyaiva saṃkruddhaḥ saṃnaddhaḥ sarvarājabhiḥ
f sunīthaḥ prayayau kṣipraṃ pārthayajñajighāṃsayā
f tataś cakragadāpāṇiḥ keśavaḥ keśihā hariḥ
f sadhvajaṃ ratham āsthāya dārukeṇa susatkṛtam
f bhīṣmeṇa dattahasto 'sau yuddhāya samupasthitaḥ
f tena pāpasvabhāvena kopitān sarvapārthivān
f āsasāda tadā kṛṣṇaḥ sajjitaikarathe sthitaḥ
f tataḥ puṣkarapatrākṣaṃ garuḍadhvajam acyutam
f divākaram ivodyantaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
f dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam athāyāntaṃ pratapantam ivaujasā
f sthitaṃ puṣparathe divye puṣpaketum ivāparam
f yathārhaṃ keśave vṛttim avaśāḥ pratipedire
f tān uvāca mahābāhur mahāsuranibarhaṇaḥ
f vṛṣṇivīras tadā rājan sāntvayan paravīrahā
f apeta sabalāḥ sarva āśvastā mama śāsanāt
f mā duṣṭān dūṣayet pāpa eṣa vai sarvapārthivān
a evam ukte tataḥ kṛṣṇo mṛdupūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
c uvāca pārthivān sarvāṃs tatsamakṣaṃ ca pāṇḍavān
a eṣa naḥ śatrur atyantaṃ pārthivāḥ sātvatīsutaḥ
c sātvatānāṃ nṛśaṃsātmā na hito 'napakāriṇām
a prāgjyotiṣapuraṃ yātān asmāñ jñātvā nṛśaṃsakṛt
b babhror bhāryām athādatte mamāpaśyanta yādavāḥ
b tadānīṃ hantum ārabdho na bhajyenam athānyatā
b tasyarthe va bhavo vadhdmā sic
tadāsan saṃvṛtaṃ nṛpān
b atiprasaṃgadoṣeṇa tām ādāya ca kevalam
b babhrave dattavān pūrvaṃ yuṣmākaṃ paśyatāṃ mithaḥ
b gomante parvate pūrvaṃ nihate māgadhe 'pi ca
b anena ca sṛgālena na vai pādidaṃ sic kila
b tataḥ kuṇḍinayātrāyāṃ kṛtavān vipriyāṇi me
b tāni sarvāṇi saṃkhyātuṃ na śakṣyāmi narādhipāḥ
b kākatālīyanyāyena sarvaṃ me ripunāśanam
b etasmin kalahe bhūpāḥ koṭiśas tu mayā hatāḥ
b kṣamā lālajjayāmy adya sic
duṣṭastrīharaṇaṃ yathā
b pitṛṣvasre priyaṃ bhūpāḥ kariṣye 'nyaṃ mahattaram
c adahad dvārakām eṣa svasrīyaḥ san narādhipāḥ
a krīḍato bhojarājanyān eṣa raivatake girau
c hatvā baddhvā ca tān sarvān upāyāt svapuraṃ purā
a aśvamedhe hayaṃ medhyam utsṛṣṭaṃ rakṣibhir vṛtam
c pitur me yajñavighnārtham aharat pāpaniścayaḥ
a sauvīrān pratipattau ca babhror eṣa yaśasvinaḥ
c bhāryām abhyaharan mohād akāmāṃ tām ito gatām
a eṣa māyāpraticchannaḥ karūṣārthe tapasvinīm
c jahāra bhadrāṃ vaiśālīṃ mātulasya nṛśaṃsakṛt
d viśālarājño duhitāṃ mama pitrā vṛtāṃ satīm
d anena kṛtvā saṃdhānaṃ karūśena jihīrṣayā
d vṛṣṇidārān vilupyaiṣa hatvā ca kukurāndhakān
d pāpabuddhir upātiṣṭhat saṃpraviśya sasaṃbhramam
d jarāsaṃdhaṃ samāśritya kṛtavān vipriyāṇi me
d tāni sarvāṇi saṃkhyātuṃ na śakṣyāmi narādhipāḥ
d evam etad aparyantam eṣa vṛṣṇiṣu kilbiṣī
d asmākam ayam ārambhāc cakāra paramānṛjuḥ
d śataṃ kṣantavyam asmābhir vadhārhāṇāṃ kilāgasām
d baddho 'smi samayair ghorair māturasyaiva saṃgare
d tat tathā śatam asmākaṃ kṣāntaṃ kṣayakaraṃ mayā
d dvau tu me vadhakāle 'smin na kṣantavyau kathaṃ cana
d yajñavighnakaraṃ hanyāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca durhṛdam
d iti me vartate bhāvas tam atīyāṃ kathaṃ nv aham
a pitṛṣvasuḥ kṛte duḥkhaṃ sumahan marṣayāmy aham
c diṣṭyā tv idaṃ sarvarājñāṃ saṃnidhāv adya vartate
a paśyanti hi bhavanto 'dya mayy atīva vyatikramam
c kṛtāni tu parokṣaṃ me yāni tāni nibodhata
a imaṃ tv asya na śakṣyāmi kṣantum adya vyatikramam
b ākālikaṃ puṣpaphalaṃ rāṣṭrakṣobhaṃ vinirdiśet
b vanaspatiḥ pūjyamānaḥ pūjito 'pūjito 'pi vā
b yadā bhajyeta vātena bhidyate namito 'pi vā
b agnivāyubhayaṃ vidyāc chreṣṭho vāpi vinaśyati
b diśaḥ sarvāś ca dīpyante jāyante rājavibhramāḥ
b bhidyamāno yadā vṛkṣo ninadec cāpi pātitaḥ
b saha rāṣṭraṃ ca patitaṃ na taṃ vṛkṣaṃ prapātayet
b athainaṃ chedayet kaś cit pratikruddho vanaspatiḥ
b chettā bhettā patiś caiva kṣipram eva naśiṣyati
b devatānāṃ ca patanaṃ maṇṭapānāṃ ca pātanam
b acalānāṃ prakampaś ca tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
b arcā yatra pranṛtyanti nadanti ca hasanti ca
b unmīlanti nimīlanti rāṣṭrakṣobhaṃ vinirdiśet
b śilā yadi prasiñcanti snehāṃś codakasaṃbhavān
b anyad vā vikṛtaṃ kiṃ cit tad bhayasya nidarśanam
b mriyante vā mahāmātrā rājā saparivārakaḥ
b purasya vā bhaved vyādhī rāṣṭre deśe ca vibhramāḥ
b devatānāṃ yadāvāse rājñāṃ vā yatra veśmani
b bhāṇḍāgārāyudhāgāre niviśeta yadā madhu
b sarvaṃ tadā bhavet sthānaṃ hanyamānaṃ balīyasā
b āgantukaṃ bhayaṃ tatra bhaved ity eva nirdiśet
b pādapaś caiva yo yatra raktaṃ sravati śoṇitam
b dantāgrāt kuñjaro vāpi śṛṅgād vā vṛṣabhas tathā
b pādapād rāṣṭravibhraṃśaḥ kuñjarād rājavibhramaḥ
b gobrāhmaṇavināśaḥ syād vṛṣabhasyeti nirdiśet
b chatraṃ narapater yatra nipatet pṛthivītale
b sarāṣṭro nṛpatī rājan kṣipram eva vinaśyati
b devāgāreṣu vā yatra rājño vā yatra veśmani
b vikṛtaṃ yadi dṛśyeta nāgāvāseṣu vā punaḥ
b tasya deśasya pīḍā syād rājño janapadasya vā
b anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoram atidurbhikṣam ādiśet
c avalepād vadhārhasya samagre rājamaṇḍale
a rukmiṇyām asya mūḍhasya prārthanāsīn mumūrṣataḥ
c na ca tāṃ prāptavān mūḍhaḥ śūdro vedaśrutiṃ yathā
a evamādi tataḥ sarve sahitās te narādhipāḥ
b garhaṇāṃ śiśupālasya vāsudevena śrāvitāḥ
b rathopasthe dhanuṣmantaṃ śarān saṃdadhataṃ ruṣā
c vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā cedirājaṃ vyagarhayan
d vihāya paramodvignāś cedirājaṃ camūmukhe
d tāṃs tu vipradrutān sarvān sāśvapattirathadvipān
d dāritān vṛṣṇivīreṇa trāsitān uruvikramān
d kṛṣṇatejohatān sarvān samīkṣya vasudhādhipān
d śiśupālo rathenaikaḥ pratyupāyāt sa keśavam
d ruṣā tāmrekṣaṇo rājañ śalabhaḥ pāvakaṃ yathā
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tato yuddhāya saṃnaddhaṃ cedirājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d dṛṣṭvā matimatāṃ śreṣṭho nāradaṃ samuvāca ha
d antarikṣe ca bhūmau ca na te 'sty aviditaṃ kva cit
d yāni rājavināśāya bhaumāni ca khagāni ca
d nimittānīha jāyante utpātāś ca pṛthagvidhāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d etad icchāmi kārtsnyena śrotuṃ tvatto mahāmune
d ity evaṃ matimān vipraḥ kururājasya dhīmataḥ
d nāradaḥ
d pṛcchataḥ sarvam avyagram ācacakṣe mahāyaśāḥ
d parākramaṃ ca mārgaṃ ca saṃnipātaṃ samucchrayam
d ārohaṇaṃ kuruśreṣṭha anyonyaṃ prati sarpaṇam
d raśmīnāṃ vyatisaṃsargaṃ vyāyāmaṃ vṛttipīḍanam
d darśanādarśanaṃ caiva adṛśyānāṃ ca darśanam
d hāniṃ vṛddhiṃ ca hrāsaṃ ca varṇasthānaṃ balābalam
d sarvam etat parīkṣeta grahāṇāṃ grahakovidaḥ
d bhaumāḥ pūrvaṃ pravartante khecarāś ca tataḥ param
d utpadyante ca loke 'sminn utpātā devanirmitāḥ
d yadā tu sarvabhūtānāṃ chāyā na parivartate
d apareṇa gate sūrye tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
d acchāye vimalacchāyā praticchāyeva lakṣyate
d yatra caityakavṛkṣāṇāṃ tatra vidyān mahad bhayam
d śīrṇaparṇapravālāś ca śuṣkaparṇāś ca caityakāḥ
d apabhraṣṭapravālāś ca tatrābhāvaṃ vinirdiśet
d snigdhapatrapravālāś ca dṛśyante yatra caityakāḥ
d īhamānāś ca dṛṣṭāś ca bhāvas tatra na saṃśayaḥ
d puṣpe puṣpaṃ prajāyeta phale vā phalam āśritam
d rājā vā rājamātro vā maraṇāyopapadyate
d prāvṛṭ charadi hemante vasante vāpi sarvaśaḥ
d akālajaṃ puṣpaphalaṃ rāṣṭrakṣobhaṃ vinirdiśet
d nadīnāṃ srotaso 'kāle dyotayanti mahābhayam
d vanaspatiḥ pūjyamānaḥ pūjito 'pūjito 'pi vā
d yadā bhajyeta vātena bhidyate namate 'pi vā
d agnivāyubhayaṃ vidyāc chreṣṭho vātra vinaśyati
d diśaḥ sarvāś ca dīpyante jāyante rājavibhramāḥ
d chidyamāno yadā vṛkṣo vinadec cāpi pātitaḥ
d saha rāṣṭraṃ ca nadati na taṃ vṛkṣaṃ prapātayet
d athainaṃ chedayet kaś cit pratikruddho vanaspatim
d chettā bhettā patiś caiva kṣipram eva vinaśyati
d devatānāṃ ca patanaṃ maṇḍapānāṃ ca ghuṣṭanam
d acalānāṃ prakampaś ca tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
d niśi cendradhanur dṛṣṭaṃ tato 'pi ca mahad bhayam
d tad draṣṭur eva bhītiḥ syān nānyeṣāṃ bharatarṣabha
d rātrāv indradhanur dṛṣṭvā tad rāṣṭraṃ parivarjayet
d devatā yatra nṛtyanti nadanti ca hasanti ca
d unmīlanti nimīlanti rāṣṭrakṣobhaṃ vinirdiśet
d śilā yatra prasiñcanti snehāṃś codakasaṃbhavān
d anyad vā vikṛtaṃ kiṃ cit tad bhayasya nidarśanam
d mriyate vā mahāmātro rājā saparivārakaḥ
d purasya vā bhaved vyādhī rāṣṭre deśe ca vibhramaḥ
d devatānāṃ yadāvāse rājñāṃ vā yatra veśmani
d bhāṇḍāgārāyudhāgāre niviśeta yadā madhu
d sarvaṃ tad dāhayet sthānaṃ hanyamānaṃ balīyasā
d āgantukaṃ bhayaṃ tatra bhaved ity eva nirdiśet
d pādapaś caiva yo yatra raktaṃ sravati śoṇitam
d dantāgrāt kuñjaro vāpi śṛṅgāgrād vṛṣabhas tathā
d pādapād rāṣṭravibhraṃśaḥ kuñjarād rājavibhramaḥ
d gobrāhmaṇavināśaḥ syād vṛṣabhasyeti nirdiśet
d chatraṃ narapater yasya nipatet pṛthivītale
d sa sarāṣṭro narapatiḥ kṣipram eva vinaśyati
d devāgāreṣu vā yatra rājño vā yatra veśmani
d vikṛtaṃ yadi dṛśyeta nāgāvāseṣu vā punaḥ
d tasya deśasya pīḍā syād rājño janapadasya vā
d anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ durbhikṣam iti nirdiśet
d bāhubhaṅge tu devānāṃ grahasthānāṃ bhayaṃ bhavet
d bhagne praharaṇe vidyāt senāpativināśanam
d āgantukā ca pratimā sthānaṃ yatra na vindati
d abhyantareṇa ṣaṇmāsād rājā tyajati tat puram
d pradīryate mahī yatra vinadaty api pātyate
d mriyate tatra rājā ca tac ca rāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati
d eṇīpadān vā sarpān vā ḍuṇḍubhān atha dīpyakān
d maṇḍūko grasate yatra tatra rājā vinaśyati
d abhinnaṃ vāpy apakvaṃ vā yatrānnam upacīyate
d jīryante vā mriyante vā tad annaṃ nopabhujyate
d udapāne ca yatrāpo vivardhante yudhiṣṭhira
d sthāvareṣu pravartante nirgacchec ca punas tataḥ
d apādaṃ vā tripādaṃ vā dviśīrṣaṃ vā caturbhujam
d striyo yatra prasūyante brūyāt tatra parābhavam
d hastinī mahiṣī gaur vā kharoṣṭram atha sūkaram
d īdṛśāni prajāyante vidyāt tatra parābhavam
d ajaiḍakāḥ striyo gāvo 'vayaś cānye 'pi yonayaḥ
d vikṛtāni prajāyante tatra tatra parābhavaḥ
d nadī yatra pratisrotam āvahet kaluṣodakam
d nāradaḥ
d diśaś ca na prakāśante tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
d etāni tu nimittāni yāni cānyāni bhārata
d keśavād eva jāyante bhaumāni ca khagāni ca
d candrādityau grahāś caiva nakṣatrāṇi ca bhārata
d vāyur agnis tathaivāpaḥ pṛthivī ca janārdanāt
d yasya deśasya hāniṃ vā vṛddhiṃ vā kartum icchati
d tasmin deśe nimittāni tāni tāni karoty ayam
d yo 'sau cedipates tāta vināśaḥ samupasthitaḥ
d nivedayati govindaḥ svair upāyair na saṃśayaḥ
d iyaṃ pracalitā bhūmir aśivaṃ vānti mārutāḥ
d rāhuś cāpy apatat somam aparvaṇi viśāṃ pate
d sanirghātāḥ patanty ulkās tamaḥ saṃjāyate bhṛśam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d cedirājavināśāya harir eṣa vijṛmbhate
d evam uktvā tu bhagavān nārado virarāma ha
d tābhyāṃ puruṣasiṃhābhyāṃ tasmin yuddha upasthite
d dadṛśur bhūmipālās te ghorān autpātikān bahūn
d tatra tair dṛśyamānānāṃ dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata
d aśrūyanta tadā rājañ śivānām aśivā giraḥ
d rarāsa ca mahī kṛtsnā savṛkṣapuraparvatā
d aparvaṇi ca madhyāhne sūryaṃ svarbhānur agrasat
d dhvajāgre cedirājasya sarvaratnapariṣkṛte
d apatat khāc cyuto gṛdhras tīkṣṇatuṇḍaḥ paraṃtapa
d āraṇyaiḥ saha saṃhṛṣṭā grāmyāś ca mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
d cakruśur bhairavaṃ tatra tasmin yuddha upasthite
d evamādīni ghorāṇi bhaumāni ca khagāni ca
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d autpātikāny adṛśyanta saṃkruddhe śārṅgadhanvini
d mahad viṣphārayan rājā tataś cedipatir dhanuḥ
d abhiyāsyan hṛṣīkeśam uvāca madhusūdanam
d ekas tvam asi me śatrus tat tvāṃ hatvādya mādhava
d tataḥ sāgaraparyantāṃ pālayiṣyāmi medinīm
d dvairathaṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ yan me tad idaṃ paryupasthitam
d cirasya bata me diṣṭyā vāsudeva saha tvayā
d adya tvāṃ nihaniṣye 'haṃ bhīṣmaṃ ca saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
d evam uktvā sa taṃ bāṇair niśitair āptatejanaiḥ
d vivyādha yudhi tīkṣṇāgraiś cedirāḍ yadupuṅgavam
d kaṅkapatracchadā bāṇāś cedirājadhanuścyutāḥ
d viviśus te tadā kṛṣṇaṃ bhujaṅgā iva parvatam
d nādadānasya caidyasya śarān atyasyato 'pi vā
d dadṛśus te 'ntaraṃ ke cid gatiṃ vāyor ivāmbare
d cedirājamahāmeghaḥ śarajālāmbumāṃs tadā
d abhyavarṣad dhṛṣīkeśaṃ payoda iva parvatam
d tataḥ śārṅgam amitraghnaṃ kṛtvā saśaram acyutaḥ
d ābabhāṣe mahābāhuḥ sunīthaṃ paravīrahā
d ayaṃ tvāṃ māmakas tīkṣṇaś cedirāja mahāśaraḥ
d bhettum arhati vegena mahāśanir ivācalam
d evaṃ bruvati govinde tataś cedipatiḥ punaḥ
d mumoca niśitān anyān kṛṣṇaṃ prati śarān bahūn
d atha bāṇārditaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śārṅgam āyamya dīptimān
d mumoca niśitān bāṇāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
d tāñ śarāṃs tu sa ciccheda śaravarṣaiś ca cedirāṭ
d ṣaḍbhiś cānyair jaghānāśu keśavaṃ cedipuṅgavaḥ
d tato 'straṃ sahasā kṛṣṇaḥ pramumoca jagatpatiḥ
d astreṇaiva mahābāhur nāśayām āsa cedirāṭ
d tataḥ śatasahasreṇa śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
d sarvataḥ samavākīrya śauriṃ dāmodaraṃ tadā
d nanāda balavān kruddhaḥ śiśupālaḥ pratāpavān
d idaṃ covāca saṃkruddhaḥ keśavaṃ paravīrahā
d adyāṅgaṃ māmakā bāṇā bhetsyanti tava saṃyuge
d hatvā tvāṃ sasutāmātyān pāṇḍavāṃś ca tarasvinaḥ
d ānṛṇyam adya yāsyāmi jarāsaṃdhasya dhīmataḥ
d kaṃsasya keśinaś caiva narakasya tathaiva ca
d ity uktvā krodhatāmrākṣaḥ śiśupālo janārdanam
d adṛśyaḥ śaravarṣeṇa sarvataḥ samavākirat
d tato 'streṇaiva bhagavān akṛntata śarān bahūn
d nikṛtya ca śarān sarvān antardhātuṃ pracakrame
d antardhānagatau vīrau śuśubhāte mahābalau
d sādhu sādhv iti bhūtāni pūjayām āsur ambare
d na dṛṣṭapūrvam asmābhir yuddham īdṛśakaṃ purā
d tataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ jaghānāśu śiśupālas tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
d kṛṣṇo 'pi bāṇair vivyādha sunīthaṃ pañcabhir yudhi
d tataḥ sunīthaḥ saptatyā nārācair ardayad balī
d tato 'tividdhaḥ kṛṣṇena sunīthaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
d vivyādha niśitair bāṇair vāsudevaṃ stanāntare
d punaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ tribhir viddhvā nanādāvasare nṛpaḥ
d tato 'tidāruṇaṃ yuddhaṃ sahasā cakratuḥ śaraiḥ
d tau nakhair iva śārdūlau dantair iva gajottamau
d daṃṣṭrābhir iva pañcāsyau tuṇḍakair iva kukkuṭau
d dārayetāṃ śarais tīkṣṇair anyonyaṃ yudhi tāv ubhau
d tato mumucatuḥ kruddhau śaravarṣam anuttamam
d śarair eva śarāñ chittvā tāv ubhau puruṣarṣabhau
d cakrāte 'stramayaṃ yuddhaṃ ghoraṃ tad atimānuṣam
d āgneyam astraṃ mumuce śiśupālaḥ pratāpavān
d vāruṇenāstrayogena nāśayām āsa keśavaḥ
d kauberam astraṃ sahasā cedirāṭ pramumoca ha
d kaubereṇaiva sahasānāśayaj jagataḥ prabhuḥ
d yāmyam astraṃ tataḥ kruddho mumuce kālamohitaḥ
d yāmyenaivāstrayogena yāmyam astraṃ vyanāśayat
d gāndharveṇa ca gāndharvaṃ mānavaṃ mānavena ca
d vāyavyena ca vāyavyaṃ raudraṃ raudreṇa cābhibhūḥ
d aindram aindreṇa bhagavān vaiṣṇavena ca vaiṣṇavam
d evam astrāṇi kurvāṇau yuyudhāte mahābalau
d tato māyāṃ vikurvāṇo damaghoṣasuto balī
d gadāmusalavarṣaṃ tac chaktitomarasāyakān
d paraśvathamusuṇṭhīnāṃ pātayām āsa cedirāṭ
d amoghāstreṇa bhagavān vyanāśayata keśavaḥ
d śilāvarṣaṃ mahāghoraṃ pātayām āsa keśave
d vajrāstreṇābhisaṃkruddhaś cūrṇam evākarot prabhuḥ
d jalavarṣaṃ tato ghoraṃ vyasṛjac cedipuṃgavaḥ
d vāyavyāstreṇa bhagavān vyākṣipac chataśo hariḥ
d nihatya sarvamāyāṃ vai sunīthasya janārdanaḥ
d sa muhūrtaṃ cakārāśu dvaṃdvayuddhaṃ mahārathaḥ
d sa bāṇayuddhaṃ kurvāṇo bhartsayām āsa cedirāṭ
d damaghoṣasuto dhṛṣṭam uvāca yadunandanam
d adya kṛṣṇam akṛṣṇaṃ tu kurvantu mama sāyakāḥ
d ity evam uktvā duṣṭātmā śaravarṣaṃ janārdane
d mumoca puruṣavyāghro ghoram āsthāya tadvapuḥ
d śarasaṃkṛttagātras tu kṣaṇena yadunandanaḥ
d rudhiraṃ parisusrāva so 'tīva puruṣottamaḥ
d na yantā na ratho vāpi na cāśvāḥ parvatopamāḥ
d dṛśyante śarasaṃchannā āvignam abhavaj jagat
d keśavaṃ tadavasthaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā bhūtāni cukruśuḥ
d dārukas tu tadā prāha keśavaṃ paravīrahā
d nedṛśo dṛṣṭapūrvo hi saṃgrāmo yādṛśo mayā
d sthātavyam iti tiṣṭhāmi tvatprabhāveṇa mādhava
d anyathā na ca me prāṇā dhārayeyur janārdana
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d iti saṃcintya govinda kṣipram eva vadhaṃ kuru
d evam uktas tu sūtena keśavo vākyam abravīt
d eṣa hy atibalo daityo hiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā
d ripuḥ surāṇāṃ daityendro varadānena garvitaḥ
d athāsīd rāvaṇo nāma rākṣasendro 'tivīryavān
d tenaiva balavīryeṇa balaṃ nāgaṇayan mama
d ahaṃ mṛtyuś ca bhavitā kāle kāle durātmanaḥ
d na bhetavyaṃ tvayā sūta naiṣa kaś cin mayi sthite
d ity evam uktvā bhagavān nanarda garuḍadhvajaḥ
d pāñcajanyaṃ mahāśaṅkhaṃ pūrayām āsa keśavaḥ
d saṃmohayitvā bhagavāṃś cakraṃ divyaṃ samādade
d ciccheda ca sunīthasya śiraś cakreṇa saṃyuge
a tatas tad vacanaṃ śrutvā śiśupālaḥ pratāpavān
c jahāsa svanavad dhāsaṃ prahasyedam uvāca ha
a matpūrvāṃ rukmiṇīṃ kṛṣṇa saṃsatsu parikīrtayan
c viśeṣataḥ pārthiveṣu vrīḍāṃ na kuruṣe katham
a manyamāno hi kaḥ satsu puruṣaḥ parikīrtayet
c anyapūrvāṃ striyaṃ jātu tvad anyo madhusūdana
a kṣama vā yadi te śraddhā mā vā kṛṣṇa mama kṣama
c kruddhād vāpi prasannād vā kiṃ me tvatto bhaviṣyati
a tathā bruvata evāsya bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ
b āgacchantaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā śiśupālaṃ sa durmatim
b pārśvasthaṃ cakram ādāya preṣayan sa durātmani
b aparādhaśataṃ tasya kṣamitvālokya sarvaśaḥ
b udapātram upālabhya cakrārthaṃ ca tadānagha
b taptacāmīkarābhāsaṃ kṣiptaṃ tasyaiva durmateḥ
b cakraṃ ca tat kṛṣṇakaraprabhāsaṃ
b jahāra tasyāṅgam anuttamaṃ tathā
b babhau pṛthivyāṃ patitaṃ sakuṇḍalaṃ
b hā heti śabdaḥ samabhūt sabhāyām
b manasācintayac cakraṃ daityavarganiṣūdanam
b etasminn eva kāle tu cakre hastagate sati
b uvāca bhagavān uccair vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
b śṛṇvantu me mahīpālā yenaitat kṣamitaṃ mayā
b aparādhaśataṃ kṣāmyaṃ māturasyaiva yācataḥ
b dattaṃ mayā yācitaṃ ca tad vai pūrṇaṃ hi pārthivāḥ
b adhunā mārayiṣyāmi paśyatāṃ vo mahīkṣitām
b evam uktvā yaduśreṣṭhaś cedirājasya tatkṣaṇāt
c vyapāharac chiraḥ kruddhaś cakreṇāmitrakarṣaṇaḥ
e sa papāta mahābāhur vajrāhata ivācalaḥ
a tataś cedipater dehāt tejo 'gryaṃ dadṛśur nṛpāḥ
c utpatantaṃ mahārāja gaganād iva bhāskaram
a tataḥ kamalapatrākṣaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ lokanamaskṛtam
b stutyaṃ trailokyavandyaṃ tam astotāram ajaṃ vibhum
c vavande tat tadā tejo viveśa ca narādhipa
a tad adbhutam amanyanta dṛṣṭvā sarve mahīkṣitaḥ
c yad viveśa mahābāhuṃ tat tejaḥ puruṣottamam
a anabhre pravavarṣa dyauḥ papāta jvalitāśaniḥ
c kṛṣṇena nihate caidye cacāla ca vasuṃdharā
a tataḥ ke cin mahīpālā nābruvaṃs tatra kiṃ cana
c atītavākpathe kāle prekṣamāṇā janārdanam
a hastair hastāgram apare pratyapīṣann amarṣitāḥ
c apare daśanair oṣṭhān adaśan krodhamūrchitāḥ
a rahas tu ke cid vārṣṇeyaṃ praśaśaṃsur narādhipāḥ
c ke cid eva tu saṃrabdhā madhyasthās tv apare 'bhavan
d ye devagandharvagaṇā rājāno bhuvi viśrutāḥ
d te praṇāmaṃ hṛṣīkeśe prakurvanti mahātmani
d ye tv āsuragaṇāt pakṣāt saṃbhūtāḥ kṣatriyā iha
d te nindanti hṛṣīkeśaṃ durātmāno gatāyuṣaḥ
d prājāpatyagaṇā ye tu madhyasthāś ca mahātmani
d brahmarṣayaś ca siddhāś ca gandharvoragacāraṇāḥ
d te vai stuvanti govindaṃ divyair maṅgaḷasaṃyutaiḥ
d parasparaṃ ca nṛtyanti gītena vividhena ca
d upatiṣṭhanti govindaṃ prītiyuktā mahātmani
a prahṛṣṭāḥ keśavaṃ jagmuḥ saṃstuvanto maharṣayaḥ
c brāhmaṇāś ca mahātmānaḥ pārthivāś ca mahābalāḥ
d śaśaṃsur nirvṛtāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇasya vikramam
a pāṇḍavas tv abravīd bhrātṝn satkāreṇa mahīpatim
c damaghoṣātmajaṃ vīraṃ saṃsādhayata mā ciram
d kururājavacaḥ śrutvā bhrātaras te tvarānvitāḥ
e tathā ca kṛtavantas te bhrātur vai śāsanaṃ tadā
a cedīnām ādhipatye ca putram asya mahīpatim
c abhyaṣiñcat tadā pārthaḥ saha tair vasudhādhipaiḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tataḥ pravavṛte yajño dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
d śāntavighnārhaṇakṣobho maharṣigaṇasaṃkulaḥ
d tasmin yajñe pravṛtte tu vāgvido hetuvādinaḥ
d hetuvādān bahūn prāhuḥ parasparajigīṣavaḥ
d dadṛśus taṃ nṛpatayo yajñasya vidhim uttamam
d upendrasyeva vihitaṃ sahadevena bhārata
d dadṛśus toraṇāny atra hematālamayāni ca
d dīptabhāskaratulyāni pradīptānīva tejasā
d sa yajñas toraṇais taiś ca grahair dyaur iva saṃbabhau
d śayyāsanavihārāṃś ca subahūn vittasaṃbhṛtān
d ghaṭān pātrīḥ kaṭāhāni kalaśāni samantataḥ
d na te kiṃ cid asauvarṇam apaśyaṃs tatra pārthivāḥ
d tadyajñe nyavasan rājan brāhmaṇā bhṛśasatkṛtāḥ
d kathayantaḥ kathā bahvīḥ paśyanto naṭanartakān
d bhuñjatāṃ caiva viprāṇāṃ svādu bhojyaṃ pṛthagvidham
d aniśaṃ śrūyate tatra muditānāṃ mahāsvanaḥ
d dīyatāṃ dīyatām eṣāṃ bhujyatāṃ bhujyatām iti
d evaṃprakārāḥ saṃjalpāḥ śrūyante smātra nityaśaḥ
d odanānāṃ vikārāṇi svādūni vividhāni ca
d subahūni ca bhakṣyāṇi peyāni madhurāṇi ca
d dadur dvijānāṃ satataṃ rājapreṣyā mahādhvare
d pūrṇe śatasahasre tu viprāṇāṃ bhuñjatāṃ tadā
d sthāpitā tatra saṃjñābhūc chaṅkho 'dhmāyata nityaśaḥ
d muhur muhuḥ praṇādas tu tasya śaṅkhasya bhārata
d uttamaṃ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ taṃ śrutvā vismayam āgatāḥ
d evaṃ pravṛtte yajñe tu tuṣṭapuṣṭajanāyute
d annasya bahavo rājann utsedhāḥ parvatopamāḥ
d dadhikulyāś ca dadṛśuḥ sarpiṣāṃ ca hradāñ janāḥ
d jambūdvīpo hi sakalo nānājanapadāyutaḥ
d rājann adṛśyataikastho rājñas tasmin mahākratau
d tatra rājasahasrāṇi puruṣāṇāṃ tatas tataḥ
d gṛhītvā dhanam ājagmus tasya rājño mahākratau
d rājānaḥ sragviṇas tatra sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalāḥ
d tān paryaviviṣur viprāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
d vividhāny annapānāni lehyāni vividhāni ca
d teṣāṃ nṛpopabhogyāni brāhmaṇebhyo daduḥ sma te
d nānāvidhāni bhakṣyāṇi svādupuṣpaphalāni ca
d gulāni svādukṣaudrāṇi dadus te brāhmaṇeṣv iha
d etāni satataṃ bhuktvā tasmin yajñe dvijādayaḥ
d parāṃ prītiṃ yayuḥ sarve modamānās tadā bhṛśam
d evaṃ samuditaṃ sarvaṃ bahugodhanadhānyavat
d yajñavāṭaṃ nṛpā dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ
d ṛtvijaś ca yathāśāstraṃ rājasūyaṃ mahākratum
d pāṇḍavasya yathākālaṃ juhuvuḥ sarvayājakāḥ
d nirākrāmaṃś ca śāstrajñā vidhivat sarvaśikṣitāḥ
d vyāsadhaumyādayaḥ sarve vidhivat ṣoḍaśartvijaḥ
d svasvakarmāṇi cakrus te pāṇḍavasya mahākratau
d nāṣaḍaṅgavid atrāsīt sadasyo nābahuśrutaḥ
d nāvrato nānupādhyāyo na pāpo nākṣamo dvijaḥ
d na tatra kṛpaṇaḥ kaś cid daridro na babhūva ha
d kṣudhito duḥkhito vāpi prākṛto vāpi mānuṣaḥ
d bhojanaṃ bhojanārthibhyo dāpayām āsa sarvadā
d sahadevo mahātejāḥ satataṃ rājaśāsanāt
d saṃstare kuśalāś cāpi sarvakarmāṇi yājakāḥ
d divase divase cakrur yathāśāstrārthacakṣuṣaḥ
d brāhmaṇā vedaśāstrajñāḥ kathāś cakruś ca sarvadā
d remire ca kathānte tu sarve tasmin mahākratau
d sā vedir vedasaṃpannair devadvijamaharṣibhiḥ
d ābabhāse tadā kīrṇā nakṣatrair dyaur ivāmalā
d tato vai hemayūpāṃś ca sarvaratnasamācitān
d śobhārthaṃ kārayām āsa sahadevo mahādyutiḥ
d dadṛśus toraṇān yatra hematālamayāni ca
d sa yajñas toraṇais taiś ca grahair dyaur iva saṃbabhau
d tālānāṃ toraṇair haimair dantair iva diśāgajaiḥ
d dikṣu sarvāsu vinyastais tejobhir bhāskarair yathā
d sakirīṭair nṛpaiś caiva śuśubhe tat sadas tadā
d daivair anyaiś ca yakṣaiś ca uragair divyamānuṣaiḥ
d vidyādharagaṇaiḥ kīrṇaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
d sa rājasūyaḥ śuśubhe dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
d gandharvagaṇasaṃkīrṇaḥ śobhito 'psarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
d sa kiṃpuruṣagītaiś ca kiṃnarair upaśobhitaḥ
d nāradaś ca jagau tatra tumburuś ca mahādyutiḥ
d viśvāvasuś citrasenas tathānye gītakovidāḥ
d ramayanti sma tān sarvān yajñakarmāntareṣv atha
d tatra cāpsarasaḥ sarvāḥ sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
d nanṛtuś ca jaguś cātra nityaṃ karmāntareṣv atha
d itihāsapurāṇāni ākhyānāni ca sarvaśaḥ
d ūcur vai śabdaśāstrajñā nityaṃ karmāntareṣv atha
d bheryaś ca murajāś caiva ḍuṇḍukā gomukhāś ca ye
d śṛṅgavaṃśāmbujāś caiva śrūyante sma sahasraśaḥ
d loke 'smin sarvaviprāś ca vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca sarvaśaḥ
d sarve mlecchāḥ sarvavarṇāḥ sādimadhyāntajās tathā
d nānādeśasamutthaiś ca nānājātibhir āgataiḥ
d paryāpta iva loko 'yaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraniveśane
d bhīṣmadroṇādayaḥ sarve kuravaḥ sasuyodhanāḥ
d vṛṣṇayaś ca samagrāś ca pāñcālāś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
d yathārhaṃ sarvakarmāṇi cakrur dāsā iva kratau
d evaṃ pravṛtto yajñaḥ sa dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
d śuśubhe ca mahābāho somasyeva kratur yathā
d vastrāṇi kambalāṃś caiva prāvārāṃś caiva sarvadā
d niṣkahemajabhāṇḍāni bhūṣaṇāni ca sarvaśaḥ
d pradadau tatra satataṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d yāni tatra mahīpebhyo labdhavān dhanam uttamam
d tāni ratnāni sarvāṇi viprāṇāṃ pradadau tadā
a tataḥ sa kururājasya kratuḥ sarvasamṛddhimān
c yūnāṃ prītikaro rājan saṃbabhau vipulaujasaḥ
a śāntavighnaḥ sukhārambhaḥ prabhūtadhanadhānyavān
c annavān bahubhakṣyaś ca keśavena surakṣitaḥ
a samāpayām āsa ca taṃ rājasūyaṃ mahākratum
c taṃ tu yajñaṃ mahābāhur ā samāpter janārdanaḥ
e rarakṣa bhagavāñ śauriḥ śārṅgacakragadādharaḥ
f kotīsahasraṃ pradadau brāhmaṇānāṃ mahātmanām
f na kariṣyati tal loke kaś cid anyo mahīpatiḥ
f yājakāḥ sarvakāmaiś ca satataṃ tatṛpur dhanaiḥ
f tataś cāvabhṛthaḥ snātaḥ sa rājā pāṇḍunandanaḥ
f vyāsaṃ dhaumyaṃ ca prayato nāradaṃ ca mahāmatim
f sumantuṃ jaiminiṃ pailaṃ vaiśaṃpāyanam eva ca
f yājñavalkyaṃ kaṭhaṃ caiva kalāpaṃ ca mahaujasam
f sarvāṃś ca viprapravarān pūjayām āsa satkṛtān
f yuṣmatprabhāvāt prāpto 'yaṃ rājasūyo mahākratuḥ
f janārdanaprabhāvāc ca saṃpūrṇo me manorathaḥ
f atha yajñaṃ samāpyānte pūjayām āsa mādhavam
f baladevaṃ ca deveśaṃ bhīṣmādyāṃś ca kurūttamān
a tatas tv avabhṛthasnātaṃ dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c samastaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatram abhigamyedam abravīt
a diṣṭyā vardhasi dharmajña sāmrājyaṃ prāptavān vibho
c ājamīḍhājamīḍhānāṃ yaśaḥ saṃvardhitaṃ tvayā
e karmaṇaitena rājendra dharmaś ca sumahān kṛtaḥ
a āpṛcchāmo naravyāghra sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitāḥ
c svarāṣṭrāṇi gamiṣyāmas tad anujñātum arhasi
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ rājñāṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c yathārhaṃ pūjya nṛpatīn bhrātṝn sarvān uvāca ha
a rājānaḥ sarva evaite prītyāsmān samupāgatāḥ
c prasthitāḥ svāni rāṣṭrāṇi mām āpṛcchya paraṃtapāḥ
e te 'nuvrajata bhadraṃ vo viṣayāntaṃ nṛpottamān
a bhrātur vacanam ājñāya pāṇḍavā dharmacāriṇaḥ
c yathārhaṃ nṛpamukhyāṃs tān ekaikaṃ samanuvrajan
a virāṭam anvayāt tūrṇaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān
c dhanaṃjayo yajñasenaṃ mahātmānaṃ mahārathaḥ
a bhīṣmaṃ ca dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
a   viduraṃ ca mahāmatim
a saṃjayaṃ ca mahātmānaṃ
b droṇaṃ droṇāyaniṃ caiva sāmātyaṃ sasuhṛdgaṇam
c droṇaṃ ca sasutaṃ vīraṃ sahadevo mahārathaḥ
a nakulaḥ subalaṃ rājan sahaputraṃ samanvayāt
b śalyaṃ tu sasutaṃ vīraṃ satyakaḥ paravīrahā
b bhagadattaṃ ca rājānaṃ kausalyaṃ ca bṛhadbalam
b bhīṣmakaṃ saha putreṇa mātulaṃ ca mahāmatim
b dākṣiṇātyāṃś ca sarvāṃś ca haiḍimbaḥ samanuvrajat
c draupadeyāḥ sasaubhadrāḥ pārvatīyān mahīpatīn
a anvagacchaṃs tathaivānyān kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
c evaṃ saṃpūjitās te vai jagmur viprāś ca sarvaśaḥ
a gateṣu pārthivendreṣu sarveṣu bharatarṣabha
c yudhiṣṭhiram uvācedaṃ vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān
d kṛtārthaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ dṛṣṭvā siṃhāsanagataṃ nṛpam
d rocamānaṃ mahendrābhaṃ vāsudevo 'bravīd balī
a āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi dvārakāṃ kurunandana
c rājasūyaṃ kratuśreṣṭhaṃ diṣṭyā tvaṃ prāptavān asi
a tam uvācaivam uktas tu dharmarāṇ madhusūdanam
c tava prasādād govinda prāptavān asmi vai kratum
a samastaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ tvatprasādād vaśānugam
c upādāya baliṃ mukhyaṃ mām eva samupasthitam
d kathaṃ tvadgamanārthaṃ me vāṇī vitarate 'nagha
a na vayaṃ tvām ṛte vīra raṃsyāmeha kathaṃ cana
c avaśyaṃ cāpi gantavyā tvayā dvāravatī purī
a evam uktaḥ sa dharmātmā yudhiṣṭhirasahāyavān
c abhigamyābravīt prītaḥ pṛthāṃ pṛthuyaśā hariḥ
a sāmrājyaṃ samanuprāptāḥ putrās te 'dya pitṛṣvasaḥ
c siddhārthā vasumantaś ca sā tvaṃ prītim avāpnuhi
a anujñātas tvayā cāhaṃ dvārakāṃ gantum utsahe
b evam uktvā tataḥ śaurir bhaginīṃ vai pitus tadā
c subhadrāṃ draupadīṃ caiva sabhājayata keśavaḥ
a niṣkramyāntaḥpurāc caiva yudhiṣṭhirasahāyavān
c snātaś ca kṛtajapyaś ca brāhmaṇān svasti vācya ca
a tato meghavaraprakhyaṃ syandanaṃ vai sukalpitam
c yojayitvā mahārāja dārukaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ
a upasthitaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā tārkṣyapravaraketanam
b yudhiṣṭhirakirīṭibhyāṃ dattahasto yayau rathe
c pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya samāruhya mahāmanāḥ
e prayayau puṇḍarīkākṣas tato dvāravatīṃ purīm
f sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmā ca ratham āruhya satvarau
f vījayām āsatus tatra cāmarābhyāṃ hariṃ tadā
f baladevaś ca deveśo yādavāś ca sahasraśaḥ
f prayayū rājavat sarve dharmaputreṇa pūjitāḥ
f tataḥ sa saṃmataṃ rājā hitvā sauvarṇam āsanam
a taṃ padbhyām anuvavrāja dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ śrīmān vāsudevaṃ mahābalam
d kāryamānuṣarūpaṃ vai viṣṇuṃ sarvaguruṃ prabhum
d vāyor dūtanaraprakhyagatiṃ kurvāṇam agrataḥ
a tato muhūrtaṃ saṃgṛhya syandanapravaraṃ hariḥ
c abravīt puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a apramattaḥ sthito nityaṃ prajāḥ pāhi viśāṃ pate
c parjanyam iva bhūtāni mahādrumam ivāṇḍajāḥ
e bāndhavās tvopajīvantu sahasrākṣam ivāmarāḥ
a kṛtvā paraspareṇaivaṃ saṃvidaṃ kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
c anyonyaṃ samanujñāpya jagmatuḥ svagṛhān prati
a gate dvāravatīṃ kṛṣṇe sātvatapravare nṛpa
b yudhiṣṭhiro mahārājaḥ praviveśa puraṃ tataḥ
c eko duryodhano rājā śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
d sūtaputraś ca rādheyaḥ saha duḥśāsanādibhiḥ
d sarvakāmaguṇopetair arcyamānās tu bhārata
e tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ divyāyām ūṣatus tau nararṣabhau
f vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
f samāpte rājasūye tu kratuśreṣṭhe sudurlabhe
f śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto vyāsaḥ purastāt samapadyata
f so 'bhyayād āsanāt tūrṇaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
f pādyenāsanadānena pitāmaham apūjayat
f athopaviśya bhagavān kāñcane paramāsane
f āsyatām iti covāca dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
f athopaviṣṭaṃ rājānaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritam
f uvāca bhagavān vyāsas tattadvākyaviśāradaḥ
f diṣṭyā vardhasi kaunteya sāmrājyaṃ prāpya durlabham
f vardhitāḥ kuravaḥ sarve tvayā kurukulodvaha
f āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi pūjito 'smi viśāṃ pate
f evam uktaḥ sa kṛṣṇena dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
f abhivādyopasaṃgṛhya pitāmaham athābravīt
f yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
f saṃśayo dvipadāṃ śreṣṭha mamotpannaḥ sudurlabhaḥ
f tasya nānyo 'sti vaktā vai tvām ṛte dvijapuṃgava
f utpātāṃs trividhān prāha nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
f divyāṃś caivāntarikṣāṃś ca pārthivāṃś ca pitāmaha
f vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
f api caidyasya patanāc channam autpātikaṃ mahat
f rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā parāśarasutaḥ prabhuḥ
f kṛṣṇadvaipāyano vyāsa idaṃ vacanam abravīt
f trayodaśa samā rājann utpātānāṃ phalaṃ mahat
f sarvakṣatravināśāya bhaviṣyati viśāṃ pate
f tvām ekaṃ kāraṇaṃ kṛtvā kālena bharatarṣabha
f sametaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ kṣayaṃ yāsyati bhārata
f duryodhanāparādhena bhīmārjunabalena ca
f svapne drakṣyasi rājendra kṣapānte tvaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
f nīlakaṇṭhaṃ bhavaṃ sthāṇuṃ kāpāliṃ tripurāntakam
f ugraṃ rudraṃ paśupatiṃ mahādevam umāpatim
f haraṃ śarvaṃ vṛṣaṃ śūliṃ pinākiṃ kṛttivāsasam
f kailāsakūṭapratime vṛṣabhe 'vasthitaṃ śivam
f nirīkṣamāṇaṃ satataṃ pitṛrājāśritāṃ diśam
f evam īdṛśakaṃ svapnaṃ drakṣyasi tvaṃ viśāṃ pate
f mā tatkṛte hy anudhyāhi kālo hi duratikramaḥ
f svasti te 'stu gamiṣyāmi kailāsaṃ parvataṃ prati
f vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
f apramattaḥ sthito dāntaḥ pṛthivīṃ paripālaya
f evam uktvā sa bhagavān kailāsaṃ parvataṃ yayau
f kṛṣṇadvaipāyano vyāsaḥ saha śiṣyaiḥ śrutānugaiḥ
f gate pitāmahe rājā cintāśokasamanvitaḥ
f niḥśvasann uṣṇam asakṛt tam evārthaṃ vicintayan
f kathaṃ tu daivaṃ śakyeta pauruṣeṇa prabādhitum
f avaśyam eva bhavitā yad uktaṃ paramarṣiṇā
f tato 'bravīn mahātejāḥ sarvān bhrātṝn yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
f śrutaṃ vai puruṣavyāghrā yan māṃ dvaipāyano 'bravīt
f tadā tadvacanaṃ śrutvā maraṇe niścitā matiḥ
f sarvakṣatrasya nidhane yady ahaṃ hetur īpsitaḥ
f kālena nirmitas tāta ko mamārtho 'sti jīvataḥ
f evaṃ bruvantaṃ rājānaṃ phālgunaḥ pratyabhāṣata
f mā rājan kaśmalaṃ ghoraṃ prāviśo buddhināśanam
f saṃpradhārya mahārāja yat kṣamaṃ tat samācara
f tato 'bravīt satyadhṛtir bhrātṝn sarvān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
f dvaipāyanasya vacanaṃ tatraiva samacintayan
f adya prabhṛti bhadraṃ vaḥ pratijñāṃ me nibodhata
f trayodaśa samās tāta ko mamārtho 'sti jīvataḥ
f na pravakṣyāmi paruṣaṃ bhrātṝn anyāṃś ca pārthivān
f sthito nideśe jñātīnāṃ yokṣye tat samudāharan
f evaṃ me vartamānasya svasuteṣv itareṣu ca
f bhedo na bhavitā loke bhedamūlo hi vigrahaḥ
f vigrahaṃ dūrato rakṣan priyāṇy eva samācaran
f vācyatāṃ na gamiṣyāmi lokeṣu manujarṣabhāḥ
f bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya vacanaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ saṃniśamya tat
f tam eva samavartanta dharmarājahite ratāḥ
f saṃsatsu samayaṃ kṛtvā dharmarāḍ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
f pitṝṃs tarpya yathānyāyaṃ devatāś ca viśāṃ pate
f kṛtamaṅgalakalyāṇo bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
f gateṣu kṣatriyendreṣu sarveṣu bharatarṣabha
f yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sahāmātyaḥ praviveśa purottamam
f duryodhano mahārāja śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
f sabhāyāṃ ramaṇīyāyāṃ tatraivāste narādhipa
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a vasan duryodhanas tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ bharatarṣabha
c śanair dadarśa tāṃ sarvāṃ sabhāṃ śakuninā saha
a tasyāṃ divyān abhiprāyān dadarśa kurunandanaḥ
c na dṛṣṭapūrvā ye tena nagare nāgasāhvaye
a sa kadā cit sabhāmadhye dhārtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ
c sphāṭikaṃ talam āsādya jalam ity abhiśaṅkayā
a svavastrotkarṣaṇaṃ rājā kṛtavān buddhimohitaḥ
b tatrāpy enaṃ jano dṛṣṭvā jahasuḥ pāṇḍavās tadā
c durmanā vimukhaś caiva paricakrāma tāṃ sabhām
d tataḥ sthale nipatito durmanā vrīḍito nṛpaḥ
a tataḥ sphāṭikatoyāṃ vai sphāṭikāmbujaśobhitām
c vāpīṃ matvā sthalam iti savāsāḥ prāpataj jale
a jale nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā kiṃkarā jahasur bhṛśam
c vāsāṃsi ca śubhāny asmai pradadū rājaśāsanāt
d jahāsa jahasuś caiva kiṃkarāś ca suyodhanam
a tathāgataṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c arjunaś ca yamau cobhau sarve te prāhasaṃs tadā
d tato 'nyasmin sabhoddeśe punar duryodhano nṛpaḥ
a nāmarṣayat tatas teṣām avahāsam amarṣaṇaḥ
c ākāraṃ rakṣamāṇas tu na sa tān samudaikṣata
a punar vasanam utkṣipya pratariṣyann iva sthalam
c āruroha tataḥ sarve jahasus te punar janāḥ
d dvāraṃ tu pihitākāraṃ sphāṭikaṃ prekṣya bhūmipaḥ
d praviśann āhato mūrdhni vyāghūrṇita iva sthitaḥ
d tādṛkṣam aparaṃ dvāraṃ sphāṭikorukapāṭakam
d vighaṭṭayan karābhyāṃ tu niṣkramyāgre papāta ha
a dvāraṃ ca vivṛtākāraṃ lalāṭena samāhanat
c saṃvṛtaṃ ceti manvāno dvāradeśād upāramat
a evaṃ pralambhān vividhān prāpya tatra viśāṃ pate
c pāṇḍaveyābhyanujñātas tato duryodhano nṛpaḥ
a aprahṛṣṭena manasā rājasūye mahākratau
c prekṣya tām adbhutām ṛddhiṃ jagāma gajasāhvayam
a pāṇḍavaśrīprataptasya dhyānaglānasya gacchataḥ
c duryodhanasya nṛpateḥ pāpā matir ajāyata
d natuṣṭo dharmarājasya yajñam āsādya taṃ tadā
d jagāma svagṛhaṃ tv anyān ṛte duryodhano nṛpaḥ
d dṛṣṭvā yajñavibhūtiṃ tāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ yaśasvinām
d paśyato duḥkhadīnasya pāpā matir ajāyata
a pārthān sumanaso dṛṣṭvā pārthivāṃś ca vaśānugān
c kṛtsnaṃ cāpi hitaṃ lokam ākumāraṃ kurūdvaha
a mahimānaṃ paraṃ cāpi pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c duryodhano dhārtarāṣṭro vivarṇaḥ samapadyata
a sa tu gacchann anekāgraḥ sabhām evānucintayan
c śriyaṃ ca tām anupamāṃ dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
a pramatto dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putro duryodhanas tadā
c nābhyabhāṣat subalajaṃ bhāṣamāṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a anekāgraṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā śakuniḥ pratyabhāṣata
c duryodhana kutomūlaṃ niḥśvasann iva gacchasi
 duryodhana uvāca
a dṛṣṭvemāṃ pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yudhiṣṭhiravaśānugām
b devarṣiyakṣagandharvās tatrāgacchanti nityaśaḥ
b kṛṣṇas tu durmanās teṣāṃ vivardhayati saṃpadaḥ
b āturās tatra nīyante vyavahāravacodhikāḥ
b gandhānāṃ nātra gacchanti vikretāro mahāprabhāḥ
b kharoṣṭrāśvājakhaḍgānāṃ vikretāras tathā nṛpāḥ
b loke 'smin kauravaḥ śabdas tatraiva parivartate
b hariprasthapuradvāraṃ sadā tu nibiḍīkṛtam
b rathahastyaśvayānānāṃ rohaṇena sadā nṛṇām
c jitām astrapratāpena śvetāśvasya mahātmanaḥ
a taṃ ca yajñaṃ tathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthasya mātula
c yathā śakrasya deveṣu tathābhūtaṃ mahādyute
a amarṣeṇa susaṃpūrṇo dahyamāno divāniśam
c śuciśukrāgame kāle śuṣye toyam ivālpakam
a paśya sātvatamukhyena śiśupālaṃ nipātitam
c na ca tatra pumān āsīt kaś cit tasya padānugaḥ
a dahyamānā hi rājānaḥ pāṇḍavotthena vahninā
c kṣāntavanto 'parādhaṃ taṃ ko hi taṃ kṣantum arhati
a vāsudevena tat karma tathāyuktaṃ mahat kṛtam
c siddhaṃ ca pāṇḍaveyānāṃ pratāpena mahātmanām
a tathā hi ratnāny ādāya vividhāni nṛpā nṛpam
c upatiṣṭhanti kaunteyaṃ vaiśyā iva karapradāḥ
a śriyaṃ tathāvidhāṃ dṛṣṭvā jvalantīm iva pāṇḍave
c amarṣavaśam āpanno dahye 'ham atathocitaḥ
d evaṃ sa niścayaṃ kṛtvā tato vacanam abravīt
d punar gāndhāranṛpatiṃ dahyamāna ivāgninā
a vahnim eva pravekṣyāmi bhakṣayiṣyāmi vā viṣam
c apo vāpi pravekṣyāmi na hi śakṣyāmi jīvitum
a ko hi nāma pumāṃl loke marṣayiṣyati sattvavān
c sapatnān ṛdhyato dṛṣṭvā hānim ātmana eva ca
a so 'haṃ na strī na cāpy astrī na pumān nāpumān api
c yo 'haṃ tāṃ marṣayāmy adya tādṛśīṃ śriyam āgatām
a īśvaratvaṃ pṛthivyāś ca vasumattāṃ ca tādṛśīm
c yajñaṃ ca tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā mādṛśaḥ ko na saṃjvaret
a aśaktaś caika evāhaṃ tām āhartuṃ nṛpaśriyam
c sahāyāṃś ca na paśyāmi tena mṛtyuṃ vicintaye
a daivam eva paraṃ manye pauruṣaṃ tu nirarthakam
c dṛṣṭvā kuntīsute śubhrāṃ śriyaṃ tām āhṛtāṃ tathā
a kṛto yatno mayā pūrvaṃ vināśe tasya saubala
c tac ca sarvam atikramya sa vṛddho 'psv iva paṅkajam
a tena daivaṃ paraṃ manye pauruṣaṃ tu nirarthakam
c dhārtarāṣṭrā hi hīyante pārthā vardhanti nityaśaḥ
a so 'haṃ śriyaṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sabhāṃ tāṃ ca tathāvidhām
c rakṣibhiś cāvahāsaṃ taṃ paritapye yathāgninā
a sa mām abhyanujānīhi mātulādya suduḥkhitam
c amarṣaṃ ca samāviṣṭaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭre nivedaya
 śakunir uvāca
a duryodhana na te 'marṣaḥ kāryaḥ prati yudhiṣṭhiram
c bhāgadheyāni hi svāni pāṇḍavā bhuñjate sadā
d vidhānaṃ vividhākāraṃ paraṃ teṣāṃ vidhānataḥ
a anekair abhyupāyaiś ca tvayārabdhāḥ purāsakṛt
b ārabdhāpi mahārāja punaḥ punar ariṃdama
b utsāhavantaḥ puruṣā nāvasīdanti karmasu
c vimuktāś ca naravyāghrā bhāgadheyapuraskṛtāḥ
a tair labdhā draupadī bhāryā drupadaś ca sutaiḥ saha
c sahāyaḥ pṛthivīlābhe vāsudevaś ca vīryavān
d ajitaḥ so 'pi sarvair hi sadevāsuramānuṣaiḥ
d tattejasā pravṛddho 'sau tatra kā paridevanā
a labdhaś ca nābhibhūto 'rthaḥ pitryo 'ṃśaḥ pṛthivīpate
c vivṛddhas tejasā teṣāṃ tatra kā paridevanā
a dhanaṃjayena gāṇḍīvam akṣayyau ca maheṣudhī
c labdhāny astrāṇi divyāni tarpayitvā hutāśanam
a tena kārmukamukhyena bāhuvīryeṇa cātmanaḥ
c kṛtā vaśe mahīpālās tatra kā paridevanā
a agnidāhān mayaṃ cāpi mokṣayitvā sa dānavam
c sabhāṃ tāṃ kārayām āsa savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
a tena caiva mayenoktāḥ kiṃkarā nāma rākṣasāḥ
c vahanti tāṃ sabhāṃ bhīmās tatra kā paridevanā
a yac cāsahāyatāṃ rājann uktavān asi bhārata
c tan mithyā bhrātaro hīme sahāyās te mahārathāḥ
a droṇas tava maheṣvāsaḥ saha putreṇa dhīmatā
c sūtaputraś ca rādheyo gautamaś ca mahārathaḥ
d sa ekaḥ samare sarvān pāṇḍavān sahasomakān
d vijeṣyati mahābāhuḥ kiṃ sahāyaiḥ kariṣyasi
d bhīṣmaś ca puruṣavyāghro gautamaś ca mahārathaḥ
d jayadrathaś ca balavān kṛtāstro dṛḍhadhanvakaḥ
a ahaṃ ca saha sodaryaiḥ saumadattiś ca vīryavān
c etais tvaṃ sahitaḥ sarvair jaya kṛtsnāṃ vasuṃdharām
 duryodhana uvāca
a tvayā ca sahito rājann etaiś cānyair mahārathaiḥ
c etān eva vijeṣyāmi yadi tvam anumanyase
a eteṣu vijiteṣv adya bhaviṣyati mahī mama
c sarve ca pṛthivīpālāḥ sabhā sā ca mahādhanā
 śakunir uvāca
a dhanaṃjayo vāsudevo bhīmaseno yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca drupadaś ca sahātmajaiḥ
a naite yudhi balāj jetuṃ śakyāḥ suragaṇair api
c mahārathā maheṣvāsāḥ kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥ
a ahaṃ tu tad vijānāmi vijetuṃ yena śakyate
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ svayaṃ rājaṃs tan nibodha juṣasva ca
d śakuner vacanaṃ śrutvā kururājas tam abravīt
 duryodhana uvāca
a apramādena suhṛdām anyeṣāṃ ca mahātmanām
c yadi śakyā vijetuṃ te tan mamācakṣva mātula
 śakunir uvāca
a dyūtapriyaś ca kaunteyo na ca jānāti devitum
c samāhūtaś ca rājendro na śakṣyati nivartitum
d kapaṭe vijayaṃ śakyam anyathā jetum akṣamaḥ
a devane kuśalaś cāhaṃ na me 'sti sadṛśo bhuvi
c triṣu lokeṣu kaunteyaṃ taṃ tvaṃ dyūte samāhvaya
a tasyākṣakuśalo rājann ādāsye 'ham asaṃśayam
c rājyaṃ śriyaṃ ca tāṃ dīptāṃ tvadarthaṃ puruṣarṣabha
a idaṃ tu sarvaṃ tvaṃ rājñe duryodhana nivedaya
c anujñātas tu te pitrā vijeṣye taṃ na saṃśayaḥ
 duryodhana uvāca
a tvam eva kurumukhyāya dhṛtarāṣṭrāya saubala
c nivedaya yathānyāyaṃ nāhaṃ śakṣye niśaṃsitum
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a anubhūya tu rājñas taṃ rājasūyaṃ mahākratum
c yudhiṣṭhirasya nṛpater gāndhārīputrasaṃyutaḥ
d viveśa hastinapuraṃ duryodhanamatena saḥ
d bāḍham ity eva śakunir dṛḍhaṃ hṛdi cakāra ha
d asvasthatāṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā dhārtarāṣṭrasya pāpakṛt
d pāpaḥ pāpātmanā tena sametya pṛthivīkṣitām
d bhāratānāṃ ca duṣṭātmā kṣayāya hi nṛpakṣayam
a priyakṛn matam ājñāya pūrvaṃ duryodhanasya tat
b vaiśasaṃ sarvalokasya hṛdi kṛtvā sudurmatiḥ
b daivena vidhinā caiva coditaḥ krūrakarmakṛt
c prajñācakṣuṣam āsīnaṃ śakuniḥ saubalas tadā
a duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipam
c upagamya mahāprājñaṃ śakunir vākyam abravīt
a duryodhano mahārāja vivarṇo hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ
c dīnaś cintāparaś caiva tad viddhi bharatarṣabha
a na vai parīkṣase samyag asahyaṃ śatrusaṃbhavam
c jyeṣṭhaputrasya śokaṃ tvaṃ kimarthaṃ nāvabudhyase
d evam uktaḥ śakuninā dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
d duryodhanaṃ samāhūya idaṃ vacanam abravīt
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a duryodhana kutomūlaṃ bhṛśam ārto 'si putraka
c śrotavyaś cen mayā so 'rtho brūhi me kurunandana
a ayaṃ tvāṃ śakuniḥ prāha vivarṇaṃ hariṇaṃ kṛśam
c cintayaṃś ca na paśyāmi śokasya tava saṃbhavam
a aiśvaryaṃ hi mahat putra tvayi sarvaṃ samarpitam
c bhrātaraḥ suhṛdaś caiva nācaranti tavāpriyam
d tvaddattaṃ caiva bhuñjāmo gāndhārī cāham eva ca
a ācchādayasi prāvārān aśnāsi piśitaudanam
c ājāneyā vahanti tvāṃ kenāsi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ
a śayanāni mahārhāṇi yoṣitaś ca manoramāḥ
c guṇavanti ca veśmāni vihārāś ca yathāsukham
a devānām iva te sarvaṃ vāci baddhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
c sa dīna iva durdharṣaḥ kasmāc chocasi putraka
d mātrā pitrā ca putrasya yad vai kāryaṃ paraṃ smṛtam
d prāptas tvam asi tat tāta nikhilāṃ naḥ kulaśriyam
d upasthitaḥ sarvakāmais tridive vāsavo yathā
d vividhair annapānaiś ca pravaraiḥ kiṃ nu śocasi
d adhītavān kṛtavidyaḥ priyo me lāḷito gṛhe
d niruktaṃ nigamaṃ chandaḥ saṣaḍaṅgārthaśāstravān
d adhītaḥ kṛtavidyas tvam aṣṭavyākaraṇaiḥ kṛpāt
d halāyudhāt kṛpād droṇād astravidyāṃ tv adhītavān
d bhrātṛjyeṣṭhaḥ sthito rājye kiṃ nu śocasi putraka
d pṛthagjanair atulyaṃ yad aśanācchādanaṃ bahu
d prabhus tvaṃ bhuñjase putra saṃstutaḥ sūtamāgadhaiḥ
d tasya te viditaprajña śokamūlam idaṃ katham
d loke 'smiñ jyeṣṭhabhāgyo 'nyas tan mamācakṣva putraka
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā mandaḥ krodhavaśānugaḥ
d pitaraṃ pratyuvācedaṃ svāṃ matiṃ saṃprakāśayan
 duryodhana uvāca
a aśnāmy ācchādaye cāhaṃ yathā kupuruṣas tathā
c amarṣaṃ dhāraye cograṃ titikṣan kālaparyayam
a amarṣaṇaḥ svāḥ prakṛtīr abhibhūya pare sthitāḥ
c kleśān mumukṣuḥ parajān sa vai puruṣa ucyate
a saṃtoṣo vai śriyaṃ hanti abhimānaś ca bhārata
c anukrośabhaye cobhe yair vṛto nāśnute mahat
a na mām avati tad bhuktaṃ śriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhire
c jvalantīm iva kaunteye vivarṇakaraṇīṃ mama
a sapatnān ṛdhyato ''tmānaṃ hīyamānaṃ niśāmya ca
c adṛśyām api kaunteye sthitāṃ paśyann ivodyatām
e tasmād ahaṃ vivarṇaś ca dīnaś ca hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ
a aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi snātakā gṛhamedhinaḥ
c triṃśaddāsīka ekaiko yān bibharti yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a daśānyāni sahasrāṇi nityaṃ tatrānnam uttamam
c bhuñjate rukmapātrībhir yudhiṣṭhiraniveśane
d śatror ṛddhiviśeṣeṇa virūpo 'nnavivarjitaḥ
a kadalīmṛgamokāni kṛṣṇaśyāmāruṇāni ca
c kāmbojaḥ prāhiṇot tasmai parārdhyān api kambalān
a rathayoṣidgavāśvasya śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c triṃśataṃ coṣṭravāmīnāṃ śatāni vicaranty uta
d rājāno balim ādāya sametā hi nṛpakṣaye
a pṛthagvidhāni ratnāni pārthivāḥ pṛthivīpate
c āharan kratumukhye 'smin kuntīputrāya bhūriśaḥ
a na kva cid dhi mayā dṛṣṭas tādṛśo naiva ca śrutaḥ
c yādṛg dhanāgamo yajñe pāṇḍuputrasya dhīmataḥ
d asatyaṃ ced idaṃ sarvaṃ saṃjayaṃ praṣṭum arhasi
a aparyantaṃ dhanaughaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā śatror ahaṃ nṛpa
c śarma naivādhigacchāmi cintayāno 'niśaṃ vibho
a brāhmaṇā vāṭadhānāś ca gomantaḥ śatasaṃghaśaḥ
c traikharvaṃ balim ādāya dvāri tiṣṭhanti vāritāḥ
a kamaṇḍalūn upādāya jātarūpamayāñ śubhān
c evaṃ baliṃ samādāya praveśaṃ lebhire tataḥ
a yan naiva madhu śakrāya dhārayanty amarastriyaḥ
c tad asmai kāṃsyam āhārṣīd vāruṇaṃ kalaśodadhiḥ
a śaikyaṃ rukmasahasrasya bahuratnavibhūṣitam
b śaṅkhapravaram ādāya vāsudevo 'bhiṣiktavān
c dṛṣṭvā ca mama tat sarvaṃ jvararūpam ivābhavat
a gṛhītvā tat tu gacchanti samudrau pūrvadakṣiṇau
c tathaiva paścimaṃ yānti gṛhītvā bharatarṣabha
d jalārthaṃ tatra rājendra ghaṭān ādāya rākṣasāḥ
d diśo yayur jalārthaṃ te varjayitvottarāṃ diśam
a uttaraṃ tu na gacchanti vinā tāta patatribhiḥ
b tatra gatvārjuno daṇḍam ājahārāmitaṃ dhanam
b kṛtāṃ baindusaroratnair mayena sphāṭikacchadām
b apaśyaṃ nalinīṃ pūrṇām udakasyeva bhārata
b utkarṣantaṃ ca vai vāsaḥ prāhasan māṃ vṛkodaraḥ
b kiṃkarāś ca sabhāpālā jahasur bharatarṣabha
b pitror arthe viśeṣeṇa prāvṛṇvaṃ tatra jīvitam
b tatra sma yadi śaktaḥ syāṃ ghātayeyaṃ vṛkodaram
b sapatnenāpahāso hi sa māṃ dahati bhārata
b tatra sphāṭikatoyāṃ hi sphāṭikāmbujaśobhitām
b sabhāṃ puṣkariṇīṃ matvā patito 'smi narādhipa
b tatra mām ahasad bhīmaḥ saha pārthena sasvaram
b draupadī ca saha strībhiḥ pātayantī mano mama
b klinnavastrasya ca jale kiṃkarā rājacoditāḥ
b dadur vāsāṃsi me 'nyāni tac ca duḥkhataraṃ mama
b astambhā iva tiṣṭhanti stambhāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
b so 'haṃ tatrāhato rājan sphaṭikābhyantare vibho
b chāyāḥ stambhā ivātiṣṭhañ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
b advāreṇa vinirgacchan dvārasaṃsthānarūpiṇā
b abhihatya śilāṃ bhūyo lalāṭenāsmi vikṣataḥ
b āmṛśan niyataṃ dṛṣṭvā mārgāntaram upāviśam
b striyaś ca tatra māṃ dṛṣṭvā jahasus tādṛśaṃ nṛpa
b idaṃ dvāram idaṃ rājan na dvāram iti māṃ prati
b agrataḥ prahasan vākyaṃ babhāṣe sa vṛkodaraḥ
b sarvaṃ hāsyakaraṃ teṣāṃ sadasyānāṃ nararṣabha
b na śrutāni na dṛṣṭāni yāni ratnāni me kva cit
b tāni me tatra dṛṣṭāni tena tapto 'smi duḥkhitaḥ
b hutāśanaṃ pravekṣyāmi praviśe vā mahodadhim
b saṃbhāvitasya cākīrtir maraṇād atiricyate
c idaṃ cādbhutam atrāsīt tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
a pūrṇe śatasahasre tu viprāṇāṃ pariviṣyatām
c sthāpitā tatra saṃjñābhūc chaṅkho dhmāyati nityaśaḥ
a muhur muhuḥ praṇadatas tasya śaṅkhasya bhārata
c uttamaṃ śabdam aśrauṣaṃ tato romāṇi me 'hṛṣan
a pārthivair bahubhiḥ kīrṇam upasthānaṃ didṛkṣubhiḥ
b aśobhata mahārāja nakṣatrair dyaur ivāmalā
c sarvaratnāny upādāya pārthivā vai janeśvara
a yajñe tasya mahārāja pāṇḍuputrasya dhīmataḥ
c vaiśyā iva mahīpālā dvijātipariveṣakāḥ
a na sā śrīr devarājasya yamasya varuṇasya vā
c guhyakādhipater vāpi yā śrī rājan yudhiṣṭhire
c   svayaṃ viṣṇor api prabho
c rākṣasādhipater vāpi
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍuputrasya śriyaṃ paramikām aham
c śāntiṃ na parigacchāmi dahyamānena cetasā
d aprāpya pāṇḍavaiśvaryaṃ śamo mama na vidyate
d avāpsye vā śriyaṃ bāṇaiḥ śayiṣye vā hataḥ paraiḥ
d atādṛśasya me kiṃ nu jīvitena paraṃtapa
d vardhante pāṇḍavā rājan vayaṃ hi sthitavṛddhayaḥ
 śakunir uvāca
a yām etām uttamāṃ lakṣmīṃ dṛṣṭavān asi pāṇḍave
c tasyāḥ prāptāv upāyaṃ me śṛṇu satyaparākrama
a aham akṣeṣv abhijñātaḥ pṛthivyām api bhārata
c hṛdayajñaḥ paṇajñaś ca viśeṣajñaś ca devane
a dyūtapriyaś ca kaunteyo na ca jānāti devitum
c āhūtaś caiṣyati vyaktaṃ dīvyāvety āhvayasva tam
c   dyūtād api raṇād api
c niyataṃ taṃ vijeṣyāmi kṛtvā tu kapaṭaṃ vibho
c ānayāmi samṛddhiṃ tāṃ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktaḥ śakuninā rājā duryodhanas tadā
c dhṛtarāṣṭram idaṃ vākyam apadāntaram abravīt
a ayam utsahate rājañ śriyam āhartum akṣavit
c dyūtena pāṇḍuputrasya tad anujñātum arhasi
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kṣattā mantrī mahāprājñaḥ sthito yasyāsmi śāsane
c tena saṃgamya vetsyāmi kāryasyāsya viniścayam
a sa hi dharmaṃ puraskṛtya dīrghadarśī paraṃ hitam
c ubhayoḥ pakṣayor yuktaṃ vakṣyaty arthaviniścayam
 duryodhana uvāca
a nivartayiṣyati tvāsau yadi kṣattā sameṣyati
b atha vā vāsudevaṃ vā bhīṣmaṃ vā kāryaniścaye
b āhūya mantraṇaṃ kuryāḥ kathaṃ vyavasitaṃ yataḥ
c nivṛtte tvayi rājendra mariṣye 'ham asaṃśayam
a sa mayi tvaṃ mṛte rājan vidureṇa sukhī bhava
c bhokṣyase pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ kiṃ mayā tvaṃ kariṣyasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ārtavākyaṃ tu tat tasya praṇayoktaṃ niśamya saḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bravīt preṣyān duryodhanamate sthitaḥ
a sthūṇāsahasrair bṛhatīṃ śatadvārāṃ sabhāṃ mama
c manoramāṃ darśanīyām āśu kurvantu śilpinaḥ
a tataḥ saṃstīrya ratnais tām akṣān āvāpya sarvaśaḥ
c sukṛtāṃ supraveśāṃ ca nivedayata me śanaiḥ
a duryodhanasya śāntyartham iti niścitya bhūmipaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭro mahārāja prāhiṇod vidurāya vai
a apṛṣṭvā viduraṃ hy asya nāsīt kaś cid viniścayaḥ
c dyūtadoṣāṃś ca jānan sa putrasnehād akṛṣyata
a tac chrutvā viduro dhīmān kalidvāram upasthitam
c vināśamukham utpannaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram upādravat
a so 'bhigamya mahātmānaṃ bhrātā bhrātaram agrajam
c mūrdhnā praṇamya caraṇāv idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a nābhinandāmi te rājan vyavasāyam imaṃ prabho
c putrair bhedo yathā na syād dyūtahetos tathā kuru
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kṣattaḥ putreṣu putrair me kalaho na bhaviṣyati
c divi devāḥ prasādaṃ naḥ kariṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
a aśubhaṃ vā śubhaṃ vāpi hitaṃ vā yadi vāhitam
c pravartatāṃ suhṛddyūtaṃ diṣṭam etan na saṃśayaḥ
a mayi saṃnihite caiva bhīṣme ca bharatarṣabhe
c anayo daivavihito na kathaṃ cid bhaviṣyati
a gaccha tvaṃ ratham āsthāya hayair vātasamair jave
c khāṇḍavaprastham adyaiva samānaya yudhiṣṭhiram
a na vāryo vyavasāyo me viduraitad bravīmi te
c daivam eva paraṃ manye yenaitad upapadyate
a ity ukto viduro dhīmān naitad astīti cintayan
a   idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a kulaṃ sabāndhavaṃ caitan
c āpageyaṃ mahāprājñam abhyagacchat suduḥkhitaḥ
 janamejaya uvāca
a kathaṃ samabhavad dyūtaṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ tan mahātyayam
c yatra tad vyasanaṃ prāptaṃ pāṇḍavair me pitāmahaiḥ
a ke ca tatra sabhāstārā rājāno brahmavittama
c ke cainam anvamodanta ke cainaṃ pratyaṣedhayan
a vistareṇaitad icchāmi kathyamānaṃ tvayā dvija
c mūlaṃ hy etad vināśasya pṛthivyā dvijasattama
 sūta uvāca
a evam uktas tadā rājñā vyāsaśiṣyaḥ pratāpavān
c ācacakṣe yathāvṛttaṃ tat sarvaṃ sarvavedavit
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śṛṇu me vistareṇemāṃ kathāṃ bharatasattama
c bhūya eva mahārāja yadi te śravaṇe matiḥ
a vidurasya mataṃ jñātvā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam uvāca vijane punaḥ
a alaṃ dyūtena gāndhāre viduro na praśaṃsati
c na hy asau sumahābuddhir ahitaṃ no vadiṣyati
a hitaṃ hi paramaṃ manye viduro yat prabhāṣate
c kriyatāṃ putra tat sarvam etan manye hitaṃ tava
a devarṣir vāsavagurur devarājāya dhīmate
c yat prāha śāstraṃ bhagavān bṛhaspatir udāradhīḥ
a tad veda viduraḥ sarvaṃ sarahasyaṃ mahākaviḥ
c sthitaś ca vacane tasya sadāham api putraka
a viduro vāpi medhāvī kurūṇāṃ pravaro mataḥ
c uddhavo vā mahābuddhir vṛṣṇīnām arcito nṛpa
a dyūtena tad alaṃ putra dyūte bhedo hi dṛśyate
c bhede vināśo rājyasya tat putra parivarjaya
d alam ardhaṃ kurūṇāṃ te rāṣṭrāṇām iha saṃmatam
d jñātibhir bhrātṛbhiś caiva sahito raṃsyase sukham
a pitrā mātrā ca putrasya yad vai kāryaṃ paraṃ smṛtam
c prāptas tvam asi tat tāta pitṛpaitāmahaṃ padam
a adhītavān kṛtī śāstre lālitaḥ satataṃ gṛhe
c bhrātṛjyeṣṭhaḥ sthito rājye vindase kiṃ na śobhanam
a pṛthagjanair alabhyaṃ yad bhojanācchādanaṃ param
c tat prāpto 'si mahābāho kasmāc chocasi putraka
a sphītaṃ rāṣṭraṃ mahābāho pitṛpaitāmahaṃ mahat
c nityam ājñāpayan bhāsi divi deveśvaro yathā
d yādṛśaṃ ca tavaiśvaryaṃ tad anyeṣāṃ sudurlabham
d ye copabhogās te rājan mayā pūrvaṃ prakīrtitāḥ
a tasya te viditaprajña śokamūlam idaṃ katham
c samutthitaṃ duḥkhataraṃ tan me śaṃsitum arhasi
 duryodhana uvāca
a aśnāmy ācchādayāmīti prapaśyan pāpapūruṣaḥ
b anyān svād adhikān rājan prapaśyann āptapūruṣaḥ
c nāmarṣaṃ kurute yas tu puruṣaḥ so 'dhamaḥ smṛtaḥ
a na māṃ prīṇāti rājendra lakṣmīḥ sādhāraṇā vibho
c jvalitām iva kaunteye śriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca vivyathe
a sarvāṃ hi pṛthivīṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiravaśānugām
c sthiro 'smi yo 'haṃ jīvāmi duḥkhād etad bravīmi te
a āvarjitā ivābhānti nighnāś caitrakikaukurāḥ
c kāraskarā lohajaṅghā yudhiṣṭhiraniveśane
a himavatsāgarānūpāḥ sarvaratnākarās tathā
c antyāḥ sarve paryudastā yudhiṣṭhiraniveśane
a jyeṣṭho 'yam iti māṃ matvā śreṣṭhaś ceti viśāṃ pate
c yudhiṣṭhireṇa satkṛtya yukto ratnaparigrahe
a upasthitānāṃ ratnānāṃ śreṣṭhānām arghahāriṇām
c nādṛśyata paraḥ prānto nāparas tatra bhārata
a na me hastaḥ samabhavad vasu tat pratigṛhṇataḥ
c prātiṣṭhanta mayi śrānte gṛhya dūrāhṛtaṃ vasu
a kṛtāṃ bindusaroratnair mayena sphāṭikacchadām
c apaśyaṃ nalinīṃ pūrṇām udakasyeva bhārata
a vastram utkarṣati mayi prāhasat sa vṛkodaraḥ
b kiṃkarāś ca sabhāpālā jahasur bharatarṣabha
c śatror ṛddhiviśeṣeṇa vimūḍhaṃ ratnavarjitam
a tatra sma yadi śaktaḥ syāṃ pātayeyaṃ vṛkodaram
b yadi kuryāṃ samārambhaṃ bhīmaṃ hantuṃ narādhipa
b śiśupāla ivāsmākaṃ gatiḥ syān nātra saṃśayaḥ
c sapatnenāvahāso hi sa māṃ dahati bhārata
a punaś ca tādṛśīm eva vāpīṃ jalajaśālinīm
c matvā śilāsamāṃ toye patito 'smi narādhipa
a tatra māṃ prāhasat kṛṣṇaḥ pārthena saha sasvanam
c draupadī ca saha strībhir vyathayantī mano mama
d bhṛtyavargaś ca yaḥ kaś cit so 'pi prahasate 'nagha
a klinnavastrasya ca jale kiṃkarā rājacoditāḥ
c dadur vāsāṃsi me 'nyāni tac ca duḥkhataraṃ mama
a pralambhaṃ ca śṛṇuṣvānyaṃ gadato me narādhipa
c advāreṇa vinirgacchan dvārasaṃsthānarūpiṇā
e abhihatya śilāṃ bhūyo lalāṭenāsmi vikṣataḥ
f striyaś ca tatra māṃ dṛṣṭvā jahasus tādṛśaṃ nṛpa
f idaṃ dvāram idaṃ rājann advāram iti māṃ prati
f agrataḥ prahasan vākyaṃ babhāṣe sa vṛkodaraḥ
a tatra māṃ yamajau dūrād ālokya lalitau kila
c bāhubhiḥ parigṛhṇītāṃ śocantau sahitāv ubhau
a uvāca sahadevas tu tatra māṃ vismayann iva
c idaṃ dvāram ito gaccha rājann iti punaḥ punaḥ
d bhīmasenena tatrokto dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajeti ca
d saṃbodhya prahasitvā ca ito dvāraṃ narādhipa
a nāmadheyāni ratnānāṃ purastān na śrutāni me
c yāni dṛṣṭāni me tasyāṃ manas tapati tac ca me
d hutāśanaṃ pravekṣyāmi praviśe vā mahodadhim
d saṃbhāvitasya cākīrtir maraṇād atiricyate
 tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ rājendra rājasūye mahākratau
 duryodhana uvāca
a yan mayā pāṇḍavānāṃ tu dṛṣṭaṃ tac chṛṇu bhārata
c āhṛtaṃ bhūmipālair hi vasu mukhyaṃ tatas tataḥ
a na vinde dṛḍham ātmānaṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ tad arer dhanam
c phalato bhūmito vāpi pratipadyasva bhārata
a aiḍāṃś cailān vārṣadaṃśāñ jātarūpapariṣkṛtān
c prāvārājinamukhyāṃś ca kāmbojaḥ pradadau vasu
a aśvāṃs tittirikalmāṣāṃs triśataṃ śukanāsikān
c uṣṭravāmīs triśataṃ ca puṣṭāḥ pīluśamīṅgudaiḥ
a govāsanā brāhmaṇāś ca dāsamīyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c prītyarthaṃ te mahābhāgā dharmarājño mahātmanaḥ
e trikharvaṃ balim ādāya dvāri tiṣṭhanti vāritāḥ
f brāhmaṇā vāṭadhānāś ca gomantaḥ śatasaṃghaśaḥ
a kamaṇḍalūn upādāya jātarūpamayāñ śubhān
b ratnāni ca hiraṇyaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ caiva kevalam
b prīyamāṇaḥ prasannātmā svayaṃ svajanasaṃvṛtaḥ
b traikharvo rathamukhyeśaḥ pāṇḍavāya nyavedayat
b yaś ca sa dvijamukhyena rājñaḥ śaṅkho niveditaḥ
b prītyā dattaḥ kuṇindena dharmarājāya dhīmate
b taṃ sarve bhrātaro bhrātre daduḥ śaṅkhaṃ kirīṭine
b taṃ pratyagṛhṇād bībhatsus toyajaṃ hemamālinam
b citaṃ niṣkasahasreṇa bhrājamānaṃ svatejasā
b ruciraṃ darśanīyaṃ ca bhūṣitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
b adhārayac ca dharmaś ca taṃ namasya punaḥ punaḥ
b yo 'nādane 'pi nadati sa nanādādhikaṃ tadā
b praṇādād bhūmipās tasya petur hīnāḥ svatejasā
b dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pāṇḍavāś ca sātyakiḥ keśavo 'ṣṭamaḥ
b sattvasthāḥ śauryasaṃpannā anyonyapriyakāriṇaḥ
b visaṃjñān bhūmipān dṛṣṭvā māṃ ca te prāhasaṃs tadā
b tataḥ prahṛṣṭo bībhatsur adadād dhemaśṛṅgiṇaḥ
b śatāny anaḍuhāṃ pañca dvijamukhyāya bhārata
b sumukhena balir mukhyaḥ preṣito 'jātaśatrave
b kuṇindena hiraṇyaṃ ca vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca
b kāśmīrarājo mādhvīkaṃ śuddhaṃ ca rasavan madhu
b baliṃ ca kṛtsnam ādāya pāṇḍavāyābhyupāharat
b yavanā hayān upādāya pārvatīyān mahājavān
b āsanāni mahārhāṇi kambalāṃś ca mahādhanān
b navān vicitrān sūkṣmāṃś ca parārdhyān supradarśanān
b anyac ca vividhaṃ ratnaṃ dvāri tiṣṭhanti vāritāḥ
b śrutāyur api kāliṅgo maṇiratnam anuttamam
b aṅgastriyo darśanīyā jātarūpavibhūṣitāḥ
b vaṅgo jāmbūnadamayān paryaṅkāñ śataśo nṛpa
b dakṣiṇāt sāgarābhyāśāt prāvārāṃś ca paraḥśatam
b audakāni ca ratnāni baliṃ cādāya bhārata
b anyebhyo bhūmipālebhyaḥ pāṇḍavāya nyavedayat
b dārdaraṃ candanaṃ mukhyaṃ bhārān ṣaṇṇavatiṃ dhruvam
b pāṇḍavāya dadau pāṇḍyaḥ śaṅkhāṃs tāvata eva ca
b candanāgaru cānantaṃ muktāvaiḍūryacitrakāḥ
b colaś ca keralaś cobhau dadatuḥ pāṇḍavāya vai
b aśmako hemaśṛṅgīś ca dogdhrīr hemavibhūṣitāḥ
b savatsāḥ kumbhadohāś ca gāḥ sahasrāṇy adād daśa
b saindhavānāṃ sahasrāṇi hayānāṃ pañcaviṃśatim
b adadāt saindhavo rājā hemamālyair alaṃkṛtān
b sauvīro hastibhir yuktān rathāṃś ca triṃśato varān
b jātarūpapariṣkārān maṇiratnavibhūṣitān
b madhyaṃdinārkapratimāṃs tejasāpratimān iva
b baliṃ ca kṛtsnam ādāya pāṇḍavāya nyavedayat
b avantirājo ratnāni vividhāni sahasraśaḥ
b hārāṅgadāṃś ca mukhyān vai vividhaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇam
b dāsīnām ayutaṃ caiva balim ādāya bhārata
b sabhādvāri naraśreṣṭha didṛkṣur avatiṣṭhate
b daśārṇaś cedirājaś ca śūrasenaś ca vīryavān
b baliṃ ca kṛtsnam ādāya pāṇḍavāya nyavedayat
b kāśirājena hṛṣṭena balī rājan niveditaḥ
b aśītigosahasrāṇi śatāny aṣṭau ca dantinām
b ayutaṃ ca nadījānāṃ hayānāṃ hemamālinām
b vividhāni ca ratnāni kāśirājo baliṃ dadau
b kṛtakṣaṇaś ca vaidehaḥ kausalaś ca bṛhadbalaḥ
b dadatur vājimukhyāṃś ca sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
b śaibyo vasātibhiḥ sārdhaṃ trigarto mālavaiḥ saha
b tasmai ratnāni dadatur ekaiko bhūmipo 'mitam
b hārāṃś ca mukhyān muktāṃś ca vividhaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇam
c evaṃ baliṃ pradāyātha praveśaṃ lebhire tataḥ
a śataṃ dāsīsahasrāṇāṃ kārpāsikanivāsinām
c śyāmās tanvyo dīrghakeśyo hemābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
e śūdrā viprottamārhāṇi rāṅkavāny ajināni ca
f te sarve pāṇḍuputrāya dvāry atiṣṭhan didṛkṣavaḥ
a baliṃ ca kṛtsnam ādāya bharukacchanivāsinaḥ
c upaninyur mahārāja hayān gāndhāradeśajān
a indrakṛṣṭair vartayanti dhānyair nadīmukhaiś ca ye
c samudraniṣkuṭe jātāḥ parisindhu ca mānavāḥ
